ādāya tṛptāḥstha śeṣam ca eva anumānya ca tat annam vikiret bhūmau dadyāt ca apaḥ sakṛt sakṛt sarvam annam upādāya sa tilam dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ucchiṣṭa sannidhau piṇḍān dadyāt vai pitṛ yajña vat mātāmahānām api evam dadyāt ācamanam tatas dattvā ca dakṣiṇām śaktyā svadhākāram udāharet vācyatām iti anujñātaḥ prakṛtebhyaḥ svadhā ucyatām viśvedevāḥ aprīyantām vipraiḥ ca uktaḥ idam japet dātāraḥ naḥ abhivarddhantām vedāḥ saṃtatiḥ eva ca vājevāje iti prītaḥ pitṛ pūrvam visarjanam yasmin te saṃśravāḥ pūrvam ardhya pātre niveśitāḥ pitṛpātram tat utthānam kṛtvā viprān visarjayet brahmacārī bhavet tām tu rajanīm saha evam pradakṣiṇa āvṛttyā vṛddhau nāndīmukhān pitṝn yajeta dadhi karkandhu miśrān piḍān yavaiḥ kṛtān ardhya artham pitṛpātreṣu pretapātram presecayet ye samānāḥ iti dvābhyām śeṣam pūrvavat ācaret sriyāḥ api arvāk sapiṇḍīkaraṇam yasya saṃvatsarāt bhavet tasya api annam sa udakuṃbham dadyāt saṃvatsaram dvije piṇḍān ca gaḥ aja viprebhyaḥ dadyāt agnau jale api vā mātsya hāriṇaka aurabhra śākuna chāga pārṣataiḥ aiṇa raurava vārāha śāśaiḥ māṃsaiḥ yathākramam māsa vṛddhyā abhitṛpyanti dattaiḥ iha pitāmahāḥ khaḍga āmiṣam mahā kalpam madhu muni annam eva ca loha āmiṣam mahāśākam māṃsam vārdhrīṇasasya ca tathā varṣā trayodaśyām maghāsu ca viśeṣataḥ kalyām kanyāvedinaḥ ca paśūn vai sat sutān api dyūtam kṛṣim ca vāṇijyam dviśapha ekaśaphaān tathā jñāti śreṣṭhyam sarva kāmān āpnoti śrāddha daḥ sadā pratipad prabhṛtiṣu ekām varjayitvā caturdaśīm svargam hi apatyam ojaḥ ca śauryam kṣetram balam tathā putrān śreṣṭhān ca saubhāgyam samṛddhim mukhya tām śubham pravṛttam cakratām ca eva vāṇijya prabhṛtīni ca arogi tvam yaśaḥ vīta śoka tām paramām gatim dhanam vidyām bhiṣaj siddhim kupī aṅgāḥ api ajāvikam vidhivat yaḥ śrāddham saṃprayacchati kṛttikā ādi bharaṇī antam sa kāmān āpnuyāt imān āstikaḥ śraddadhānaḥ ca vyapeta mada matsaraḥ vasu rudrāt iti sutāḥ pitaraḥ śrāddha devatāḥ prīṇayanti manuṣyāṇām pitṝn śrāddhena tarpitāḥ āyuḥ prajām dhanam vidyām svargam mokṣam sukhāni ca prayacchanti tathā rājyam nṛṇām prītāḥ pitāmahāḥ iti evam kathitam kiñcid kalpa adhyāye viśeṣataḥ jñātavyam vaidike tantre purāṇa antarake api ca yaḥ imam cintayet vidvān kalpādhyāyam muni īśvara yaḥ śṛṇoti naraḥ bhaktyā daive pitrye ca karmaṇi dhanam vidyām yaśaḥ putrān paratra ca gatim parām atas param vyākaraṇam tubhyam vedamukha abhidham kathayiṣye samāsena śṛṇuṣva su samāhitaḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne dvitīya pāde eka pañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha vyākaraṇam vakṣye saṃkṣepāt tava nārada sup tiṅ aṃtam padam vipra supām sapta vibhaktayaḥ svaujasaḥ prathamā proktā sā prātipadika ātmikā dvitīyā karmaṇi proktā antara antareṇa saṃyute ṭābhyām bhisaḥ tṛtīyā syāt karaṇe kartari īritā ṅe bhyām bhyasaḥ caturthaḥ syāt sam pradāne ca kārake pañcamī syāt ṅasi bhyāṃbhyaḥ hi apādāne ca kārake ṅas os āmaḥ ca ṣaṣṭhī syāt svāmi saṃbandha mukhyake ṅyoḥ supaḥ saptamī tu syāt sā ca adhikaraṇe bhavet ādhāre ca api vipra indra rakṣā arthānām prayogataḥ īpsitam ca anīpsitam yat tat apādānakam smṛtam lakṣaṇā itthaṃbhūtaḥ abhiḥ abhāge ca anu pari prati dvitīyā ca caturthī syāt ceṣṭāyām gati karmaṇi aprāṇiṣu vibhaktī dve manya jīvāyām karka ādau koṭi jam phalam tad bāhu phala varga aikyāt mūlakarṇaḥ cala abhidhaḥ saṃśodhyam tu tri jīvāyām karka ādau koṭi jam phalam tad bāhu phala varga aikyāt mūlam karṇaḥ cala abhidhaḥ labdhasya cāpam liptā ādi phalam śaidhryam idam smṛtam etat ādau kuja ādīnām caturthe ca eva karmaṇi śairdhyam mādyam punar māndyam śairghyam catvāri anukramāt ajāḥ dika indre sarveṣām māndye śairghye ca karmaṇi dhanam grahāṇām liptā ādi tulā ādau ṛṇam eva tat karka ādau tad dhanam tatra makara ādau ṛṇam smṛtam sva manda paridhi kṣuṇṇāḥ bhagaṇa aṃśa uddhṛtāḥ kalāḥ manda sphuṭa kṛtā bhuktiḥ śīghna ucca bhuktitaḥ tad śeṣam vivareṇa atha hanyāḥ trijyā aṅka karṇayoḥ ṛṇam ūne adhike prohya śeṣam vakra gatiḥ bhavet kṛta ṛtu candraiḥ veda indraiḥ śūnya tri ekaiḥ guṇa aṣṭabhiḥ śara rudraiḥ caturya aṃśuka indra aṃśeḥ bhūsuta ādayaḥ kramajyāḥ viṣuvat bhā ghnī kṣiti jyā dvādaśa uddhṛtā trijyā guṇā dina vyāsa bhaktā cāpam ca śatravaḥ bha bhogaḥ aṣṭaśatīḥ liptāḥ svāśiva śailoḥ tathā ā t titheḥ ravi indu yoga liptāḥ tu yoga ābha bhoga bhājitāḥ gatagamyāḥ ca ṣaṣṭi ghnāḥ bhukti yoga āpta nāḍikāḥ gatagamyāḥ ca ṣaṣṭi ghnāḥ na atas bhuktatara uddhṛtāḥ tithayaḥ śukla pratipadaḥ dvi ghnāḥ sā ekā na gāhatāḥ śeṣam bavaḥ bālavaḥ ca kaulavaḥ taitilaḥ garaḥ bhavet viṣṭiḥ kṛṣṇa bhūta apara arddhataḥ śakuniḥ nāgāḥ ca catuṣpada kiṃstughnam eva ca tatra śaka aṅgulaiḥ iṣṭaiḥ sama maṇḍalam ālikhet tad madhye sthāpayet śaṅkum kalpanā ddvādaśa aṅgulam tad chāyā agram spṛśet yatra dattam pūrva aparāhnayoḥ yāmya uttara diśoḥ madhye timinā pūrva paścimā caturaḥ tam bahis kuryāt sūtraiḥ madhyāt viniḥsṛtaiḥ bhuja sūtra aṅgulaiḥ tatra dattaiḥ iṣṭa prabhā matā prāṅ paścima āśritā rekhā procyate sama maṇḍalam bha maṇḍalam ca viṣuvat maṇḍalam parikīrtitam rekhā prācī aparā sādhyā viṣuvat bhā agrayā tathā iṣṭa chāyau iṣuvatoḥ madhye hi agrā abhidhīyate śaṅku chāyā ākṛti yuteḥ mūlam vargataḥ prohya śaṅku kṛte mūlam chāyā śeku viparyayāt triṃśat kṛtyaḥ yuge bhānām cakram prāk parilaṃbate vijñeyāḥ ayatānidhāḥ tad saṃsva kṛtāt hahāt kānti chāyā vara dala ādikam śaṅku chāyā hate trijye viṣuvat karka bhājite laṃba akṣa jye tayoḥ chāye laṃba akṣau dakṣimau sadā śeṣa hyāna aṃśāḥ sūryasya tad vāhujyā atha koṭijāḥ śaṅku māna aṅgula abhyaste bhuja trijye yathāṅkramam koṭī jyayā a vibhajya āpte chāyā karma abahirddale sva akṣa arka nata bhāgānām diś sāmye ataram anyathā graha udayāḥ prāṇa hatāḥ kha kha aṣṭa eka uddhatā gatiḥ cakra asavaḥ labdha yutī svar ahar rātra asavaḥ smṛtāḥ tri bhadyu karṇa arddha guṇā sva ahorātra arddha bhājitāḥ kramāt eka dvi tri bhagha ājyā tad cāpāni pṛthak pṛthak sva adhodhas praviśodhya atha meṣāt laṅkā udaya asavaḥ śara tri ekam himāṃśavaḥ sva deśa cara khaṇḍa ūnāḥ bhavanti iṣṭa udaya asavaḥ utkrameṇa ṣaṭ eva ete bhavanti iṣṭāḥ tulā ādayaḥ gata bhogya asavaḥ kāryāḥ sa ayanāḥ sva iṣṭa bhāskarāḥ sva udayāt su hatāḥ bhaktāḥ bhakta bhogyāḥ sva mānataḥ abhiṣṭa dhaṭikā asubhyaḥ bhogya asūn praviśodhayet tadvat eva eṣya lagna asūn evam vyāptāḥ tathā kramāt śeṣam triṃśat kramāt hi astam aśuddhena vibhājitam bhāga yuktam ca hīnam ca vyayana aṃśam tanuḥ kuje prāk paścāt nata nāḍībhyaḥ tadvat laṅkā udayāsubhiḥ bhogya asūn ūnakasya atha bhukta asūn adhikasya ca sapiṇḍyā antara lagna asūn evam syāt kāla sādhanam virāhu arka bhuja aṃśāḥ ced indra alpāḥ syāt grahaḥ vidhoḥ teṣām śiva ghnāḥ śaila āptāḥ śara aiṅgulaiḥ chādya chādaka māna ardham śara ūnam grāhya varjitam tat svacchannam ca māna aikya arddha aṃśa ṣaṣṭam daśa āhatam sthiti arddham ghaṭikā ādi syāt dvi aṅga bāhu aṃśa saṃmitaiḥ iṣṭaiḥ palaiḥ tat ūna āḍhyam vyagau ūneḥ a kaṣa aṅguṇaḥ grāsena su āhate chādyamāna āme syuḥ viśopakāḥ pūrṇa antam madhyam atra syāt darśa anta iñjam tri bhonakam pṛthak tad krānti akṣa bhāga saṃskṛtau syuḥ nata aṃśakāḥ tad dighna aṃśa kṛti dvi ūna arddha arka yutā hariḥ tri bha ana aṅga arka viśleṣa aṃśoḥ purandarāḥ śara ūna ulaṃbana ṣaṣ aghne tad lava āḍhya ūna vi tribhāt prādhṛtaḥ tad vivarjita śabda indu liptaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ tu bhakta ānatiḥ natiḥ nata aṃśa diś tayoḥ nāṭya ūha bhinna eka diś śaraḥ sphuṭa tām vrajet saṃskṛteḥ tābhyām sthiti arddhe bhavataḥ sphuṭe tābhyām hīna yutaḥ madhya darśaḥ kālau mukha anta gau arka ādi ūnāḥ viśve īśāḥ nava pañcadaśa aṃśakāḥ kāla aṃśāḥ taiḥ ūna yukte ravau hi asta udayau vidhoḥ dṛṣṭvā hi ādau kheṭa biṃbam dṛś auñcye laṃbam īkṣya ca tad luṃba pāpa biṃba antar dṛṇau vyāpta ravi ghna bhās aste sa avayavāḥ jñeyāḥ gataiṣyāḥ tithayaḥ budhaiḥ saṃskāra dika laṃbanam aṅgula ādyam prajāyate sa iṣu aśa ūnāḥ sitam tithyaḥ balat nāśa unnatam vidhoḥ śṛṅgam anyatra udvācyam balana aṅgula lekhanāt pañcatve goṅka viśikhāḥ śeṣa karṇa hatāḥ pṛthak vikṛjyaka aṅga siddha agni bhakta ālabdha ūna saṃyutāḥ trijyā adhika ūne śravaṇe vapūṃṣi syuḥ hṛtāḥ kujāt yutiḥ yāmya udak kheṭa vivaram mānaukya addhā ulpakam yadā yadā sphuṭa artham sūrya parva vat eka ayana gatau syātām sūryācandramasau yadā vipaṭīta ayana gatau candra ākāraiḥ krānti liptikāḥ samāḥ tadā vyatīpātaḥ bhagaṇa arddhe tapaḥ yutau dṛś kalpa sādhita aṃśa ādi yuktayoḥ svau apakramau atha ūja pada gamyā indoḥ krāntiḥ vikṣepa saṃskṛtāḥ yadi syāt adhikā bhānoḥ krānteḥ pātaḥ gataḥ tadā nyūnā ced syāt tadā bhāvī vāmam yugma padasya ca yadā anya tvam vidhoḥ krāntiḥ kṣepāt ced yadi śuddhi ati tad ca apa antar marddha vāyoḥ jya bhāvina śītagau śodhyam candrāt gate pāte tat sūya gati tāḍitam candra bhuktyā hṛtam bhānau liptā ādi śaśi vat phalam tat ūcchaśāṅka pātasya phalam deyam viparyayāt karma etat asakṛt tāvat krāntī yāvat sametayoḥ krāntyoḥ sama tve pātaḥ atha prakṣipta aṃśa ūnite vidhau bhāvī tātkālike adhikā sthirīkṛtā arddharā dvayoḥ vivara liptakāḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ ca a candra bhuktā āptā pāta kālasya nāḍikāḥ ravi indvoḥ māna yoga arddham ṣaṣṭyā saṃguṇya bhājayet tayoḥ bhuktaiḥ antareṇa āptam sthiti amarddhām nāḍikā ādi vat tasya saṃbhava kālaḥ syāt tad saṃyoga ikta saṃjñakaḥ ādi anta kālayoḥ madhye kālaḥ jñeyaḥ ati dāruṇaḥ jātakam vācmi samayāt rāśi saṃjñā puraḥsaram iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne dvitīya pāde jyotiṣavarṇanam nāma catuḥpañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ mūrddha āsya bāhu hṛd kroḍa antar vasti vyañjasaḥ nakhaḥ jānu jaṅghā aṅghni yugalam kāla aṅgāni kriyā ādayaḥ guru manda ārki guravaḥ meṣa ādīnām adhīśvarāḥ hore viṣama bheḥ kedoḥ samaye śaśi sūryayoḥ ādi pañca nava adhīśa dreṣkāṇa īśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ pañca iṣṭa aṣṭa adri pañca aṃśā kuja arkī jyaiḥ jña śukra gāḥ oje viparyayāt yugme triśa aṃśa īśāḥ samīritāḥ kriyaṇa tauli karka ādyāḥ meṣa ādiṣu nava aṃśakāḥ sva bhāt dvādaśa bhāga īśāḥ ṣa ṛḍgam rāśi pūrvakam gojāḥ ca karka yugmena rātri ākhyā pṛṣṭaka udayāḥ śeṣāḥ dina ākhyāḥ tu ubhayam timiḥ krūraḥ saumyaḥ pumān pumān srī ca klībaḥ cara sthira dvis svabhāvakāḥ meṣa ādyāḥ pūrvatas diś sthāḥ sva sva sthāna carāḥ tathā aja ukṣeṇa aṅganā kīṭa jhaṣa jūkāḥ ina āditaḥ uccāni dvi tri manu yuj tithi iṣubha nakha aṃśakaiḥ tad tad saptama nīcāni prāk madhya antya aṃśakāḥ kramāt varga uttamāḥ ca rādheṣu bhāvāt dvādaśa mūrtimān siṃha ukṣā visraḥ catau likubhāḥ sūryā trikoṇa bham catur asram tūrya mṛtyu tri koṇam nava pañcamam nṛpādaḥ kīṭa paśavaḥ bala āḍhyāḥ kendra gāḥ kramāt raktaḥ śvetaḥ śuka nibhaḥ pāṭalaḥ dhūmra pāṇḍurau citraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pīta piṅgau babhruḥ svacchaḥ prabhā kriyāt sāmyāśākhya plava tvam syāt dvitīye vaśiḥ arka bhāt kāla ātma arke manaḥ cadraḥ kujaḥ sattvam vacaḥ budhaḥ jīvaḥ jñānam sukham śukraḥ kāmaḥ duḥkham dineśajaḥ nṛpau ravi indū netā asṛk kumāraḥ jñaḥ kavi ijyakau tāmra śukla rakta harit pīta citra asitāḥ raveḥ varṇāḥ vaḥ avyaha harīdrā śacī kaudhipa araveḥ kṣīṇa indu arka āra ravi jāḥ pāpā pāpa yutaḥ budhaḥ klibau budha arkī śukra indū sriyau śeṣāḥ narāḥ smṛtāḥ śikhi bhūmi payaḥ vāri vāsinaḥ bhūsuta ādayaḥ kavi ijyau kuja sūryauṃ ca vedaḥ jñaḥ varṇa pāḥ kramāt candra arka jīva ajña sitau kuja arkī sāttvika ādikāḥ sphuṭitam ravitaḥ tāṃmram tāre tāmrapuniḥ tathā hema kāṃsya ayasī tri aṃśaiḥ śiśira ādyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ tri āśa trikoṇa turya aṣṭa saptama anyena vṛddhitaḥ saura ijyā ara apare pūrṇe kramāt paśyanti nārada ayana kṣaṇa ghasra ṛtu māsa arddha śaradaḥ raveḥ kaṭu tikta kṣāra miśra madhura amla kaṣāyakāḥ trikoṇāt sāṃtya dhā adharma āyuḥ sukha khodya paḥ suhṛd jīvaḥ jīvajñau sitajñau vyarkāḥ vyārāḥ kramāt amī vi indu arkāḥ vi kuja indu arkāḥ suhṛdaḥ anya iraveḥ dhṛtāḥ dhī ekā anubhaktā mayān jñātvā miśrīdīt sahajān mune sva ucca trikoṇa gehā pranava aṃśaiḥ sthāna jam balam dikṣu saumya ijyayoḥ sūrya arayoḥ saure sita abjayoḥ uttara sthāḥ dīpta karāḥ ceṣṭāḥ vīrya yutāḥ matāḥ niśi indu kuja saurāḥ ca sarvadā kṣohni ca apare krūrāḥ kṛṣṇe site saumyāḥ matam kāla balam budhaiḥ pāpāḥ tu balinaḥ saumyāḥ vivakṣāḥ kaṇṭaka upage klībe candra arka aṃśa samam januḥ sva aṃśe pāpāḥ para aṃśa sthāḥ saumya ālagnam viyoni jam nirbalam ca tat ādeśyam viyoneḥ janma paṇḍitaiḥ śīrṣam vakra gale pādau aṃsau pṛṣṭam uraḥ tathā pārśve kukṣī tu apāna aṅghrī meḍhra muṣkau tathā sphijau puccham catuṣpada aṅgeṣu meṣa ādyāḥ rāśayaḥ smṛtāḥ lagna aṃśāt graha yuj dṛṣṭvā varṇān bala yutāt vadet dṛś samāna pramāṇān ca iṣṭe rekhām smara sthitaiḥ khaga tri aṃśe bala agni īge carama aṃśe graha anvite vāṃśe sthalāṃbujaḥ saureḥ dvīkṣā yoga bhavāḥ dvijāḥ sthala aṃbu bha indu śakṛtaḥ ca itareṣām udāhṛtaḥ sthala aṃbu ca patiḥ kheṭaḥ lagnāt yāvat mite gṛhe antaḥsārāḥ ravau saure durbhagāḥ kṣīriṇaḥ vidhau bhaume kaṇṭakinaḥ vṛkṣāḥ jñe sa phala aphalau puṣpitāḥ bhārgave snigdhāḥ candre atha kaṭukāḥ kuje aśubha ṛkṣe śubhaḥ kheṭaḥ śubham vṛkṣam ku bhūmi jam kuryāt viloma gaḥ vā api sva aṃśa ukta para gaiḥ samam kuja indu hetukam srīṇām pratimāsam iha ārtavam na iṣṭa stha ijye anyathā āste pāpa yukta īkṣite dyūne ruṣā prītyā śubha grahaiḥ śukra arka indu jaiḥ sva aṃśa sthaiḥ ījya ca aṅga trikoṇa ge bhavet apatyam vipra indra puṃsām sat vīrya śālinām śukra ārkrau mātṛ pitarau divā naktam śaśīnajau mātṛṣvasṛ pitṛvya ākhyau vā padmeji same śubhau pāpa dṛṣṭe śubhe kṣīṇe tuṅge vā lagna ge yame kṣīṇa indu kuja saṃdṛṣṭe mṛtyum etya gatāḥ dhruvam yadā tadā garbha yutā nārī mṛtyum avāpnuyāt yat māsa adhipatiḥ naṣṭaḥ tad māsam saṃsrave tyajet lagna indu gaiḥ śubhaiḥ kheṭaiḥ sri koṇa artha asta bhū khagaiḥ sukhī garbhaḥ ravi īkṣitaḥ yāma sthāna gataiḥ vācyam sriyaḥ janma manīṣibhiḥ dvi aṅga sthāḥ budha saṃdṛṣṭāḥ sva pakṣa iyam malaṅkarāḥ lagnam vinā oja bhāva sthaḥ sauraḥ puñjanma kṛt tathā mithas ravi indu ūrjñā arkī vā paśyataḥ samagam raviḥ kuja īkṣite pumāṃśeduhitā klība janmadā same sita indū oja sthā jñārā aṅga ujyāḥ nṛ vīkṣitau graha udaya stha āndi aṅga aṃśān paśyati jñe sva bhāga ge tritayam jña aṃśakāt yugmam amiśraiḥ samam ādiśet vīrya āḍhya jña ārkisa dṛṣṭaiḥ kośa stha āvaha voginaḥ sitārka ijyā arka candra arki jñāṅga īśa urka indavaḥ adhipāḥ māsānām tat samam vācyam garbaga sthasya śubha aśubham avāk āvāṭau aśubhaiḥ bha saṃdhi sthaiḥ prajāyate vīra ansa gīḥ ca daṣṭa idhvaṣṭa arka atabha saṃhitāḥ ārā arkī ca ijya bha aṃśa sthau sa dantaḥ garbhakaḥ ta dāḥ parguḥ mīne yame dvāraiḥ daṣṭa itha aṅga ibha gha saṃdhi ge pāpaiḥ jaḍaḥ vidhau garbhaḥ śubha dṛṣṭi vivarjite mṛga antya ge vāmanakaḥ saura idra arka nirīkṣite dhīna yodapa gaiḥ tri aṃśaiḥ pāpāḥ taiḥ asi rohradāḥ ravi indu yukte siṃha iṅge māheya arki nirīkṣite netra hīnāḥ miśra kheṭaiḥ dṛṣṭe vyayejaḥ vāma nayanam dakṣam sūryaḥ vināśayet na iṣṭāḥ yogāḥ śubhaiḥ dṛṣṭāḥ pāpāḥ syuḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ dvādaśa abde śaśini evam sutau api vicintayet ādhāna indu dvādaśa aṃśā pāpāḥ tad rāśibhiḥ puras śaśāṅke janma bhāga ādi dvi ghnam iṣṭa kalāḥ smṛtāḥ pāpa aṅga ibje tri bhāge lau svāyagaiḥ sadbhiḥ udgataḥ sūryaḥ tad dṛṣṭi gaḥ vā api jñeyaḥ jyotiḥ vidām varaiḥ catuṣpada ṛkṣa ge bhānau śerṣaibala yutaiḥ khagaiḥ sārkya āra siṃha ujñā ja aṃse bha aṃśa tutya aṅga nāla yuj lagnam indum ca sa arka indum na paśyati yadā guruḥ sa pāpa gorake jāyaḥ vā para vīrya prasūti kṛt pāpa bha sthau pāpa kheṭaiḥ sūrya argha ana trikoṇa gau videśa gaḥ pitā avṛddhaḥ khevāḥ rāśi vaśa atyaye pūrṇaḥ iṇḍhau svabhe śejñe śubhe muvi aṃvu je tanau dyūna sthe vā vidhau yātā iṅganā nārī prasūyate abdha aṅgam anbhagaḥ pūrṇe jyaḥ vā paśyati nārada sūtiḥ salile na atra saṃsayaḥ pāpa dṛṣṭe yame gudyām janma aṅga aja vyaya sthite karkāti lagna ga īśaure vaṭe janma abja vīkṣite krīḍā sthāne deva gehe pyūṣare ca kramāt janiḥ śmaśāne lagna dṛś asṛj rāmya sthāna ibja bhārgavau agnihotra gṛhe jīva ūrake bhūṣā ābharaṇe gṛhe bhāsamāne sare mārge sthire sva ṛkṣa aṃśa ge gṛhe trikoṇa gajaḥ ārā arkyā uraste vā sṛjyate ambayā guru dṛṣṭe tu dīrgha āyuḥ param ca prāpyate punar bhave kuja arkyoḥ saṃdṛṣṭe para hasta gataḥ sukhī pitṛ mātṛ gehe janma tad adhīśa balāt mune etad lakṣaṇa saṃpannā prasītiḥ vijane tadā manda ṛkṣa aṃśe vidhau turye manda dṛṣṭe abja ge api vā śīrṣe pṛṣṭa udaye janma tadvat eva vinirdiśet candra asta sukha gaḥ pāpaiḥ mātuḥ pīḍām samādiśet jīrṇa uddhṛtam gṛham mande sṛji dagdham na vā vidhau kāṣṭa āḍhyam adṛḍham sūya bahu śilpa yutam budhe vṛṣe paścāt mṛge siṃhe dakṣiṇe vasatiḥ bhavet gṛha prācya ādi gau dvau dvau v di aṅgāḥ koṇeṣu aja ādayaḥ parthaṅke vāstuvat pāda asriṣad aṅka antya rāśayaḥ candra aga antara gaiḥ kheṭaiḥ sūtikāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ cakrāt hi bahis antar ca dṛśya a dṛśya upare anyathā vā candra nanda aṃśa vat varṇaḥ śīrṣa ādi aṅga vibhāga yuj śīrṣakam nāsā kapola hanavaḥ mukham kaṇṭha aṃsa pārśva hṛd dvār ūṣaḥ kroḍam nābhiḥ ca bāstikāḥ śiṃśnā pāte ca vṛṣaṇau jaghane jānunī tathā bhujeḥ ake kāṣṭa paśu jaḥ jetuḥ śṛṅgi aja yoni jaḥ yasmin saṃjñā srayaḥ kheṭāḥ aṅge syuḥ tatra niścitam vraṇa ūśubha kṛtaḥ pṛṣṭa itanau rāśi samāśrite tilakṛt masakṛt aṣṭa saumyaiḥ yuktaḥ ca lakṣmavān vṛtaḥ vāta kaphī prājñaḥ manda vāc śubha dṛś śaśī tridhā an upavṛtiḥ hāsya ruci jñaḥ śliṣṭa vāc tathā piṅgake ślakṣaṇaḥ dīrghaḥ kaphī dhīmān guruḥ mataḥ su vapuḥ locanaḥ kṛṣṇa vakra keśaḥ bhṛguḥ sukhī dīrghaḥ kapila dṛś bhandaḥ nilī khara kaca ulasaḥ candra aṅga pāpaiḥ bhāntya sthaiḥ sa iṃvu pāpa catuṣṭayaiḥ cakra pūrva apare pāpa saumyaiḥ kīṭa tanau mṛtiḥ udaya asta gatau pāpau candraḥ krūra yutaiḥ śubhaiḥ kṣīṇe abje vyaya ge pāpaiḥ lagna aṣṭa sthaiḥ śubhāḥ na ced kendreṣu smara antya mṛti lagna gaḥ kendra ādyāḥ hasta san kheṭaiḥ adṛṣṭaḥ mṛtyu daḥ tathā mṛtyuḥ śubha īkṣite sama aṣṭake miśra kheṭaiḥ dṛṣṭe mṛtiḥ śiśoḥ kṣīṇa ibja iṅge randhra kende pāpe pāpa antara sthite bhū dyūna nidhane vā abje lagne api evam śiśoḥ mṛtiḥ pāpaiḥ candra asta gaiḥ mātrā sārddham sa dṛṣṭim antarā śubha adṛṣṭe bhānti aga ibje trikoṇa uparataiḥ khalaiḥ lagne ravau tu śasreṇa sa vīrya asadbhiḥ aṣṭagaiḥ sva tuṅga stheṣu aśeṣeṣu parama āyuḥ prakīrtitam śubhaiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sa vīrya yoge kendra sthe ca āyuḥ artha daḥ lagna adhipe bala yuta śīti abdam tu āyuḥ īritam laya īśe dharmagejīva iṣṭa sthe krūra kṣite jitāḥ lagna aṣṭama īśau aṣṭa sthau bha abdam āyuḥ karau matau lagne aśubha ijyau glau dṛṣṭau mṛtyau kaścana ca ākṛtiḥ śata abdam gīṣpatau karke kaṭakastha sitejyayoḥ laya īśa iṅge śubhaiḥ hīne aṣṭame rava abdhi mitam vayaḥ lagne tanu sthe pañca vatsaram etat yoga jam āyuḥ syāt atha spaṣṭam udīyate bale paiṇḍam nisargāt ca vidhoḥ bale aṃśa āyuḥ sa bale lagne tad sādhanam atho śṛṇu go bjāḥ tattva atithī sūryāḥ tithiḥ svargāḥ nakhāḥ kramāt nakhāḥ vidhuḥ dvau aṅkāḥ ca dhṛtiḥ sva akṣi kha mārgaṇāḥ piṇḍe nisarge rava ucce no grahaḥ ṣaṣ bha alpakaḥ yadā cakra śuddhaḥ tadā grāhyā isya aṃśāḥ āyuṣi saṃmatāḥ aṃśa ūnāḥ kāryāḥ graham vakragatim vinā hāni dvaye adhikāḥ kāryāḥ yadā krūraḥ tanau tadā vihāya arīn aṃśa ādyaiḥ hanyāt āyuḥ lavān bhajet bhagaṇa aṃśaiḥ labdha hīnāḥ teṣām kāryāḥ vicakṣaṇaiḥ pāpasya aṃśāḥ saumyasya arddha vivarjitāḥ spaṣṭāḥ te ṛṃśāḥ kha ṣaṣ tri āsāḥ guṇayitvā svakaiḥ gaṇaiḥ varṣāṇi śeṣam arkadhnam hārāt saṃ māsakāḥ smṛtāḥ tad śeṣaḥ ca tri guṇitaḥ tena eva āptam dināni ca śeṣe ṣaṣṭyā hate bhakte hāreṇa ghaṭikā ādikam hitvā bhāji aṅga bhāga ādīn kalīkṛtya kha kha akṣibhiḥ bhajet varṣāṇi śeṣe tu guṇite dvādaśa ādibhiḥ dvi sapta aṃśe ca māsa ādi lagra āyuḥ jāyate sphuṭam aśa āyuṣī sa lagnānām kheṭānām aṃśakāḥ hṛtāḥ kha yugaiḥ āyuḥ aṃśāḥ syuḥ tad saṃskāram vadāmi te graha na lagnam ṣaṣ rātyam ced saṃskāraḥ anyathā nahi tad aṃśaḥ sva agnayaḥ bhaktāḥ labdha ūnaḥ bhūḥ guṇaḥ bhavet yadā aikālyam tadā asta aṃśāḥ sva agrya āpta ūnā ca bhūḥ guṇaḥ gumakadhnāḥ ca āyuḥ aṃśāḥ saṃskāraḥ ayam udāhṛtaḥ āyuḥ aṃśa kalā bhaktāt viṃśati abdāḥ ina āhatam śeṣam dviśata bhaktam syuḥ māsāḥ śeṣāḥ dina ādikam lagna āyuḥ aṃśāḥ triguṇāḥ diś bhiktā syuḥ samāḥ tatas śeṣeḥ aka ādi guṇe bhakte diś bharma āsa ādikam bhavet aṃśa dvi dhnam akṣa aṃśam māsāḥ khatri ādi saṃguṇāt śeṣāḥ dina ādikam yojyam na etat piṇḍa nisargayoḥ bahu āyuryaḥ vīrya sāmya irka ādi utasya prāk yācakaḥ ṣaṣ varga arddhasya triṃśasya trikoṇa gaḥ ca smara gaḥ pākapasya abdhi nāgāḥ ca hi arṇavā sahagasya ca trikoṇa sthasya ca aṣṭa akṣi sūryāḥ dyūna gatasya ca turya aṣṭagasya tu svargāḥ guṇakāḥ parikīrtitāḥ daśāguṇaiḥ hatāḥ bhaktyā guṇa aikyena samāgatāḥ śeṣeḥ aka ādi hate bhakte māsa ādi aikyena nārada antardaśāsu vidaśāḥ tāsu ca upadaśāḥ tathā daśa īśa mitra sva ucca kṣaṅga ubja ubdhi eka adri vṛddhi gaḥ jīvikā ādi phalam sarvam daśāyām tasya yojayet viśani āpad daśāyām yaḥ vairi dṛṣṭaḥ vipatti kṛt śubham atra īkṣitaḥ ca iṣṭa sat varga sthaḥ ca yaḥ grahaḥ tad kāle balavān āpanna āśa kṛt samudāhṛtaḥ yasya aṣṭavarga jam ca api phalam pūrṇa śubham bhavet śreṣṭham śubhataram vācyam viparīta gatasya tu na iṣṭam utkaṭam iṣṭam tu su alpam jñātvā balam vadet care sat madhya duṣṭābhyām aṅga bhaṅge viparyayāt sthire na iṣṭa ṣṭa madhyā ca horāyāḥ tryam śakaiḥ phalam svāmi jyajña yutā horā dṛṣṭā vā sat pala āvahā ca pāpa antara gatā anyathā prāk dhvāṅkṣā bandhu mṛtyāya tayoḥ dyūne raviḥ sva bhāt vakrāt sva ādi vasān ca arke śukrāt yūnām tu ṣaṣ rataḥ dharma dhyāya ari gaḥ jīva ādika tri ari gaḥ vidhoḥ sujñāḥ tatovṛddhi antyabandhurāḥ svārāt śaśī śubhaḥ sva dū vṛdh yasta ādiṣu pṛ dhāt sa sa aṣṭau pañca yaḥ upagaḥ ṣaṣ tryāya dhī sthaḥ mandāt dvi tryāya aṣṭaka indra gaḥ ijyāḥ vā jña jyāyāḥ tatra sve kaveḥ maṅgāḥ māyā ari gaḥ vidhoḥ kendra aṣṭa apārtha gaḥ sva ṛkṣāt mandāt goṣṭāyaka indra gaḥ ṣaṭ tridhī bhavataḥ saumyāt ṣaṣ vā aṃśa aṣṭagaḥ bhṛgoḥ karma āya vyaya ṣaṣṭa sthaḥ jīvāt bhaumaḥ śubhaḥ smṛtaḥ kaveḥ ṛddhyā ṣaṣṭamaḥ udhyāye sat jñaḥ mandān sa dhī traye sākṣāḥ te bhūmi jāt jīva ādyayā ari bhava mṛtyu gaḥ sva bhāt ṣaṣ khāya aṣṭa abdhi kha ūṣu ijyāt saha ādyeṣu vilagnataḥ diśvā aṣṭa ādi asta bandhyāye kujāt khāt sa trike guruḥ san raveḥ śukrāt dhī khagaḥ diś bhava ari gaḥ candrāt vīśa artha goḥ teṣu mandāt dhī tri ṣaṣ antya gaḥ go bdhi dhī ṣaṣ kha kha ādyāḥ ye vilagnataḥ āśu śubhaḥ svāt sa jñeṣu tri dhī ga ubdhī diś chidra asi gata ūrka jāt randhra aya vyaca gaḥ sūryādoḥ ṭadhī khe sa goḥ guro jña abdhi tri āya ari go rātri ṣaṣ dhi adhi āntya goṣu ca tridhīśa ariṣu mandaḥ khāt sa akṣa antyeṣu śubho sṛjaḥ kendrāya aṣṭa dhaneṣu arkāḥ lagnāt vṛddhi ādya bandhuṣu go dhvaṣṭā pāri kha antyejñāt candrāt lābha triṣadbhataḥ ṣaṣ aṣṭa antya gataḥ śukrāt gurīḥ dvi īśa antya śatruṣu ukta sthāneṣu rekhā ādaḥ hi anukteṣu tu bindu dāḥ kaṣṭam artha kṣayaḥ kleśaḥ samatā artha sukha āgamaḥ dhana āptiḥ sukham iṣṭa āptiḥ iti rekhā phalam kramāt pitṛ mātṛ dviṣat mitra bhrātṛ strī bhṛtaka ādraveḥ svāmila grājayoḥ svasthāt bheda ṛka sva yaśaḥ śayāt tṛṇa svarṇa aśva dhoraṇa ādyaiḥ arka aṃśe vṛttim ādiśet kṛṣi aṃbuja srībhyaḥ ubja aṃśe kauje dhātu asra sāhasaiḥ tathā jyā raiḥ ukta eka aṅge nṛ dvāviṃśa bhūpāḥ tuṅga isṛk cāpa irka indū yama stanau sita asṛjaḥ gurau karke sa arāje lagna ge nṛpāḥ suhṛd jāyā khagaiḥ nṛpaḥ mande mṛga aṅga itri aryaka aṃśa sthaiḥ aja ādibhiḥ nṛpa mṛgamukhe kuje tuṅgeḥ ṛkṣa bhāgevau meṣe arke bhūmi pā sa indau eṣe ṣa aṅgre rerkapa pa asṛjaḥ siṃha kuṃbha mṛga sthāḥ ced bhūpaḥ sāreta nāvā je ārkejīve tanau vā api nṛpaḥ athoḥ kuja bhāskarau mṛga āsya lagna gaiḥ saura ija abja ṛkṣa harayaḥ sa yāḥ vakṣyamāṇaiḥ nṛpa sutaḥ jñeyaḥ bhūyas muni īśvara siṃha īrake meṣa lagne aje mṛge bhaume ghaṭe aṣṭame cāpe dharānāthaḥ syāt atha sva ṛkṣa ge bhṛgau pātāla ge dharma ge abje śubha dṛṣṭe yute mune tri lagna bhava gaiḥ śeṣaiḥ dharādhīśaḥ prajāyate meṣūraṇāya tanugāḥ śaśi sūryaja sūrayaḥ jñārau dhaneśita ravā hibuke bhūpatiḥ tadā vṛṣā iṃ'ge abja udhana ari sthaḥ jīva arkī lāṃbhagāḥ pare karma lagna gara veṭasya daśāyām rājya saṃgatiḥ prabalasya daśāyām vā śatru nīcāḥ diś ārti dāḥ śṛṅgāṭakam dhi gauga sthaiḥ lagna āya sthaiḥ halam matam vimiśraiḥ kamalam prāhuḥ vāyākaṇṭaka bāhya gaiḥ lagnāt catur bhugaiḥ yūpaḥ śaraḥ tūryāt catur bhugaiḥ śaktiḥ da kha ādi catur bhagaiḥ ṣahyu sthāneṣu vīṇā ādyāḥ sama sapta ṛkṣa gaiḥ vīṇā dāma pāśa kedāra bhū śūla yuga golakāḥ grahaiḥ carabhagaiḥ rājayogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ bhālā kendra sthitaiḥ saumyaiḥ pāpaiḥ sarpaḥ udāhṛtaḥ vīṇā udbhava ūti nipuṇā gīta nṛtya ruciḥ bhṛśam dātā samṛddhaḥ dāma āsthaḥ pāśa jaḥ dhana śīla yuj kedāra utthaḥ kṛṣi karaḥ śūle śūra ukṣataḥ dhanaḥ yugam pāṣaṇḍayuḥ gole vidhanaḥ malinaḥ tathā subhaga aṅga ūrddha caṃpāt sukhī śūraḥ ca cāmaraḥ mitraḥ u pakāra kṛt chatre kūṭe ca anṛta bandha rāj tyāgī yajvā ātmavān yūthe hiṃsraḥ guhya adhipaḥ śaraiḥ śaktau nīcaḥ alasaḥ niḥsvaḥ daṇḍe priya viyoga bhāj vyarkaiḥ sva antya ubhaya gataiḥ kheṭaiḥ syāt sva upārjita artha bhuj dātā dhanī sukhī nīrogaḥ śīlavān khyātaḥ su veṣaḥ ca anaphaābhavaḥ bhogī sukhī dhanī dānī tyāgī duru dhura udbhavaḥ yantryā aśmakāraṃśā jokaḥ dhvagaḥ sujñaḥ sukīrtiḥ nipuṇam vidvāṃsam dhaninam tathā sa mandaḥ dhātu kuśalam tathā mune kūṭa snyā śava paṇya aṭham nasā asṛj indgaḥ prasū dviṣam kuryāt sa jñāḥ ūrtha nipuṇam namram sat kīrti saṃyutam āre sajñe vāhu yodhī pura adhyakṣaḥ sagīṣpatau nṛtya gīta āḍhyaḥ māyā dakṣaḥ sa śukre vākpatau vidvān sa asite anna ghaṭaṅkaraḥ kuja jña ijyā ja śukra arki sūryaḥ parivrajet naraḥ śākya ājīvaka vṛddha arthi ca mandaḥ vā janmapam naṣṭam tathā ca mandakā gaṇe bhauma arka aṃśe saura dṛṣṭe candre vā dīkṣitaḥ bhavet surūpaḥ bhūṣita gaḥ aśinyām dakṣaḥ satyavacāḥ yame brāhmaḥ dhanī mṛge bhogī raudre hiṃstraḥ śaṭhaḥ agha kṛt dāntaḥ rogī śubhaḥ adityām puṣyarya janmā kaviḥ sukhī dhūrtaḥ śaṭhaḥ kṛtaghnaḥ ahau pāpaḥ sarva aśanaḥ bhavet dhanī bhogī naroḥ yama ṛkṣe stenaḥ dhṛṣṭaḥ ghṛṇī kare citra aṃbaraḥ sudṛś tvāṣṭre na ca dharma dayā paraḥ dvīśe lubdhaḥ paṭuḥ krodhī āṭhanaḥ videśa gaḥ śākre dharma paraḥ tuṣṭaḥ mūle mānī dhanī sukhī āpye mānī dṛṣṭaḥ vaiśve namraḥ ca dhārmikaḥ karṇe dhanī sukhī khyātaḥ dātā śūraḥ dhanī vasau vyasanī srī jitaḥ budhne vaktā sukhī kāntaḥ pauṣṇe śūraḥ dhanī śuciḥ kāmī śūraḥ kṛtajñaḥ aje kāntaḥ tyāgī kṣamī vṛṣe yugme srī dyūta śāsra jñaḥ sraiṇaḥ hrasvaḥ svabhe vidhau srī dviṣ krodhī harau mānī vikrāntaḥ sthira dhīḥ sukhī dharmī ślakṣṇaḥ sudhīḥ ṣaṣṭe prājñaḥ prāṃśuḥ dhanī ghaṭe rogī pūjyaḥ kṣatī kārairpye kaviḥ śilpī ijya bhe dhanī mṛge alasaḥ aṭanaḥ svakṣaḥ paradāra artha hṛt haṭe khyātaḥ srī dviṣ dhanī tīkṣṇa ujñaḥ kaviḥ śaiṇḍikaḥ dhanī baudhe kṛtajñaḥ jaive tu khyātaḥ śaukre anya dārikaḥ mṛge bahu ātmaja dhanaḥ kuṃbhe duḥkhya nṛtī khalaḥ srīdveṣyaḥ sva jana dveṣī niyaratyaḥ sadhīyanaḥ samāna arthaḥ sa putra srī sarṇaḥ sūrya ādibhe budhe senā nīḥ strī artha putra āḍhyaḥ dakṣa maiśyaḥ paricchadī maṇḍala īśaḥ sārtha sukhaḥ sa ṛṇa svāmi arka bhādgurau strī āpta arthaḥ manda śoka āḍhyaḥ bandhu dveṣī dhana aghavān sārthaḥ prājñaḥ samaḥ khyātiḥ mṛgau sat putra strīdhanaḥ rājā grāme śoka ādibhiḥ irka je bhūpa jña guṇi paura āsvādṛṣṭa ibjejesṛj ādibhiḥ niḥ svastena nṛpāḥ prajña preṣya āma vi nṛ yugma ge dhātu ājīvī nṛpa jña abhī tantuvāya adhanāḥ su abhe yuyutsu kavi sūrī jya dhātu jīvi dṛś āmayāḥ jyotirjña āḍhyeji anu khalu nṛpejña ādi karharau ṣaṣṭe śubhaiḥ nṛpa camūpa naipuṇya vatita āśayāḥ jūke bhūpa svarṇakāra vaṇijaḥ śeṣa dṛś yute jñāti kṣmā janayāḥ ca āye sadbhiḥ darmī śaṭhaḥ tathā bhūpa maṇḍita sakha ijyāmṛge bhūyānya dārikau kuṃbhe śeṣaiḥ ca hāsya jña nṛpa jñāḥ sadbhiḥ antya bhe hāra īśa ṛkṣa dala sthaiḥ tu dṛṣṭaḥ yuktaḥ śaśī śubhaḥ dvādaśa aṃśe phalam proktam nava aṃśe api atha kīrtyate kalahaḥ kṣitijāṃsthe śaukre mūrkhaḥ anya dāradaḥ kaviḥ sukhī budha aṃśe tu naṭa caura jña śilpinaḥ krodhī nidhi īśaḥ mātyaḥ vā nṛpaḥ hiṃsraḥ sutaḥ hareḥ jīva aṃśe hāsya vidyā dhāḥ balī mantrī ca dhārmikaḥ nu tadvat eva phalam vadet puṣṭam madhyam laghu jñeyam yadi ca aṃśa patiḥ balī rāśi īkṣaṇa phalam ruddhvā dadāti aṃśa palam spuṭam dvitīye īrake bahu dhanaḥ nṛpa daṇḍyaḥ mukha āmayī suta artha sukha bhā bhāraye daśame śruta śaurya vāt mūka udhaḥ badhiraḥ preṣyaḥ jege khāñca ajage dhanī alpa agni kāmaḥ tīkṣṇa ūrau īṣ yusta tri mada ujña rave vyādhi pūḍā anvitaḥ mṛtyau bhānuḥ dhana ge mitra dhana anvitaḥ vidvān dhanī ca pravaraḥ paṇḍitaḥ saciva ūriyuj vidvān sa vācyaḥ kṛpaṇī sukha akṣaḥ ripu gṛddhimān nīcaḥ tapasvī caṣṇa vanī lobhī duṣṭaḥ tanoḥ guro niḥśvas rogī kāma vaśaḥ malinaḥ śaiśava ārti yuj grāma adhipaḥ sa vidvān ca cāru aṅgaḥ anyatra sūrya vat pūrṇam uccetha pāda ūna phalam mūla trikoṇa ge śatru bhe alpam tathā phala śūnya tā kha bharāka ādike kheṭe kula tulyaḥ kula adhikaḥ bandhu pūjyaḥ atha dhanavān sukhī bhogī nṛpaḥ kramāt nṛpaḥ ca mitra bhā stheṣu kheṭe vreka ādiṣu kramāt viṣama ṛkṣeḥ aka horāyām sa sthite śubha bheṣu ca khyātaḥ mahā udyamī ca ati tejāḥ dhīmān dhanī balī śubheṣu candra horāyām sthiteṣu sama rāśiṣu sūrya horā gataḥ pāpaḥ sama bheṣu tu madhyamāḥ viṣama ṛkṣeṣu bhāskaryā saumyāḥ na ukta phala pradāḥ sva mitra tri aṃśa gaḥ candraḥ surūpam guṇinam naram vyāla āyudhe catuṣpāda aṃ'jeṣu ca tri aṃśake ca tīkṣṇe ati hiṃsraḥ ca bhavet guru talpa gata uṭanaḥ stenaḥ bhoktā sa dhana dhīḥ nṛpaḥ klībaḥ ca śatru hā viṣṭi kṛt dāsa vṛttiḥ ca pāpaḥ hiṃsnaḥ amatiḥ bhavet meṣa ādika uttama aṃśeṣu dvādaśa aṃśeṣu rāśi vat jāyā bala vibhūṣā āḍhyaḥ sattva yuktaḥ ati sāhasī tejasvī ca naraḥ khāye triṃśa aṃse sṛji saṃsthite āmayī vā sva bhāryāyām viṣamaḥ pāradārikaḥ sukha dhī dhana kīrti ālaḥ tejasvī loka pūjitaḥ nīra guhya bhavān bhogī jīve kha triṃśa bhāga ge medhā kalā kāvya śilpa vivāda kapaṭa āñcitaḥ śāstra artha sāhasa yutaḥ budhe sva triṃśa bhāga ge lalita aṅgaḥ syāt bhārgave svake candra arkkau ced kuja ādigau mūla trikoṇa sva ṛkṣa ucce kaṇṭha sthāḥ tu ca ye grahāḥ anyonya kārakāḥ te syuḥ karma gaḥ tu viśeṣataḥ a śūnyeṣu ca kendreṣu kāraka ākhya gṛheṣu ca guru janma īśa lagna īśāḥ kendra sthāḥ madhya saukhya ādāḥ pṛṣṭa ubhava ka uda pa ṛkṣa sthita astu antya antara āduṣu candrārkī phala dāvantye sadā jñaḥ phala dāyakaḥ syāt tayoḥ saṃpadaḥ sva tvam anyathā atha aṅga tā udayaḥ si mā turya aṣṭagaiḥ krūraiḥ yat vā krūra antare sitaḥ sat graha ayuta dṛṣṭaḥ ced agni pātāt mṛtiḥ striyāḥ pāṇi gatayoḥ śaśi ravyoḥ saha striyā pāpe dhī sthe vidhau kṣīṇa janmā suta kalatriṇaḥ śanau khage aste sa śukre tad dṛṣṭe pāradārikaḥ tau ced sa iṃdusriyā sārddham puṃścalaḥ jāyate naraḥ śubhaiḥ dṛṣṭau tau dvau pariṇata aṅgakau rava asta ambu gaiḥ indu śukra pāpaiḥ vaṃśa vināśakaḥ śilpī tri eśe budha yute kendra saṃsthā ārki vīkṣite dāsyām aṃśa gayoḥ śūlī ravi indvoḥ yutayoḥ kṛśaḥ nidhana ari dhana antya sthāḥ ravi indvāra yamāḥ yadā saumyāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ na vāyatri dhī gatāḥ pāpa khecarāḥ karṇa upaghātakāḥ dyūne rada vaikṛtya kārakāḥ sarpa śṛṅkhalayā śāṭhyaiḥ dṛkkaiḥ balya śubha īkṣitaiḥ sa mande abje vakra dṛṣṭe pasmārī durvacāḥ kṣayī ravi manda kujaiḥ rava sthaiḥ saumya dṛṣṭaiḥ sa maṇḍalaiḥ bhṛtakāḥ pūrva muditaiḥ vara madhya adhamāḥ narāḥ puñjanau tu phalam puṇya srīṇām yogyam vadet ca tat tad svāmiṣu akhilam kāryam tad bhartṛ maraṇam mṛtau yugmeṣu lagna śaśinoḥ vanitā prakṛti sthitā sat śīla bhūṣaṇa yutā śubha saṃdṛṣṭayoḥ tayoḥ puruṣa ākṛti śīla āḍhyā tayoḥ oja sthayoḥ matā atha pāpāḥ guṇa ūnāḥ ca kuja ārkī jya jña śukrāṇām kuja ṛkṣe kramaśas aṅganā bālya duṣṭā tathā dāsī sādhvī māyāvatī tvarā dṛṣṭā vā ākṛti śīlā syāt tayoḥ oja sthayoḥ matā atha pāpāḥ guṇa ūnāḥ ca pāpa vīkṣitayoḥ tayoḥ duṣṇavāc punarbhūḥ sa guṇā vijñā khyātā sphujidgrṛhe baudhe samā yā klīvā ca satī guṇavatī calā dvandva bhe guṇa āḍhyā śilpikā adhamā vācāṭā kulaṭā siṃhe rāgī pundhīḥ agamya tā jaive guṇa āḍhya alpa ratiḥ guṇa jñā jñāninī satī dāsī nīca ratā sādhvī mānde duṣṭā napatyakā lagna indu yuktaiḥ riṃśa aṃśaiḥ phalam etat vala anugam mithas ṛṃśe śukra arkī śaukre ced vā ghaṭa aṃśake strībhiḥ strī maithunam yāti madana anala dīpitā śūnye kāpuruṣaḥ dyūne bale klīvaḥ na sadṛśi budha arkyoḥ carabhe nityam para deśa parāyaṇaḥ tad sṛṣṭā mada ge sūrye strī bāla vidhavā kuje pāpa dṛṣṭe śanau dyūne kanyā eva āpadyate jarām śītaraśmiḥ yadā dyūne tadā bhartuḥ anusayā mātrā sārddham asat dṛṣṭe tathā kaujeṃśake asta ge manda dṛṣṭe vyādhi yoniḥ sat graha aṃśe pati priyā manda ṛkṣe vā aṃśake dyūne vṛddhau mūrkhaḥ patiḥ striyāḥ strī lolaḥ krodhanaḥ kauje baudhe vidvān ca naipuṇaḥ jita indriyaḥ gṛṇī jaive cāndre kāmī mṛduḥ tathā śukra abjayoḥ lagna gayoḥ sukhinī īrṣyā samanvitā kalāsu nipuṇā sukhitā ca guṇa anvitā śukra jñayoḥ tu śubhagā kalā jñā rucira aṅganā krūre aṣṭame aṣṭama īśa aṃśe yasya syāt tat vayaḥ same śeṣaiḥ sa vīryaiḥ oja ṛkṣe lagne ku rūpiṇī bhavet vikhyātā anaika śāstra jñā vanitā brahma vādinī mṛtyu sthānam paśyatām syāt valinā dhātu kopataḥ nṛṇām mṛtyu hitam yuktam tṛṣ kṣudh bhavaḥ ca aṣṭama sthaiḥ sūrya ādyaiḥ ca vara ādiṣu para sva adhva pradeśeṣu mṛtyuḥ sūrya mahījayoḥ striyām hima ūṣa aṇa karayoḥ sva janāt pāpa dṛś tayoḥ toyamṛtaḥ dyu bhaya udaye putra dharma sthasyoḥ vandhāt pāpayoḥ sat adṛṣṭayoḥ sa thāsa ravi saṃyutaiḥ lakuṭena atha taiḥ eva kha aṅka aṅga tanaya sthitaiḥ dhūma a nibandhanaiḥ kāryaḥ kudanaiḥ maraṇam bhavet saure dvāraiḥ sva aṃbu rava sthaiḥ kṣata kremi aṅgayā tatas bhauma arki dṛkkaiḥ ādyaiḥ pūrva māsaḥ tithiḥ tatra anupātataḥ viloma janma bhāgaiḥ ca velā rātri dyu saṃjñake daśa aṣṭa sapta viṣaye guṇyāḥ śeṣāḥ kha saṃkhyayā jīva bhauma ka vijñāḥ syuḥ bhānām nityaḥ vidhiḥ kheṭa vaśā vat hargaṇāḥ tathā sapta ṛghnam bha hṛtam śeṣam ṛkṣam nava dhana ṛṇataḥ saptaghnam pumān paraśu dhṛk kṛṣṇaḥ rakta dṛś rakṣitum kṣamaḥ dṛṣṭa ṛtika pada āśvāsyā rakta vastrā ghaṭa ākṛtiḥ kṣut tṛṣā ārtaḥ udugdha paṭaḥ lūna kuñcita mūrdhajaḥ malinaḥ kṣudh paroja āsyaḥ dakṣaḥ kṛṣi ādi karmaṇi dvipa kāyaḥ sarabhayāt piṃpagalaḥ vyākula antaraḥ śaucikī rūpiṇī sādhvī hi apraja ucchrita pāṇikā āṅkriyā aṃśāḥ stu ṣatriṃśat udītāḥ kramāt etat saṃkṣepataḥ proktam jātakam muni sattama iti śrī nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge dvitīya pāde bṛhat upākhyāne jātakanirūpaṇat nāma pañcapañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ kramāt caitra ādi māseṣu meṣa ādyāḥ saṃkramāḥ matāḥ caitra śukla pratipadi yaḥ vāraḥ sa nṛpaḥ smṛtaḥ meṣapraveśe senā nīḥ karkaṭe bhavet neṣṭaḥ kujaḥ budhaḥ jīvaḥ bhṛguḥ tu ati śubhaṅkaraḥ adhamaḥ ravi jaḥ vācyaḥ jñātvā ca eṣām balābalam daṇḍa ākāre kabandhe vā dhvāṅkṣa ākāre atha kīlake dṛṣṭeḥ a kamaṇḍale vyādhiḥ bhrāntiḥ cora artha nāśanam sita raktaiḥ pīta kṛṣṇaiḥ vaṇaiḥ vipra ādi pīḍanam pītaḥ śīte vṛṣṭau grīṣme lohita bhāraviḥ roga anāvṛṣṭi bhaya kṛt kramāt uktaḥ muni īśvara śaśa rakta nibhe bhānau saṃgrāmaḥ na cirāt bhuvi mayūra patra saṃkāśaḥ dvādaśa abdam na varṣati candramāḥ sadṛśaḥ bhānuḥ kuryāt bhūpa antaram kṣitau arke śyāme kīṭa bhayam bhasma ābhe rāṣṭra jam tathā chidreḥ a kamaṇḍale dṛṣṭam mahā rāja vināśanam ghaṭa ākṛtiḥ kṣudh bhaya kṛt pura hā toraṇa ākṛtiḥ chatra akṛte deśa hatiḥ khaṇḍa bhānu nṛpa anta kṛt tadā nṛpa vadhaḥ jñeyaḥ tu athavā rāja vigrahaḥ pakṣam pakṣa arddham arka indu pariviṣṭau aharniśam yāmya śṛṅga unnattaḥ candraḥ śubhadī mīna meṣayoḥ saumya śṛṅga unnataḥ śreṣṭhaḥ nṛ yuj makarayoḥ tathā ghaṭa ukṣṇaḥ tu samaḥ karka cāpayoḥ śara sannibhaḥ cāpavat kaurma hṝrṃyoḥ ca śūlabat tula karkayoḥ āṣāḍha dvaya mūla indra dhiṣṇyānām yāmya gaḥ śaśī viśākhā mitrayoḥ yāmya pārśva gaḥ pāpa gaḥ śaśī śubhaḥ madhya go dvāra dakṣāṇi atītya navavāsavāt yama indra ahi īśa noya īśa marutaḥ ca arddhatārakāḥ dhruva āditi dvi daivāḥ syuḥ adhyarddhān ca aparāḥ samāḥ yāmya śṛṅga unnataḥ na iṣṭaḥ śubhaḥ śukle pipīlikā kārya hāniḥ kārya vṛddhiḥ hāniḥ vṛddhiḥ yathākramam subhikṣa kṛt viśāla induḥ aviśāla ogha nāśanaḥ kuja ādyaiḥ nihate śṛṅge maṇḍale vā yathākramam kṣema ādyam vṛṣṭi bhūpāla jana nāśaḥ prajāyate satya aṣṭa navama ṛkṣeṣu sa udayāt vikrime kuje tat vakram uṣṇam saṃjñam syāt prajā pīḍā agni saṃbhavaḥ daśama ekādaśe ṛkṣe dvādaśa arvā agratīpayaḥ kūkram vakramukham jñeyam sasya vṛṣṭi vināśa kṛt bāla āsya cakram tat tasmin sasya vṛṣṭi vināśanam pañcadaśe ṣoḍaśa ṛkṣe vakre syāt rudhira ānanam durbhikṣam kṣudh bhayam rogān karoti kṣitinandanaḥ aṣṭādaśe saptadaśe tat vakram muśala āhvayam durbhikṣam dhana dhānya ādi nāśane bhaya kṛt sadā asta gaḥ catur āsya ārkṣe loka traya vināśa kṛt uditaḥ śravaṇe puṣye vaktṛ go śvana hāni daḥ avṛṣṭi śastra bhaya daḥ pīḍyam devāḥ pitṛ dvi daiva dhātṝṇām bhidyante gaṇḍa tārakāḥ durbhikṣam maraṇam rogam karoti kṣitijaḥ tadā triṣu uttarāsu rohiṇyām nairṛte śravaṇe mṛge a vṛṣa aṭidaḥ caran bhaumaḥ dakṣiṇe rohiṇī sthitaḥ bhūmi jaḥ sarva dhiṣṇyānām uda gāmī śubhagha pradaḥ yāmya gaḥ aniṣṭa phala daḥ bhavet bheda karaḥ nṛṇām vinā utpātena śaśinaḥ kadācid na udayam vrajet anāvṛṣṭa agni bhaya kṛt anartha nṛpa vigraha ṛ vasu vaiṣṇava viśva indu dhātṛ bheṣu caran budhaḥ bhinatti yadi tat tārām bādhā vṛṣṭi bhayaṅkaraḥ ārdra ādi pitṛ bha anteṣu dṛśyate yadi candrajaḥ tadā durbhikṣa kalaha roga anāvṛṣṭi bhīti kṛt hasta ādi ṣaṭsu tārāsu vicaran indu nandanaḥ kṣemam subhikṣam ārogyam kurute roga nāśanam bhiṣaj taraṅga vāṇijya vṛttīnām kṣudh śastra anala caurebhyaḥ bhaya daḥ prāṇinām tadā yāmya agni dhātṛ vāyavya dhiṣṇayeṣu prākṛtā gatiḥ raudra indu sārpa pitryeṣu jñeyā miśra āhvayā gatiḥ bhāgya aryama ijyā ditiṣu saṃkṣiptā gatiḥ ucyate gati tīkṣṇa aja caraṇa ahiḥ budhi abha āśri bheṣu yā ghorā gatiḥ haritvāṣṭra vasu vāruṇabheṣu ca indra agni mitra mārtaṇḍabheṣu pāpa āhvayā āgatiḥ yāvanti eva dināni eṣa dṛśyaḥ tāvati adṛśya gaḥ catvāriṃśat kramātriṃśat ravi indra bhūsutaḥ nava pañcadaśa ekādaśabhiḥ divasaiḥ śaśinandanaḥ prākṛtāyām gataḥ saumyaḥ kṣema ārogya subhikṣa kṛt miśra sa kṣiptayoḥ madhye phala daḥ anyāsu vṛṣṭi daḥ vaiśākha śrāvaṇe pauṣe āṣāḍhe abhyuditaḥ budhaḥ jagatām pāpa phala daḥ tu itareṣu śubha pradaḥ iṣa ūrja māsayoḥ śastra durbhikṣa agni bhaya pradaḥ uditaḥ candrajaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ rajata sphaṭika upayaḥ śubha daḥ jyeṣṭaḥ nṛṇām madhya phala pradaḥ śuciḥ madhyaḥ nabhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ bhādraḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kvacid naraḥ kārtikaḥ mārgaśīrṣaḥ ca nṛṇām duṣṭa phala pradaḥ mādhavaḥ śubha daḥ jyeṣṭaḥ nṛṇām madhya phala pradaḥ śuciḥ madhyaḥ nabhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ bhādraḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kvacid nara atiśreṣṭhaḥ iṣaḥ proktaḥ māsānām phalam īdṛśam saumye bhāge caran bhānām kṣema ārogya subhikṣa kṛt pīta agni śyāma harita rakta varṇaḥ girāḥ kramāt vyādhi agni caura śastra astra bhaya daḥ prāṇinām bhavet anāvṛṣṭim bhūmna nibhaḥ karoti sura pūjitaḥ divā dṛṣṭaḥ nṛpa vadhyā mayam vārāṣṭra nāśanam saṃvatsara śarīram syāt kṛttikā rohiṇī tathā nābhiḥ tu āpāṭha yugalam ādrī hṛd kusumam maghā durbhikṣa agni marut bhītiḥ śarīram krūra pīḍite nābhyām kṣudh tṛṣ bhayam puṣye samyak mūla phala kṣayaḥ hṛdayeśasya nidhanam śubham syāt saṃyutaiḥ śubhaiḥ śasya vṛddhiḥ prajā ārogyam yuddham jīva atya varṣaṇam iti dvijāti madhyām tu go nṛpa strī sukham mahat niḥsvana avṛṣṭi phaṇi bhiḥ vṛṣṭiḥ svāsthyam mahā utsavaḥ mahārgham api saṃpattiḥ deśa nāśaḥ ativarṣaṇam a vairam rogam abhayam roga bhīḥ sasya varṣaṇe rogaḥ dhānyam nabhaḥ adṛṣṭi maghā ādi ṛkṣa gate gurau nāgebhairāvatāḥ ca eva vṛṣabha uṣṭra khara āhvayāḥ mṛgāñja dahana ākhyāḥ syuḥ yāmaya antāḥ vīthayaḥ nava saumya mārge ca tisṛṣu caran vīthiṣu bhārgavaḥ dhānya artha vṛṣṭi sasyānām paripūrti karoti hi pūrvasyām diśi meghaḥ tu śubha daḥ pitṛ pañcake svāti traye paścimāyām tasyām śukraḥ tathāvidhaḥ viparīte tu anāvṛṣṭi dṛś budha saṃyutaḥ kṛṣṇa aṣṭamyām caturdaśyām amāyām ca yadā sitaḥ undayā astamanam yāti tadā jala mayī mahī mithas saptama rāśi sthau paścāt prāc vīthi saṃsthitau guru śukrau anāvṛṣṭi durbhikṣa samara pradau kujajña jīva ravijāḥ śukrasya agresarāḥ yadi yuddha anti vāyuḥ durbhikṣa jala nāśa karāḥ matāḥ jalamitra aryama ahi indra nakṣatreṣu subhikṣa kṛt śravaṇa anila hta ārdra ābharaṇī bhāgyam eṣu ca nṝṇām subhikṣa ārogya sya kṛt hṛdaye pañca ṛkṣāṇi vāma haste catuṣṭayam vāma pāde tathā trīṇi dakṣiṇe trīṇe bhāni ca āyāsaḥ śreṣṭha yātrā ca dhana lābhaḥ kramāt phalam karoti eva samaḥ sāmyam śīghra geṣu utkramāt phalam viṣṇu cakra utkṛtta śirāḥ haṅguḥ pūyūṣa pānataḥ vikṣepa avanateḥ vaṅgāt gāhuḥ dūra gataḥ tayoḥ ṣaṣ māsa vṛddhyā grahaṇam śodhaya indra vicandrayoḥ parva īśāḥ tu tathā satyadevā khyā āditas kramāt brahma indru indra dhana adhīśa varuṇa agni yama āhvayoḥ paśu sasya dvijātīnām vṛddhiḥ brahme tu parvaṇi tadvat eva phalam saumye śleṣma pīḍā ca parvaṇi dhaninām dhana hāniḥ syāt kauberam dhānya vardhanam nṛpāṇām aśivam kṣemam itareṣām ca vāruṇe pravarṣaṇam sasya vṛddhiḥ kṣemam hautāśaparvaṇi anāvṛṣṭiḥ sasya hāniḥ durbhikṣam yāmya parvaṇi velā hīne sya hāniḥ nṛpāṇām dāruṇam raṇam virodhaḥ dharaṇīśānām artha vṛṣṭi vināśanam saumyāyane kṣatra viprān itarān hanti dakṣiṇe dvijātīn ca kramāt hanti rāhu dṛṣṭa uraga āditaḥ tathā eva grāma bhedāḥ syuḥ mokṣa bhe dāḥ tathā daśa no śaktāḥ lakṣitum devāḥ kim punar prākṛtāḥ janāḥ ānīya kheṭān gaṇitān teṣām vāram vicintayet śubha aśubha anyaiḥ kālasya grāhayāmaḥ hi lakṣaṇam tasmāt anveṣaṇīyam tad kāla jñānāya dhīmatā utpāta rūpāḥ ketūnām udaya astamayāḥ nṛṇām divya āntarikṣāḥ bhaumāḥ te śubha aśubha phala pradāḥ yajña dhvaja astra bhava narakṣa vṛddhiṅgaja upamāḥ stambha śūla aṅkuśa ākārāḥ āntarikṣāḥ prakīrtitāḥ nakṣatra saṃsthitāḥ divyāḥ bhaumāḥ ye bhūmi saṃsthitāḥ ekaḥ api bhinna rūpaḥ syāt jantuḥ nāma śubhāya vai yāvantaḥ divasān ketuḥ dṛśyate vividha ātmakaḥ tāvat māsaiḥ phalam yacchati aṣṭau sāravya vatsaraiḥ ye divyāḥ ketavaḥ te api śaśvat jīva phala pradāḥ hrasvaḥ snigdhaḥ su prasannaḥ śveta ketuḥ su vṛṣṭi kṛt kṣiprāt astamayam yāti dīrgha ketu ra vṛṣṭi kṛt aniṣṭa daḥ dhūmaketuḥ śakra cāpa sama prabhaḥ dvi tri catur śūla rūpaḥ sa ca rājya anta kṛt mataḥ maṇi hāraḥ tuvarṇa ābhāḥ dīptimantaḥ arka sūnavaḥ ketavaḥ coditāḥ pūrva aparayoḥ nṛpa hāni dāḥ vaṃsuka biṃba kṣitija chukatuṇḍa ādi sannibhāḥ hutāśana uditāḥ te api ketavaḥ phala dāḥ smṛtāḥ bhūsutāḥ jala taila ābhāḥ vartulāḥ kṣudh bhaya pradāḥ subhikṣa kṣema dāḥ śveta ketavaḥ soma sūnavaḥ pitāmaha ātmajaḥ ketuḥ tri varṇaḥ tridaśa anvitaḥ brahmadaṇḍāt dhūmaketuḥ prajānām anta kṛt mataḥ aiśānyām bhārgava sutāḥ śveta rūpāḥ tu aniṣṭa dāḥ aniṣṭadāḥ paṅgusutāḥ viśikhāḥ kamaka āhvayāḥ vikaca ākhyāḥ gurusutāḥ veṣṭāḥ yāmye sthitāḥ api sūkṣmāḥ śuklāḥ budha sutāḥ caura roga bhaya pradāḥ kuja ātmajāḥ kuṅkuma ākhyāḥ raktāḥ śūlāḥ tu aniṣṭa dāḥ agni jāḥ viśva rūpa ākhyāḥ agni varṇāḥ sukha pradāḥ aruṇāḥ śyāmala ākārāḥ arka putrāḥ ca pāpa dāḥ śukra jāḥ ṛkṣa sadṛśāḥ ke tavaḥ śubha dāyakāḥ kṛttikāsu bhavaḥ dhūmaketuḥ nūnam prajā kṣayaḥ prāsāda vṛkṣa śaileṣu jātaḥ rājñām vināśa kṛt āvarta ketu saṃdhyāyām śaśiraḥ na iṣṭa dāyakaḥ cāndramārkṣam guroḥ mānam iti mānāni vai navaḥ eteṣām nava mānānām vyavahāraḥ atra pañcabhiḥ teṣām pṛthak pṛthak kāryam vakṣyate vyavahārataḥ grahāṇām nikhilaḥ cāraḥ gṛhyate saura mānataḥ vṛṣṭeḥ vidhānam strī garbhaḥ sāvanena eva gṛhyate pravarṣaṇām same garbhaum nākṣatreṇa pragṛhyate yātrā udvāha vrata kṣaure tithi varṣa īśa nirṇayaḥ parva vāstu upavāsa ādi kṛtsnam cāndreṇa gṛhyate guru madhyama cāreṇa ṣaṣṭi abdāḥ prabhāva ādayaḥ aṅgirāḥ śrīmukhaḥ bhāvaḥ yuvā dhātā tathā eva ca īśvaraḥ bahudhānyaḥ ca pramāthī vikramaḥ vṛṣaḥ citrabhānuḥ subhānuḥ ca tāraṇaḥ pārthivaḥ avyayaḥ sarva jit sarva dhārī ca virodhī vikṛtaḥ kharaḥ hemalaṃbaḥ vilaṃbaḥ ca vikārī śārvarī lavaḥ śubhakṛt śobhanaḥ krodhī viśvāvasu parābhavau plavaṅgaḥ kīlakaḥ saumyaḥ sāma āptaḥ ca virodha kṛt paribhāvī pramādī ca ānandaḥ rākṣasaḥ analaḥ piṅgalaḥ kāla yuktaḥ ca siddhārthaḥ raudra durmatīḥ nāma tulya phalāḥ sarve vijñeyāḥ ṣaṣṭi vatsarāḥ yugam syāt pañcabhiḥ varṣaiḥ yugāni evam tu dvādaśa teṣām īśāḥ kramāt jñeyāḥ viṣṇuḥ devapurohitaḥ purandaraḥ lohitaḥ ca tvaṣṭā ahirbudhnya saṃjñakaḥ pitaraḥ ca tatas viśve śaśi indrāt agni yaśinaḥ bhagaḥ tathā yugasya varṣe śāstu agninā indu vidhi īśvarāḥ atha a dveśa camū nātha sasyapānām balābalam tad kālam graha cāram ca samyak jñātvā phalam saumyāḥ yanam māsa ṣaṭkam mṛga ādyam bhānu bhuktitaḥ ahar surāṇām tat rātriḥ karka ādyam dakṣiṇāyanam gṛha praveśa vaivāha pratiṣṭā maiñjibandhanam madhā ādau maṅgalam karma vidheyam ca uttarāyaṇe mādha ādi māsau dvau dvau ca ṛtavaḥ śiśira ādayaḥ mṛgāt śiśiḥ avasaṃtaḥ ca grīṣmāḥ syuḥ ca uttarāyaṇe varṣā śaraḥ ca hemantaḥ karkāt vai dakṣiṇāyane cāndraḥ darśīvadhiḥ sauraḥ saṃkrātyā sāvanaḥ dineḥ triṃśadbhiḥ candra bhagaṇaḥ māsaḥ nākṣatra saṃjñakaḥ madhuḥ ca mādhavaḥ śukraḥ śuciḥ ca atha nabhaḥ tatas nabhasyaḥ iṣaḥ ūrjaḥ ca sahāḥ ca eva sahasyakaḥ tapāḥ tapasya kramaśas caitra ādīnām samāhvayā yasmin māse paurṇamāsī yena dhiṣṇena saṃyutā tad nakṣatra āhvayaḥ māsaḥ paurṇamāsī tad āhvayā tad pakṣau śukla kṛṣṇau tathā apare śubha aśubhe karmaṇi ca praśastau bhavataḥ sadā kramāt tithīnām brahma agnī viriñci viṣṇu śailajāḥ mahendra vāsavau nāga durgā daṇḍadhara āhvayaḥ śiva viṣṇu hari ravī kāmaḥ sarvaḥ kalī tataḥ candra viśvedarśa saṃjña tithi īśāḥ pitaraḥ smṛtāḥ pūrṇāḥ syuḥ tithayaḥ punar tris āvṛttyā kramāt jñeyāḥ na iṣṭa madhya iṣṭa dāḥ site kṛṣṇa pakṣe tu iṣṭa madhya aniṣṭa dāḥ kramaśas tadā aṣṭamī dvādaśī ṣaṣṭī caturthī ca caturdaśī tithayaḥ pakṣa randhra ākhyāḥ hi ati rūkṣā prakīrtitāḥ samudra manu randhra aṅka tattva saṃkhyāḥ tu nāḍikāḥ tyājyāḥ syuḥ tāsu tithiṣu kramāt pañca ca sarvadā amāvāsyā ca navamī hitvā viṣama saṃjñikā ṣaṣaaṭyām tailam tathā aṣṭamyām māsam kṣauram kaleḥ tithau pūrṇimā darśayoḥ nārī sevanam parivarjayet derśe ṣaṣṭyām pratipadi dvādaśyām pratiparvasu vyatīpāte ca saṃkrāntau ekādaśyām ca parvasu arka bhauma dine ṣaṣṭyām na abhyaṅgaḥ vaidhṛtau tathā yaḥ karoti daśamyām ca snānam āmalakaiḥ naraḥ putra hāniḥ bhavet tasya traṃyodaśyām dhana kṣayaḥ artha putra kṣayaḥ tasya dvitīyāyām na saṃśayaḥ amāyām ca navamyām ca saptamyām ca kula kṣayaḥ yā paurṇimā divā candramatī sā anumatī smṛtā rātrau candravatī rākā api amāvāsyā tathā dvidhā sinīvālī ca indumatī kuhūḥ nā indumatī matā kārtike śukla navamī tu ādiḥ kṛta yugasya ca tretā ādiḥ mādhave śukle tṛtīyā puṇya saṃjñitā kṛṣṇā pañcadaśī māghe dvāpara ādim udīritā kalpādiḥ syāt kṛṣṇapakṣe nabhaḥ tasya trayodaśī caitre bhādrapade ca eva tṛtīyā śukla saṃjñitā ekādaśī sitā pauṣe hi āṣāḍheḥ deśamī sitā māghe ca saptamī śuklā nabhasye tu asitā aṣṭamī śrāvaṇe māsi amāvāsyā phaālgune māsi paurṇimā āṣāḍhe kārtike māsi jyaṣṭe caitre ca paurṇimā manu ādayaḥ mānavānām śrāddheṣu atyanta puṇya dā bhādre kṛṣṇa trayodaśyām maghām induḥ kare raviḥ gajacchāyā tadā jñeyā śrāddhe hi atyanta puṇya dā vidyate sā tu akhaṇḍā syāt nyūnā ced khañja saṃjñitā titheḥ pañcadaśaḥ bhāgaḥ kramāt pratipad ādayaḥ kṣaṇa saṃjñāḥ tad arddhāni tāsām arddha pramāṇataḥ laghuḥ ījyaḥ mṛduḥ śukraḥ trīkṣṇaḥ dinakara ātmajaḥ ṛkṣa īśe kānti bhāj bhaume vyādhi saubhāgyam indu je laṅkā udayāt syāt vāra ādiḥ tasmāt ūrdhvam adhas api vā deśa antara sva cara arddha nāḍībhiḥ apare bhavet indu jña jīva śukrāṇām vāsarāḥ sarva karmasu dūrvā varṇaḥ vudhaḥ jīvaḥ pīta śvetaḥ tu bhārgavaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sauriḥ sva vāreṣu sva sva varṇa kriyāḥ hitāḥ adri vāṇāḥ ca yaḥ tarka pātāla vasudhā dharāḥ bāṇa agni locana ānihya vedabāhu śilīmukhāḥ kulikāḥ ca upakulikāḥ vāravelāḥ stathā kramāt prahara arddha pramāṇāḥ te vijñeyāḥ sūrya vāsarāt yasmin vāre kṣaṇaḥ vāra dṛṣṭaḥ tad vāsara adhipaḥ ādyaḥ ṣaṣṭaḥ dvitīyaḥ asmat tad ṣaṣṭhaḥ tu tṛtīyakaḥ ṣaṣṭaḥ ṣaṣṭaḥ ca itareṣām kāla horā adhipāḥ smṛtāḥ sārddha nāḍī dvayena eva divā rātrau yathākramāt nakṣatra īśāḥ kramāt dasra yama vahni pitāmahāḥ candra īśa aditi jīva ahi pitaraḥ bhaga saṃjñakaḥ aryama arka tvaṣṭṛ marut śakra agni mitra vāsavaḥ ajā ekapād ahirbudhnyā pūṣā ca iti prakīrtitāḥ pūrvā trayam śilpa karma kalā kūpa nikṣepa uddharaṇa ādi yat mitra indu tvāṣṭra hasta indra aditi bhānti āśvi vāyubham brahma viṣṇu maheśa ārya śata tārā vasu uttarāḥ ūrddhāsyam navakam bhānām proktam atra vidhīyate nṛpa abhiṣeka māṅgalya vāraṇa dhvaja karma ca prāsāda toraṇa ārāma prākāra ādyam ca siddhi ati sthiram rohiṇī uttara ākhyam kṣipram sūrayā aśvi puṣya bham sādhāraṇam dvidaivatyam vahnibham ca prakīrtitam vasu aditi aṃvu puṣyāṇi viṣṇubham cara saṃjñitam mūla ārdra ahi indra bham tīkṣṇam sva nāma sadṛśam phalam citra āditya aṃbu viṣṇu ambā antya adhimitra vasu uḍuṣu sa mṛga ijyeṣu bālānām karṇavedhaṅkriyā hitā vāji karma akhilam kāryam sūryavāre viśeṣataḥ darśa aṣṭabhyām caturdaśyām paśūnām na kadācana mṛdu dhruva kṣipra cara viśākhā pitṛ bheṣu ca hala pravāham prathamam vidadhyāt mūlabhe vṛṣaiḥ ha l ādau vṛṣa anāśāya bha trayam sūrya mukta bhāt śūla traye api navakam maraṇāya ca pañcakam śriyai puṣṭyai trayam śreṣṭham syāt cakre lāṅgala āhvaye mṛdu dhruva kṣi prabheṣu pitṛ vāyu vasu ūṅṣu sa mūlabheṣu bīja uptiḥ atyuntkṛṣṭam phala pradā bhavet bha tritayam mūrghni dhānya nāśāya rāhu bhāt nistaṃhula tvam lāṅgūle bha catuṣṭaya bhīti dam sthireṣu aditi sārpa antya pitṛ māruta bheṣu ca na kuryāt roga muktasya snānam āhīm puṣya arka pauṣṇa dhiṣṇyeṣu nṛtya āraṃbhaḥ praśasyate pūrva arddha yuñji ṣaṅ bhani pauṣṇabhāt udabhāt tatas madhyayuñji dvādaśa ṛkṣāṇi indrabhāt navabhāni ca kramaśas saṃprītiḥ dampateḥ mathaḥ jaghanyāḥ toyapa ārdra ahi pavana antaka nākapāḥ krama aditi dvi daivatyāḥ bṛhat tārāḥ parāḥ samāḥ tāsām pramāṇa ghaṭikāḥ triṃśat navati di aṣṭayaḥ aśvagri indvījya nairṛtya tvāṣṭrajatti uttarābhavāḥ pitṛ dvi daiva vasu ākhyāḥ tārāḥ syuḥ kula saṃjñikāḥ dhātṛ jyeṣṭa aditi svātī pauṣṇa arka hari devatāḥ aja ahi antyaka bhaujaṅga tārāḥ ca eva ākula āhvayāḥ śeṣāḥ kulākulāḥ tārāḥ tāsām madhye kuloḍuṣu bheṣu upakula saṃjñeṣu jayam āpnoti niścitam saṃdhiḥ vā api tayoḥ sāmyam kula ākula gaṇa uḍuṣu arka ārki bhauma vāre ced bhadrāyāḥ viṣama aṅghri bham tri puṣkaram triguṇa dam dviguṇam yamala ahi bham tat yāt tad doṣa nāśāya go trayam mūlyam eva vā dvi puṣkare dvayam dadyāt na doṣaḥ tu ṛkṣabhaḥ api vā vinā pāṇigraham sarva maṅgaleṣu iṣṭa daḥ sadā rāma agni ṛtu bāṇa agni bhūveda agni śareṣu ca netra bāhu śara idvindu bāhu veda agni saṃkarāḥ tārā saṃkhyāḥ ca vijñeyāḥ dasra ādīnām pṛthak pṛthak yāḥ dṛśyante dīpta tārāḥ sva gaṇe yoga tārakāḥ vṛṣaḥ vṛkṣoḥ ca bhāyāmi adhiṣṇyeyam akaraḥ taruḥ uḍuṃbaraḥ ca agni dhiṣṇye rohiṇyām jaṃbukaḥ taruḥ indubhāt khadiraḥ jātaḥ kṛṣṇaplakṣaḥ ca raudrabhāt saṃbhūtaḥ aditibhāt vaṃśaḥ pippalaḥ puṣya saṃbhavaḥ sarva dhiṣṇyāt nāgavṛkṣaḥ vaṭaḥ pitṛ bha saṃbhavaḥ pālāśaḥ bhāgyabhāt jātaḥ akṣaḥ ca aryama saṃbhavaḥ svāti ukṣa jaḥ ajunaḥ vṛkṣaḥ dvidaivatyāt vikaṅkataḥ mitrabhāt bakulaḥ jātaḥ viṣṭiḥ paurandara ṛkṣa jaḥ sarjjavṛkṣaḥ mūlabhāñca vañjulaḥ vāridhiṣṇyajaḥ panasaḥ vaiśvabhāt jātaḥ ca arkavṛkṣaḥ ca viṣṇubhāt vasudhiṣṇyāt śamīvṛkṣaḥ kadaṃbaḥ vāruṇa ṛkṣa jaḥ madhu vṛkṣaḥ pauṣṇa dhiṣṇyāt dhiṣṇyavṛkṣāḥ prakīrtitāḥ yasmin śaṃnā aiśvaraḥ dhiṣṇye tad ṛkṣaḥ arcyaḥ prayatnataḥ yogeśāḥ yama viśva indu dhātṛ jīva niśākarāḥ gaṇeśa rudra dhanada tvaṣṭṛ mitra ṣaḍānanāḥ sāvatrī kamalā gaurī nāsatyau pitaraḥ aditiḥ vaidhṛtiḥ ca vyatīpātaḥ mahāpātau ubhau sadā viṣkaṃbha vajrayoḥ tisraḥ ṣaḍ vā vyāga ghāte nava śūle tu pañca nāḍyaḥ hi garhitāḥ jñeyāni sahacitrāṇi mūrddhabhāni yathākramam eka argalaḥ dṛṣṭipātaḥ ca abhijit varjitāni vai vināḍībhiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ rahitam ghaṭikā dvayam yogam prakaraṇam yogāḥ kramāt tu saptaviṃśatiḥ indraḥ prajāpatiḥ mitraḥ tvaṣṭā abhū hariti priyā kīnāśaḥ tithi arddha īśāḥ tu ahiḥ marut bava ādi vaṇija antāni śubhāni karaṇāni ṣaḍ parītā viparītā vā viṣyiḥ na iṣṭā tu maṅgale mukhe pañca gale ca ekā vakṣasi ekādaśa smṛtaḥ nābhau catasraḥ ṣaḍ kaṭyām tisraḥ puccha ākhya nājikāḥ kārya hāniḥ mukhe mṛtyuḥ gale vakṣasi niḥsva tā kaṭyām unmatta tā nābhau cyutiḥ pucche dhruvam jayaḥ sthirāṇi madhyamāni eṣām madhya nāga catuṣpadau divāmuhūrtā rudra ahi mitra pitṛ vasu udakam aryamā bhaga saṃjñaḥ ca vijñeyāḥ daśa pañca ca īśa aja pāda ahirbudhnya pūṣa aśvi yama vahnayaḥ dhātṛ indra aditi ijyā ākhyāḥ viṣṇu arka tvaṣṭṛ vāyavaḥ ahnaḥ pañcadaśaḥ bhāgaḥ tathā rātri pramāṇataḥ muhūrta mānam dvarā vakṣaṇa ṛkṣāṇi sama īśvaram rākṣasa ākhyau brāhma pitryau bharga aja aṃśa avalina ādiṣu vāreṣu varjanīyāḥ te muhūrtāḥ śubha karmasu yeṣu ṛkṣeṣu yat karma kathitam nikhilam ca tat tad daivatye muhūrte api kāryam yātrā ādikam sadā bhūkaṃpaḥ sūrya bhāt saptama ṛkṣe vidyut ca pañcame śūlaḥ aṣṭame ca daśame śāniḥ aṣṭādaśe tatas ketuḥ pañcadaśe daṇḍaḥ ulkāḥ ekonaviṃśatau nirghāta pāta saṃjñaḥ ca jñeyaḥ sa nava pañcame moha nirghātakam pāḥ ca kuliśam pariveṣaṇam vijñeyāḥ ekaviṃśa ṛkṣāt ārabhya ca yathākramam sūrya bhāt sarva pitrya ṛkṣam tvāṣṭra mitra pta bheṣu ca sa viṣa aṇu bheṣu kramaśas hasta bhān candra saṃyutaḥ caṇḍīśa caṇḍāyudha ākhyaḥ tasmin na eva ācaret śubham vijñeyaḥ śubha karma vināśa kṛt ānandaḥ kāladaṇḍa ākhyaḥ dhūmradhātṛ sudhākarāḥ dhvāṅkṣadhvaja ākhya śrīvatsa vajramudgara chatrakāḥ kāṇa siddhiśubhāḥ mṛtyu muśala anta karku jarāḥ rākṣasa ākhya vara sthairya varddhamānāḥ kramāt amī yogāḥ sva saṃjñā phala dāḥ aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ īritāḥ vaiśvadevāt bhagu sute vāruṇāt bhāskara ātmaje saumye mitrabham ācāryam tiṣyaḥ pauṣṇam bhṛgoḥ sute rohiṇī mandavāre ca siddhi yoga āhvayāḥ amī āditya bhaumayoḥ nandā bhadrā śukra śaśāṅkayoḥ jaya asaumye gurau riktā śanaupūrṇā iti no śubhāḥ nandā tithiḥ śukravāre saumye bhadrā kuje jayā riktā mande guroḥ vāre pūrṇā siddha āhvayāḥ amī ekādaśyām induvāraḥ dvādaśyām arkavāsaraḥ ṣaṣṭī gurau tṛtīyā jñe aṣṭamī śukre śanaiścare navamī pañcamī bhaume dagdhayogāḥ prakīrtitāḥ budhe śraviṣṭā aryam abhe gurau jyeṣṭā bhṛgoḥ dine viśākhā ādi catur vargam arkam arka vāra ādiṣu kramāt utpāta mṛtyu kāraṇa ākhya siddhi yogāḥ prakīrtitāḥ tithi vāra udbhavāḥ na iṣṭāḥ yogāḥ vāra ṛkṣa saṃbhavāḥ hūṇa vaṅga khaseṣu anya deśeṣu ati śubha pradāḥ ghora aṣṭākṣī mahodaryaḥ mandā mandākinī tathā miśrā rākṣasikā sūrya vāra ādiṣu yathākramam śūdra taskara vaiśya kṣmā deva bhūpa gavām kramāt anuktānām ca sarveṣām ghora ādyāḥ sukha dāḥ smṛtāḥ pūrvāhne nṛpatīn hanti viprān madhyandine viśaḥ aparāhne asta ge śūdrān pradoṣe ca piśācakān niśi rātri carān nāṭya kārān apararātrike gopān uṣasi saṃdhyāyām liṅginaḥ ravi saṃkramaḥ rātrau subhikṣam atulam saṃdhyayoḥ vṛṣṭi nāśanam hari śārdūla vārāha khara kuñjara māhiṣāḥ pāda āyudhāḥ karaṇa vāhanāḥ bhuśuḍī ca gadā khaḍgau daṇḍaḥ iṣa avāsa tomarau kunta pāśa aṅkuśa astra iṣūn bibharti karayoḥ tvinaḥ annam ca pāyasam bhaikṣyam sa yūṣam ca payaḥ dadhi miṣṭānnam guḍa madhu ājya śarkarāḥ vavataḥ haviḥ bālave gocara sthitau catuḥ pāde tila nāge suptaḥ krāntim karoti hi dharma āyuḥ vṛṣṭiṣu samam śreṣṭham naṣṭam phalam kramāt āyudham vāhana āhārau yad jātīyam janasya ca svāpa upaviṣṭāḥ tiṣṭhantaḥ te lokāḥ kṣemam āpnuyuḥ andhakam manda saṃjñam ca madhya saṃjñam sulocanam papīyāt gaṇayodbhāni rohiṇī ādi caturvidham sthira bheṣu arka saṃkrāntiḥ jñeyā viṣṇu pada āhvayā ṣaḍaśīti mukhāḥ jñeyāḥ dvi svabhāveṣu rāśiṣu tulā ghaṭa ajayoḥ jñeyaḥ viṣuvat sūrya saṃkramaḥ yāmya ayane sthire tu ādyāḥ parāḥ saumya indu mūrtibhaiḥ medhyāḥ viṣuvati proktāḥ puṇyanāḍyaḥ tu ṣoḍaśa saṃdhyā tri nāḍī pramitā arka biṃba ūrddha udayāḥ tatas prāk paścāt yāmya saumye ced puṇyam pūrvām pare ahani yādṛśena indunā bhānoḥ saṃkrāntiḥ tādṛśam phalam naraḥ prāpnoti tad rāśau śītāṃśoḥ sādhu asādhu ca saṃkrānteḥ paratas bhānuḥ bhuktvā yāvadbhiḥ aṃśakaiḥ raveḥ ayana saṃkrāntiḥ tadā tad rāśi saṃkramāt sa krānti graha ga ṛkṣam vā janmani ubhaya pārśvayoḥ vrata udvāha ādikeṣu eva dvayam na iṣṭam tu tad kramāt tatra hema vinikṣipya dadyāt doṣa apavṛttayeḥ tārā balena śītāṃśuḥ balavān tad vaśāt raviḥ balī saṃkramamāṇaḥ tu tadvat kheṭāḥ bala adhikāḥ śubha urake janmataḥ tri āya daśa ṣaṭsu muni īśvara śubhaḥ janma ṛkṣataḥ candraḥ dyūna āṅgāya ari su a triṣu tri āyāriṣu kujaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ janmanā ced na vidhyate vyayeṣu aṅka sthitaiḥ sauri saumya sūryaiḥ śubha auṣadhāt jñaḥ svāyāri aṣṭa ravayiṣu janmataḥ ced na vidhaayate dhī tryakā ādi gaja antasthaiḥ śaśāṅka rahitaiḥ śubhaiḥ janma rāśeḥ guruḥ śreṣṭhaḥ svāya gaḥ adhyasta gaḥ na ced vidhyata intya aṣṭa rava ambu tri gataiḥ rava eṭaiḥ muni īśvarā janma bhādā suta aṣṭa aṅka antyāyeṣu iṣṭaḥ bhṛgoḥ sutaḥ ced na viddhaḥ aṣṭa sapta aṅgam rava aṅka ādyāya ari rāma gaiḥ tasmāt vedham vicārya atha kathanīyam śubha aśubham vāmabheda vidhānena duṣṭaḥ api syāt śubhaṅkaraḥ saumya īkṣitaḥ aniṣṭa phalaḥ śubha daḥ pāpa vīkṣitaḥ nīca rāśi gataḥ svasya śatroḥ kṣetra gataḥ api vā śubha aśubha phalam nā eva dadyāt astamitaḥ upi vā graheṣu viṣama stheṣu śāntim kuryāt prayatnataḥ hāniḥ vṛddhiḥ graha adhīnā tasmāt pūjyatamāḥ grahāḥ maṇiḥ muktāphalam vidruma ākhyam maraka tam tathā puṣparāgam tathā vajram nīlam gomeda saṃjñitam dūryyam bhāskara ādīnām tuṣṭya dhāryam yathākramam sa pakṣaḥ tasya śubha daḥ kṛṣṇa pakṣaḥ nyathā śubhaḥ śuklapakṣe śubhaḥ candraḥ dvitīya nava pañcame janma tri pañca sapta ākhyāḥ tārāḥ na iṣṭa phala pradāḥ śākam guḍam ca lavaṇam sa tilam kāñcanam kramāt aniṣṭa phala nāśāya dadyāt etat dvijātaye kṛṣṇe balavatī tārā śuklapakṣe balū śaśī candrasya dvādaśa avasthāḥ rāśau rāśau yathākramam yātrā udvāha ādi kāryeṣu nāma tulya phala pradāḥ ṣaṣṭi ghnam gata candra ṛkṣam tad kāla ghaṭikā anvitam pravāsa naṣṭa ākhya mṛtā jayaḥ hāsyam rati mudā śinibhuktiḥ jvaraḥ kaṃpaḥ susthitiḥ nāma sannibhāḥ paṭṭabandhana yāna ugra saṃdhi vigraha bhūṣaṇam kṛṣi vāṇijya paśu ādi duṣṭa lagne prasiddhi ati kalā vijñāna śilpāni bhūṣaṇa āhava saṃśravam vāpī kūpa taḍāga ādi vāribandhana mokṣaṇam pauṣṭikam lipi lekhā ādi kartavyam karkaṭa udaye ikṣu dhānya vaṇij paṇya kṛṣi sevā ādayaḥ sthire vidyā śilpa auṣadham kṛtyam bhūṣaṇam ca cara sthiram kṛṣi vāṇijya yānam ca paśu udvāha vrata ādikam tulāyām akhilam karma tulā bhāra āśrite ca yat sthira karma akhilam kāryam rāja sevā abhiṣecanam caurya karma sthira āraṃbhāḥ kartavyāḥ vṛścika udaye vrata udvāha prayāṇa aśva gaja śilpa kalā ādikam cāpa bandhana mokṣa astra kṛṣi go śva ādikam yat prasthānam paśu dāsa ādi kartavyam makara udaye kṛṣi vāṇijya paśu aṃbu śilpa ṅkarma kalā ādikam jala pātra astrā śastra ādi kartavyam kalaśa udaye vrata udvāha abhiṣeka aṃbu sthāpanam sanniveśanam bhūṣaṇam jala pātra aśva karma mīna udaye śubham meṣa ādiṣu kligneṣu śuddheṣu evam prasiddhi ati krūra graha īkṣiteṣu ugra saṃyuteṣu ugram eva hi go yugma karka kanyā antya tulā cāpa dharāḥ śubhāḥ śubha ṛkṣa tva aśubha asatyaḥ itarā pāpa rāśayaḥ ādhāra bhūtena ādheyam dhīyate paridhiṣṭinam ca induḥ induḥ śubha daḥ sarve grahāḥ śubha phala pradāḥ aśubhaḥ ced aśubha dāḥ varjayitvā dhanādhipam lagnasya abhyuditāḥ ye iṃśāḥ teṣu aṃśeṣu sthitaḥ grahaḥ evam sthāneṣu śeṣeṣu ca evam evam prakalpayet doṣa alpatvam guṇa ādhikyam bahu saṃtatam iṣyate doṣāt duṣṭaḥ hi kālaḥ tam api mārṣṭum pitāmahaḥ api aśauca tuṇa ādhikyam doṣa anyatte tatas hi te amārikta aṣṭamī ṣaṣṭī dvādaśī pratipatsu api saṃdhyāsu upaplave viṣṭyām aśubham prathama ārttavam rugṇā pati priyā duḥkhī putriṇī bhogamī tathā pativratā keśa yuktā sūrya vāra ādiṣu kramāt yāma agni raudrabhāgya yāhi dvīśa indra ādi hi upadviṣāḥ tārakāḥ na hitāḥ māsāḥ madhu ūrja śuci pauṣakāḥ bhadrā ca saṃkramaḥ nidrā rātriḥ candra arkayoḥ grahaḥ kulaṭā pāpa bhogeṣu nindya ṛkṣe nindya vāsare tila ājya dūrvāḥ juhuyāt gāyatryā aṣṭaśatam budhaḥ ādyāḥ niśaḥ catasraḥ tu tyājyāḥ hi api samāḥ paraiḥ oja rāśi aṃśa ge candre lagne puṅgraha vīkṣite putra arthī puruṣaśas tyaktvā pauṣṇa mūla ahi pitrya bham māse puṃsavanam kāryam sīmantam ca yathā tathā caturthe māsi ṣaṣṭe vā api aṣṭame vā tad īśvare tīkṣṇa miśra arka varjyeṣu śubha graha yute dṛṣṭe pāpa dṛṣṭi vivarjite krūra grahāṇām ekaḥ api lagnāt antya ātmaja aṣṭagaḥ sīmantinīm vā tad garbham balī hṝnti na saṃśayaḥ tasmin janma muhūrte api sūtaka ante pi vā śiśoḥ nāma pūrvam praśastam syāt maṅgalaiḥ su samīkṣitaiḥ deśa kāla upaghāta ādyaiḥ kāla atikramaṇam yadā an asta ge bhṛgau ījye tad kārye ca uttarāyaṇe candrā tārā bala upete divase ca śiśoḥ pituḥ śubha lagne śubha aṃśe ca nidhane śuddhi saṃyute ṣaṣṭe māsi aṣṭame vā api puṃsām strīṇām tu pañcame saptame māsi vā kāryam nava anna praśanam śubham riktām dinakṣayam nandām dvādaśīm aṣṭamīm atha tyaktvā anya atithiṣu proktam praśanam śubha vāsare daśame śuddhi saṃyukte śubha lagne śubha aṃśake pūrva arddhe saumya kheṭena saṃyukte vīkṣite api vā tri ṣaṣṭa lābha gaiḥ krūraiḥ kendra dhī dharma gaiḥ śubhaiḥ tṛtīye pañcame ca abde sva kula ācārataḥ api vā bālānām janmataḥ caulam sva gṛhya ukta vidhānataḥ saumya ayane na asta gayoḥ sura ari sura mantriṇoḥ dasra aditi ijya candra indra pūṣabhāni śubhāni ca caula karmaṇi ca viṣṇu bhāt paṭṭabandhana caula annaprāśane ca upanāyane aṣṭame śuddhi saṃyuktem śubha lagne śubha aṃśake janma aṣṭame na śīta aṃśau ṣaṣṭa aṣṭa antya vivarjite kṣaura karma mahīpānām pañcame pañcame ahani nṛpa vipra ājñayā yajñe maraṇe bandha mokṣaṇeṃ udvāhe akhila vāra ṛkṣa tithiṣu kṣauram iṣṭa dam kartavyam maṅgaleṣu ādau maṅgalāya kṣura arpaṇam tṛtīye bīja nakṣatre śubha vāre śubha udaye samyak gṛhāṇi alaṅkṛtya vitāna dhvaja toraṇaiḥ āśiṣaḥ vācanam kāryam puṇyam puṇya aṅganā ādibhiḥ saha vāditra nṛtya ādyaiḥ gatvā prāc uttarām diśam tatra mṛda tatas tīkṣṇāḥ gṛhītvā punar āgataḥ mṛṇyaye api athavā vaiṇave api pātre prapūrayet aneka bīja saṃyuktam toyam puṣpa abhiśobhitam ādhānāt aṣṭame varṣe janmataḥ vā agrajanmanām maiñjībandhanam dvādaśe viśām janmataḥ pañcame varṣe upavītī yatas śrīmān kāryam tatra upanāyanam bālasya bala hīnaḥ apari sitaḥ jīvaḥ śubha pradaḥ dṛśyamāna gurau śukre śākhā īśe ca uttarāyaṇe vedānām adhipāḥ jīva śukra bhauma budhāḥ kramāt śarad grīṣma vasaṃteṣu vyutkramāt tu dvijanmanām mukhyam sādhāraṇam teṣām tapaḥ māsa ādi pañcasu vidhi jñaḥ ca arthavān caitre veda vedāṅga pāragaḥ vaiśāṣe dhanavān venda śāstra vidyā viśāradaḥ upanītaḥ bala āḍhyaḥ ca jyeṣṭhe vidhi vidām varaḥ śuklapakṣe dvitīyā ca tṛtīyā pañcamī tathā śreṣṭhā tu ekādaśī ṣaṣṭī dvādaśī anyāḥ tu madhyamāḥ dvi tri iṣu saṃkhyāḥ ca tithyaḥ anyāḥ hi ati ninditāḥ dhiṣṇāni arka traya anta ijya rudra āditya uttarāṇi ca viṣṇutraya aṃśvi mitra abjayoni bhāni upanāyane janma bhāt daśamam karma saṃghāta ṛkṣam tu ṣoḍaśam aṣṭādaśam samudayam trayoviṃśam vināśanam mānasam mānasam pañcaviṃśa ṛkṣam na ācaret śubham eṣu tu ācārya saumya kāvyānām vārāḥ śastāḥ śaśīnayoḥ dvitīye mānuṣam kāryam tṛtīye ḥṃśe ca paitṛkam sva nīca ge tad aṃśe vā sva aribhe vā tad aṃśake guru śikhinoḥ ca śākhā īśe kalā śīla vivarjitaḥ svādhi śatru gṛha sthe vā tad aṃśa sthe atha vā vratī śākhā īśe vā gurau śukre mahāpātaka kṛt bhavet sva ucca saṃsthe tad aṃśe vā sva rāśau rāśi ge gaṇe śākhā īśe vā gurau śukre kendra ge vā trikoṇa ge atīva dhanavān ca eva veda vedāṅga pāragaḥ parama ucca gate jīve śākhā īśe vā atha vā sate vratī viśuddhe nidhane veda śāstra viśāradaḥ gurau bhṛgau vā śākhā īśe vidyā dhana samanvitaḥ śākhādhipati vāraḥ ca śākhādhipa balam śiśoḥ tasmāt vedvāṃśa ge candre vratī vidyā viśāradaḥ pāpa aṃśa ge vā daridraḥ nitya duḥkhitaḥ śravaṇa ādini nakṣatre karka aṃśa sthe niśākare tadā vratī veda śāstra dhana dhānya samṛddhimān śubha lagne śubha aṃśe ca naidhane śuddhi saṃyute sthāna ādi bala saṃpūrṇaiḥ caturbhiḥ vā śubha anvitaiḥ īkṣan na eva atra ekaviṃśa mahā doṣa vivarjite rāśayaḥ sakalāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ śubha graha yuta īkṣitāḥ śubha nava aṃśaka gatāḥ grāhyāḥ te śubha rāśayaḥ na kadācid karkaṭa aṃśa śubha īkṣita yutaḥ api vā tasmāt go mithuna aṃśāḥ ca tulā kanyā aṃśakāḥ śubhāḥ triṣaṣ āya gataiḥ pāpaiḥ ṣaṣ aṣṭa antya vivarjitaiḥ śubhaiḥ ṣaṣṭa aṣṭa lagna antya varjitena himāṃśunā sva uñca saṃsthaḥ api śītāṃśuḥ vratinaḥ yadi lagna gaḥ na karoti śiśum niḥsvam sarvatas kṣaya rogiṇam sphūrjite kendra ge bhānau vratinām pitṛ nāśanam pañca doṣa ūnitam lagnam śubha dam ca upanāyane vinā vasaṃta ṛtunā kṛṣṇapakṣe galagrahe anadhyāye viṣṭi ṣaṣṭyoḥ na tu saskāram arhati caturthī vā śubhāḥ proktāḥ aṣṭāv ete galagrahāḥ kṣurikābandham vakṣye nṛpāṇām prāk karagrahāt vivāha ukteṣu māseṣu śuklapakṣe api an asta ge jīve śukre ca bhūputre candra tārā bala anvite śuddhe aṣṭame vidhau lagne ṣaṣṭa aṣṭa antya vivarjite kṣurikā bandhanam kāryam arcayitvā amarān pitṝn tatas su lagne badhnīyāt kaṭyām lakṣaṇa saṃyutām āyāma arddha agra vistāra pramāṇena eva chedayat tad cheda khaṇḍa anyāyāḥ syuḥ dhvaja āye ripu nāśanam ghūmrāye maraṇam siṃhe jayaḥ śuni ca rogi tā atyanta saṃprītiḥ dhvāṅkṣe vitta vināśanam khaḍga putrikayoḥ mānam gaṇayet sva aṅgulena tu māna aṅguleṣu paryāyām ekādaśa mitām tyajet śeṣāṇām agulīnām ca phalāni syuḥ yathākramam putra lābhaḥ śatru vadhaḥ strī lābhaḥ gamana śubham artha hāniḥ ca artha vṛddhiḥ siddhi jayaḥ stutiḥ sthitaḥ dhvaje vṛṣāye vā naṣṭā ced pūrvatas vraṇam atha uttarāyaṇe śukra jīvayoḥ ddaśyamānayoḥ dvijātīnām guroḥ gehāt nivṛttānām yata ātmanām citra uttara āditī jyā antya harimitra vidhātṛṣu bha iṣu arka indu jña ijya śukra vāra lagna aṃśakeṣu ca pratipad parva riktāḥ mā ca aṣṭamī ca dina trayam hitvā anya divase kāryam samāvartana muṇḍanam sarva āśramāṇām vipra indra hi uttamaḥ ayam gṛhāśramaḥ sukham tatra api bhāminyām śīlavatyām sthitam tatas pitāmaha uktam saṃvīkṣya lagna śuddhim pravacmi aham puṇye ahni lakṣaṇa upetam sukha āsīnam su cetasam tāṃbūla phala puṣpa ādyaiḥ pūrṇa añjaliḥ upāgataḥ daṃpatyoḥ maraṇa varṣāṇām aṣṭakāt purā vijñeyam bhartṛ maraṇam aṣṭa varṣa anttare budhaiḥ lagnāt pañcama gaḥ pāpaḥ śatru dṛṣṭaḥ ca nīca gaḥ mṛta putrā atha vā kanyā kulaṭā vā na saṃśayaḥ tṛtīya pañca sapta āya karma gaḥ vā niśākaraḥ lagnāt karoti saṃbandham daṃpatyoḥ guru vīkṣitaḥ tulā gokarkaṭāḥ lagna saṃsthaḥ śukra indu saṃyutāḥ vīkṣitāḥ pṛcchatām nṝṇām kanyā lābhaḥ bhavet tadā strī dreṣkāṇaḥ strī nava aṃśe yugma lagnam samāgatam vīkṣitam candra śukrābhyām kanyā lābhaḥ bhavet tadā evam strīṇām bhartṛ labdhiḥ pum lagne pum nava aṃśake kṛṣṇa pakṣe praśna lagna ādyasya rāśī yadā pāpa dṛṣṭaḥ atha vā randhre na saṃbandhaḥ bhavet tadā pañcāṅga śuddhi divase candra tārā bala anvite bhūṣaṇaiḥ puṣpa tāṃbūla phalaiḥ gandha akṣata ādibhiḥ śukla aṃbaraiḥ gīta vādyaiḥ vighna āśīrvacanaiḥ saha tadā kuryāt pitā tasyāḥ pradānam prīti pūrvakam varāya ca rūpavatīm kanyām dadyāt yavīyasīm saṃpūjya prārthayitvā ca śacīm devīm guṇa āśrayām trailokya sundarīm divya gandha mālya aṃbara āvṛtām sarva lakṣaṇa saṃyuktām sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitām anargha maṇi mālābhiḥ bhāsayantīm digantarān vilāsinī sahasra ādyaiḥ sevamānām aharniśam evaṃvidhām kumārīm tām pūjā ante prārthayet iti vivāhe bhāgyam ārogyam putra lābham ca dehi me yugme abde janmataḥ strīṇām pīti dam pāṇipīḍanam etat puṃsām ayugme abde vyatyayena aśanam tayoḥ māgha pha ālguna vaiśākha jyeṣṭa māsāḥ śubha pradāḥ madhyamā kārtikaḥ mārgaśīrṣaḥ vai ninditāḥ pare na kadācid vaśa ṛkṣeṣu bhānoḥ ārdrā praveśanāt vivāhaḥ devatānām ca pratiṣṭām ca upanāyanam na astaṅgate site jīve na tayoḥ bāla vṛddhayoḥ na gurau siṃha rāśi sthe siṃha aṃśaka gate pi vā paścāt prāc uditaḥ śukraḥ daśa tri divasam śiśuḥ buddhaḥ pañca dinam pakṣam guruḥ pakṣam ca sarvatas aprabuddhaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ yāvat tāvat na maṅgalam jyeṣṭa māse tayoḥ eka jyeṣṭhe śreṣṭhaḥ ca na anyathā utpāta grahaṇāt ūrddham sapta aham akhila grahe na akhile tri dinam na iṣṭam tridyu spṛś ca kṣayam tathā grastāḥ te tri dinam pūrvam paścāt grasta udaye athavā saṃdhyāyām tri dinam tadvat niśīthe sapta eva ca māsa ante pañca divasān tyajet riktām tathā aṣṭamīm vyatīpātam vaidhṛtim ca saṃpūrṇam parigha arddhakam vivāhe daṃpatyoḥ guru sūryayoḥ ced pūjā yatnataḥ kāryā durbala grahayoḥ tayoḥ gocaram vedha jam ca aṣṭavarga jam rūpa jam balam candra tārā balam vīkṣya tatas pañca aṅga jam balam tithiḥ ekaguṇā vāraḥ dviguṇaḥ triguṇam ca bham yogaḥ caturguṇaḥ pañcaguṇam tithi arddha saṃjñitam tatas balavatī horā dreṣkāṇaḥ balavān tatas tatas nava aṃśaḥ balavān dvādaśa aṃśaḥ balī tatas triṃśa aṃśaḥ balavān tasmāt vīkṣyam etat balābalam śubha īkṣita yutāḥ śastāḥ udvāhe akhila rāśayaḥ candra arka ijyā ādayaḥ paca yasya rāśeḥ tu khecarāḥ iṣṭāḥ tat śubha dam lagnam catvāraḥ api bala anvitāḥ ekaviṃśati doṣāṇām nāma rūpa phalāni ca vakṣyante atra samāsena śṛṇu nārada sāṃpratam pañcāṅga śuddhi rāhityam doṣaḥ tu ādyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ udaya asta śuddhiḥ hāniḥ dvitīyaḥ sūrya saṃkramaḥ tṛtīyaḥ pāpa ṣaḍvargaḥ bhṛguḥ ṣaṣṭaḥ kujaḥ aṣṭamaḥ gaṇḍa antam kartarī riṣa apha ṣaṣ aṣṭa indu gataḥ grahaḥ daṃpatyoḥ aṣṭamam lagnam rāśiḥ viṣa ghaṭī tathā durmuhīrtaḥ vāra doṣaḥ khārjūrika sama aṅghribham grahaṇa utpāta bham krūra viddha ṛkṣam krūra saṃyutam kunavāṃśaḥ mahāpātaḥ vaidhṛtiḥ ca ekaviṃśatiḥ tithi vāra ṛkṣa yogānām karaṇasya ca melanam pañcāṅgam asya śuddhiḥ tu pañcāṅga śuddhiḥ īritā tyajet pañcaiṣṭikam ca api viṣa saṃyukta dugdha vat varasya mṛtyuḥ syāt tābhyām sapta sapta udaya aṃśakau tyājyāḥ sūryasya saṃkrānteḥ pūrvatas paratas tathā vivāha ādiṣu kāryeṣu nāḍyaḥ ṣoḍaśa ṣoḍaśā ṣaḍvargaḥ śubha daḥ śreṣṭhaḥ vivāha sathāpana ādiṣu bhṛgu ṣaṣṭha āhvayaḥ doṣaḥ lagnāt ṣaṣṭha gate site kujaḥ aṣṭamaḥ mahā doṣaḥ lagnāt aṣṭama ge kuje pūrṇānanda āṅkhyayoḥ tithyoḥ saṃdhiḥ nāḍī dvayam yadā gaṇḍa antam mṛtyu dam janmayātrā udvāha vrata ādiṣu kulīra siṃhayoḥ kīṭa cāpayoḥ mina meṣayoḥ syāt haṭikā arddham mṛti pradam sārpa aindra pauṣṇa ubheṣu antya ṣoḍaśa īśāḥ bha saṃdhayaḥ tad agni meṣu ādya pādāḥ bhānām gaṇḍāta saṃjñakāḥ ugram ca saṃdhi tritayam gaṇḍātam trividham mahat sā kartarī iti vijñeyā daṃpatyoḥ gala kartarī ṣaṣ aṣṭa riṣpha ge candre lagna doṣaḥ sva saṃjñakaḥ śaśāṅke graha saṃyukte doṣaḥ saṃgraha saṃjñakaḥ daurbhāgyam guruṇā yukte sa apatyam bhārgaveṇa tu pravrajyā sūryaputreṇa rāhuṇā mūla saṃkṣayaḥ ketunā saṃyute candre nityam kaṣṭam daridra tā doṣāyanam bhavet lagnam daṃpatyoḥ śreyase sadā karoti maraṇam tayoḥ daṃpatyoḥ aṣṭamam lagnam aṣṭamaḥ rāśiḥ eva ca sa rāśiḥ śubha saṃyuktaḥ lagnam vā śubha saṃyutam lagnam vivarjayet yatnāt tad aṃśa aṃśa tad īśvarām daṃpatyoḥ dvādaśam lagnam rāśiḥ vā yadi lagna gaḥ kha mārgaṇāḥ vedapakṣāḥ kha rāmāḥ vedamārgaṇāḥ vahni candrāḥ rūpa dasrāḥ kha rāmāḥ vyoma bāhavaḥ dvi rāmāḥ śūnya dasrāḥ kuñjara bhūmayaḥ rūpapakṣāḥ vyomadasrāḥ vedacandrāḥ caturddaśa śūnyacandrāḥ vedacandrāḥ ṣaṣ ṛkṣāḥ vedabāhavaḥ śūnya dasrāḥ śūnya candrāḥ pūrṇa candrāḥ gata indravaḥ tarkacandrāḥ vedapakṣāḥ kha rāmāḥ ca aśvibhāt kramāt ābhyāḥ parāḥ tu ghaṭikāḥ catasraḥ viṣa saṃjñitāḥ vivāha ādiṣu kāryeṣu viṣa nāḍīm vivarjayet bhāskara ādiṣu vāreṣu ye muhūrtāḥ ca ninditāḥ vivāha ādiṣu te varjyāḥ api lakṣa guṇaiḥ yutāḥ nihita avāra doṣāḥ ye sūrya vāra ādiṣu kramāt grahaṇa utpāta bham tyājyam maṅgaleṣu ṛtu trayam yāvat ca śaśinā bhuktvā mukta bham dagdha kāṣṭa vat maṅgaleṣu tyajet śeṭaiḥ viddham ca krūra saṃyutam akhila ṛkṣam pañcagavyam surā bindu yutam tathā krūra viddham yutam dhiṣṇyam nikhilam na eva maṅgalam tulā mithuna kanyā aṃśāḥ dhanuḥ antya arddha saṃyutāḥ ete nava aṃśāḥ śubha dāḥ vṛṣabhasya aṃśakāḥ khalu antya aṃśāḥ te pi śubha dāḥ yadi varga uttama āhvayāḥ anye nava aṃśāḥ na grāhyāḥ yatas te ku nava aṃśakāḥ ku nava aṃśaka lagnam yat tyājyam sarva guṇa anvitam anuktāḥ su alpa doṣāḥ syuḥ vidyut nīhāra vṛṣṭayaḥ lattā upagrahapāta ākhyā māsadagdha āhvayā tithiḥ dagdha lagna andha badhira paṅgu saṃjñāḥ ca rāśayaḥ evamādyāḥ tatas teṣām vyavasthā kriyate adhunā akāla jāḥ bhavanti ete vidyut nīhāra vṛṣṭayaḥ doṣāya maṅgale nūnam adoṣāya eva kālatas bṛhaspatiḥ kendra gataḥ śukraḥ vā yadi vā budhaḥ tiryak pañca ūrddhū gāḥ pañca rekhāḥ dve dve ca koṇayoḥ dvitīye śaṃbhu koṇe agni dhiṣṇyam cakre pravinyaset puratas dina ṛkṣam lattayanti yat arka ākṛti guṇa ādi naṅga bāṇa aṣṭa nava saṃkhya bham sūryabhāt sārppa pitrya antya tvāṣṭra mitra uḍu viṣṇubham saṃkhyāyāḥ saurāṣṭre śālva deśe tu lattitam bham vivarjayet kaliṅga vaṅga deśeṣu pātitam na śubha pradam bāhlike kuru deśe ca anyasmin deśe na dūṣaṇam madhyadeśe vivarjyāni na dṛṣṭāni itareṣu ca ṣaṅgvam dha ka aṇa lagnāni māsa śūnyāḥ ca rāśayaḥ gauḍa mālavayoḥ tyājyāḥ anya deśe na garhitāḥ doṣa duṣṭam sadā kālam sat nimārṣṭum na śakyate api dhātuḥ atas grāhyam doṣa alpa tvam guṇa adhikam evam su lagne daṃpatyoḥ kārayet samyak īkṣaṇam staṃbhaḥ caturbhiḥ su ślakṣṇaiḥ vāma bhāge tu sanna tām sa maṇḍapām catur dikṣu sopānaiḥ atiśobhitām prāc udak pravaṇām raṃbhā staṃbhaiḥ haṃsa śuka ādibhiḥ vicitritām citra kuṃbhaiḥ vividhaiḥ toraṇa aṅkuraiḥ śṛṅgāra puṣpa nicayaiḥ varṇakaiḥ samalaṅkṛtām vipra āśīrvacanaiḥ puṇya srībhiḥ divyaiḥ manoramām vāditra nṛtya gīta ādyaiḥ hṛdaya ānandinīm śubhām evaṃvidhām samārohet mithunam sva agni vedikām aṣṭadhā rāśi kūṭam ca svādu uḍu gaṇa rāśayaḥ rāśi īśa yoniḥ varṇa ākhya ṛtavaḥ putra pautra dāḥ eka rāśau pṛthak diṣṇye daṃpatyoḥ pāṇi pījanam uttamam madhyamam bhinnam rāśya eka tvam yayoḥ tayoḥ eka ṛkṣe tu eka rāśau hi vivāhaḥ prāṇa hāni daḥ strī dhiṣṇyāt ādi a navake strī dūram ati ninditam dvitīye madhyamam śreṣṭham tṛtīye navake nṛbham tisraḥ pūrva uttarāḥ dhātṛ yāmya māheśa tārakāḥ iti martya gaṇe jñeyaḥ syāt amartya gaṇaḥ paraḥ hari āditya arka vāyu anti amitra aśvi ijyā indu tārakāḥ rakṣaḥ gaṇaḥ pitṛ tvāṣṭra dvi daiva agni indra tārakāḥ vasu vārīśa mūla ahi tārakābhiḥ yutāḥ tatas madhyamā deva martyānām rākṣasānām tayoḥ mṛtiḥ mṛtyuḥ ṣaṣṭa aṣṭake pañca navame tu anapatya tā dvis dvādaśe anyeṣu daṃpatyoḥ prītiḥ uttamā eka adhipe mitra bhāve śubha dam pāṇipīḍanam trikoṇe ca na kadācid ṣaṣ aṣṭake aśva ibha meṣa sarpa ahi hya utumeṣa utumūṣakāḥ ākhu go mahiṣa vyāghra kālī vyāghra mṛga dvayam śvānaḥ kapariḥ babhru yuge kapi siṃha turaṅgamāḥ siṃha godantinaḥ bhānām yonayaḥ syuḥ yathā aśvi bhāt śvaiṇam babhraragam meṣa vānarau siṃha vāraṇam go vyāghram ākhu mārjāram mahiṣa aścam ca śātravam jhaṣa ali karkaṭāḥ viprāḥ ta dūrdhvāḥ kṣatriya ādayaḥ pum varṇa rāśeḥ strī rāśau sati hīne yathāśubham catur tri vdi aṅghri bha utthāyāḥ kanyāyāḥ ca aśvi bhāt kramāt vahni bhāt indu bhāt nāḍī tri catur pañca parvasu gaṇayet saṃkhyayā ca eka nāḍyām mṛtyuḥ na pārśvayoḥ prājāpatya brāhma daivāḥ vivāhāḥ ca ārṣa saṃyutāḥ ukta kāle tu kartavyāḥ catvāraḥ phala dāyakāḥ gandharva asura paiśāca rākṣasa ākhyāḥ tu sarvadā prācyāḥ na ca kaliṅgānām mukhyam godhūlikam smṛtam abhijit sarva deśeṣu mukhyaḥ doṣa vināśa kṛt nāśayati akhilān doṣān pinākī tripuram yathā putra udvāhāt param putrī vivāhaḥ na ṛtu traye vivāhaḥ ca ekajanyānām ṣaṣ māsa abhyantare yadi na evam kadācid udvāhaḥ na ekadā muṇḍana dvayam divā jātaḥ tu pitaram rātrau tu jananīm tathā ātmānam saṃdhyayoḥ hanti na asti gaṇḍe viparyayaḥ sutaḥ sutā vā niyatam śvasuram mūla jaḥ tad antya pāda jaḥ nā eva tathā āśleṣa ādya pāda jaḥ jyeṣṭa antya pāda jau jyeṣṭam bālaḥ na bālikā na bālikā aṃbu mūla ṛkṣe mātaram pitaram tathā ārabhya udvāha divasāt ṣaṣṭe vā api aṣṭame dine saṃtyajya hi atiśukre api yātrā vaivāhikī śubhā śrī pradam sarva gīrvāṇa sthāpanam ca uttarāyaṇe gīrvāṇa pūrva gīrvāṇa matriṇoḥ dṛśyamānayoḥ vicaitreṣu eva māseṣu māgha ādiṣu ca pañcasu śuklapakṣeṣu kṛṣṇeṣu tad ādiṣu aṣṭasu śubham dvatīya ādi dvaye pañcamyā ādeḥ tisṛṣu kramāt daśamī ādeḥ catasṛṣu paurṇamāsyām viśeṣataḥ sa aśvi dhātṛ jala adhīśa harimitra vasuṣu api rāśayaḥ sakalāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ śubha graha yuta īkṣitāḥ pañca aṣṭake śubhe lagne naidhane śuddhi saṃyute lagna sthāḥ candra sūrya āra rāhu ketu arka sūnavaḥ karttuḥ mṛtyu pradāḥ ca anye dhana dhānya sukha pradāḥ dvitīye na iṣṭa dāḥ pāpāḥ vitta dāḥ tṛtīye nikhilāḥ kheṭāḥ putra pautra sukha pradāḥ caturthe sukha dāḥ saumyāḥ krūrāḥ kheṭāḥ ca duḥkha dāḥ glāni dāḥ pañcame krūrāḥ saumyāḥ putra sukha pradāḥ ṣaṣṭe śubhāḥ śatru dāḥ syuḥ pāpāḥ śabru kṣayaṅkarāḥ vyādhi dāḥ saptame pāpāḥ saumyāḥ śubha phala pradāḥ aṣṭama sthāḥ khagāḥ sarve kartuḥ mṛtyu pradāyakāḥ dharme pāpāḥ ghnanti saumyāḥ śubha dāḥ maṅgala pradāḥ karma gāḥ duḥkha dāḥ saumyāḥ candraḥ ca kīrti dāḥ lābha sthāna gatāḥ sarve bhūri lābha pradāḥ grahāḥ vyaya sthāna gatāḥ śaśvat bahu vyaya karāḥ grahāḥ kartāram mantra hīnāḥ tu ṛtvijam sriyam lakṣaṇa hīnāḥ tu na pratiṣṭā samaḥ ripuḥ surāṇām sthāpanam tatra kartuḥ iṣṭa artha siddhi dam nirmāṇa āyatana grāma gṛha ādīnām samāsatas kṣetram ādau parīkṣeta gandha varṇa rasa aṃśakaiḥ sitam raktam ca haritam kṛṣṇa varṇam yathākramam madhuram kaṭukam tiktam kaṣāyaka rasam kramāt atyanta vṛddhi dam nṝṇām īśāna prāc udak plavam anya dikṣu plave teṣām śaśvat atyanta hāni dam tathā niśā ādau tat kṛtvā pānīyena prapūrayet prātar dṛṣṭe jale vṛddhiḥ samam paṅke kṣayaḥ kṣaye evam lakṣaṇa saṃyuktam samyak kṣetram samīkṣyate dvādaśa aṅgulakam śaṅkum sthāpya īkṣet tatra diś tramam caturasrīkṛte kṣetre ṣaḍvarga pariśodhite āyāmeṣu catur dikṣu prāc ādiṣu ca satsu api aṣṭau aṣṭau pratidiśam dvārāṇi syuḥ yathākramam pradakṣiṇa kramāt teṣām amūni ca phalāni vai anāntakam vyādhi bhayam niḥsattvam dakṣiṇā diśi putra hāniḥ śatru vṛddhiḥ lakṣmī prāptiḥ dhana āgamaḥ saubhāgyam ati daurbhāgyam duḥkham śokaḥ ca paścime kalatra hāniḥ niḥ sattvam hāniḥ dhānya dhana āgamaḥ saṃpad vṛddhiḥ māsa bhītiḥ āmayam diśi śītagoḥ evam gṛha ādiṣu dvāra vistārāt dviguṇa ucchritam paścime dakṣiṇe vā api kapāṭam sthāpayet gṛhe prākāra antar kṣitim kuryāt ekāśīti padam yathā dvātriṃśat aṃśāḥ prākāra samīya aṃśāḥ samantataḥ piśāca aṃśe gṛha āraṃbhe duḥkha śoka bhaya pradaḥ śeṣa āśāḥ syuḥ ca nirmāṇe putra pautra dhana pradāḥ śirāḥ syuḥ vāstunoḥ rekhāḥ diś vidiś madhya saṃbhavāḥ brahma bhāgāḥ piśāca aṃśāḥ śirāṇām yatra saṃhatiḥ tatra tatra vijānīyāt vāstunaḥ marma saṃdhayaḥ marmāṇi saṃdhayaḥ na iṣṭāḥ svasthe api evam niveśane saumya pha ālguna vaiśākha māgha śrāvaṇa kārtikāḥ māsāḥ syuḥ gṛha nirmāṇe putra ārogya dhana pradāḥ akāra ādiṣu bhākṣu dikṣu prāc ādiṣu kramāt khara uśvaḥ utha hariḥ śva ākhyaḥ sa pokhu gaja śāśakāḥ diś vargāṇām iyam yoniḥ sva vargāt pañcamaḥ ripuḥ sādhya vargaḥ puras sthāpya pṛṣṭatas sādhakam nyaset vyatyaye nāśanam tasya ṛṇa madhyam dhanāt śubham ārabhya sādhakam ghiṣṇyam sādhyam yāvat caturguṇam vibhejet saptabhiḥ śeṣam sādhakasya dhanam tadā tasmāt dhana adhanāya ṛkṣa vāra aṃśāḥ saṃkhyayā kramāt dhana adhikam gṛham vṛddhyai ṛṇa adhikam aśobhanam viṣa māyaḥ śubhaghāya eva sa māyaḥ nirdhanāya ca ghana kṣayaḥ tṛtīya ṛkṣe pañcama ṛkṣe paraḥ kṣayaḥ ṣaṭka aṣṭakam mṛtyave syāt śubha dāra āśayaḥ pare sūrya aṅgāraka vārāṃśāḥ vaiśvānara bhaya pradāḥ itare graha vāra aṃśāḥ sarva kāma artha siddhi dāḥ nabhasya ādiṣu māseṣu triṣu triṣu yathākramam pūrva ādika śiraḥ vāma pārśva īśāya apradakṣiṇam yad diś mukhaḥ vāstu pumān kuryāt tat diś mukham gṛham vṛtya iṭikām svarṇa reṇu dhānya śaivala saṃyutam catur viśa trayorviṃśat ṣoḍaśa dvādaśa aṅgulaiḥ vipra ādīnām kukṣimānam svarṇa vastra ādi alaṅkṛtam raktacandana pālāśa raktaśāna viśāla jam śakum tridhā vibhajya andyam catur asram tatas param aṣṭa asram ca tṛtīyā asau manu asram mṛdum avraṇam evam lakṣaṇa saṃyuktam parikalpya śubhe dine ṣaḍvarga śuddhi sūtreṇa sūtrite dharaṇī tale vyarka āra cara lagneṣu pāpe ca aṣṭama varjite naidhane śuddhi saṃyukte śubha gha lagne śubha aṃśake śubha īkṣite atha vā yukte lagne śaṅkum vinikṣipet puṇya aha ghoṣaiḥ vāditraiḥ puṇya puṇya aṅganā ādibhiḥ lagna aṃśa aṣṭa ari candreṇa daivajña arcana pūrvakam eka dvi tri catur śālāḥ sapta śālāḥ daśa āhvayāḥ tāḥ punar ṣaḍvidhāḥ śālāḥ pratyekam daśa ṣaḍvidhāḥ dhruvam dhānyam jayam nandam kharaḥ kāntam manoramam sumukham durmukham krūram śatrum svarṇa pradam kṣayam ākrandam vipula ākhya ca vijayam ṣoḍaśam gṛham gṛhāṇi gaṇayet evam teṣām prastāra bhedataḥ kuryāt laghu pade alindam gṛha dvārāt pradakṣiṇam pūrvā digeṣu alindeṣu gṛha bhedāḥ tu ṣoḍaśa snāna āgāram diśi prācyām āgneyyām pāka mandiram yāmyām ca śayanāgāram nairṛtyām śāsra mandiram pratīcyām bhojanagṛham vā yavyām dhānya madiram kauberyām devatāgāram īśānyām kṣira mandiram śayyā mūtra astra tad vid ca bhojanam maṅgala āśrayam dhānya strī bhoga vittam ca śṛṅgāra āyatanāni ca īśānī ādi kramaḥ teṣām gṛha nirmāṇakam śubham eteṣu etāni śastrāṇi svam sthāpyāni sva dikṣu api dhvajaḥ dhūmraḥ utha siṃhaḥ śvā saurameyaḥ kharaḥ gajāḥ dhvāṅkṣaḥ ca eva bhavanti aṣṭau pūrva ādipāḥ kramāt amī plakṣa uduṃbara cūta ākhyāḥ niṃbaḥ tu hi vibhītakāḥ kaṭakāḥ dugdhavṛkṣāḥ vṛkṣa aśvattha kapitthakāḥ agasti siṃdhuvāla ākhya tintiḍīkāḥ ca ninditāḥ pitta vā agra ja dehaḥ syāt paścime dakṣiṇe tathā gṛhapāda agṛhastabhāḥ samāḥ śastāḥ ca na asamāḥ na ati ucchritam na ati nīcam kuḍya utsedham yathāruci gṛha upari gṛha ādīnām evam sarvatra cintayet gṛha ādīnām gṛhaśrāvam kramaśas aṣṭavidham smṛtam pāñcāla mānam vaideham kauravam ca kujanyakam māgadham śūrasenam ca gāndhārāvatikā smṛtam pāñcāla mātulānām ca hi uttarottara vṛddhitaḥ vaideha ādīni aśeṣāṇi mānāni syuḥ yathākramam pāñcāla mānam sarveṣām sādhāraṇam atas param avanti mānam viprāṇām gāndhāram kṣatriyasya ca kaujanya mānam vaiśyānām vipra ādīnām yathottaram uṣṭra kuñjara śālānām vā gaje paśu śālāḥ ca śālānām vā gaje dvāra śayyā aśana amatra dhvajāḥ siṃha vṛṣa dhvajāḥ vāstu pūjā vidhim vakṣye nava veśma praveśane hasta mātrāḥ likhet rekhāḥ daśa pūrvāḥ daśa uttarāḥ gṛha madhye taṇḍula upari ekāśīti padam bhavet pañca uttarān vakṣyamāṇān catvariṃśat surān likhet pūjyāḥ tatra antar sthāḥ rayodaśa teṣām sthānāni nāmāni vakṣyāmi kramaśas adhunā īśāna koṇataḥ bāhyaḥ dvātriṃśat tridaśāḥ amī kṛpīṭayoniḥ parjanyaḥ jayantaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ sūryaḥ śaśī mṛga ākāśau vāyuḥ pūṣā ca nairṛtiḥ gṛhākṣataḥ daṇḍadharaḥ gāndharvaḥ bhṛgurājakaḥ mṛgaḥ pitṛ gaṇa adhiśaḥ tatas dauvāri kāhvayaḥ sāmaḥ sūryaḥ aditi ditī dvātriṃśa tridaśāḥ amī atha īśāna ādi koṇa sthāḥ cātvāraḥ tad samīpa gāḥ āpaḥ sāvitragha saṃjñaḥ ca jayaḥ rudraḥ kramāt amī ekāntarā syuḥ prāc ādyāḥ paritas brahmaṇaḥ smṛtāḥ aryamā savitā rājayakṣmā ca tathā pṛthvīdhara āhvayaḥ āpavatsaḥ aṣṭamaḥ pañcacatvāriṃśat surāḥ amī yad dikkānām ca vargaḥ ayam evam koṇeṣu aśeṣatas aryamā ca vivasvān ca mitraḥ pṛthvī dharā āhvayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ dikṣu catvāraḥ tripadāḥ smṛtāḥ vāstu mantreṇa vāstu jñaḥ dūrvā dadhi akṣata ādibhiḥ āvāhana ādi sarva upacārān ca kramaśas tathā tāmbūlam ca tatas kartā prārthayet vāstupūruṣam mad gṛhe dhana dhānya ādi samṛddham kuru sarvadā iti prārthya yathāśaktyā dakṣiṇām arcakāya ca anena vidhinā samyak vāstu pūjām karoti yaḥ ārogyam putra lābham ca dhanam dhānyam labhet naraḥ a kṛtvā vāstu pūjām yaḥ praviśet nava mandiram rogān nānāvidhān kleśān aśnute sarva saṃkaṭam gṛham na praviśet evam vipadām ākaram hi tat atho yātrā nṛpa ādīnām abhīṣṭa phala siddhaye syāt tathā tām pravakṣyāmi samyak vijñāta janmanām ajñāta janmanām nṝṇām phala āptiḥ ghuṇa varṇa vat ṣaṣṭi aṣṭamī dvādaśīṣu rikta amā pūrṇimāsu ca yātrā śukla pratipadi nirddhanāya kṣayāya ca maitra āditi indu ārka antya aśvi
