hā gitiṣya vasu uḍuṣu a sapta pañca tri ādyeṣu yātrā abhīṣṭa phala pradāḥ sita arkayeḥ na pratīcīm na udīcīm jñārayoḥ ddine indra aja pāda catur āsya aryama ṛkṣāṇi pūrvatas śūlāni sarva dvārāṇi mitra arka ijyā aśva bhāni ca kramāt diś dvāra bhāni syuḥ sapta sapta agni dhiṣṇyataḥ parigham laṅghayet daṇḍam na agni śvasana ṛdiś gamam āgneyam pūrva diś dhiṣṇyaiḥ vidiśaḥ ca evam eva hi digrāśayaḥ tu kramaśas meṣa ādyāḥ ca punar punar digīśvare lalāṭa sthe yātuḥ na punarāgamaḥ lagna sthaḥ bhāskaraḥ prācyām diśi yātuḥ lalāṭa gaḥ dvādaśa ekādaśaḥ śukraḥ lalāṭa gaḥ daśama sthaḥ kujaḥ lagna ādyābhyām yātuḥ lalāṭa gaḥ navama aṣṭama gaḥ rāhuḥ naiṛtyām tu lalāṭa gaḥ lagnāt saptama gaḥ sauriḥ pratīcyām tu lalāṭa gaḥ ṣaṣṭaḥ pañcama gaḥ candraḥ vāyavyām ca lalāṭa gaḥ caturtha sthāna gaḥ saumyaḥ ca uttarasyām lalāṭa gaḥ dvi tri sthāna gataḥ jīvaḥ īśānyām vai lalāṭa gaḥ tad abhāve divārātrau yāyāt yātuḥ vadhaḥ anyathā mūḍhe śukre kārya hāniḥ pratiśukre parājayaḥ pratiśukra kṛtam doṣam hṝntum śaktāḥ grahāḥ na hi vāsiṣṭa kāśyapeya ātri bhāradvājāḥ sa gautamāḥ eteṣām pañca gotrāṇām pratiśukraḥ na vidyate nīcagaḥ ari gṛha sthaḥ vā vakra gaḥ vā parājitaḥ yātuḥ bhaṅga pradaḥ śukraḥ sva uñca sthaḥ ced jaya pradaḥ sva aṣṭa lagna iṣṭa rāśau vā śatru bhāt tu aṣṭame pi vā teṣām īśa stha rāśau vā yātuḥ mṛtyuḥ na saṃśayaḥ janma rāśi aṣṭama ṛkṣa uttha doṣāḥ bhāktaḥ vasu antya arddha ādi pañca ṛkṣe saṃgraham tṛṇa kāṣṭayoḥ tābhyām yātuḥ śatru kṣayaḥ bhavet vā lagne yātuḥ śatru kṣayaḥ tadā tayoḥ īśa sthite rāśau yātuḥ śatru kṣayaḥ bhavet vakraḥ panthāḥ mīna lagne yātuḥ mīna aṃśake api vā nindyaḥ nikhila yātrāsu ghaṭa lagnaḥ ghaṭa aṃśakaḥ jala lagnaḥ jala aṃśaḥ vā jalayoneḥ śubha āvahaḥ mūrtiḥ kośaḥ dhanvinaḥ ca vāhanam mantra saṃjñakam śatru mārgaḥ tathā āyuḥ ca manaḥ vyāpāra saṃjñikam prāptiḥ aprāptiḥ udayāt bhāvāḥ syuḥ dvādaśa eva te ghnanti krūrāḥ tri āpti vargam bhāvān sūrya mahīsutau na nighnataḥ hi vyāpāram saumyāḥ ḍha puṣṇanti arim vinā śukraḥ astam ca na puṣṇāti mūrtim mṛtyum ca candramāḥ yāmya diś gamanam tyaktvā sarva kāṣṭhāsu yāyinām abhijit kṣaṇa yogaḥ ayam abhīṣṭa phala siddhi daḥ yātrā yogāḥ vicitrāḥ tān yogān vakṣye yatas tatas phala siddhiḥ yāga lagnāt rājñām vipraśya dhiṣṇyataḥ muhūrta śaktitaḥ anyeṣām śakunaiḥ taskarasya ca kendra trikoṇe hi ekena yogaḥ śukra jña sūriṇām yoga adhiyoge kṣemam ca vijaya artha vibhūtayaḥ vyāpāra śatru mūrti sthaiḥ candra manda divākaraiḥ raṇe gatasya bhūpasya jaya lakṣmīḥ pramāṇikā śukra arka jña ārki bhaumeṣu lagna adhvasta triśatruṣu yātaḥ ariṣṭatanām keśavaḥ pūtanām iva trikoṇe kendra gāḥ saumyāḥ krūrāḥ tryāya ari gāḥ yadi yasya yāteḥ alakṣmīḥ tam upaiti iva abhisārikā trikhaḍāyeṣu mandārau balavantaḥ śubhāḥ yadi yātrāyām nṛpataḥ tasya hasta sthā śatru medinī gataḥ rājā ripūn hati pinākī tripuram yathā gataḥ rājā ripūn hṝnti kumāraḥ tārakam yathā gataḥ dahati arī vrājā kṛṣṇavartmā yathā vanam nṛpāḥ śuṣyanti arīn grīṣme hradinīm vārka raśmayaḥ śatrūn hanti gataḥ rājā hi andhakāram yathā raviḥ vināśayati arī trājā tṛla rāśim iva analaḥ nṝpaḥ ripūn sarvān pāpān pañcākṣaraḥ yathā hari smṛtiḥ yathā agha oghān hṝnti śatrūn gataḥ nṛpaḥ sagotra arīn nṛpān yathā gotrān ca gotrabhid śatrūn hṝnti gataḥ rājā bhujaṅgān garuḍaḥ yathā vināśayati arīn rājā pāpān bhāgīrathī yathā ye nṛpāḥ yānti arīn jetum teṣām yogaiḥ nṛpa āhvayaiḥ upaiti śāntim kopa agniḥ śatru yoṣā aśru bindubhiḥ bala kṣaya pakṣa daśamī māsi iṣe vijayā abhidhā vijayaḥ tatra yātṝṇām sadhiḥ vā na parājayaḥ nimitta śakuna ādibhyaḥ pradhānam hi manaḥ udayaḥ utsava upanaya udvāha pratiṣṭā śauca sūtake a samāpte na kurvīta yātrām martyaḥ jijīviṣuḥ ghṛta annam tila piṣṭa annam matsya annam ghṛta pāyasam prāc ādi kramaśas bhuktvā yāti rājā jayati arīn kṣīram tilodanam bhuktvā bhānuvāra ādiṣu kramāt kulmāṣān ca tila annam ca dadhi kṣaudram ghṛtam payaḥ mṛga māṃsam ca tad sāram pāyasam ca khagam mṛgam śaśa māṃsam ca ṣāṣṭikyam priya guṅkam apūpakam citra aṇḍa ja palam kūrma śvāvidh godhān ca śāsvakam haviṣyam kṛsara annam ca mudga annam yava piṣṭikam hutāśanam tilaiḥ hutvā pūjayeta digīśvaram praṇamya deva bhūdevān āśīrvādaiḥ nṛpaḥ vrajet indram airāvata ārūḍham śacyā saha virājitam vajra pāṇim svarṇa varṇam divya ābharaṇa bhūṣitam sapta hastam sapta jihvam ṣaṣ mukham meṣa vāhanam svāhā priye rakta varṇam srukū sruva āyudha dhāriṇam daṇḍāyudham lohitārkṣam yamam mahiṣavāhanam śyāmalam sahitam rakta varṇaiḥ ūrddhva mukham śubham khaḍga carma dharam nīlam nirṛtim nakha āhanam urddhva keśam virūpa akṣam dīrgha grīvā yutam vibhum nāgapāśa dharam pīta varṇam makaravāhanam varuṇam kālikā nātham ratna ābharaṇa bhūṣitam prāṇinām prāṇa rūpam tam dvi bāhum daṇḍa pāṇikam vāyum kṛṣṇa mṛga ārūḍham pūjayet añjanīpatim aśva ārūḍham kuṃbha pāṇim dvi bāhum svarṇa sannibham pinākinam vṛṣa ārūḍham gaurīpatim anuttam śveta varṇam candra maulim nāga yajña upavītinam aprayāṇe svayam kāryā prekṣayā bhūbhujaḥ tathā kāryam nigamanam chatram dhvaja śastra astra vāhanaiḥ sva sthānāt nirgama sthānam daḍānām ca śatam dvayam catvāriṃśat dvādaśa eva prasthitaḥ sa svayam gataḥ akāla jeṣu nṛpatiḥ vidyut garjita vṛṣṭiṣu sntā kuḍya śivā kāka kapotānām giraḥ tathā jhajhebhu khema vakṣīra svarāṇām vāmataḥ gatiḥ pītakāra bharadvāja pabhiṇām dakṣiṇā gatiḥ cāṣam tyaktvā catuṣpād tu śubha dāḥ āmataḥ matāḥ kṛṣṇam tyaktvā prayāṇe tu kṛkalāsena vīkṣitaḥ vārāha śaśa godhā astu sarpāṇām kīrtanam śubham hṛta īkṣaṇam na iṣṭam eva a vyapatyayam kapi ṛkṣayoḥ mayūra chāga nakula cāṣa pārāvatāḥ śubhāḥ dṛṣṭa mātreṇa yātrāyām vyastam sarvam praveśane yātrā siddhiḥ bhavet dṛṣṭe śaverāt anavajite praveśe rodana yutaḥ śavaḥ śava pradaḥ tathā patita klība jaṭila matta vānta auṣadha ādibhiḥ abhyakta vasā asthi carma aṅgāra dāruṇa rogibhiḥ guḍa kārpāsa lavaṇa ripu praśna tṛṇa uragaiḥ vandhyā kuñjaka kāṣāya mukta keśa bubhukṣitaiḥ prayāṇa samaye nagnaiḥ dṛṣṭaiḥ siddhiḥ na jāyate prajvala agnīn su turaga nṛpa asana pura aṅganāḥ gandha puṣa apa akṣata chatra cāmara āndolikam nṛpaḥ bhakṣya ikṣu phala mṛtsna anna madhu ājya dadhi go dayāḥ madya māṃsa sudhā dhauta vastra śaṅkha vṛṣa dhvajāḥ puṇya strī puṇya kalaśa ratna bhṛṅgāra go dvijāḥ bherī mṛdaṅga paṭaha ghaṇṭā vīṇā ādi niḥsvanāḥ veda maṅgala ghoṣāḥ syuḥ yāḥ yinām kārya siddhi dāḥ ādau viruddha śakunam dṛṣṭvā yāyi iṣṭadevatām smṛtvā dvitīye viprāṇām kṛtvā pūjām nivartayet sarva dikṣukṣutam na iṣṭam gokṣutam nidhana pradam para strī dvija deva svam tatra pṛśet diggaja aśvakān ādau saumyāyane kāryam nava vāstu praveśanam vidhāya pūrva divase vāstu pūjā bali kriyām māgha pha ālguna vaiśākha jyeṣṭa māseṣu śobhanam śaśi ijyā anteṣu varuṇa tvāṣṭra mitra sthira uḍuṣu śubhaḥ prevaśaḥ devejya śukrayoḥ ddṛśyamānayoḥ vyarka āravāre tithiṣu rikta amāvarjiteṣu ca divā vā yadi vā rātrau praveśaḥ maṅgala pradaḥ lagra antya aṣṭama ṣaṣṭa stha varjitena praveśa lgne syām ṛddhiḥ anya bhe śoka niḥsva tā ramyam kṛtvā arkam vāmatas vidvān bhṛṅgāram ca agratas viśet varṣā praveśe śaśini jala rāśi gate pi vā kendra ge vā śuklapakṣe ca ati vṛṣṭiḥ śubha īkṣite alpa vṛṣṭiḥ pāpa dṛṣṭe prāvṛṣ kāle acirāt bhavet prāvṛṣi induḥ sitāt sapta rāśi gaḥ śubha vīkṣitaḥ sadyas vṛṣṭi karaḥ śukraḥ yadā budha samīpa gaḥ tayoḥ ṃmadhya gate bhānau bhavet ṣṭi vināśanam maghā ādi pañca dhiṣṇya sthaḥ pūrve svāti traye pare pravarṣaṇam bhṛguḥ kuryāt viparīte na varṣaṇam puratas pṛṣṭatas bhānoḥ grahāḥ yadi samīpa gāḥ tadā vṛṣṭim prakurvanti na te ced pratiloma gāḥ vāma bhāga sthitaḥ śukraḥ vṛṣṭi kṛt ced tu yāmya gaḥ udayāḥ teṣu vṛṣṭiḥ syāt bhānoḥ ārdrā praveśane saṃdhyayoḥ sasya vṛddhiḥ syāt sarva saṃpad ṛṇāt niśi stoka vṛṣṭiḥ anarghaḥ syāt avṛṣṭiḥ sasya saṃpadaḥ pūrvāṣāḍhāḥ gataḥ bhānuḥ jīmūtaiḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ varṣati ārdra ādi mṛla antam pratyakṣam pratyaham tathā vṛṣṭiḥ ced pauṣṇabhem tasmāt daśa ṛkṣeṣu na varṣati siṃhe bhinne kujaḥ vṛṣṭiḥ abhinne karkaṭe tathā ahirbudhnyam pūrva śasyam para śasyā ca revatī bharaṇī sarva sasyā ca sarva nāśāya ca aśvinī tadā ativarṣaṇam bhūri prāvṛṣ kāle bala ujjhite ā saptama ṛkṣam śaśinaḥ pariveśa gata uttarā vidyut prapūrṇa maṇḍūkā svana avṛṣṭiḥ bhavet tadā yadā a pratyak natāḥ maghāḥ kha sapta upari saṃsthitāḥ patanti dakṣiṇa sthāḥ ye bhavet vṛṣṭiḥ tadā acirāt nakhaiḥ likhantaḥ mārjārāḥ ca avanim loha saṃyute rathyāyām setu bandhāḥ syuḥ bālānām vṛṣṭi hetavaḥ pipīlikā śreṇayaḥ chinnāḥ khadyotāḥ bahavaḥ tadā druma ādi rohaḥ sarpāṇām prītiḥ durvṛṣṭi sūcakāḥ udaya astamaye kāle vā śaśī madhu varṇaḥ ati vāyuḥ ced ati vṛṣṭiḥ bhavet tadā prāc mukhasya tu kūrmasya nava aṅgeṣu dharām imām vibhajya navadhā khaṇḍe maṇḍalāni pradakṣiṇam antarvedāḥ ca ṣāñcālaḥ tasya idam nābhi maṇḍalam prācyāḥ māgadha lāṭa utthāḥ deśāḥ tad mukha maṇḍalam strī kaliṅga kirāta ākhyāḥ deśāḥ tad bāhu maṇḍalam avantī draviḍāḥ bhillāḥ deśāḥ tad pārśva maṇḍalam gauḍa kaiṅkaṇa śālva āndhra pauḍraḥ tad pāda maṇḍalam siṃdhu kāśi mahārāṣṭra saurāṣṭrāḥ puccha maṇḍalam pulinda cīna yavana gurjarāḥ pāda maṇḍalam kuru kāśmīram ādreya matsyāḥ tad pārśva maṇḍalam khasāṃga vaṅga bāhlīkam kāṃbojāḥ pāṇi maṇḍalam kṛttikā ādīni dhiṣṇyāni trīṇi triṇi kramāt nyaset nābhi ādiṣu nava aṅgeṣu pāpaiḥ duṣṭam śubhaiḥ śubham adhomukhāḥ adhitiṣṭanti sthānāt sthānam vrajanti ca evamādyāḥ hi dṛśyante vikārāḥ pratimāsu ca mahā utkā patanam kāṣṭa tṛṇa rakta pravarṣaṇam gāndharvam deha diś dhūmam bhūmikaṃpam divā niśi niśi indracāpa maṇḍūkam śikhare śveta vāyasaḥ dṛśyante visphuliṅgāḥ ca go gaja aśva uṣṭra gātrataḥ prātar sūryāḥ catasṛṣu hi ardita ayugapad raveḥ jambūka grāma saṃvāsaḥ ketūnām ca pradarśanam kākānām ākulam rātrau kapotānām divā yadi akāle puṣpitāḥ vṛkṣāḥ dṛśyante phalitāḥ yadi kāryam tad chedanam tatra tatas śāntiḥ manīṣibhiḥ evamādyāḥ mahā utpātāḥ bahavaḥ sthāna nāśa dā madhyāt bhayam yaśaḥ mṛtyuḥ kṣayaḥ kīrtiḥ sukha asukham ityādiṣu ca sarveṣu utpāteṣu dvijasattama atas param pravakṣyāmi chandaḥ śāstram anuttamam iti śrī bṛhat na pūrva bṛhat upākhyāne dvitīya pāde ṣaṭpañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ mātrā varṇa vibhedena tat ca api dvividham punar kāraṇam chandasi proktāḥ chandaḥ śāstra viśāradaiḥ sarvagaḥ magaṇaḥ proktaḥ mukhalaḥ yagaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ taga ṇaḥ uṃ 'ta laghuḥ khyātaḥ madhya gaḥ jaḥ bha ādi gaḥ caturlāḥ tu gaṇāḥ pañca proktāḥ ārya ādi saṃmatāḥ saṃyogaḥ ca visargaḥ ca anusvāraḥ laghutaḥ paraḥ samam arddhasamam vṛttam viṣamam ca api nārada eka akṣarāt samārabhya varṇa ekaikasya vṛddhitaḥ ṣaḍviṃśati akṣaram yāvat pādaḥ tāvat pṛthak pṛthak tad param caṇḍa vṛṣṭi ādi daṇḍakāḥ parikalpitāḥ tribhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ padaiḥ gāthāḥ śṛṇu saṃjñāḥ yathottaram uktā atyuktā tathā madhyā pratiṣṭā anyā su pūrvikā gāyatrī uṣṇih anuṣṭaṣṭap ca bṛhatī paṅktiḥ eva ca triṣṭubh ca jagatī ca eva tathā atijagatī matā śakkarī sā atipūrvā ca aṣṭi atyaṣṭī tatas smṛte dhṛtiḥ ca vidhṛtiḥ ca eva kṛtiḥ prakṛtiḥ ākṛtiḥ vikṛtiḥ saṃkṛtiḥ ca eva tathā atikṛtiḥ utkṛtiḥ iti etāḥ chandasām saṃjñāḥ prastārāt bheda bhāgikāḥ naṣṭa aṅka arddhe same laḥ syāt vipam saḥ eva sa ūrddha gaḥ uddiṣṭe dviguṇān ādyāt aṅgān saṃmolya la sthitān kṛtvā sekān vadait saṃkhyām iti prāhuḥ purāvidaḥ vaṇān sekān vṛtta bhavān uttara adharataḥ sthitān uddiṣṭa aṅka samāhāraḥ sa ekaḥ vā janayet imām iti etat kiñcid ākhyātam lakṣaṇam chandasām prastāra ukta prabhedānām nāma anāṃstyam pragāhate iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne dvitīya pāde saṅkṣiptacchandovarṇanam nāma saptapañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca anūcāna prasaṃgena vedāṅgāni akhilāni ca śrutāni tvad mukha aṃbhojāt samāsa vyāsa yogataḥ śuka utpattim samācakṣva vistareṇa mahāmate meru śṛṅge kila purā karṇikāravanāyate śailarājasutā ca eva devī tatra abhavat purā tatra divyam tapaḥ tepe kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ yogena ātmānam āviśya yoga dharma parāyaṇaḥ vīryeṇa saṃmataḥ putraḥ mama bhūyāt iti sma ha saṃkalpena atha saḥ anena duṣprāpamaka gṛta ātmabhiḥ atiṣṭat māruta āhāraḥ śatam kila samāḥ prabhuḥ ārādhayat mahādevam bahu rūpam umāpatim lokapālāḥ ca sādhyāḥ ca vasubhiḥ ca aṣṭabhiḥ saha ādityāḥ ca eva rudrāḥ ca divākara niśākarau viśvā vasuḥ ca gandharvaḥ siddhāḥ ca apsarāsā aṃgaṇāḥ tatra rudraḥ mahādevaḥ karṇikāra mayīm śubhām dhārayānaḥ srajam bhāti śāradī iva niśākaraḥ āsthitaḥ paramam yogam vyāsaḥ putra artham udyataḥ trayāṇām api lokānām tat adbhutam iva abhavat jaṭāḥ ca tejasā tasya vaiśvānara śikhā upamāḥ maheśvaraḥ prasanna ātmā cakāra manasā matim tad bhāva bhāgī tad buddhiḥ tad ātmā tad upāśrayaḥ tejasā tasya lokān trīn yaśaḥ prāpsyati kevalam evam labdhvā varam devaḥ vyāsaḥ satyavatī sutaḥ araṇim tu atha saṃgṛhya mamantha agni cikīrṣayā atha rūpam param vipra bibhratīm svena tejasā ghṛtācīm nāma apsarasam dadarśa bhagavān nṛṣiḥ sa tām apsarasam dṛṣṭvā sahasā kāma mohitaḥ sā tu kṛtvā tadā vyāsam kāma saṃvigna mānasam śukībhūyā mahā ramyā ghṛtācī samupāgamat sa tām apsarasam dṛṣṭvā rūpeṇa anyena saṃvṛtām sa tu mahatā nigṛhṇan hṛcchayam muniḥ na śaśāka niyantum tam vyāsaḥ pravisṛtam manaḥ bhāvi tvāt ca eva bhāvyasya ghṛtācyā vapuṣā hṛtam yatnāt niyacchataḥ ca api mune etat cikīrṣayā śukre nirmathyamāne asyām śukaḥ jajñe mahā tapāḥ parama ṛṣiḥ mahā yogī araṇī garbha saṃbhavaḥ tathā rūpaḥ śukaḥ jajñe prajvalan iva tejasā tam gaṅgām saritām śreṣṭhām meru pṛṣṭhe svarūpiṇīm abhyetya snāpayāmāsa vāriṇā svena nārada kṛṣṇājinam ca antarikṣāt śuka arthe bhuvi avāpatat jagīyanta ca gandharvāḥ nanṛtuḥ ca apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ hāhā hūhūḥ ca gandharvaum tuṣṭuvuḥ śuka saṃbhavam tatra śakra purogāḥ ca lokapālāḥ samāgatāḥ divyāni sarva puṣpāṇi pravavarṣa ca mārutaḥ jaṅgamam sthāvaram ca eva prahṛṣṭam abhavat jagat tam mahātmā svayam prītyā devyā saha mahā dyutiḥ jāta mātram muneḥ putram vidhinā upānayat tadā dadau kamaṇḍalum prītyā devāḥ vāsāṃsi ca abhitas haṃsāḥ ca śatapatrāḥ ca sārasāḥ ca sahasraśas pradakṣiṇam avartanta śukāḥ cāṣāḥ ca nārada āraṇe yaḥ tadā divyam prāpya janma mahā muniḥ tatra eva uvāsa medhāvī vrata cārī samāhitaḥ utpanna mātram tam vedāḥ sa rahasyāḥ sa saṃgrahāḥ upatasthuḥ muni śreṣṭham yathā asya pitaram tathā bṛhaspatim sa vavre ca veda vedāṅga bhāṣya vid upādhyāyam dvijaśreṣṭha dharmam eva anucintayan itihāsam ca kārtsnyena veda śāstrāṇi ca abhitas gurave dakṣiṇām dattvā samāvṛttaḥ mahā muniḥ ugram tapaḥ samārebhe brahmacārī samāhitāḥ devatānām ṛṣīṇām ca bālye api su mahā tapāḥ saṃmatraṇīyaḥ janyaḥ ca jñānena tapasā tathā triṣu gārhasthya mūleṣu mokṣa dharma anudarśinaḥ prāha abhivādya ca tadā śreyaḥ rathī vinaya anvitaḥ yathā eva manasaḥ śāntiḥ paramā saṃbhavet mune śṛtvā putrasya vacanam parama ṛṣiḥ uvāca tam adhīṣva mokṣa śāstram vai dharmān ca vividhān api pituḥ nideśāt jagrāha śukaḥ brahma vidām varaḥ yoga śāstram ca nikhilam kāpilam ca eva nārada śatam brāhmyā śriyā yuktam brahma tulya parākramam mene putram yathā vyāsaḥ mokṣa śāstra viśāradam praṣṭum dharmasya niṣṭām vai mokṣasya ca parāyaṇam uktaḥ ca mānuṣeṇa tvam tathā gaccha iti avismitaḥ ārjavena eva gantavyam na sukhāya kṣaṇāt tvayā na draṣṭavyāḥ viśeṣāḥ hi viśeṣāḥ hi prasaṃginaḥ sa dharma kuśalaḥ rājā mokṣa śāstra viśāradaḥ yathā yathā ca te brūyāt tat kāryam aviśaṅkayā evam uktaḥ sa dharma ātmā jagāma mithilām muniḥ pabhdyām śaktaḥ untarikṣeṇa krāntum bhūmim sa sāgarām sa girīm śca api atikramya bhāratam varṣam āsadat sa deśān vividhān sphītān atikramya mahā muniḥ rājadvāram samāsādya dvārapālaiḥ nivāritaḥ //ṭa tasthau tatra mahā yogī kṣudh pipāsā ādi varjitaḥ teṣām tu dvārapālānām ekaḥ tatra vyavasthitaḥ madhyaṅgatam iva ādityam dṛṣṭvā śukam avasthitam jūjayitvā yathānyāyam abhivādya kṛtāñjaliḥ prāveśayat tatas kakṣaām dvitīyām rāja veśmanaḥ suvibhakta jala ākrīḍam ramyam puṣpita pādapam darśayitvā āsane sthāpya rājānam ca vyajijñapat śrutvā rājā śukam prāptam vāra strīḥ sa nyayuṅkta ca tam cāru keśyaḥ śuśreṇyaḥ taruṇyaḥ priya darśanāḥ sūkṣma rakta aṃbara dharāḥ tapta kāñcana bhūṣaṇāḥ saṃlāpa ālāpa kuśālāḥ bhāva jñāḥ sarva kovidāḥ param pañcāśataḥ tasya pādya ādīni vyakalpayan krīḍantyaḥ ca hasaṃtyaḥ ca gāyantyaḥ ca eva tāḥ śukam udāra satvam satva jñāḥ sarvāḥ paryacaran tadā āraṇeyaḥ tu śuddha ātmā jita krodhaḥ jita indriyaḥ pāda śaucam tu kṛtvā vai śukaḥ saṃdhyām upāsya ca niṣasāda āsane puṇye tam eva artham vyacintayat pūrvarātre tu tatra asau bhūtvā dhyāna parāyaṇaḥ madhyarātre yathānyāyyam nidrām āhārayat prabhuḥ tatas prātar samutthāya kṛtvā śaucam anantaram strībhiḥ parivṛttaḥ dhīmān dhyānam eva anvapadyata tām ca rātrim nṛpa kule vartayāmāsa nārada iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne dvitīya bhāge śukapralobhanam nāma aṣṭañcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ puras purohitam kṛtvā sarvāṇi antar purāṇi ca śirasā ca ardhyam ādāya guru putram samabhyagāt tatra upaviṣṭam tam kārṣṇi śāstra dṛṣṭena karmaṇā pādyam nivedya prathamam sa arghyam gām ca nyavedayat sa ca tām mantrataḥ pūjām pratigṛhya dvijottamaḥ paryapṛcchat mahā tejāḥ rājñaḥ kuśalam avyayam āvedya kuśalam bhūmau niṣasāda tad ājñayā saḥ api vaiyāsakim bhūyas pṛṣṭvā kuśalam avyayam śukaḥ uvāca tatra tvam gaccha tūrṇam vai sa te hṛdaya saṃśayam saḥ aham pituḥ niyogāt tvā mā upapraṣṭum iha āgataḥ tat me dharma bhṛtām śreṣṭha yathāvat vaktum arhasi kim kāryam brāhmaṇena iha mokṣa arthaḥ ca kimātmakaḥ katham ca mokṣaḥ kartavyaḥ jñānena tapasā api vā tapasā guru vṛttyā ca brahmacaryeṇa ca anvitaḥ devatānām pitṝṇām ca hi atṛṣṇaḥ ca anasūyakaḥ anasūyuḥ yathānyāyam āhitāgniḥ an ādṛte tān eva agnīn yathānyāyam pūjayan atithi priyaḥ śukaḥ uvāca utpanne jñāna vijñāne pratyakṣe hṛdi śaśvate na vinā guru saṃvāsāt jñānasya adhigamaḥ smṛtaḥ kim avaśyam tu vastavyam āśrameṣu na vā nṛpa na vinā jñāna vijñāne mokṣasya adhigamaḥ bhavet na vinā jñānasya adhigamaḥ tathā ācāryaḥ plāvitā tasya jñānam plavaḥ iha ucyate vijñāya kṛtakṛtyaḥ tu tīrṇaḥ tatra ubhayam tyajet an ucchedāya lokānām an ucchedāya karmaṇām kṛtvā śubha aśubham karma mokṣaḥ nāma iha labhyate bhāvitaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ cāryam bahu saṃsāra yoniṣu āsādayati śuddha ātmā mokṣam hi prathama āśrame tam āsādya tu muktasya dṛṣṭa arthasya vipaścitaḥ rājasān tāmasān ca eva nityam doṣān visarjayeta sāttvikam mārgam āsthāya paśyet ātmānam ātmanā sarva bhūteṣu ca ātmānam sarva bhūtāni ca ātmani atra gāthāḥ purā gītāḥ śṛṇu rājñā yayātinā dhāryate yā dvijaiḥ tāta mokṣa śāstra viśāradaiḥ svayam ca śakyam tat draṣṭum su samāhita ṛcatasā yadā bhāvam na kurute sarva bhūteṣu pāpakam pūrvaiḥ ācaritaḥ dharmaḥ catur āśrama saṃjñakaḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā brahma saṃpadyate tadā tapasā ātmānam īrṣyām utsṛjya mohinīm yadā śrāvye ca dṛśye ca sarva bhūteṣu ca avyayam śītam uṣṇam tathā eva artham anarntham priyam apriyam jīvitam maraṇam ca eva brahma saṃpadyate tadā prasārya iha yathā aṅgāni kūrmaḥ saṃharate punar tartha idriyāṇi manasā saṃyantavyāni bhikṣuṇā tamaḥ parigatam veśya yathā dīpena dṛśyate tathā buddhi pradīpena śakyaḥ ātmā nirīkṣitum brahmarṣe vidita śvā asi viṣaya antam upāgataḥ tasya ca eva prasādena prādurbhūtam mahā muneḥ jñānam divyam samādīptam tena asi viditaḥ viditaḥ mama bālyāt vā saṃśayāt vā api bhayāt vā api vimeṣa jāt utpanne ca api vijñā ne na adhigacchanti tāṅgatim vyavasāyena śuddhena madvidhaiḥ chinna saṃśayāḥ vimucya hṛdaya granthīn ārtim āsādayanti tām mavān ca utpanna vijñānaḥ sthirabaguddhiḥ a lolupaḥ na asti te sukha duḥkheṣu viśeṣaḥ na asti vastuṣu na autsukyam nṛtya gīteṣu na rāgaḥ upajāyate paśyāmi tvām mahābhāga tulya nindā ātma saṃstutim aham ca tvā anupaśyāmi ye ca anye api manīṣiṇaḥ āsthitam paramam mārge akṣayam ca api anāmayam yat phalam brāhmaṇasya iha mokṣa arthaḥ ca apada ātmakaḥ etat śutvā tu vacanam kata ātmā kṛta niścayaḥ ātmanā ātmānam āsthāya dṛṣṭvā ca ātmānam ātmanā kṛta kāryaḥ sukhī śāntaḥ tūṣṇīm prāyāt udak mukhaḥ śaiśiram girim āsādya pārāśaryam dadarśa ca śiṣyān adhyāpayantam ca paila ādīn veda saṃhitāḥ ārarṇeyaḥ viśuddha ātmā divākara sama prabhaḥ pituḥ jagrāha pādau caja sa ādaram hṛṣṭa mānasaḥ tatas nivedayāmāsa pituḥ sarvam udāra dhīḥ śukaḥ janaka rājena saṃvādam mokṣa sādhanam tat śatvā vedakartā asau prahṛṣṭena antarātmanā samāliṅgya sutam vyāsaḥ sva pārśva stham cakāra ca tatas paila ādayaḥ viprāḥ vedān vyāsāt adhītya ca śailaśṛṅgāt bhuvam prāptāḥ yājana adhyāpane ratāḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne ekonaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ avatīrṇeṣu vipreṣu yāsaḥ putra sahāyavān tūrṣṇīm dhyāna paraḥ dhīmān ekānte samupāviśat tam uvāca aśarī vāc vyāsam putra samanvitam ekaḥ dhyāna paraḥ tūṣṇī kim āḥse cintayan iva tasmāt adhīṣva bhagavan sārddha putreṇa dhīmatā tat śutvā vacanam vyāsaḥ nabhaḥ vāṇī samīritam vātaḥ atimātram pravavau samudra anila vījitaḥ ākhyātum arhati bhavān sarvam vāyoḥ vicaiṣṭitam śukasya etat vacaḥ śrutvā vyāsaḥ parama vismitaḥ divyam te cakṣuḥ utpannam svastham te niścalam manaḥ deva yāna caraḥ viṣṇoḥ pitṛ yānaḥ ca tāmasaḥ dvau etau pratyayam yātau divam ca adhas ca gacchataḥ pithivyām antarikṣe ca yatas saṃyānti vāyavaḥ sapta te vāyu mārgāḥ vai tān nibodha anupūrvaśas tatra deva gaṇāḥ sādhyāḥ samabhūvan mahā balāḥ teṣām api abhavat putraḥ samānaḥ nāma durjayaḥ apānaḥ ca tatas jajñe prāṇaḥ ca api tatas param pṛthā ṛkkṃmāṇi teṣām tu pravakṣyāmi yathā tathā prāṇinām sarvatas vāyuḥ ceṣṭāḥ vartayate pṛthak prīṇanāt ca eva sarveṣām prāṇaḥ iti abhidhīyate preṣayati abhra saṃghātān dhūma jān ca ūṣma jān tathā udayam jyotiṣām śaśvat soma ādīnām karoti yaḥ antar deheṣu ca udānam yam vadanti manīṣiṇaḥ yaḥ addhiḥ saṃyojya jīmūtān parjanyāya prayacchatī udvahaḥ nāma baṃhiṣṭhaḥ tṛtīyaḥ sa sadāgatiḥ saṃnīyamānāḥ bahudhā yena nīlāḥ mahā ghanāḥ varṣa mokṣa kṛta āraṃbhāḥ te bhavanti ghana aghanāḥ yaḥ asau vahati devānām vimānāni vihāyasā caturthaḥ saṃvahaḥ nāma vāyuḥ sa giri mardanaḥ yena vegavatā rugṇāḥ kriyante taru jāḥ rasāḥ pañcamaḥ sa mahā vegaḥ vivahaḥ nāma mārutaḥ puṇyam ca ākāśagaṅgāyāḥ toyam tiṣṭati tiṣṭati ṣaṣṭhaḥ parivahaḥ nāma sa vāyuḥ jīvatām varaḥ sarva prāṇabhṛtām a ta kāle nirasyati samyak anvīkṣatā buddhyā śāntayā adhyātma nityayā dhyāna abhyāsa abhirāmāṇām yaḥ amṛta tvāya kalpate yam samāsādya vegena diśām antam prapedire dakṣasya daśa putrāṇām sahasrāṇi prajāpateḥ yena vṛṣṭyā parābhūtaḥ toya anyena nivartate evam ete diteḥ putrāḥ marutaḥ parama adbhutāḥ an āramantaḥ sarva aṅgāḥ sarva cāriṇaḥ kaṃpitaḥ sahasā tena pavamānena vāyunā viṣṇoḥ niḥśvāsa vātaḥ ayam yadā vega samīritaḥ vāyoḥ vāyu bhayam hi uktam brahma tat pīḍitam bhavet etāvat uktvā vacanam parāśara sutaḥ prabhuḥ uktvā putram adhīṣva iti vyomagaṅgām agāt tadā tatas vyāse gate snātum śukaḥ brahma vidām varaḥ tatra svādhyāya saṃsaktam śukam vyāsa sutam mune utthāya satkṛtaḥ tena brahma putraḥ hi kārṣṇinā tatas provāca vipra indra śukam vidām varaḥ kim karoṣi mahābhāga vyāsa putra mahā dyute śukaḥ uvāca svādhyāye saṃpravṛttaḥ aham brahma putra adhunā sthitaḥ kiñcid tvām praṣṭum icchāmi tattvam mokṣa artha sādhanam tat vadasva mahābhāga yathā tat jñānam āpnuyām na asti vidyā samam cakṣuḥ na asti vidyā samam tapaḥ na asti rāga samam duḥkham na asti tyāga samam sukham nivṛttiḥ karmaṇaḥ pāpāt satatam puṇya śīla tā sat vṛttiḥ samudācāraḥ śreyaḥ etat anuttamam na alam sa duḥkha mokṣāya saṃgaḥ vai duḥkha lakṣaṇaḥ moha jāla āvṛtaḥ duḥkham iha amutra tathā aśnute kāryaḥ śreyaḥ arthinā tau hi śreyaḥ ghāta artham udyatau nityam krodhāt tapaḥ rakṣet śriyam rakṣet ca matsarāt vidyām māna avamānābhyām ātmānam tu pramādataḥ ānṛśaṃsyam paraḥ dharmaḥ kṣamā ca paramam balam ātma jñānam param jñānam satyam hi paramam hitam asajjamānaḥ śānta ātmā nirvikāraḥ samāhitaḥ adarśanam asaṃsparśaḥ tathā eva abhāṣāṇam sadā na hiṃsyāt sarva bhūtāni bhūtaiḥ maitrāyaṇaḥ caret ākiñcanyam su saṃtoṣaḥ nirāśiṣṭvam acāpalam etat āhuḥ param śreyaḥ ātma jñasya jita ātmanaḥ aśokam sthānam ātiṣṭe iha ca amutra ca abhayam nirāśiṣaḥ na śocanti tyajet āśiṣam ātmanaḥ parityajya āśiṣam saumya duḥkha grāmāt vimokṣyase ajitam jetu kāmena bhāvyam saṃgeṣu asaṃginā guṇa saṃgeṣu eṣu anāsaktaḥ eka caryāḥ rataḥ sadā dvandva ārāmeṣu bhūteṣu varākaḥ ramate muniḥ kiñcid prajñāna tṛptaḥ asau jñāna tṛptaḥ na śocati saṃsāram paśyate jantuḥ tat katham na avabudhse saṃveṣṭyamānam bahubhiḥ moha tantubhiḥ ātma jaiḥ kośakāra vat ātmānam veṣṭitaḥ na avabudhyase putra dāra kuṭuṃbeṣu saktāḥ sīdanti jantavaḥ saraḥ paṅka arṇave magnāḥ jīrṇāḥ vana gajāḥ iva moha jāla samākṛṣṭān paśya jantūn su duḥkhitān kuṭuṃbam putra dāram ca śarīram dravya saṃcayam pārakyam adhruvam sarvam kim svam sukṛta duṣkṛte aviśrāntam anālaṃbam apātheyam a daiśikam nahi tvām prasthitam kaścid pṛṣṭatas anugamiṣyati sukṛtam duṣkṛtam ca tvām gacchantam anuyāsyataḥ nibandhinī rajjuḥ eṣā yā grāme vasataḥ ratiḥ chitvā enām su kṛtaḥ yānti na enām chindanti duṣkṛtaḥ tulya jāti vayaḥ rūpān hṛtān pasyasi mṛtyunā rūpa kūlām manaḥ srotām sparśa dvīpām rasa āvahām gandha paṅkām śabda jalām svarga mārga durāruhām kṣamā aritrām satya mayīm dharma sthairya kara akarām tyāga vāta adhva gām śīghrām buddhi nāvam nadīm taret asthi sthūṇam snāyu yutam māṃsa śoṇita lepanam dharma avanaddham durgandhim pūrṇam mūtra purīṣayoḥ jarā śoka samāviṣṭam roga āyatanam asthiram rajasvalam anityam ca bhūtāvāsam samutsṛja mahābhūta ātmakam sarvam asmāt yat paramāṇumat iti eṣa saptadaśakaḥ rāśi khyakta saṃjñakaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ iti eṣa vyakta avyakta mayaḥ gaṇaḥ trivargaḥ atra sukham duḥkha jīvitam maraṇam tathā loke vihitam ātmānam lokam ca ātmani paśyati parāvara dṛśaḥ śaktiḥ jñāna velām na paśyati paśyataḥ sarva bhūtāni sarva avasthāsu sarvadā jñānena vividhāt kleśāt na nivṛttiḥ ca deha jāt akartāram amūḍham ca bhagavān āha tīrta vid ajasram eva moha antaḥ duḥkheṣu sukha saṃjñitaḥ tatas nivṛttaḥ bandhāt svāt karmaṇām udayāt iha saṃyamena ca saṃbandhāt nivṛttyā tapasaḥ balāt samprāptāḥ bahavaḥ siddhim a vyābādhām sukha udayām iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge dvitīya pāde bṛhat upākhyāne ṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ aśokam śoka nāśa artham śāstram śānti karam śivam harṣa sthāna sahasrāṇi śoka sthāna śatāni ca divase divase mūḍham āviśanti na paṇḍitam aniṣṭa saṃpraṃyogāḥ ca viprayogāt priyasya ca tān an ādriyamāṇaḥ ca sneha bandhāt vimucyate aniṣṭa buddhi tām yacchet tatas kṣipram virājate mṛtam vā yadi vā naṣṭam yaḥ atītam anuśocati duḥkha upaghāte śārīre mānase ca api upasthite prajñayā mānasam duḥkham hanyāt śārīram auṣadhaiḥ etat vijñāya sāmarthyam na vā anyaiḥ sama tām iyāt anityam jīvitam rūpam yauvanam dravya sañcayaḥ ārogyam priya saṃvāsam na mṛdhyet paṇḍitaḥ kvacid na ajñāna prabhavam duḥkham ekam śocitum arhati sukhāt priyataram duḥkham jīvite na atra saṃśayaḥ bhajanti hi śārīrāṇi rogāḥ śarīra mānasāḥ sāyakāḥ iva tīkṣṇa agrāḥ prayuktāḥ dṛḍha dhanvibhiḥ āmayasya vināśāya śarīram anukṛṣyate āyuḥ ādāya martyānām rātri ahāni punar punar apayanti ayam atyantam pakṣayoḥ śukla kṛṣṇayoḥ jātam martyam jarayati nimiṣam na avatiṣṭate sukha duḥkha abhibhūtānām ajaraḥ jarayati asūn a dṛṣṭa pūrvān ādāya bhāvān a pariśaṅkitān iṣṭa aniṣṭāḥ manuṣyāṇām matam gacchanti rātrayaḥ yaḥ yat icchet yathākāmam kāmānām tat tat āpnuyāt yadi syāt na para adhīnam puruṣasya kriyā phalam saṃyatāḥ ca eva takṣāḥ ca matimantaḥ ca mānavāḥ dṛśyante niṣphalāḥ saṃtaḥ prahīnāḥ ca sva karmabhiḥ apare niṣphalāḥ santaḥ nirguṇāḥ puruṣa adhamāḥ āśābhiḥ aṇya saṃyuktāḥ dṛśyante sarva kāminaḥ bhūtānām aparaḥ kaścid hiṃsāyām satata utthitaḥ vañcanāyām ca lokeṣu sa sukheṣu eva jīyate a ceṣṭamānam āsīnam śrīḥ kañcid upatiṣṭati aparādhān samācṣṭum puruṣasya svabhāvataḥ keṣāñcid putra kāmānām anusantānam icchatām siddhau prayatamānānām na eva aṇḍam upajāyate garbhāt udvijamānānām kruddhāt aśīviṣāt iva āyuṣmān jāyate putraḥ katham pretaḥ pitā iva saḥ devān iṣṭvā tapaḥ taptvā kṛpaṇaiḥ putra hetubhiḥ daśa māsān paridhṛtā jāyate kula pāṃsanāḥ apare dhana dhānyāni bhogān ca pitṛ saṃcitān śrutvā eva na adhigamanam nāśam eṣām na cintayet anyām anyām dhana avasthām prāpya vaiśeṣikāḥ narāḥ atṛptāḥ yānti vidhvaṃsam santoṣam yānti paṇḍitāḥ sarve kṣaya antāḥ nicayāḥ patana antāḥ samucchrayāḥ saṃyogāḥ viprayoga antāḥ maraṇa antam hi jīvitam antaḥ nā asti pipāsāyāḥ tuṣṭiḥ tu paramam sukham tasmāt saṃtoṣam eva iha dhanam śaṃsanti paṇḍitāḥ bhūteṣu bhāvam saṃcintya ye buddhyā tamasaḥ param na śocanti gata adhvānaḥ paśyanti paramām gatim saṃcinvan ekam eva enam kāmān ā vitṛptakam vyāghra paśum iva āsādya mṛtyuḥ ādāya gacchati atha api upāyam saṃpaśyet duḥkhasya asya vimokṣaṇe vāc saṃprayogāt bhṛtānām na asti duḥkham anāmayam praṇayam parisaṃhṛtya saṃstuteṣu itareṣu ca adhyātma gata mālīnaḥ nirapekṣaḥ nirāmiṣaḥ na enam prajñā su niyatam trāyate na api pauruṣam svabhāvāt yatnam ātiṣṭhet yatnavān na avasīdati tāni pūrva śarīrāṇi nityam ekam śarīriṇam prāṇinām prāṇa saṃrodhe māṃsa śleṣma viceṣṭitam vinaśyati vināśa ante nāvi nāvam iva acalām anna pānāni jīryante yatra bhakṣyāḥ ca bhakṣitāḥ garbhe mūtra purīṣāṇām svabhāva niyatā gatiḥ dhāraṇe vā visarge ca na kartum vidyate avaśaḥ āgamena mahān yeṣām vināśaḥ upapadyate garbhasya saha jātasya saptamīm īdṛśīm daśām prāpnuvanti tatas pañca na bhavanti śata āyuṣaḥ na abhyutthāne manuṣyāṇām yogāḥ syuḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ vyādhibhiḥ ca vivadhyante vyāghraiḥ kṣudra mṛgāḥ iva vyādhibhiḥ bhakṣyamāṇānām tyajatām vipulam dhanam vedanāḥ na apakarṣanti yatamānāḥ cikitsakāḥ te ca api vividhāḥ vaidyāḥ saṃmata auṣadhāḥ vyādhibhiḥ parikṛṣyante mṛgāḥ jyāghraiḥ iva arditāḥ te pibanti kaṣāyān ca sarpīṣi vividhāni ca dṛśyante jarayā bhagnāḥ nāgaiḥ nāgāḥ iva uttamāḥ kaiḥ vā bhuvi roga ārttāḥ mṛga pakṣiṇaḥ śvāpadāḥ ca daridrāḥ ca prāyas na ārtāḥ bhavanti te ghorān api durādharṣān nṛpatīn ugra tejasa ākramya rogaḥ ādatte paśūn paśu pacaḥ yathā srotasā mahasā kṣipram hriyamāṇam balīyasā svabhāvāḥ hi ativartante ye nirmuktāḥ śarīriṣu apramattāḥ śaṭhāḥ krūrāḥ vikrāntāḥ paryupāsate śokāḥ pratinivartante keṣāñcid asamīkṣatām mahat ca phala vaiṣamyam dṛśyate karma saṃdhiṣu śibikām anye yānti anye śibikā ruhaḥ sarveṣām ṛddhi kāmānām anye ratha puras sarāḥ manujāḥ ca gata śrīkāḥ śataśas vividhāḥ striyāḥ dvandva ārāmeṣu bhūteṣu gacchanti ekaikaśas narāḥ dharmam ca api tyaja ā dharmam tyaja satya anṛtām dhiyam sarvam tyaktvā sva rūpa sthaḥ sukhī bhava nirāmayaḥ iti uktvā vyāsa tanayam samāpṛcchya mahā muniḥ śukaḥ api yoginām śreṣṭhaḥ samyak jñātvā hi avasthitam tatas pitrā samāgamya praṇamya ca mahā muniḥ śukaḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya yayau kailāsa parvatam vyāsaḥ tad virahāt dūnaḥ putra sneha samāvṛtaḥ kṣaṇa ekam sthīyatām putraḥ iti ca krośa durmanāḥ nirapekṣaḥ śukaḥ bhūtvā niḥsnehaḥ mukta bandhanaḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne dvitīya pāde ekaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca etat śrṛtvā tu vacanam nāradaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ nāradaḥ uvāca bhagavan sarvam ākhyātam tvayā ati karuṇa ātmanā yat śrṛtvā mānasam me adya śāntim agryām upāgatam punar ca mokṣa śāstram me tvam ādiśa mahā mune nahi sampūrṇa tām eti tṛṣṇā kṛṣṇa guṇa arṇave ye tu saṃsāra nirmuktāḥ mokṣa śāstra parāyaṇāḥ tam chindhi su mahābhāga tvattaḥ nā anyaḥ vidām varaḥ sanaṃ u dhārayāmāsa ca ātmānam yathāśāstram mahā muniḥ pādāt prabhṛti gātreṣu krameṇa krama yoga vid pāṇi pādam samādhāya vinīta vat upāviśat sa dadarśa tadā ātmānam sarva saṃga viniḥsṛtaḥ prajahāsa tatas hāsam śukaḥ samprekṣya bhāskaram mahā yogi īśvaraḥ bhūtvā saḥ atyakrāmat vihāyasam antarīkṣa caraḥ śrīmān vyāsa putraḥ su niścitaḥ dadṛśuḥ sarva bhūtāni manaḥ māruta raṃhasam yathāśakti yathānyāyam pūjayāñcakrire tathā tam dṛṣṭvā vismitāḥ sarve gandharva apsarasām gaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca eva saṃsiddhāḥ kaḥ ayam siddhim upāgataḥ tatas asau sva āhrayam tebhyaḥ kathayāmāsa nārada uvāca ca mahā tejāḥ tān ṛṣīn saṃpraharṣitaḥ pitā yadi anugacchet mām krośamānaḥ śuka iti vai tamaḥ hi aṣṭavidham tyaktvā jahau pañcavidham rajaḥ saṃśliṣṭe śveta pīte ca rukma rūpya maye śubhe te śṛṅge atyanta saṃśliṣṭe sahasā eva dvidhā kṛte adṛśyetām dvijaśreṣṭha tat adbhutam iva abhavat tatas parvata śṛṅgābhyām sahasā eva viniḥsṛtaḥ tatas mandākinīm divyām upariṣṭāt abhivrajan śukaḥ dadarśa dharma ātmā puṣpita druma kānanam tasyām krīḍāsu niratāḥ snānti ca eva apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ nirākāram tu sa ākārāt adṛśuḥ tam vivāsasaḥ tam prakramantam ājñāya pitā sneha samanvitaḥ uttamām gatim āsthāya pṛṣṭataḥ anusasāra ha śukaḥ tu mārutāt ūrddhvam gatim kṛtvām tarikṣa gām darśayitvā prabhāvam svam sarva bhūtaḥ abhavat tadā atha yoga gatim vyāsaḥ samāsthāya mahā tapāḥ nimeṣa antara mātreṇa śuka abhipatanam yayau sa dadarśa dvidhā kṛtvā parvata agram gatam śukam śaśaṃsuḥ munayaḥ siddhāḥ gatim tasmai sutasya tām tatas śuka iti śabdena dīrgheṇa kranditam tadāḥ svayam pitrā svareṇa uñcais trīn lokān anunādya vai śukaḥ sarva gatiḥ bhūtvā sarva ātmā sarvatomukhaḥ pratyabhāṣata dharma ātmā bhoḥ śabdena anunādayan tatas eka akṣaram nādam bhoḥ iti evam udīrayan tatas prabhṛti vā adya api śabdān uñcāritān pṛthak giri gahvara pṛṣṭeṣu vyājahāra śukam prati antarhita prabhāvam tam darśayitvā śukaḥ tadā mahimānam tu tam dṛṣṭvā putrasya amita tejasaḥ paśyasi vipra na āyāntam brahma bhūtam nija antire śva āśramam sa śukaḥ brahma bhūtaḥ lokān cacāra ha tata kāla antare brahman vyāsaḥ satyavatī sutaḥ nara nārāyaṇau draṣṭum yayau badarikāśramam tatra dṛṣṭvā tu tau devau tapyamānaḥ mahat tapaḥ śvetadvīpam gataḥ tāta yatra tvam agamaḥ purā tatra dṛṣṭa prabhāvaḥ tu śrīmān nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ śruti vimṛgyaḥ hi devadevaḥ janārdanaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ asmi yogi indra sarva deva rahaḥ sthitaḥ sanatkumāra ādiṣṭena siddhaḥ yogena vāḍava iti uktaḥ vāsudevena tam natvā araṇi saṃbhavaḥ vaimānikaiḥ suraiḥ juṣṭam virajā pariceṣṭitam yam bhāntam anubhānti ete lokāḥ sarve api nārada yatra viduma sopānāḥ svarṇa ratna vicitritāḥ vāpyaḥ utpalam saṃchannāḥ sura strī krīḍana ākulāḥ divyaiḥ haṃsa kulaiḥ ghuṣṭāḥ su accha aṃbu nibhṛtāḥ sadā tatra dvāḥsthaiḥ catur hastena ārnā ābharaṇa bhūṣitaiḥ viṣvaksena anugaiḥ siddhaiḥ kumuda ādyaiḥ avāḥ ritaḥ śāntam prasanna vadanam pīta kauśeya vāsasam kaṭī sūtra brahmasūtra kaṭaka aṅgada bhūṣitam bhrājat kirīṭa valayam maṇi nūpura śobhitam tam dṛṣṭvā bhakti bhāvena tuṣṭāva madhusūdanam śukaḥ uvāca jagat bīja svarūpāya pūrṇāya nibhṛta ātmane haṃsāya matsya rūpāya vārāha tanu dhāriṇe nṛsiṃhāya dhruva ijyāya sāṃkhya yoga īśvarāya ca catuḥsanāya kūrmāya pṛthave svasuḥ rava ātmane nābheyāya jagaddhātre vidhātre iṃ'takāraya ca bhārgava indrāya rāmāya rāghavāya parasmai ca kṛṣṇāya vedakartre ca buddha kalki svarūpiṇe nara nārāyaṇa ākhyāya śiṣi viṣṭāya viṣṇave ṛta dhāmne vidhāmne ca suparṇāya sva rociṣe ṛbhave suvrata ākhyāya sudhāmne ca ajitāya ca viśvarūpāya viśvāya sṛṣṭi sthiti anta kāriṇe yajñāya yajñabhokte ca sthaviṣṭhāya aṇave arthine sākṣiṇe ajāya bahu śīrṣa aṅghri bāhave śrīśāya śrīnivāsāya bhakta vaśyāya śārṅgiṇe aṣṭa prakṛti adhīśāya brahmaṇe ananta saktaye bṛhat āraṇya vedyāya hṛṣīkeśāya vedhase puṇḍarīka nibha akṣāya kṣetrajñāya vibhāsine satyāya satya saṃdhāya vaikuṇṭhāya acyutāya ca adhokṣajāya dharmāya vāmanāya tri dhātave ghṛta arciṣe viṣṇave te anantāya kapilāyaya ca viriñcaye tri kakude ṛk yajuḥ sāma rūpiṇe ekaśṛṅgāya ca śuciśravase śāstra yonaye vṛṣākapaye ṛddhāya prabhave viśvakarmaṇe bhūḥ bhuvuḥ svar svarūpāya daitya ghne nirguṇāya ca nirañjanāya nityāya hi avyayāya akṣarāya ca namaḥ te pāhi mām īśa śaraṇa āgata vatsala āraṇeyam uvāca idam bhṛśam praṇata vatsalaḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca vidyām āpnuhi bhaktim ca jñānī tvam mama rūpadhṛk yat rūpam mama dṛṣṭam prāk śvetadvīpe tvayā dvija saḥ aham eva avatāra artham sthitaḥ viśvaṃbharā ātmakaḥ vara lokān yathā vāyuḥ yathā ravam savitā tathā tām labdhvā na aparam kiñcid labdhavyam avaśiṣyate ā kalpa antaḥ tapaḥ saṃsthau nara nārāyaṇau ṛṣī kartā bhāgavatam śāstram tat adhīṣva bhuvam vraja atha tam su antike dṛṣṭvā pārāśaryaḥ pratāpavān putram prāpya prahṛṣṭa ātmā tapasaḥ nivavarta ha nārāyaṇam namaskṛtya naram ca eva narottamam āraṇeya samāyuktaḥ sva āśramam samupāgamat nārāyaṇa niyogāt tu tvad mukhena muni īśvara cakāra saṃhitām divyām nānā ākhyāna samanvitām nivṛtti niratam putram śukam adhyāpayan ca tām ātma ārāmaḥ api bhagavān pārāśarya ātmajaḥ śukaḥ adhītavān saṃhitām vai nityam viṣṇu jana priyām evam ete samākhyātāḥ mokṣa dharmāḥ tava an adha paṭhatām śṛṇvatām ca api hari bhakti vivarddhanāḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge dvitīya pāde bṛhat upākhyāne mokṣadharṃmanirūpaṇam nāma dviṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ ca ayam dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ śaunakaḥ uvāca sūta sādho ciram jīva sarva śāstra viśāradaḥ yat tvayā pāyitāḥ vidvan vayam kṛṣṇa kathā amṛtam mānasāḥ brahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ sanaka ādyāḥ muni īśvarāḥ nāradaḥ api mahābhāga nityam kṛṣṇa parāyaṇaḥ teṣām samāgame bhadrā kā kathā loka pāvanī sūtaḥ uvāca sādhu pṛṣṭam mahābhāga tvayā loka upakāriṇā kathayiṣyāmi tat sarvam yat pṛṣṭa nārada ṛṣiṇā śrutvā sanandana proktān mokṣa dharmān sanātanān nāradaḥ bhārgava śreṣṭha punar papraccha tān munīn nāradaḥ uvāca samārādhyaḥ saḥ eva atra sarvaiḥ sarva artha kāṅkṣibhiḥ kaiḥ mantraiḥ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ samārādhyaḥ muni īśvarāḥ ke devāḥ pūjanīyāḥ ca viṣṇu pāda parāyaṇaiḥ dīkṣaṇam prātar ādyam ca kṛtyam syāt yat tat ucyatām prīyeta paramātmā vai tat brūta mama mānadāḥ sūtaḥ uvāca śṛṇu nārada vakṣyāmi tantram bhāgavatam tava yat jñātvā amalayā bhaktyā sādhayet viṣṇum avyayam tripada artham catuṣpādam mahātantram pracakṣate bhoga mokṣa kriyā caryā āhvayā pādāḥ prakīrtitāḥ pādārthāḥ tu paśupatiḥ paśu pāśāḥ trayaḥ eva hi patiḥ tatra śivaḥ hi ekaḥ jīvāḥ tu paśavaḥ smṛtāḥ yāvat moha ādi saṃyogāḥ sva rūpa ābodha lakṣaṇāḥ tāvat paśu tvam eteṣām dvaita vat paśya nārada pāśāḥ pañcavidhāḥ tu eṣām pratyekam teṣu lakṣaṇam paśavaḥ trividhāḥ ca api vijñātāḥ kala saṃjñikāḥ talapākala saṃjñaḥ ca sakalaḥ ca iti nāmataḥ mala māyā karma yutaḥ tṛtīyaḥ parikīrtitaḥ māyeyaḥ ca tirodhāna śakti jaḥ bindu jaḥ paraḥ pravāha nityam tat bīja aṅkura nyāyena saṃsthitam iti etau prathamau ca atha māyā iyā ādyān śṛṇu dvija sañcidānanda vibhavaḥ parama ātmā sanātanaḥ varvarti dṛkkriyā rūpam tat tejaḥ śāṃbhavam param tad śaktim ādyām ekāntām vid rūpa ākhyām vadanti hi tayā ca ujjṛṃbhitaḥ binduḥ dikkriyā ātmā śiva abhidhaḥ aśeṣa tattva jātasya kāraṇam vibhuḥ avyayam asmin nilīnāḥ nikhilāḥ icchāyāḥ śaktayaḥ svakam kṛtyam kurvanti tena idam sarva anugrāhakam mune cit jaḍa anugraha arthāya yasya viśvam sisṛkṣataḥ ādya unmeṣaḥ asya nāda ātmā śānti ādi bhuvana ātmakaḥ tatas jñāna kriyā śaktyoḥ tathā utkarṣa apakarṣayoḥ dṛkśaktiḥ yatra nyagbhūtā kriyāśaktiḥ viśiṣyate īśvara ākhyam tu tat tattvam proktam sarva artha kartṛkam yatra kriyā hi nyagbhūtā jñāna ākhya udrekam aśnute tat tattvam ca eva vidyā ākhyam jñāna rūpam prakāśakam nādaḥ binduḥ ca sakalaḥ sat ākhyam tattvam āśritau vidyeśāḥ punar aiśam tu mantrāḥ vidyā abhidham punar sākṣāt nimittam īśaḥ atra iti upādāna sa bindu rāj pañcānām kāla rāhitya akramaḥ na asti iti niścitam vyāpāra vasataḥ hi eṣām vihitā khalu kalpanā śaktam yām vṛtti bhedāt tu vihitāḥ khalu kalpanāḥ cit jaḍa anugraha arthāya kṛtvā rūpāṇi vai prabhuḥ anādi mala ruddhānām kurute anugraham citām muktim ca viśveṣām sva vyāpāre samarthetām vidhatte jaḍa vargasya sarva anugrāhakaḥ śivaḥ śiva sāmānya rūpaḥ hi mokṣaḥ tu cit anugrahaḥ karttā upādāna karaṇaiḥ vinā kārye na dṛśyate śaktayaḥ karaṇam ca atra māyā upādānam iṣyate nityā ekā ca śivā śaktyā hi anādinidhanā satī sādhāraṇī narāṇām vai bhuvanānām ca kāraṇam viśvī sūkṣmā parā māyā vikṛtaiḥ parattu sā karmāṇi āvekṣya vidyeśaḥ māyām vikṣobhya śaktibhiḥ vidhatte jīva bhoga artham vapūṃṣi karaṇāni ca sṛjati ādaḥ kāla tattvam nānā śakti mayī ca sā sūte hi anantaram māyā śaktim niyamana ātmikām sarvam niyamayati eṣā tena iyam niyatiḥ smṛtā anantaram ca sā māyā nityā viśva vimohinī ekatas tu nṛṇām yena kalayitvā malam tatas vyāpāram vidadhāti eṣā bhū paryantam svakīyakam pradarśanā atha vai puṃsaḥ viṣayāṇām ca sā punar prakāśa rūpam vidyā ākhyam tattvam sūte kalā eva hi vidyā tu āvaraṇam bhitvā jñānaśakteḥ sva karmaṇā viṣayān darśayati eṣā ātmanā aṃśa akāraṇam hi atas udbuddha śaktiḥ puruṣaḥ pracodya mahat ādikān bhogye bhogam ca bhoktāram tat param karaṇam tu sā sukha ādi rūpaḥ viṣaya ākārā buddhiḥ samāsatas yadi arka vat prakāśā dhīḥ karma tvāt ca tathā api hi karaṇa antara sāpekṣā śaktā grāhayitum ca tam saṃsiddhā kartṛ tā asya tu akartṛ tva abhyupagame bhoktṛ tva ākhyā vṛthā asya tu karaṇa ādi prayoktṛ ātvam vidyayā eva asya saṃmatam anantaram kalā rāgam sūte bhidi aṅga rūpakam ebhiḥ tattvaiḥ ca bhoktṛ tva daśāyām kalitaḥ yadā nityaḥ tadā ayam ātmā tu labhate puruṣa abhidhām guṇānām avibhāgaḥ atra hi ādhāre kṣmā ādi bhāga vat ādhāraḥ api ca yaḥ teṣām tat avyaktam ca gīyate trayaḥ eva guṇāḥ hi aṣām avyaktāt eva saṃbhavaḥ sattvam rajaḥ tamaḥ prakhyā vyāpāra niyama ātmikā guṇataḥ dhīḥ ca viṣaya adhyavasāya svarūpiṇī guṇataḥ trividhā sā api proktā karma anusārataḥ jātaḥ saṃraṃbha vṛttimān saṃbhodāt asya viṣayaḥ prāpnoti vyavahārya tām taijasaḥ rājasaḥ ca eva tāmasaḥ ca iti nāmataḥ rājasān ca kriyā hetoḥ tathā karmendriyāṇi tu tāmasān ca eva jāyante tanmātrāḥ bhūtayonayaḥ icchā rūpam ca saṃkalpa vyāpāram tatra vai manaḥ indriyāṇām ca sāmarthyam saṃkalpena ātma vṛttinā karoti antar sthitam bhūyas tatas antar karaṇam manaḥ manaḥ ahṝṅkāra buddhi ākhyam asti antar kāraṇam tridhā icchā saṃraṃbha bodha ākhyāḥ vṛttayaḥ kramatas asya tu jñāna indriyāṇi śrotram tvac cakṣuḥ jihvā ca nāsikā grāhyāḥ ca viṣayāḥ hi eṣām jñeyāḥ śabda ādayaḥ mune śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhāḥ śabda ādayaḥ matāḥ vāc pāṇi pāda pāyu upasthāḥ tu karmendriyāṇi api karaṇāni ca siddhinā na kṛtiḥ karaṇaiḥ vinā daśadhā karaṇaiḥ ceṣṭām kāryam āviśya kāryate ceṣṭante kāryam ālaṃbya vibhu tvāt karaṇāni tu tanmātrāṇi tu kha vāyuḥ tejaḥ ambhaḥ kṣmā iti pañca vai tebhyaḥ bhūtāni eka guṇāni ākhyātāni bhavanti hi iti pañcasu śabdaḥ ayam sparśaḥ bhūta catuṣṭaye rūpam triṣu rasaḥ ca eva dvayoḥ gandhaḥ kṣitau tathā kāryāṇi eṣām krameṇa eva avakāśaḥ vyūha kalpanam pākaḥ ca saṃgrahaḥ ca eva dhāraṇam ca iti kathyate ā śīta uṣṇau mahā vādyau śīta uṣṇau vāri tejasoḥ bhāsvat agnau jale śuklam kṣitau śukla ādi anekadhā rūpam triṣu rasaḥ uṃ abhaḥ su madhuraḥ ṣaḍidhaḥ kṣitau gandhaḥ kṣitau asurabhiḥ surabhiḥ ca prakīrtitaḥ tanmātram tad bhūta guṇam karaṇam poṣaṇam tathā bhūtasya tu viśeṣaḥ ayam viśeṣa rahitam tu tat imāni pañcabhūtāni saṃniviṣṭāni sarvatas pañcabhūta ātmakam sarvam jagat sthāvara jaṅgamam śarīra saṃniviṣṭa tvam eṣām tāvat nirūpyate dehe asthi māṃsa keśa tvac nakha dantāḥ ca pārthivāḥ hṛdi paṅktau dṛśoḥ pitte tejaḥ tad dharma darśanāt prāṇa ādi vṛtti bhedena vāyuḥ ca eva atra saṃsthitaḥ viyat sarvāsu nāḍīṣu garbha vṛti anuṣaṅgataḥ prayokti ādi mahī prāntam etat aṇḍa artha sādhanam tattvāni evam kalā ādyāni prati pum niyatāni hi māyā iyaḥ ca eva pāśaḥ ayam yena āvṛtam idam jagat aśuddha adhvā mataḥ hi eṣa dharaṇī ādi kalā avadhiḥ tatra bhū maṇḍala sthaḥ asau sthāvaraḥ jaṅgama ātmakaḥ sthāvarāḥ giri vṛkṣa ādyāḥ jaṅgamaḥ trividhaḥ punar sveda jāḥ ca aṇḍa jāḥ ca eva tathā eva ca jarāyu jāḥ cara acareṣu lakṣāṇām catura aśīti yonayaḥ bhramamāṇaḥ teṣu jīvaḥ kadācid mānuṣam vapuḥ tatra api bhārate khaṇḍe brāhmaṇa ādi kuleṣu ca janiḥ ca pum striyoḥ yogaḥ śukra śoṇita yogataḥ mala karma ādi pāśena kaścid ātmā niyantritaḥ atha tatra ahṛtaiḥ mātrā pāna annādyaiḥ ca poṣitaḥ duḥkha ādyaḥ pīḍitaḥ ca eva ācchanna dehaḥ jarāyuṇā smaran tiṣṭati duḥkha ātma āpīḍyamānaḥ muhur muhur kāla krameṇa bālaḥ asau mātaram pīḍayan api saṃpīḍitaḥ niḥsarati yoniyantrāt avāṅmukhaḥ kṣaṇam tiṣṭati niśceṣṭaḥ tatas roditum icchati evam krameṇa loke asmin dehinām deha saṃbhavaḥ mānuṣam durlabham prāpya sarva loka upakārakam yaḥ tārayati na ātmānam tasmāt pāpataraḥ atra kaḥ paśu ādīnām ca sarveṣām ca sarveṣām sādhāraṇam iti īritam caturṣu eva anuraktaḥ yaḥ sa mūrkhaḥ hi ātma dhātakaḥ manuṣyāṇām ayam dharmaḥ rava bandha chedana ātmakaḥ dīkṣā jñāna ākhyayā śaktyā hi apadhvaṃsita bandhanaḥ śuddha ātma tattva nāmā asau nirvāṇa padam aśnute sva śakti ātmikayā dṛṣṭyā śivam dhyāyati paśyati yajate śivam mantraiḥ ca rava pareṣām hitāya saḥ śiva arka śakti dīdhityā samarthīkṛta cit ṛśā śiva śakti ādibhiḥ sārddham paśyati ātma gata āvṛttiḥ antaḥkaraṇa vṛttiḥ yā bodha ākhyā sā maheśvaram na prakāśayitum śaktā pāśa tvāt nigaḍa ādi vat dīkṣā eva paramaḥ hetuḥ pāśa vicchedane punar atas śāstra ukta vidhinā matra dīkṣām samācaret dīkṣitaḥ tantra vidhinā sva varṇa ācāra tatparaḥ anuṣṭānam prakurvīta nitya namittika ātmakam nija varṇa āśrama ācārān manasā api na laṅghayet yaḥ yasmin āśrame tiṣṭan dīkṣām prāpnoti mānavaḥ ekam tu phala dam karma mantra anuṣṭhāna saṃbhavam mantra ārādhana sāmarthyāt tat bhuktvā mokṣam aśnute nityam naimittikam dīkṣām prāpya yaḥ na ācaret naraḥ kañcid kālam piśāca tvam prāpya ante mokṣam aśnute anuṣṭhānam ca tena asya dīkṣām prāpya anumīyate dīkṣayā guru mūrti sthaḥ sarva anugrāhakaḥ śivaḥ dṛṣṭa ādi artha tayā yasya guru bhaktiḥ tu kṛtrimā iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde triṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ dīkṣā vidhim pravakṣyāmi mantra sāmarthya dāyakam divyam bhāvam yatas dadyāt kṣiṇuyāt duritāni ca atas dīkṣā iti sā proktā sarva āgama viśāradaiḥ mananam sarva vedi tvam trāṇam saṃkhāri anugrahaḥ strī pum napuṃsaka ātmānaḥ te mantrāḥ tu tridhā matāḥ strī mantrāḥ tu dviṭha antāḥ syuḥ pum mantrāḥ huṃ phaṭ antakāḥ klībāḥ ca eva narmaḥ smuḥ mantrāṇām jātayaḥ smṛtāḥ put daivatāḥ tu syuḥ vidyāḥ strī daivatāḥ matāḥ ṣaṭ kramasu praśastāḥ te manavaḥ trividhāḥ punar tāra antya rephaḥ svāhā astu tatra āgneyāḥ samīritāḥ saumyāḥ tu bhṛgu pīyūṣa bīja ḍhyāḥ kathitāḥ mune agnīṣoma ātmakāḥ hi evam mantrāḥ jñeyāḥ manīṣibhiḥ bodham āyānti ca āgneyāḥ śvasane piṅgala āśrite sarve mantrāḥ prabudhyante vāyau nāḍi dvaya āśrite pratyekam mantram uñcārya nāvyānām tān samuñcaret krūre karmāṇi ca āgneyāḥ saumyāḥ saumya phala pradāḥ śānta jñāna iti raudreya śānti jāti samanvitaḥ śāntaḥ api raudra tām eti huṃ phaṭī pallava yojanāt chinnaḥ ruddhaḥ śakti hīnaḥ tatas ca eva parāṅmukhaḥ karma hīnaḥ netra hīnaḥ kīlitaḥ staṃbhitaḥ tathā dagdhaḥ srastaḥ ca bhītaḥ ca malinaḥ ca tiraskṛtaḥ hatavīryaḥ bhrāntasaṃjñaḥ pradhvastaḥ bālakaḥ tathā kumāraḥ atha yuvā prauḍhaḥ vṛddhaḥ nistriṃśakaḥ tathā nirbījaḥ sidvi hīnaḥ ca mandaḥ kūṭaḥ niraṃśakaḥ sattva hīnaḥ kekaraḥ ca bīja hīnaḥ ca dhṛmitaḥ āliṅgitaḥ mohitaḥ ca kṣudhā ārtaḥ ca ati dīptakaḥ aṅga hīnaḥ ati kruddhaḥ ca ati krūre vrīḍitaḥ tathā praśānta mānasaḥ sthāna bhraṣṭaḥ ca vikalaḥ tathā ati vṛddhaḥ ati niḥsnehaḥ pīḍitaḥ ca tathā punar doṣāḥ hi ete samākhyātāḥ vakṣyāmi eṣām ca lakṣaṇam saṃyuktam vā viyuktam vā tridhā vā svara saṃyutam caturddhā pañcadhā vā api sa mantraḥ chinna saṃjñakaḥ tāra varma trayā lakṣmīḥ evam hīnaḥ tu yaḥ manuḥ śakti hīnaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ cira kāla phava pradhaḥ kāmabījam mukhe māyā ahi ante ca eva aṅkuśam tathā asau parāṅmukhaḥ jñeyaḥ bhajatām cira siddhi daḥ ādi madhya avasāneṣu sakāraḥ dṛśyate yadi netra hīnaḥ tu vijñeyaḥ kleśena api na siddhi daḥ ādi madhya avasāneṣu haṃsaḥ prāsāda vāgbhavau haṃsa iṃduḥ vā sakāraḥ vā phakāraḥ varma vā punar mā a prāḥ namāmi ca padam nā asti yasmin sa kīlitaḥ sa sa arṇaḥ dṛśyate yaḥ tu sa mantraḥ dagdha saṃjñakaḥ asram dvābhyām tribhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ dṛśyate akṣareḥ hakāraḥ śaktiḥ athavā bhītaḥ mantraḥ saḥ eva hi hṛdayam śīrṣe vaṣaṭ vauṣaṭka madhyamaḥ tri akṣaraḥ haṃsa hīnaḥ yaḥ suṣuptaḥ kīrtitaḥ tu saḥ vidyā vā api athavā mantraḥ bhavet saptadaśa akṣaraḥ ṣaṣ kāra pañcaka ādiḥ yaḥ mada unmattaḥ tu sa smṛtaḥ virāma sthāna gam ca asram hatavīryaḥ saḥ ucyate jñātavyaḥ bhrāntaḥ iti eṣa yaḥ syāt aṣṭā daśa akṣaraḥ punar viśati varṇaḥ vā yaḥ mantraḥ smara saṃyutaḥ hṛllekhā kuṃśa bīja āḍhyaḥ pradhvastaḥ sa kathyate sapta arṇaḥ bālamantraḥ tu kumāraḥ vasu varṇavān ṣoḍaśa arṇaḥ yuvā prauḍhaḥ catvāriṃśati varṇakaḥ triṃśat varṇaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭi varṇaḥ ca api śata akṣaraḥ catur śata akṣaraḥ mantraḥ vṛddhaḥ iti abhidhīyate śikhā varma ca yasya ante netram asram ca dṛśyate śiva śaktyā arṇa hīnaḥ vā nirbījaḥ sa manuḥ smṛtaḥ ādi anta madhye phaṭkāraḥ ṣoḍhā yasmin pradṛśyate sa manuḥ siddhi hīnaḥ syāt mandaḥ paṅkti akṣaraḥ manuḥ kūṭaḥ eka akṣaraḥ mantraḥ saḥ eva uktaḥ niraṃśakaḥ dvi varṇaḥ sattva hīnaḥ syāt kekaraḥ catur akṣaraḥ ṣaṣ varṇaḥ bīja hīnaḥ vā sārddha sapta akṣaraḥ api vā sārddha dvādaśa varṇaḥ vā dhūmitaḥ rniditaḥ tu saḥ triṃśat varṇaḥ ca ekaviṃśat varṇaḥ cārliṅgitaḥ tu saḥ caturviśati varṇaḥ vā saptaviṃśati varṇavān ekādaśa akṣaraḥ vā api pañcaviṃśati varṇakaḥ trayorviṃśati varṇaḥ vā sa manuḥ dṛpta saṃjñakaḥ ṣaḍviṃśati akṣaraḥ vā api ṣaṭtriṃśat varṇa aṅkaḥ api vā ekona triṃśat arṇaḥ vā mantraḥ hīna aṅgakaḥ smṛtaḥ aṣṭāviṃśati varṇaḥ vā tathā ekatriṃśat arṇakaḥ catvāriṃśat samārabhya triṣaṣṭi antaḥ tu yaḥ manuḥ vrīḍitaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ sarva karmasu na kṣamaḥ pañcaṣaṣṭi akṣarāḥ mantrāḥ jñeyāḥ vai śānta mānasāḥ pañca ṣaṣa aṭi arṇam ārabhya nava nanda akṣara avadhi ye mantrāḥ te tu vijñeyāḥ sthāna bhraṣṭāḥ muni īśvara trayodaśa arṇāḥ ye mantrāḥ tithi arṇāḥ ca tathā punar vikasāḥ teṃ samākhyātāḥ sarva tantra viśāradaiḥ śatam sārddhaśatam vā api śata dvayam atha api vā ye mantrāḥ varṇa saṃkhyākāḥ niḥsnehāḥ te prakīrtitāḥ catuḥśatam samārabhya sahasra arṇa avadhi dvija ati vṛddhāḥ prayogeṣu śithilāḥ te samīritāḥ sahasra varṇa dadhikāḥ mantrāḥ te pīḍita āhvayāḥ tat vā ūrddhvam ca eva ye mantrāḥ stotra rūpāḥ tu te smṛtāḥ evaṃvidhāḥ samākhyātāḥ manavaḥ doṣa saṃyutāḥ doṣān etān a vijñāya mantrān etān japanti ye siddhiḥ na jāyate teṣām kalpa koṭi śataiḥ api chinna ādi doṣa duṣṭānām mantrāṇām sādhanam bruve savya pāṣṇi gude sthāpya dakṣiṇam ca dhvaja upari pāraṃparya krama prāptaḥ nitya anuṣṭāna tatparaḥ guru anujñā rataḥ śrīmān abhiṣeka samanvitaḥ suṃdaraḥ sumukhaḥ śāntaḥ kulīnaḥ sulabhaḥ vaśī nirapekṣaḥ muniḥ dāntaḥ hita vādī vicakṣaṇaḥ tattva niṣkāsane dakṣaḥ vinayī ca su veṣavān āśramī dhyāna nirataḥ saṃśaya chid su vuddhimān nitya anuṣṭāna saṃyuktaḥ tu ācāryaḥ parikīrtitaḥ śāntaḥ vinītaḥ śuddha ātmā sarva lakṣaṇa saṃyutaḥ śama ādi sādhana upetaḥ śraddhāvān susthira āśayaḥ śuddha dehaḥ anna pāna dyaiḥ dhārmikaḥ śuddha mānasaḥ dṛḍha vrata samācāraḥ kṛtajñaḥ pāpa bhīrukaḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde catuḥṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ parīkṣya śiṣyam tu guruḥ mantra śodhanam ācaret prāc pratyak dakṣiṇa udak ca pañca sūtrāṇi pātayet catuṣṭayam catuṣkānām syāt evam nṛpakoṣṭake tṛtīya ādye tṛtīyam syāt ca turtha ādye turīyakam tad tad āgneya koṣṭeṣu tat tat pañcamam akṣaram nāma ādi akṣaram ārabhya yāvat mantra ādi varṇakam prādakṣiṇyāt tat dvitīyam sādhya ākhyam parikīrtitam tṛtīyam puṃsi siddha ākhyam turīyam ari saṃjñakam tad dvitīye tu mantra arṇe siddhasādhyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ nāma arṇa anya catuṣkāt tu dvitīye mantra varṇake catuṣke ced tadā pūrvam yatra nāma akṣaram sthitam tṛtīye ced catuṣke tu yadi syāt mantra varṇakaḥ tadā pūrva ukta rītyā tu kramāt dveyam manīṣibhiḥ turīye ced catuṣke tu tadā evam gaṇayet sudhīḥ dviguṇāt sādhya siddhaḥ tu sādhya sādhyaḥ vilaṃbataḥ sādhyaḥ susiddhaḥ dviguṇāt sādhya ariḥ hanti bāndhavān tad su siddha prāpti mātrāt susiddhāriḥ kuṭuṃba hṛt evam saṃśodhya mantram tu śuddhe kāle sthale tathā dīkṣayet ca guruḥ śiṣyam tad vidhānam udīryate nityakṛtyam vidhāya atha praṇamya guru pādukām prārthayet sat gurum bhaktyā abhīṣaaṭa artham ādṛtaḥ saṃpūjya vastra alaṅkāra go hiraṇya dhara ādibhiḥ kṛtvā svasti vidhānam tu maṇḍala ādi ca tuṣṭimān guruḥ śiṣyeṇa sahitaḥ śuciḥ yāga gṛham viśet sāmānya argha udakena atha saṃprokṣya dvāram astrataḥ divyān utsārayet vighnān nabhasthān arcya vāriṇā pārṣṇighātaiḥ tribhiḥ bhauṃmān tatas karma samācaret astra prakṣālitam kuṃbham yathāśakti vinirmitam viloma mātṛkā mūlam uñcaran śuddha vāriṇā āpūrya kuṃbham tatra arcet somasya vidhivat kalāḥ dhūmra arciḥ ūṣmā jvalinī jvālinī visphuliṅginī suśrīḥ surūpā kapilā havya kavya vahā tathā vahneḥ daśa kalāḥ proktāḥ procyante atha raveḥ kalāḥ tapinī tāpinī dhūmrā marīcijvālinī ruciḥ suṣumṇā bhoga dā viśvā bodhinī dhāriṇī kṣamā atha indroḥ ca kalā jñeyā hi amṛtā mānadā punar pūṣā tuṣṭiḥ ca puṣṭiḥ ca ratiḥ ca dhṛti saṃjñikāḥ śaśinī candrikā kātiḥ jyotsnā śrīḥ prītiḥ aṅgadā pūrṇā apūrṇā amṛtā ca iti proktāḥ candramasaḥ kalāḥ vasra yugmena saṃveṣṭya tasmin sarva oṣadhīḥ kṣipet panasa āmra vaṭa aśvattha vakula iti ca tān viduḥ muktā māṇikya vaiḍūrya gomeda anvajra vidrumau padmarāgam marakatam nīlam ca iti yathākram evam ratnāni nikṣipya tatra āvāhya iṣṭadevatām saṃpūjya vidhivat mantrī tatas śiṣyam su alaṅkṛtam vedyām saṃveśya saṃprokṣya prokṣaṇī sthena vāriṇā bhūtaśuddhi ādikam katvā tad śarīre vidhānataḥ aṣṭottaraśatena atha mūlamantreṇa mantritaiḥ abhiṣiñcet priyam śiṣyam japan mūlamanum hṛdi śiṣṭa udakena vā ācamya paridhāya aṃbaram śiśuḥ gurum praṇamya vidhivat saṃviśet puratas śuciḥ atha śiṣyasya śirasi hastam da tvā guruḥ tatas japet aṣṭottaraśatam deya mantram vidhānataḥ tad karṇe pravadet vidyām aṣṭa vāram samāhitaḥ saṃprāpta vidyaḥ śiṣyaḥ api nipatet guru pādayoḥ kīrti śrī kānti putra āyuḥ bala ārogya sadā astu te dadyāt ca dakṣiṇām tasmai vitta śāṭhya vivarjitaḥ saṃprāpya evam guroḥ mantram tat ārabhya dhana ādibhiḥ su aṣṭadevam yajet madhye da tvā puṣpa añjalim tatas agni nairṛti vāgīśān krameṇa paripījayet yadā madhye yajet viṣṇum bāhya ādiṣu vināyakam ravim śivām śivam ca eva yadā madhye tu śaṅkaram ravim gaṇeśam aṃbām ca harim ca atha yadā śivām īśam vighna arka govindāt madhye ced gaṇanāyakam śivam śivām ravim viṣṇum ravau madhya gate punar gaṇeśam viṣṇum aṃbām ca śivam ca iti yathākramam brāhme muhūrtte hi utthāya kṛtvā acā vaśyakam budhaḥ a śaṅkitaḥ vā śayyāyām svakīya śirasi smaret sahasra dala śukla abja kārṇaka āstha du maṇḍale vāme śaktyā yutam dhyātvā mānasaiḥ upacārakaiḥ ārādhya pādukā mantram daśadhā prajapet sudhīḥ vā māyā śrīḥ bhaga indu āḍhyāḥ viyat haṃsa khaka agnayaḥ tatas bhṛgu ākāśa rava agni bhaga indu āḍhyāḥ tatas śrīḥ cāmuka ante tu nandanāthā āmukī punar devī aṃbā ante śrīpāndukām pūjayāmi hṛd antime ayam śrī pādukā mantraḥ sarva siddhi pradaḥ nṛṇām akhaṇḍa maṇḍala ākāram vyāptam yena carācaram tat padam darśitam yena tasmai śrī gurave namaḥ ajñāna timira andhasya jñāna añjana śalākayā cakṣuḥ unmīlitam yena tasmai śrī gurave namaḥ yasya vāc amṛtam viṣam saṃsāra saṃjñakam om namaḥ te nātha bhagavān śivāya guru rūpiṇe vidyā avatāra saṃsiddhyai svīkṛta aneka vigraha navāya tana rūpāya paramārtha eka rūpiṇe sta tantrāya dayā kṷpta vigrahāya śiva ātmane paratra trāya bhaktānām bhavyānām bhāva rūpiṇe vivekinām vivekāya vimarśāya vimarśinām prakāśānām prakāśāya jñāninām jñāna rūpiṇe purastāt pārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭe namaḥ tubhyam upari adhas tvad prasādāt aham deva kṛta akṛtyaḥ asmi sarvatas māyā mṛtyu mahā pāśāt vimuktaḥ asmi śivaḥ asmi vaḥ prātar prabhṛti sāya antam sāṃya ādi prātar antataḥ tatas ca guru pāda abja galita amṛta dhārayā kṣālitam nijam ātmānam liḥ malam bhāvayet sudhīḥ mūla ādi brahmarandhra antam mūlavidyām vibhāvayet mūlādhārāt adhas bhāge vartulam vāyu maṇḍalam trikoṇam maṇḍalam vahneḥ tatra stha vahni bījataḥ utpannena agninā mūla ādhāra avasthita vigrahām prasupta bhujaga ākārām svayaṃbhū liṅga veṣṭinīm visa tantu nibhām koṭi vidyut ābhām tanīyasīm kulakuṇḍalinīm dhyātvā kūrcena utthāpayet ca tām suṣumṇā vartma nātām ca ṣaṣ cakra krama bhedinīm tatrastha amṛta saṃmagnīkṛtya ātmānam vibhāvayet punar tām sva sthalam nītvā hṛdidevam vicintayan dṛṣṭvā ca mānasaiḥ dravyaiḥ prārthayet manunā amunā prātar samutthāya tava priya artham saṃsāra yātrām tu anuvartayiṣye ṣaṣ śatāni divā rātrau sahasrāṇi ekaviṃśatiḥ ajapā ākhyām tu gāyatrīm jīvaḥ japati sarvadā ṛṣiḥ haṃsaḥ tathā avyakta gātrī chandaḥ īritam devatā paramaḥ haṃsaḥ ca ādyante bīja śaktikam tatas ṣaḍaṅgam kurvīta sūryaḥ somaḥ nirañjanaḥ nirābhāsaḥ ca dharmaḥ ca jñānam ca iti tathā punar kramāt etān haṃsa pūrvān ātmanepada paścimān jāta yuktān sādhaka indra ṣaḍaṅgeṣu niyojayet hakāraḥ sūrya saṃkāśa tejāḥ saṃgacchate bahis sakāraḥ tādṛśaḥ ca eva praveśe dhyānam īritam evam dhyātvā arpayet dhīmān vahni arkeṣu vibhāgaśaḥ mūlādhāre vā ādi sāṃta bīja yukte catur dale bandhūka ābhe sva śaktyā tu ca pāśa aṅkuśa sudhā pātra modaka ullāsa pāṇaye ṣaṭśatam tu gaṇeśāya vāc adhīśāya ca arpayet svādhiṣṭāne vidruma ābhe vādi lānta arṇa saṃyute vāma aṅga śakti yuktāya vidyā adhipataye tathā brahmaṇe ṣaṣ sahasram tu haṃsa ārūḍhāya ca arpayet maṇipūre śaṅkha cakra gadā paṅka dhāriṇe sa śriye ṣaṣ sahasram ca viṣṇave vinivedayet anāhateḥ a ka patre ca ka ādi ṭha anta arṇa saṃyute śukle śūla abhaya vara sadhā kalaśa dhāriṇe vāma aṅge śakti yuktāya vidyā adhipataye sudhīḥ vṛṣa ārūḍhāya rudrāya ṣaṣ sahasram nivedayet viśudde ṣoḍaśadale svara āḍhye śukna traṇake mahājyoti prakāśāya indriya adhipataye tatas sahasram arpayet prāṇa śaktyā yukteḥ carāya ca sadāśivāya gurave parā śakti yutāya vai vilasat mātṛkā varṇe vara āmaya karāya ca ṣaṣ śata adhika saṃkhyā asyāḥ dajapāyāḥ vibhāgaśaḥ saṃkalpena mokṣa dātā viṣṇuḥ me prīyatām iti asyāḥ saṃkalpa mātreṇa mahā pāpaiḥ pramucyate brahmā eva aham na saṃsārī nitya muktaḥ na śoka bhāj sañcidānanda rūpaḥ aham ātmānam iti bhāvayet tatas samācaret deha kṛtyam deva arcanam tathā tad hidhānam pravakṣyāmi sat ācārasya lakṣaṇam iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde pañcaṣaṣṭimaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatas śvāsa anusāreṇa da tvā pādam mahī tale viṣṇu vatni namaḥ tubhyam pāda sparśam kṣamasva me rakṣaḥ koṇe tatas grāmāt gatvā mantram udīrayet gacchantu ṛṣayaḥ devāḥ piśācāḥ ye ca guhyakāḥ pitṛ bhūta gaṇāḥ sarve kariṣye mala mocanam iti tāla trayam da tvā śiraḥ prāvṛtya vāsasā dakṣiṇa abhimukham rātrau divā sthitvā hi udak mukhaḥ malam visṛjya saucam tu mṛdā adbhiḥ samupācaret ekā liṅge gude tisraḥ daśa vāma kare mṛdaḥ evam śaucam vidhāya atha gaṇḍūṣān dvādaśa eva tu kṛtvā vanaspatim ca atha prārthayet manunā amunā āyuḥ balam yaśaḥ varcaḥ prajāḥ paśu vasūni ca śriyam prajñām ca medhām ca tvam naḥ dehi vanaspate saṃprārthya evam dantakāṣṭam dvādaśa aṅgula saṃmitam gṛhītvā kāmamantreṇa kuryāt mantrī samāhitaḥ hṛd antaḥ kāmabīja āḍhyam dantān ca anena śodhayet devāgāram tatas gatvā nirmālyam apasārya ca paridhāya aṃbaram śuddham maṅgala ārārtikam caret asreṇa pātram saṃprokṣya mūlena jvālayet ca tam saṃpūjya pātram ādāya utthāya ghaṇṭām ca vādayet vādyaiḥ gītaiḥ manojñaiḥ ca devasya arārtikam bhavet iti nīrājanam kṛtvā prārthayitvā nija īśvaram snātum yāyāt nimraga ādau kīrtayan devatā guṇān gatvā tīrtham namaskṛtya snānīyam ca nidhāya vai mūla abhimantrita mṛdam ādāya kaṭi deśataḥ vilipya pāda paryantam kṣālayet tīrtha vāriṇā tatas ca pañcabhiḥ pādau prakṣālya antar jale punar praviśya nābhi mātre tu mṛdam vāma karasya ca kṛtvā aṅgulyā gāṅga mṛgam ādāya astreṇa tat punar tala sthām ca ṣaḍaṅgeṣu tad mantraiḥ pravilepayet vibhāvya iṣṭa mayam sarvam āntaram snānam ācaret anantā āditya saṃkāśam nija bhūṣā āyudhaiḥ yutam mantra mūrtim prabhum smṛtvā tad pāda udaka saṃbhavām dhārām ca brahmarandhreṇa praviśantīm nijām tanum tad kṣaṇāt virajāḥ mantrī jāyate sphaṭika upamaḥ tatas śrauta ukta vidhinā snātvā mantrī samāhitaḥ deśa kālau ca saṃkīrtya prāṇāyāma ṣaṣ aṅgakaiḥ kṛtvā arka maṇḍalāt tīrthāni āhvayet muṣṭi mudrayā brahmāṇḍa udara tīrthāni karaiḥ spṛṣṭāni te raveḥ go mudrayā amṛtīkṛtya kavacena avaguṇṭhya ca saṃrakṣya astreṇa tad paścāt cakra mudrām pradarśayet pūjāyantram ca tad madhye sva antāt āvāhya devatām snāpayitvā arcayet tām ca mānasaiḥ upacārakaiḥ siṃhāsana sthām tām natvā tat jalam praṇamet sudhīḥ ādhāraḥ sarva bhātānām viṣṇoḥ atula tejasaḥ tad rūpāḥ ca tatas jātāḥ āpaḥ tāḥ praṇamāmi aham sisṛkṣoḥ nikhilam viśvam muhur śukram prajāpateḥ mātaraḥ sarva bhūtānām āpaḥ devyaḥ punantu mām alakṣmīḥ mala rūpā yā sarva bhūteṣu saṃsthitā kṣālayanti ca tām sparśāt āpaḥ devyaḥ punantu mām yat me keśeṣu daurbhāgyam sīmante yat ca mūrddhani lalāṭe karṇayoḥ akṣṇoḥ āpaḥ tat hantu vaḥ namaḥ āyuḥ ārogyam aiśvaryam ari pakṣa kṣayam śubham santoṣaḥ kṣāntiḥ āstikyam vidyā bhavatu vaḥ namaḥ vipra pāda udakam pītvā śālagrāma śilā jalam pṛthivyām yāni tīrthāni dakṣa aṅghrau tāni bhūsure sva iṣṭadevam samudvāsya mantrī mārtaṇḍa maṇḍale tatas tīram samāgatya am vastram saṃkṣālya yatnataḥ vāsasī paridhāya atha kuryāt sandhyā ādikam sudhīḥ roga ādi aśaktaḥ manujaḥ kuryāt tatra agharma ṣaṇam athavā bhasmanā snātaḥ rajobhiḥ ca eva vā akṣamaḥ keśavena tathā nārāyaṇena mādhavena ca saṃprāśya toyam govinda viṣṇubhyām kṣālayet karau vāmana śrīdharābhyām ca mukham hastau spṛśet tatas hṛṣīkeśa padmanābhābhyām spṛśet caraṇau tatas dāmodareṇa mūrddhānam mukham saṃkarṣaṇena ca aniruddha puruṣottamābhyām netre spṛśet tatas adhokṣaja nṛsiṃhābhyām śravaṇe saṃspṛśet tathā nābhim spṛśet acyutena janārdanena vakṣasi hariṇā viṣṇu na aṃsau ca vaiṣṇava ācamanam tu idam praṇava ādyaiḥ ṅe nta svāhā antaiḥ keśava ādika nāmabhiḥ mukhe nasoḥ pradeśinyā anāmayāḥ netra karṇayoḥ kaniṣṭhayā nābhi deśam sarvatra aṅguṣṭi ojanam ātma vidyā śivaiḥ tattvaiḥ svāhā antaiḥ śaivam īritam ātma vidyā sivaiḥ eva śaivam svāhāvasānikaiḥ vāc lajjā śrī mukhaiḥ proktam śāktam svāhā avasānikaiḥ vāc lajjā śrī mukhaiḥ proktam dvija ācamanam artha dam tilakam ca tatas kuryāt bhāle suṣṭhu gadā ākṛti śārṅga bāṇam mastake ca vinyaset kramaśas sudhīḥ karṇa mūle pārśvayoḥ ca pṛṣṭe nābhau kakudi api evam tu vaiṣṇavaḥ kuryāt mṛdbhiḥ tīrtha udbhava ādibhiḥ kramāt tatpuruṣa aghora sadyojāta ādi nāmabhiḥ pañca kuryā tripuṇḍrāṇi bhāla aṃsa udara hṛtsu ca śaivam śāktaḥ trikoṇā bham nārī vat vā samācaret kṛtvā tu vaidikīm saṃdhyām tāntrikīm ca samācaret ācamya vidhivat mantrī tīrthāni āvāhya pūrvavat tatas ca prāṇān āyamya kṛtvā nyāsam ṣaṣ aṅgakam ādāya vāma hasta iṃ'bu dakṣeṇa ācchādya pāṇinā sva śiraḥ saptadhā prokṣya avaśiṣṭam tat punar jalam kṛtvā tad akṣaram mantrī nāsikā antikam ānayet jalam tejaḥ mayam tat ca ākṛṣya antar ca iḍayā punar prakṣālya antargatam tena kalmaṣam tat jalam punar kṛṣṇa varṇam piṅgalayā recayet sva agratas tathā ravi maṇḍala saṃsthāya devāya arghyam prakalpayet sva kalpa uktām ca gāyatrīm japet aṣṭa uttaram śatam aṣṭāṃviṃśati vāram vā guhya iti manunā arpayet udyat āditya saṃkāśām pustaka akṣa kara aṃbujām kṛṣṇa ajina aṃbarām brāhmīm dhyāyet tāra aṅkite ambare madhyāhne vara dām devīm pārvatīm saṃsmaret parām śukla aṃbarām vṛṣa ārūḍhām tri netrām ravi biṃba gām varam pāśam ca śūlam ca dadhānām nṛ karoṭikām sāyāhne ratna bhūṣā āḍhyām pīta kauśeya vāsasām śyāma raṅgām catur hastām śaṅkha cakra lasat karām gadā padma dharām devīm sūrya āsana kṛta āśrayām tatas devān ṛṣīn ca eva pitṝn ca api vidhāna vid guru paṅktim ca saṃtarpyam sa aṃgam sa āvaraṇam tathā sa āyudham vainateyam saṃtarpayāmi iti tarpayet nāradam parvatam jiṣṇum niśaṭha uddhava dārukān pūjā āgāram samāgatya prakṣālya aṅghrī upaspṛśet pūjā sthalam samāgatya dvāra pūjām samācaret gaṇeśam ca ūrddhva śākhāyām mahālakṣmīm ca dakṣiṇe sarasvatīm vāma bhāge dakṣe vighneśvaram punar kṣetrapālam tathā vāme dakṣe gaṅgām prapūjayet vāme ca yamunām dakṣe dhātāram vāmatas tathā vidhātāram śaṅkha padma nidhīn ca vāma dakṣayoḥ dvārapālān tatas abhyarcet tad tad kalpa uditān sudhīḥ nandaḥ sunandaḥ caṇḍaḥ ca pracaṇḍaḥ pracalaḥ balaḥ bhadraḥ subhadraḥ ca ityādyāḥ vaiṣṇavāḥ dvārapālakāḥ nandī bhṛṅgī riṭī skandaḥ gaṇeśa umā maheśvarāḥ vṛṣabhaḥ ca mahākālaḥ śaivāḥ vai dvārapālakāḥ brāhmayā ādyāḥ mātaraḥ aṣṭau tu śaktyaḥ dvār sthitāḥ svayam sa iṃduḥ sva nāma agha ṛṇa ādyāḥ ṅe namaḥ oṃ tāḥ ime smṛtāḥ tatas sthitvā āsane dhīmān ācamya prayataḥ śuciḥ divya āntarikṣa bhaumān ca vighnān utsārya yatnataḥ keśava ādyām mātṛkām tu nyaset vaiṣṇava sattamaḥ keśavaḥ kīrti saṃyuktaḥ kāntyā nārāyaṇaḥ tathā mādhavaḥ tuṣṭi sahitaḥ govindaḥ puṣṭi saṃyutaḥ viṣṇuḥ tu dhṛti saṃyuktaḥ śānti yuj madhusūdanaḥ śrīdharaḥ medhayā yuktaḥ hṛṣīkiśaḥ ca harṣayā padmanābha yutā śraddhā lajjā dāmodara anvitā vāsudevaḥ ca lakṣmī yuj saṃkarṣaṇa sarasvatī cakrī jaya āyutaḥ paścādgadī durgā samanvitaḥ śārṅgī tu prabhayā yuktaḥ khaḍgī yuktaḥ tu satyayā śaṅkhī caṇḍā samāyuktaḥ halī vāṇī samāyutaḥ musalī ca bilāsinyā śūlī vijayayā anvitaḥ pāśī virajayā kuśī viśva samanvitaḥ nindī smṛtyā samāyuktaḥ naraḥ vṛddhyā samanvitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ buddhyā yutaḥ satyaḥ bhuktyā muktyā atha sātvataḥ bhūdharaḥ kledinī yuktaḥ viśvamūrtiḥ ca klinnayā balī tu parayā yuktaḥ bala anuja parāyaṇe bāla sūkṣme vṛṣa ghnaḥ tu saṃdhyā yuj prajñayā vṛṣaḥ haṃsaḥ prabhā samāyuktaḥ varāhaḥ niśayā yutaḥ vimalaḥ dhārayā yuktaḥ nṛsiṃhaḥ vidyutā yutaḥ keśava ādi mātṛkāyāḥ muniḥ nārāyaṇaḥ mataḥ amṛtā ādyā ca gāyatrī chandaḥ viṣṇuḥ ca devatā cakra ādi āyudha saṃyuktam kuṃbha ādarśa dharam harim lakṣmī yutam vidyut ābham bahu bhūṣā yutam bhajet evam dhyātvā nyaset śaktim śrī kāma puṭita akṣaram vadet tat viṣṇu śaktibhyām hṛdayam praṇava ādikam tvac aṃsṛj māṃsa medaḥ asthi majjā śukrāṇi asūn vadet prāṇam krodham tathā mabhyām antāni ādi daśasu api ekam tu rasanā mūle grīvāyām ekam eva ca kavargam dakṣiṇe bāhau cavargam vāma bāhuke pṛṣṭhavaṃśe vam iti uktam nābhau bhaṃ hṛdaye tu mam ya ādi saptā api dhātu sthāḥ haṃ prāṇe laṃ tathā ātmani kṣaṃ krodhe kramatas nyasya viṣṇu pūjā kṣamaḥ bhavet pūrṇa udaryā tu śrīkaṇṭhaḥ hi anantaḥ vijarā anvitaḥ maheśvaraḥ vartula akṣyā adhīṃśaḥ vai dīrghaghoṇayā dirgha mukhyā bhārabhūtiḥ tithi īśaḥ gomukhī yutaḥ sthāvara īśaḥ dirgha jihvā yuj dharaḥ kuḍodarī yutaḥ urddhakeśyā tu jhiṇṭīśaḥ bhautikaḥ vikṛta āsyayā akrūraḥ āsyayā yuktaḥ mahā senaḥ vidyayā yutaḥ krodhīśaḥ ca mahākālyā caṇḍeśena sarasvatī pañca antakaḥ siddha gauryā yuktaḥ ca atha śira uttamaḥ lambodaryā catur vakraḥ hi aja īśaḥ drāviṇī yutaḥ sarveśaḥ nāgarī yuktaḥ someśaḥ khecarī yutaḥ maryādayā lāṅgalīśaḥ dārukeśena rūpiṇī vāruṇyā tu arddhanārīśaḥ umākāntaḥ guni īśvaraḥ kākodaryā tathā āṣāḍhī pūtanā saṃyuktaḥ mataḥ mīneśaḥ śaṅkhinī yuktaḥ meṣeśaḥ tarjayanī yutaḥ lohitaḥ kālarātryā ca śikhīśaḥ kujanīyutaḥ chalagaṇḍaḥ kapardinyā dvis aṇḍa īśaḥ ca vajrayā mahābalaḥ jayāyuktaḥ balīśaḥ sumukhā īśvarī bhujaṅgaḥ revatī yuktaḥ pinākī mādhavī yutaḥ khaḍgīśaḥ vāruṇī yuktaḥ bakeśaḥ vāyavī yutaḥ śveta uraskaḥ vidāriṇyā bhṛguḥ sahajayā yutaḥ lakulīśaḥ ca lakṣmī yuj śiva īśaḥ vyāpinī yutaḥ saṃvartake mahāmāyā proktā śrīkaṇṭha mātṛkā muniḥ syāt dakṣiṇāmūrtiḥ gāyatrī chandaḥ īritam devatā ca arddhanārīśaḥ viniyogaḥ akhila āptaye ha laḥ bījāni ca uktāni svarāḥ śaktayaḥ īritāḥ kuryāt bhṛgu stha ākāśena ṣaṣ dīrgha āḍhyena ca aṅgakam bandhūka svarṇa varṇāgam vara akṣa aṅkuśa pāśinam dhyātvā evam śiva śaktīḥ ca caturthī hṛdaya antim saubīja mātṛkā pūrve vinyaset mātṛkā sthale vighneśaḥ ca hriyā yuktaḥ vighnarājaḥ śriyā yutaḥ vināyakaḥ tathā puṣṭyā śānti yuktaḥ śiva uttamaḥ svāhayā gaṇanāthaḥ ca ekadantaḥ sumedhayā dīrghajihvaḥ pārvatī yuj jvālinyā śaṅkukarṇakaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ nandayā ca sureśyā gaṇanāyakaḥ gaja indaḥ kāmarūpiṇyā śūrpa karṇaḥ tathā umayā mahānandaḥ ca vighneśyā catur mūrti svarūpiṇī sadāśivaḥ kāma dayā hi āmodaḥ madajihvayā dvijihvaḥ mahiṣī yuktaḥ jabhinyā śūra nāmakaḥ vīraḥ vikarṇayā yuktaḥ ṣaṇmukhaḥ bhṛkuṭī yutaḥ vara daḥ lajjayā vāmadevaṃśaḥ dīrghaghoṇayā dhanurddharyāḥ vakratuḍaḥ dviṃraṇḍaḥ yāminī yutaḥ senā nīḥ rātri saṃyuktaḥ kāma andhaḥ grāmaṇī yutaḥ matta vāhaḥ cañcalayā jaṭī dīpti samanvitaḥ muṃhī subhagayā yuktaḥ khaḍgī durbhagayā yutaḥ vareṇyaḥ ca śivā yuktaḥ bhagayā vṛṣaketanaḥ bhakṣyapriyaḥ bhaginyā ca gaṇeśaḥ bhaginī yutaḥ meghanādaḥ subhagayā vyāpī syāt kālarātri yuj gaṇeśvaraḥ kāliṅkayā proktāḥ vighneśa mātṛkāḥ gaṇeśa mātṛkāyāḥ tu gaṇaḥ munibhiḥ īritaḥ trivṛt gāyatrikā chandaḥ devaḥ śakti gaṇa īśvaraḥ ṣaṣ dīrgha āḍhyena bījena kṛtvā aṅgāni tatas smaret pāṃśa aṅkuśa abhaya varān dadhānam kañja hastayā patnī āśliṣṭam rakta tanum tri netram gaṇape bhavet evam dhyātvā nyaset svīya bīja pūrva akṣara anvitam nivṛttiḥ ca pratiṣṭhā ca vidyā śāntiḥ tatas idhikāḥ dīpikā recikā ca api mocikā ca para abhidhā sūkṣma asūkṣma amṛtā jñāna amṛtā ca āpyāyinī tathā vyāpinī vyomarūpā ca anantā sṛṣṭiḥ samṛddhikā smṛtiḥ medhā tatas kāntiḥ lakṣmīḥ ddhṛtiḥ sthirā sthitiḥ siddhiḥ jarā pālinī ca kṣāntiḥ īśvarīkā ratiḥ kāmikaḥ varadā vā atha hlādinī prīti saṃyutā dīrghā tīkṣṇā tathā raudrā proktā nidrā ca tandrikā kṣudhā ca krodhinī paśca akriyā kārī sa mṛtyukā pītā śretā aruṇā paścāt asitā anantayā yutā uktā kalā mātṛkā evam tad tad bhaktaḥ samācaret kalā āyuḥ mātṛkāyāḥ tu muniḥ proktaḥ prajāpatiḥ gāyatrī chandaḥ ākhyātam devatā śārada abhidhā hrasva dīrgha antara sthaiḥ ca tāraiḥ kuryāt ṣaṣ aṅgakam padma cakra guṇa eṇān ca dadhatīm ca tri locanām pañcavakrām bhāratīm tām muktā bhūṣām bhajet sudhīḥ dhyātvā evam tāra pūrvām tām nyaset ṅanta kalā anvitām tatas ca mūlamantrasya ṣaḍaṅgāni samācaret namaḥ svāhā vaṣaṭ hum vauṣaṭ phaṭ jātayaḥ īritāḥ tatas dhyātvā iṣṭadevam tam bhūṣā āyudha samanvitam nyasya aṅga ṣaṭkam tad mūrtaum tatas pūjanam ārabhet iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge buhadupākhyāne tṛtīya pāde saṃdhyādinirūpaṇam nāma ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha vakṣye deva pūjām sādhaka abhīṣṭa siddhi dām tri koṇam catur asram vā vāma bhāge prakalpya ca sampūjya ā asreṇa saṃkṣālya hṛd ādhāram nidhāya ca tatra agni maṇḍalam ced vā pātram saṃkṣālya ca asrataḥ ādhāre nāmasam sthāpya tatra ced ravi maṇḍalam klimamātṛkā catreñju maṇḍalam prārcya tīrthāni āvāhya pūrvavat gomudrayā amṛtīkṛtya kavacena avaguṇṭhayet saṃkṣālya asreṇa praṇavam tad upari aṣṭadhā japet sāmānya argham idam proktam sarva siddhi karam nṛṇām tat jalam prokṣiṇyā sādhaka uttamaḥ ātmānam yāga vastūni tena saṃprokṣayet puthak ātma vāma agratas kuryāt ṣaṣ ṭkoṇa anta srikoṇakam caturasreṇa saṃveṣṭya saṃkṣālya argha udakena ca tatas tu sādhaka śreṣṭhaḥ staṃbhayet śaṅkha mudrayā āgneya ādiṣu koṇeṣu hṛd ādi aṅga catuṣṭayam netram madhye dikṣu ca asram trikoṇe pūjayet tatas mūla khaṇḍa trayeṇa atha ādhāra śaktim tu madhya gām evam saṃpūjya vidhivat asram saṃkṣālitam hṛdā pratiṣṭāpya tripadikām pūjayet manunā amunā mam vahni maṇḍalā yā iti tatas deśa kalā ātmane amuka ārdhyā iti pātra ante caturviṃśati varṇaḥ ayam ādhārasya arcane manuḥ sva mantra kṣālitam śaraṃvam saṃsya āpyāya samarcayet tāraḥ kārṃmamahān te tu tatas jalacarāya ca varma phaṭ hṛdayam pāñcajanyāya hṛdayam maneḥ tatra arka maṇḍalāya iti dvādaśānte kalā ramane sampūjya tena tatra arcet dvādaśa arka kalāḥ kramāt tatas śuddha jalaiḥ mūlam viloma mātṛkām paṭhan śaṅkham āpūrayet tasmin pūjayet manunā amunā om soma maṇḍalāya iti ṣoḍaśānte kalā ātmane amuka ardhya amṛtāya iti hṛd manuḥ ca ardhya pūjane tatra ṣoḍaśa saṃkhyākāḥ yajet candramasaḥ kalāḥ tatas tu tīrthāni āvāhya gaṅge ca ityādi pūrvavat go mudrayā amṛtīkṛtya ācchādayet matsma mudrayā kavacena avaguṇṭhya atha rakṣet astreṇa tat punar śaṅkha mauśa lacaka ākhyāḥ paramīkaraṇam tatas mahāmudrām yonimudrām darśayet kramatas sudhīḥ gāruḍī gālinī ca eva mukhye mudre prakīrtite aṣṭa kṛtvas japet mūlam praṇavam ca aṣṭadhā tathā śaṅkhāt dakṣiṇa digbhāge prokṣaṇī pātram ādiśet prokṣaṇyām tat jalam kiñcid kṛtvā ātmānam tridhā tatas ātma tattva ātmane hṛd ca vidyā tattva ātmane namaḥ prokṣet puṣpa akṣataiḥ ca api maṇḍalam vidhivat sudhīḥ athavā mūla gāyatryā pūjā dravyāṇi prokṣayet madhuparka artham api uta pātrāṇi ādhāra yuktāni sthāpayet vidhinā puras pādyam śyāmāka dūrvā abja viṣṇukrānta jalaiḥ smṛtam ardhyam puṣpa akṣata yavaiḥ kuśa agra tila sarṣapaiḥ gandha dūrvā dalaiḥ proktam tatas ca ācamanīyakam jātīphalam ca kaṅkolam lavaṅgam ca jala anvitam śaṅkara arka arcane śaṅkha mayena eva praśasyate śveta a kṛṣṇa aruṇa apīta a śyāma ārakta asita asitāḥ rakta aṃbara abhaya kara adhyeyāḥ spuḥ pīṭha śaktayaḥ svarṇa ādi likhite yantre śālagrāme maṇau tathā vidhinā sthāpitāyām vā pratimāyām prapūjayet aṅguṣṭa ādi vitasti anta mānā svarṇa ādi dhātubhiḥ vakrām dagdhām khaṇḍitām ca bhinna mūrddha dṛśam spaṣṭām vāpya ntyaja ādyaiḥ ca pratimām na eva pūjayet bāṇa ādi liṅge vā abhyarcet sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣite mūlena mūrtim saṃkalpya dhyātvā devam yathā uditam āvāhā pūjayet asyām parivāra gaṇaiḥ saha śālagrāme sthāpitāyām na āvāhana visarjane puṣpa añjalim samādāya dhyātvā mantram udīrayet ātma saṃstham ajam śuddham tvām aham parameśvara araṇyām iva havya āśam mūrtau āvāhayāmi aham tava iyam hi mahā mūrtiḥ tasyām tvām sarvagam prabho bhakti reva hasam ākṛṣṭam dīpa vat sthāpayāmi aham sarva antaryāmiṇe devam sarva bīja maya śubham param śuddham āsanam kalpayāvi aham sāṃnidhyam kuru tasyām tvam bhakta anugrāha kāraka dṛśā pūyūṣa varṣiṇyā pūrayan yajña viṣṭare mūrtaum vā yajña saṃpūrtyai sthitaḥ bhava maheśvara abhakta vāc manaḥ cakṣuḥ śrotra dūrāyita dyute sva tejaḥ pañjareṇa āśu veṣṭitaḥ bhava sarvatas yasya darśanām icchanti devāḥ sva abhīṣṭa siddhaye tasmai te parameśāya svāgatam svāgatam ca me kṛtārthaḥ anugṛhītaḥ asmi saphalam jīvitam mama āgataḥ devadeveśaḥ sukhāgatam idam punar tasmai me paraṇa abjāya pādyam śuddhāya kalpyate vedānām api vedāya devānām devatā ātmane ācāmam kalpayāmi īśa śuddhānām śuddhi hetave sarva kāluṣya hīnāya paripūrṇa sukha ātmane avacchiṣṭaḥ api aśuciḥ vā api yasya smaraṇa mātrataḥ sneham gṛhāṇa snehena lokanātha mahā āśaya sa aṃga upāṅgam idam snānam kalpayāmi aham īśa te sahasram vā śatam vā api yathāśakti ādareṇa ca gandha puṣpa ādikaiḥ īśa manunām ca abhiṣiñcet nirāvaraṇa vijñāna vāsaḥ te kalpayāmi aham yam āśritya ma hāmāyā jagat saṃmohinī sadā raktam śakti arka vighneṣu pītam viṣṇau sitam śive taila ādi dūṣitam jīrṇam sa chidram malinam tyajet svabhāva sundara aṅgāya nānā śakti āśrayāya te bhūṣaṇāni vicitrāṇi kalpayāmi amara arcita gṛhāṇa parama gandha kṛpayā parameśvara turīya vana saṃbhūtam nānā guṇa manoharam japa akṣata arka dhattūrān viṣṇau na eva arpayet kvacid ketakīm kuṭajam kundam bandhūkam kesaram japām śaktau dūrvā arka mandārān gaṇeśe tulasīm tyajet viṣṇukrāntā nāgavallī dūrvā apāmārga dāḍimau dhātrī muni yutānām ca patraiḥ deva arcanam caret kadalī badarī dhātrī tintiṇī bījapūrakam āmra dāḍima jaṃbīra jaṃbū panasa bhūruhāḥ eteṣām tu phalaiḥ kuryāt devatā pūjanam budhaḥ śuṣkaiḥ tu na arcayet devam patraiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalaiḥ api dhātrī khadira bitvānām tamālasya dalāni ca chinna bhinnāni api mune na dūṣyāṇi jaguḥ budhāḥ sarvadā tulasī śuddhā bilva patrāṇi vai tathā palāśa kāśa kusumaiḥ tamāla tulasī dalaiḥ chātrī dalaiḥ ca dūrvābhiḥ na arcayet jagat aṃbikām āghreyam devadeveśa dhūpam bhaktyā gṛhāma me su prakāśam mahā dīpam sarvadā timira apaham ghṛta vartī samāyuktam gṛhāṇa mama satkṛtam annam caturvidham svādu rasaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ samanvitam bhaktyā gṛhāṇa me deva naivedya antuṣṭi daṃsadā karpūra ādi sugandha āḍhyam yat dattam tat gṛhāṇa me dadyāt puṣpa añjalim paścāt kuryāt āvaraṇa arcanam yad āśā abhimukhaḥ bhūtvā pūjanam tu samācaret sā eva prācī tu vijñeyā tatas anyāḥ vidiśaḥ daśa keśareṣu agni koṇa ādi hṛdaya ādīni pūjayet śukla śveta sita śyāma kṛṣṇa rakta arciṣaḥ kramāt vara abhaya karāḥ dhyeyāḥ sva sva dikṣu am ga śaktayaḥ amuka āvaraṇa ante tu devatāḥ iti saṃvadet sa alaṅkārāḥ tatas paścāt sa aṃgāḥ sa paricārikāḥ sa vāhanāḥ sa āyudhāḥ ca tatas sarva upacārakaiḥ saṃpūjitāḥ tarpitāḥ ca vara dāḥ saṃtu idam paṭhet abhīṣṭa siddhim me dehi śaraṇa āgata vatsala iti uñcārya kṣipet puṣpa añjalim devasya mastake tatas tu abhyarcyanīyāḥ syuḥ kalpa uktāḥ ca āvṛtīḥ kramāt sa āyudhān tatas indra ādyān sva sva dikṣu prapūjayet īśānaḥ atha vidhiḥ ca evam adhastāt panna ga adhipaḥ airāvataḥ tathā meṣaḥ mahiṣaḥ pretaḥ timiḥ mṛgaḥ vājī vṛṣaḥ haṃsa kūrma om vāhanāni viduḥ budhāḥ vajram śaktim daṇḍa khaḍgau pāśām kuśa gadāḥ api triśūlam padma cakre ca kramāt indra ādi hetayaḥ samāpya āvaraṇa arcām tu devatā rārtikam caret śaṅkha toyam parikṣipya udvāhuḥ nṛtyan patet kṣitau daṇḍavat ca api athā utthāya prārthayitvā nije śvaram dakṣiṇe sthaṇḍilam kṛtvā tatra saṃskāram ācaret mūlena īkṣaṇam astreṇa prokṣaṇam tāḍanam punar pradāpya tatra juhuyāt dhyātvā ca eva iṣṭadevatām mahāvyāhṛtibhiḥ yaḥ tu samastābhiḥ catuṣṭayam juhuyāt sarpiṣā bhaktaiḥ tilaiḥ vā pāyasena vā sa ghṛtaiḥ sādhaka śreṣṭhaḥ pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyayā visṛjya agni devatāyai dadyāt ācamanīyakam avaśiṣṭena haviṣā gandha puṣpa akṣata anvitam yoginyaḥ hi ugra rūpāḥ ca gaṇānām adhipāḥ ca ye vighna bhūtāḥ tathā ca anye diś vidikṣu samāśritāḥ iti aṣṭa dikṣu da tvā ca punarbhūta balim caret pānīyam amṛtīkṛtya mudrayā dhenu saṃjñayā devatāyāḥ kare dadyāt punar ca ācamanīyakam maheśvarasya caṇḍeśaḥ viṣvaksenaḥ tathā hareḥ caṇḍāṃśuḥ taraṇeḥ vaktatuṇḍaḥ ca api gaṇeśituḥ śakteḥ ucchiṣṭa cāṇḍālī proktāḥ ucchiṣṭa bhojinaḥ ṛṣi ādikam smṛtvā kṛtvā mūla ṣaṣ aṅgakam guhya ati guhya goptā tvam gṛhāṇa asmad kṛtam japam tatas parāṅmukham ca argham kṛtvā puṣpaiḥ prapūjayet dorbhyām ca jānubhyām urasā śirasādṛśā manasā vacasā ca iti praṇāmaḥ aṣṭa aṅgaḥ īritaḥ bāhubhyām ca sa jānubhyām śirasā vacasā api vā pañca aṅgakaḥ praṇāmaḥ syāt pūjāyām pravarau ubhau natvā ca daṇḍa vat mantrī tatas kuryāt pradakṣiṇāḥ viṣmu soma arka vighnānām veda ardha indu adri vahnayaḥ itas pūrṇam prāṇa buddhi deha dharma adhikārataḥ vācā hastābhyām ca padbhyām udareṇa tatas param śiṣṇa ante yat smṛtam paścāt yat uktam yat kṛtam tatas mām madīyam ca sakalam viṣṇave ca samarpaye praṇava ādyaḥ aṣṭa vasu arṇaḥ hi anena ātmānam arpayet ajñānāt vā pramādāt vā vaikalyāt sādhanasya ca dravya hīnam kriyā hīnam mantra hīnam mayā anyathā kṛtam yat tat kṣamasva īśa kṛpayā tvam dayā nidhe tat sarvam tāvakī pūjā bhūyāt bhūtyai ca me prabho bhūmau skhalita pādānām bhūmiḥ eva avalaṃbanam tvayi jāta aparādhānām tvam eva śaraṇam prabho anyathā śaraṇam nā asti tvam eva śaraṇam mama tasmāt kāruṇya bhāvena kṣamasva parameśvara aparādha sahasrāṇi kriyante aharnniśam mayā dāsaḥ ayam iti mām matvā kṣamasva jagatām pate āvāhanam na jānāmi na jānāmi visarjanam pūjām ca eva na jānāmi tvam gatiḥ parameśvara saṃprārthya evam tatas mantrī mūla ante ślokam uñcaret yat na brahma ādayaḥ devāḥ jānanti ca sadāśivaḥ iti puṣpa añjalim da tvā tatas saṃhāra mudrayā nidhāya devam sa aṃgam ca svīya dṛt sarasīruhe suṣumṇā vartmanā puṣpam āghrāya udvāsayet budhaḥ śaṅkha cakra śilā liṅga vighna sūrya dvayam tathā akāla mṛtyu haraṇam sarva vyādhi vināśan sarva pāpa kṣaya karam viṣṇu pāda udakam śubham agrāhyam śiva nirmālyam patram puṣpam phalam jalam śālagrāma śilā sparśāt sarvam yāti pavitra tām pūjā pañcavidhā tatra kathitā nārada akhilaiḥ āturī sautikī trāsī sādhanā bhāvinī tathā daurbodhī ca kramāt āsām lakṣaṇāni me vilokya pūjām devasya mūrtim vā sūryya maṇḍalam roge nivṛtte snātvā atha natvā saṃpūñcet gurum dvijān api ca saṃpūjya yathāśaktyā pratoṣya ca tebhyaḥ ca āśiṣam ādāya devam prāgvat tatas racayet sūtakam dvividham proktam jāta ākhyam mṛta saṃjñakam tatra snātvā mānasīm tu kṛtvā saṃdhyām samāhitaḥ nivṛtte sūtake prāgvat saṃpūjya ca gurum dvijān tebhyaḥ ca āśiṣam ādāya tatas nityakramam caret eṣā tu sautikī proktā trāsī ca atha nigadyate duṣṭebhyaḥ trāsam āpannaḥ yathālabdha upacāraṅkaiḥ mānasaiḥ vai yajet devam trāsī sā parikīrtitā pūjā sādhana vastūnām sāmarthye tu sarvatas sādhana abhāvinī hi eṣā daurbodhīm śṛṇu nārada striyaḥ vṛddhāḥ stathā bālāḥ mūrkhāḥ taiḥ tu yathākramam yathā ajñāna kṛtā sā tu daurbodhī iti prakīrtitā evam yathā kathañcid tu pūjām kuryāt hi sādhakaḥ deve niveditam paścāt bhuñjīta sva gaṇaiḥ svayam ācamya ānana śuddhim ca kṛtvā tiṣṭet kiyat kṣaṇam purāṇam itihāsam ca śṛṇuyāt sva janaiḥ saha iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde devapūjānirūpaṇam nāma saptaṣaṣṭittamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī sanatkumāraḥ uvāca atha vakṣye gaṇeśasya mantrān sarva iṣṭa dāyakān smṛtiḥ māṃsa iṃdu manu āḍhyā sā punar candraśekharā vahniḥ priya antaḥ mantraḥ a yaṣṭāviṃśati varṇavān gaṇakaḥ asya muniḥ chandaḥ gāyatrī viyut ādikā gaṇeśaḥ devatā bījam ṣaṣṭa śaktiḥ tad ādikā śrīmat mahāgaṇapati prītaye viniyogakaḥ ṛṣim śirasi vakre tu chandaḥ ca hṛdi devatām guhye bījam padoḥ śaktim nyaset sādhaka sattamaḥ ṣaṣ dīrgha āḍhyena bījena yam ca bīja ādinā punar ṣaḍ aṅgāni nyaset asya jāti yuktāni mantra vid śaivī ṣaḍaṅga mudrāya nyastavyā hi ṣaḍaṅgake gām ādyam ca eva bhūrlokam nābhi antam pādayoḥ nyaset gīm ādyam ca bhuvarlokam kaṇṭha antam nābhitas nyaset svarlokam ca eva gūma ādyam kaṇṭha di mastaka avadhi vyāpakam mūlamantreṇa nyāsaḥ ayam bhuvana abhidhaḥ mūlamantram samuñcārya mātṛkā varṇam īrayet tad ante api ca mūlam syāt namaḥ om atam mātṛkā sthale kṣāntam vinyasya mūlena vyāpakam racayet sudhīḥ pañca tri bāṇa vahni indu candra akṣi nigamaiḥ kramāt vibhaktaiḥ mūlagāyatryā hṛd antaiḥ aṣṭabhiḥ padaiḥ bhāla deśe mukhe kaṇṭhe hṛdi nābhi ūru jānuṣu vakratuṇḍāya śabda ante dhīmahi iti samīrayet eṣā uktā mūlagāyatrī sarva siddhi pradāyinī evam nyāsa vidhim kṛtvā dhyāyet evam hṛd aṃbuje udyat mārtaṇḍa sadṛśam loka sthiti anta kāraṇam sa śaktikam bhūṣita aṅgam danta cakra ādi udāyudham evam dhyātvā catuścatvāriṃśat sāhasra saṃyutam catur lakṣam japet mantram aṣṭa dravyaiḥ daśa aṃśataḥ ikṣavaḥ saktavaḥ mocā phalāni cipiṭāḥ tilāḥ modakāḥ nārikelāni lājāḥ dravyāṣṭakam smṛtam pīṭham ādhāra śakti ādi para tatva antam arcayet ṣaṭkoṇa antar trikoṇam ca bahis aṣṭadalam likhet bhūpuram tad bahis kṛtvā gameśam tatra pūjayet tīvrā ākhyā jvālinī nandā bhogadā kāmarūpāṇī agrā tejovatī satyā navamī vidhna nāśinī sarva ādi śakti kamala āsanāya hṛdaya antikaḥ tatra āvāhya gaṇādhīśam madhye sampūjya yatnatas śriyam śriyaḥ patim ca eva gaurīm gaurī patim tathā ratim ratipatim pāścāt mahīpūrva ca potriṇam gaurī pāśa aṅkuśa dharā ṭaṅka śūla dharaḥ haraḥ ratiḥ padmakarā puṣpabāṇa cāpa dharaḥ smaraḥ śūka vrīhi agra hastā bhūḥ potrī cakra gadā dharaḥ deva agre pūjayet lakṣmī sahitam tu vināyakam pūjayet ṣaṭsu koṇeṣu hi āmoda ādyān priyā yutān īśa koṇe yajet kīrti saṃyutam sumukham tathā vāruṇe madanāvatyā saṃyutam durmukham yajet drāviṇyā vighna kartāram vāyu koṇe samarcayet pāśa aṅkuśa abhaya karān taruṇa arka sama prabhān ṣaṣ koṇa ubhaya pārśve tu śaṅkha padma nibhau kramāt keśareṣu ṣaḍ aṅgāni patreṣu aṣṭau tu mātaraḥ indra ādyān api vajjra ādīn pūjayet
