haraṇī gṛhe catuścatvāriṃśat āḍhyam catuḥ śatam atandritaḥ tarpayet aṃbuṣu śuddhaiḥ gajāsyam dinaśas sudhīḥ padmaiḥ tu vaśayet bhūpān tad patnīḥ ca utpalaiḥ tathā kumudaiḥ mantriṇaḥ aśvattha samidbhiḥ vāḍavān śubhaiḥ vāsāṃsi labhate hutvā kusuṃbha kusumaiḥ śubhaiḥ atha sarva iṣṭa dam vakṣye catur āvṛtti tarpaṇam pūrva mantra akṣaraiḥ mantraiḥ svāhā antaiḥ ca catuḥ catuḥ mithuna ādīn tatas paścāt pūrvavat saṃpratarpayet devena sahitām śaktim śaktyā ca sahitam tu tam evañca ṣaḍviṃśatidhā mithunāni bhavanti hi sva nāma ādi arṇa bījāni tāni santarpayet kramāt bhavet saṃbhūya sa catuścatvāriṃśat catuḥ śatam evam saṃtapya tat paścāt pūrvavat sa upacārakaiḥ sarva abhīṣṭam ca saṃprārthya praṇamya udvāsayet sudhīḥ bhādra kṛṣṇa caturthī ādi pratimāsam atandritaḥ tāvat na upaviśet bhūmau jita vāc kriyā mānasaḥ pūrva ukta vidhinā samyak nānā puṣpa upahārakaiḥ ekaviṃśati saṃkhyākān modakān ca nivedayet tatas karpūra kāśmīra rakta puṣpaiḥ sa candanaiḥ ardhyam dadyāt tu mūla ante ṅeṃ te gaṇapatim tatas ardhyam dadyāt catur vāram pūjayitvā gurum tatas nivediteṣu viprāya dadyāt ardhān ca modakān evam kṛte api pūrva uktam phalam āpnoti niścitam gaṇiśa pratimām danti dantena kapinā api vā gaja bhagrena niṃbena sita arkeṃṇa athavā punar kṛtvā tasyām samāvāhya prāṇa sthāpana pūrvakam spṛṣṭrā ca eva nirahāraḥ tām śikhāyām samudvahan bījam varāhaḥ binddha āḍhyau manu indvānnau kalau tatas smṛtiḥ māṃsa iṃdu manu āgrā karṇa ucchiṣṭa gaṇe vadet bakaḥ sa dīrghapavanaḥ mahā yakṣāya yam baliḥ hastī iti ca piśācī iti likhet ca eva agriṃsuṃdarī nava arṇaḥ ayam samuddiṣṭaḥ bhajatām sarva siddhi daḥ padaiḥ mantreṇa pañcāṅgāni prakalpayet anyat sarvam samānam syāt pūrva mantreṇa nārada sa dīrghaḥ dārakaḥ vāyuḥ varma antaḥ ayam rasa arṇakaḥ bhārgavaḥ asya muniḥ chandaḥ anuṣṭubh devaḥ gaṇādhipaḥ vakratuṇḍa abhidhaḥ bījam vaṃ śaktiḥ kavacam punar kṛtvā ṣaṣ aṅga mantra arṇān bhrū madhye ca gale hṛdi udyat arka dyutim hastaiḥ pāśa aṅkuśa vara abhayān dadhatam gaja vaktram ca rakta bhūṣā aṃbaram bhajet dhyātvā evam prajapet tarka lakṣam dravyaiḥ daśa aṃśataḥ aṣṭabhiḥ juhuyāt pīṭhe mūrtim mūrtena saṃkalpya tasyām āvāhya pūjayet ṣaṣ koṇeṣu ṣaḍ aṅgāni patreṣu aṣṭau tu śaktayaḥ yajet vidyām vidhātrīm ca bhoga dām vipra ghātinīm nidhi pradīpām pāpa ghnīm puṇyām paścāt śaśi prabhām dala agreṣu vakratuṇḍe ekadaṃṣṭra mahodarau gajāsya laṃba udarakau vikaṭau vidhnarāj tathā dhūmra varṇaḥ tatas bāhye lokeśān heti saṃyutān evam āvaraṇaiḥ iṣṭvā pañcabhiḥ gaṇanāyakam sādhaṃyet akhilān kāmān vakratuṇḍa praṃsādataḥ labdhvā guru mukhāt mantram dīkṣā saṃskāra pūrvakam brahmacārī haviṣya āśī satya vāc ca jita indriyaḥ japet arka sahasram tu ṣaṣ māsam homa saṃyutam dāridṣam tu parābhūya jāyate dhanada upamaḥ aṣṭottaraśatam nityam hutvā prāgvat phalam labhet aṅgārakacaturthyām tu devam iṣṭvā vidhānataḥ evam saṃvatsaram kṛtvā mahatīm śriyam āpnuyāt atha anyat sādhanam vakṣye lokānām hita kāmyayā iṣṭvā gaṇeśam pṛthukaiḥ pāyasa apūpa modakaḥ vacām niṣka arddha bhāgam ca tad arddham vā manum japet viśodhya cūrṇam prasṛtau gavām mūtre vinikṣipet snātām ṛtu dine śuddhām śukla aṃbara dharām śubhām devasya puratas sthāpya pāyayet auṣadham sudhīḥ gocarma mātrām dharaṇīm upalipya prayatnataḥ kapila ājyena saṃpūrṇam śarāvam nūtanam śubham ṣaṣ aṣṭa akṣara mantrābhyām dīpam āropayet śubham dīpe devam samāvāhya gandha puṣpa ādibhiḥ yajet snātām kumārīm athavā kumāram pūjayet sudhīḥ pradīpe sthāpite paśyet dvija rūpam gaṇeśvaram pṛṣṭaḥ tatas saṃpadi vā naṣṭam ca eva api anāgatam sakalam pravadet evam kumārī vā kumārakaḥ ṣaṣ akṣaraḥ hṛd antaḥ ced bhavet aṣṭa akṣaraḥ manuḥ kintu atra yat na sādhyam syāt triṣu lokeṣu sādhakaiḥ aṣṭaviṃśa rasa arṇābhyām tat na paśyet api kvacid etat gaṇeśa mantrāṇām vidhānam te mayā uditam śaṭhebhyaḥ para śiṣyebhyaḥ vañcakebhyaḥ api mā vada iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde gaṇeśamantravidhānanirūpaṇam nāma aṣṭaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha vakṣye trayī mūrteḥ vidhānam tu abjinīpateḥ mantrāṇām yat samārādhya sarva iṣṭam sasargāḥ bāma karṇa uḍhyaḥ bhṛguḥ vaḍhyāsanaḥ marut devabhāgaḥ muniḥ chandaḥ gāyatrī devatā raviḥ māyā vījam ramā śaktiḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭe niyogakaḥ satyāya hṛdayam paścāt brahmaṇe śiraḥ īritam viṣṇave tu śikhā varma rudrāya parikīrtitam netram syāt agraye paścāt śarvāya asram udāhṛtam netraḥ jvālā manaḥ hum phaṭ svāhā antāḥ manavaḥ gaṇāḥ punar ṣaṣ arṇaiḥ hrī lakṣmyāḥ kṛtvā antar sthaiḥ ṣaṣ aṅgakam śiṣṭa arau jaṭhare pṛṣṭe tayoḥ ṅeṃta ākhyayā nyaset ādityam ca ravim paścāt bhānum bhāskaram eva ca sūryam ca mūrdhni vadane hṛdi guhye ca pādayoḥ sadya ādi pañca hrasva ādyān nyaset ṅeṃ hṛdaya ūm atimān hrīṃ ramā madhya gām aṣṭau varṇān tāra ādikān nyaset mūrddha āsya kaṇṭha hṛd kukṣi nābhi liṅga gudeṣu ca sa candra svara pūrvam tu ṅetam śītāṃśu maṇḍalam sparśān sa iṃdūn samuñcārya ṅeṃtam bhāskara maṇḍalam nyaset kaṇṭha ādinā abhyantam dhyāyan pradyotanam hṛdi ya ādīn sa candrān uñcārya ṅetam ca vahni maṇḍalam proktaḥ ayam maṇḍala nyāsaḥ mahā tejaḥ vidhāyakaḥ ādi ṭha anta arṇa pūrvam ṅeṃ namaḥ ntam soma maṇḍalam mūrddha ādi hṛdaya antam tu vinyaset sādhaka uttamaḥ ḍakāra ādi kṣakāra anta varṇa ādyam pahni maṇḍalam ṅeṃtam hṛd ādi pāda antam vinyaset su samāhitaḥ agrīṣoma ātmakaḥ nyāsaḥ kathitaḥ sarva siddhi daḥ nyaset sa iṃdūn mātṛkā arṇān jaya anta puruṣa ātmane namaḥ nte vyāpakam mantrī haṃsnayāsaḥ ayam īritaḥ aṣṭau aṣṭau svarān śeṣān pañca pañca mitān punar ādhāra liṅgayoḥ nābhau hṛdi kaṇṭhe mukha antare haṃsa ākhyam agnīṣoma ākhyam maṇḍala trayam eva ca evam nyāsa vidhim kṛtvā dhyāyet sūryam hṛda buje dāna abhaya abja yugalam dhārayantam karaiḥ ravim kuṇḍalām gada keyūra hāriṇam ca trayī tanum dhyātvā evam prajapet mantrī vasu lakṣam daśa aṃśataḥ prathamam pīṭhayajane dharma ādīnām sthale yajet prabhūtam vimalam śāram samārādhyam anantaram soma agni maṇḍalam pūjya ravi maṇḍalam arcayet dīptā sūkṣmā jayā bhadrā vibhūtiḥ vimalā tathā amoghā vidyutā sarvatomukhī pīṭha śaktayaḥ hrasva traya ukti jāḥ klība hī nā vahni indu saṃyutāḥ svarāḥ bījāni śaktīnām tad ādyāḥ tāḥ brahma viṣṇu śiva ātmā te sṛṣṭiḥ śeṣa anvitā api asau evam ca ante yoga pīṭha ātmane hṛdayam īrayet tāra ādyaḥ ayam pīṭha mantraḥ tu anena āsanam ādiśet nava arṇāya ca manave mūrtim saṃkalpayet sudhīḥ sākṣiṇam jagatām tasyām āvāhya vidhivat yajet tatas ṣaḍaṅgām ārādhya dvikṣu aṣṭa aṅgam prapūjayet saṃpūjya madhye vā ādityam ravim bhānum ca bhāskaram sūryam diśāsu sadya ādi pañca hrasva ādikān imān sva sva nāma ādi varṇa ādyāḥ śaktayoḥ acyāḥ vidikṣu ca uṣām prajñām prabhām saṃdhyām tatas brahma ādikān yajet dikṣu aryam ādikān iṣṭvā bhūmijam ca śanaiścaram rāhum ketum ca koṇeṣu pūrvavat paripūjayet indra ādyān api vajra ādyān pūjayet pūrvavat sudhīḥ prāṇān āyamya sat bhūmau nyāsān kṛtvā purā uditān vidhāya maṇḍalam bhānoḥ pīṭham pūrvavat arcayet viloma mātṛkā mūlam uñcaran pūrayet jalaiḥ kuṅkumam rojanām rājīm candanam raktacandanam karavīram japā śāli kuśa śyāmāka taṇḍulān tila veṇu yavān ca eva nikṣipet salile śubhe sa aṃgam sa āvaraṇam tatra āvāhya arkam pūrvavat yajet prāṇāyāma trayam kṛtvā kuryāt aṅgāni pūrvavat tena ācchādya ardhya pātram ca japet manum an anya dhīḥ aṣṭottaraśata āvṛttyā punar saṃpūjya bhāskaram hastābhyām pātram ādāya jānubhyām avanīm gataḥ āmūrdhni pātram uddhṛtya aṃbareṇa varaṇe raveḥ dṛṣṭim ca ādhāya manasā pūjayitvā ravim punar dattvā puṣpa añjalim bhūyas japet aṣṭa uttaram śatam tena tuṣṭaḥ dineśaḥ asmai dadyāt vittam yaśaḥ sukham putrān pautrān abhīṣṭam ca yat yat sarvam prayacchati gāyatrī ārādhana āsaktaḥ saṃdhyā vandana tatparaḥ vikartanāya nirmālyam evam saṃpūjya dāpayet mārtaṇḍabhairava ākhyam hi bījam trailokya mohanam pūrvavat sakalam ca anyat atra jñeyam manīṣibhiḥ bhṛguḥ jala indu manu āḍhyaḥ somāya hṛdaya antimaḥ ṣaṣ akṣaraḥ mantra rājaḥ muniḥ asya bhṛguḥ mataḥ ādyam bījam namaḥ śaktiḥ viniyogaḥ akhila āptaye ṣaṣ dīrgheṇa sva bījena ṣaṣ aṅgāni samācaret sphaṭika bham nīla alakala sat mukham vibhrāṇam iṣṭam kumudam dhyāyet muktā srajam vidhum ṛtu lakṣam japet mantram pāyasena sa sarpiṣā juhuyāt tad daśa aṃśena pīṭhe soma anta pūjite kesareṣu aṅga pūjā syāt patreṣu etāḥ ca śaktayaḥ rohiṇī kṛttikā ca eva revatī bharaṇī puraḥ rātriḥ ārdrā tatas jyetsnā kalā hāra sama prabhā su śukla mālya vasanā muktā hāra vibhūṣitāḥ sarvāḥ stana bhara ākrāntāḥ racita añjalayaḥ śubhāḥ samabhyarcyāḥ saroja akṣyaḥ pūrṇa indu sadṛśa ānanāḥ dala agreṣu samabhyarcyāḥ tu aṣṭau sūrya ādikāḥ grahāḥ śukra ketu yutāḥ hi ete pūjyāḥ patra graga agrahāḥ rakta aruṇa śveta nīla pīta dhūmra sita asitāḥ vāma ūru nyasta tad hastāḥ dakṣiṇena dhṛta abhayāḥ sokapālān tad astrāṇi tad vāhye pūjayet sudhīḥ eva saṃsādhitaḥ mantraḥ prayacchet iṣṭam ātmanaḥ paurṇamāsyām jita āhāraḥ dadyāt ardhyam vidhūdaye kuryāt prāc pratyak āyatam bhuvi paścime maṇḍale sthitvā pūjā dravyam ca madhyame aṣṭottaraśatam paścādvidyā mantreṇa mantra vid dadyāt niśākarāya ardhyam sarva abhīṣṭa artha siddhaye vaṣa antareṇa sa vaṣṭam prāpnoti bhuvi mānavaḥ candra mukhi dviṭha antaḥ ayam vidyā mantraḥ udāhṛtaḥ dhanam dhānyam sutān pautrān saubhāgyam labhate acirāt ṣa antaḥ sargī ca caṇḍīśau krama ardi du visargiṇai ṣaṣ arṇaḥ ayam mahā mantraḥ maṅgalasya akhila iṣṭa daḥ virūpākṣaḥ muniḥ chandaḥ gāyatram devatā kujaḥ mantra arṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ aṅgāni krurvan dhyāyet harātmajam meṣa stham rakta vasra aṅgam śūla śakti gadā varān karaiḥ bibhrāṇam īśāna sveda jam bhūṃsutam smaret japet prāc aṅgāni samārādhya hi ekaviṃśati koṣṭakam maṅgalaḥ bhūmi putraḥ ca ṛṇa hartā dhana pradaḥ sthira āsanaḥ mahā kāyaḥ sarva karma avarodhakaḥ lohitaḥ lohita akṣaḥ ca sāmagānām kṛpā karaḥ maṅgala ādīn yajet mantrī sva sva sthāna sthitān kramāt suta kāmā kuraṅgākṣī bhaumavratam upācaret mārgaśīrṣe atha vaiśākhe vrata āraṃbhaḥ praśasyate aruṇa udaya velāyām utthāya āvaśyakam punar vinirvartya radā andhā veda pāmārgeṇa vāgyatā snātvā rakta aṃbara dharā rakta mālya vilepanā naivedya ādīn ca saṃbhārān raktān sarvān prakalpayet yogyam vipram samāhūya kujam arcet tad ājñayā ācamya deśa kālau ca smṛtvā kāmya samuccaran maṅgala ādīni nāmāni svakīya aṅgeṣu vinyaset mukhe pravinyaset sādhvī sāmagānām kṛpā karam dharā ātmajam nasoḥ akṣṇoḥ kujam bhaumam lalāṭake aṅgārakam śikhāyām ca sarvāṅge ca mahīsutam mūrddha ādi vṛṣṭi kartāram ā pāda antam nyaset sudhīḥ vinyaset ṛṣṭi hartāram mūrddha antam caraṇa āditaḥ nābhau hṛdi śirasi āram vakre bhūmijam eva ca mānasaiḥ upacāraiḥ ca saṃpūjya ardhyam nidhāpayet ekaviṃśati koṣṭha āḍhye tri koṇe tāmra patra ge āvāhya aṅgārakam tatra rakta puṣpa ādibhiḥ yajet aṅgāni pūrvam ārādhya maṅgala ādīn prapūjayet ekaviṃśati koṣṭheṣu cakramāram ca bhūmijam trikoṇeṣu ca sampūjya bahis aṣṭau ca mātṛkāḥ indra ādīn atha vajra ādīn bāhye saṃpūjayet punar rakta puṣpa akṣata phalāni ākṣipya ardhyam samarpayet suta arthinī prapannā tvām gṛhāṇa ardhyam namaḥ astu te mahīsuta mahābhāga gṛhāṇa ardhyam namaḥ astu te ekaviṃśati pūrva uktaiḥ ṅe namaḥ ntaiḥ ca nāmabhiḥ tārā ādyaiḥ praṇamet paścāt tāvatyaḥ ca pradakṣiṇāḥ kumāram śakti hastam ca maṅgalam praṇamāmi aham tatas rekhā trayam kuryāt khadira aṅgārakeṇa ca mārjayet vāma pādena mantrābhyām ca samāhitā duḥkha daurbhāgya nāśāya putra saṃtāna hetave ṛṇa duḥ kha vināśāya manaḥ bhīṣṭa artha siddhiye stuvīta dharaṇīputram puṣpa añjali karā tatas dhyāyantī tad pada aṃbhojam pūjā sāṃga tva siddhaye ṛṇa hartre namaḥ tubhyam duḥkha dāridraya nāśine tapta kāñcana saṃkāśa taruṇa arka sama prabha sukha saubhāgya dhana da ṛṇa dāridṣa nāśaka prasādam kuru deveśa sarva kalyāṇa bhājana deva dānava gandharva yakṣa rākṣasa pannagāḥ āpnuvanti śivam sarve sadā pūrṇa manorathāḥ ācirāt eva loke asmin yasya ārādhanataḥ janāḥ yaḥ vakra gatim āpannaḥ nṛṇām duḥkham prayacchati pūjitaḥ sukha saubhāgyam tasmai kṣmā sūnave namaḥ meṣavāhana rudra ātman dehi putrān dhanam yaśaḥ evam stutvā praṇamya atha visṛjya dharaṇī sutam yathāśaktyā pradāya svam gṛhṇīyāt braṇa āśiṣaḥ gurave dakṣiṇām dattvā bhuñjīyāt tad niveditam tilaiḥ hemam vidhāya atha śata arddham bhojayot dvijān bhauma mūrtim svarṇa mayīm ācāryāya samarpayet evam vrata parā nārī prāpnuyāt subhagān sutān ṛṇa nāśāya vitta artham vratam kuryāt pumān api aṅgārakasya gāyatrīm vakṣye yajana siddhaye aṅgārakāya śabda ante vidmahe padam īrayet śakti hastāya varṇa ante dhīmahi iti samuñcaret bhaumasya eṣā tu gāyatrī japtuḥ sarva iṣṭa siddhi dā pha antaḥ karṇa indu saṃyuktaḥ budhaḥ ṅeḥ te ha t antimaḥ rasāṇā om budha mantraḥ ayam muni brahmā asya kīrtitaḥ paṅktiḥ chaidaḥ devatā tu budhaḥ sarva iṣṭa daḥ nṛṇām ādyam bījam namaḥ śaktiḥ viniyogaḥ akhila āptaye vande budham sadā bhaktyā pīta ambara vibhūṣaṇam jānu stha vāma hasta āḍhyam sa abhaya itara pāṇikam daśa aṃśam juhuyāt ājyaiḥ pīṭhe pūrva uditeḥ acayet aṅgamātṛ diśāpāla hetibhiḥ budham arcayet tasya āśu graha jā pīḍā naśyati eva na saṃśayaḥ budhasya ārādhanam proktam guroḥ ārādhanam śṛṇu bṛṃhaspati padam ṅeṃtam sa iṃdu ādi arṇa agha maṇḍitam chandaḥ anuṣṭubh surā ācāryaḥ devatā bījam ādimam nyasta vāma karam rāśau ratnānām dakṣiṇāt karāt kirantam pīta puṣpa alaṅkāra ālepa aṃśuka arcitam lakṣam japaḥ daśa aṃśena ghṛtena annena vā hunet dharma ādi pīṭhe prayajet aṅga dikpāla hetibhiḥ evam siddhe manau mantrī sādhayet iṣṭam ātmanaḥ hutvā dina trayam mantrī niśā puṣpaiḥ ghṛta plutaiḥ sa viṃśati śatam śīghram vāsāṃsi labhate mahīm guroḥ ārādhanam proktam śṛṇu śukrasya sāṃpratam vasram me dehi śukrāya ṭha dvaya antaḥ dhruva ādikaḥ bhūnetra candranetra agninetra arṇaiḥ syāt ṣaṣ aṅgakam śukla aṃbara ālepa bhūṣam kareṇa dadatam dhanam vāmena śukram vyākhyāna mudrā doṣam smaret sudhīḥ ayutam prajapet mantram daśa aṃśam juhuyāt ghṛtaiḥ dharma ādi pīṭhe prayajet aṅga indra ādi tad āyudhaiḥ śveta puṣpaiḥ sugandhaiḥ ca juhuyāt bhṛgu vāsare ekaviṃśati vāram yaḥ maṇīn bhakti yuktāya śiṣyāya deyā vā nija sūnave iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde mantravidhānanirūpaṇam nāma ekonasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha vakṣye mahā viṣṇoḥ mantrān lokeṣu durlabhān yān prāpya mānavāḥ tūrṇam prāpnuvanti nija īpsitam yeṣām uñcāraṇena iva pāpa saṃghaḥ pralīyate brahma ādayaḥ api yān jñātvā samarthāḥ syuḥ jagat kṛtau tāra hṛd pūrvakam ṅeṃtam nārāyaṇa padam bhavet aṣṭa akṣaraḥ manuḥ ca asya sādhyaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ muniḥ chandaḥ proktam ca gāyatrī devatā viṣṇu khyayaḥ om bījam yam ca tathā śaktiḥ viniyogaḥ akhila āptaye kruddha ulkāya hṛd ākhyātam mahā ulkāya śiraḥ smṛtam vīrolkāya śikhā proktā dyulkāya kavacam matam mahā ulkāya iti ca asram syāt ittham pañcāṅga kalpanā punar ṣaṣ aṅga mantra utthaiḥ ṣaṣ varṇaiḥ ca samācaret avaśiṣṭau nyaset kukṣi pṛṣṭayoḥ mantra varṇakau nyāsam vakṣye vibhūtipañcaram mūla arṇān sva tanau nyasyet ādhāre hṛdaye mukhe dos pad mūleṣu nāsāyām prathamā āvṛttiḥ īritā gale nābhau hṛdi kuca pārśva pṛṣṭeṣu tad parāḥ mūrddha āsya netra śravaṇa ghrāṇeṣu ca tṛtīyakāḥ dos pāda saṃdhi aṅguliṣu veda āvṛttyā ca vinyaset śiraḥ netrā sya hṛd kukṣi sa ūru jaṅghā pada dvaye nyaset hṛd aṃsoḥ upadeṣu arṇān veda mitān manoḥ kha gadā aṃbhoja padeṣu sva sva mudrayā śeṣān ca nyāsa varyaḥ ayam vibhūtipañjara abhidhaḥ nyaset mūla arṇam ekaikam sa candram tāra sampuṭam tattva nyāsam tatas kuryāt dhiṣṇu bhāva prasiddhaye aṣṭa arṇaḥ aṣṭa prakṛti ātmā gaditaḥ pūrva sūribhiḥ pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni tatas ahṝṅkāram eva ca mahān ca prakṛtiḥ ca eva iti aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ matāḥ sarva aṅge vyāpakam kuryāt ekena sādhaka uttamaḥ mantra arṇa hṛd parāya ādyam ātmane hṛdaya antimam mūrtīn yaṃset dvādaśa vai dvādaśa āditya saṃyutāḥ dvādaśa akṣara varṇa ādyāḥ dvādaśa āditya saṃyutāḥ aṣṭa arṇaḥ ayam manuḥ ca aṣṭa prakṛti ātmā samīritaḥ tāsām ātma catuṣkasya yogāt arka akṣaraḥ bhavet lalāṭa kukṣi hṛd kaṇṭha dakṣa pārśva aṃsakeṣu ca gale ca vāma pārśvām sa gala pṛṣṭeṣu anantaram dhātrā tu keśavam nyasya aryamṇa nārāyaṇam punar viṣṇum ca eva aṃśunā yuktam bhagena madhusūdanam vāmanam ca pūṣṇā śrīdharam eva ca hṛṣīkeśam nyaset paścāt parjanyena samanvitam tvaṣṭrā yutam padmanābham dāmodaram ca viṣṇunā vyāpakam vinyaset paścāt kirīṭa manunā sudhīḥ dhruvaḥ kirīṭa keyūra hāra ante makara iti ca kuṇḍala ante cakra śaṅkha gadā ante iṃ abhoja hastataḥ pīta aṃbara ante śrīvatsām kitava kṣaḥ sthala iti ca namaḥ ntaḥ bāṇa ṣaṣ varṇaiḥ kirīṭa manuḥ īritaḥ evam nyāsa vidhim kṛtvā dhyāyet nārāyaṇam vibhum udyat koṭi arka sadṛśam śaṅkham cakram gadā aṃbujam dadhatam ca karaiḥ bhūmi śrībhyām pārśva dvaya āñcitam hāra keyūra valaya aṅgadam pīta aṃbaram smaret viṣṇoḥ samīpam āpnoti veda lakṣa japān naraḥ tathā ca nirmalam jñānam pañca lakṣa japāt bhavet lakṣa ṣaṣṭena ca āpnoti mantrī viṣṇau sthirā matim sapta lakṣa japāt mantrī viṣṇoḥ sārūpyam āpnuyāt aṣṭa lakṣam japet mantrī nirvāṇam adhigacchati evam japtvā tatas prājñaḥ daśa aṃśam sarasīruhaiḥ maṇḍūkāt para tatva antam pīṭhe saṃpūjya yatnatas vimala utkarṣiṇī jñānā kriyā yogā tatas parā prahvī satyā tathā īśāna anugrahā navamī matā saṃyoga yoga padma ante pīṭhāya hṛdaya antimaḥ ṣaḍviṃśat akṣaraḥ pīṭha mantraḥ anena āsanam diśet mūrtim saṃkalpya mūlena tasyām āvāhya pūjayet ādau ca aṅgāni saṃpūjya mantrāṇām keśareṣu ca prāc ādi diś dale vāsudevam saṃkarṣaṇam tathā pradyumnam aniruddham ca śaktīḥ koṇeṣu atha arcayet śāntim śriyam sarasvatyāḥ ratim saṃpūjayet kramāt hema pīta tamāla indranīla ābhāḥ pīta vāsasaḥ caturbhujāḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā aṃbha ghoja dharāḥ ime sita kāñcana go dugdha dūrvā varṇāḥ ca śaktayaḥ dala agreṣu cakra śaṅkha gadā paṅkaja kaustubhān pūjayet musalam khaḍgam vanamālām yathākramāt rakta aja pīta kanaka śyāma kṛṣṇa asita arjunān pārśvayoḥ pūjayet paśca aṅkha padma nidhī kramāt muktā māṇikya saṃkāśau paścime dhvajam aparcayet raktam vighnam tathā āgneye śyāmam āryam ca rākṣase durgām śyāmām vāyu koṇe senānyam pītam aiśvare lokeśāḥ na āyudhaiḥ yuktān bahis saṃpūjayet sudhīḥ kṣetra dhānya suvarṇānām dhāraṇīm smaret devīm dūrvā dala śyāmām dadhānām śāli mañjarīm cintayet bhāratīm devīm vīṇā pustaka dhāriṇīm dakṣiṇe devadevasya pūrṇa candra nibha ānanām kṣīrābdhi phena puñja ābhe vasānām śveta vāsasī nārasiṃham iva ātmānam devam dhyātvā ati bhairavam śaśtram saṃmantrya mantreṇa śabrūn hatvā nivartate nārasiṃhena bījena mantram saṃyojya sādhakaḥ śatam aṣṭa uttaram jaṇtvā vāma hasta abhimantritāḥ punar punar apaḥ siṃcet sarpa daṣṭaḥ api jīvati gāruḍena ca saṃyojya pañcārṇena japet tadā nirviṣīkaraṇe dhyāyet viṣṇum garuḍa vāhanam aśoka phalake tārkṣyam ālikhya aśoka saṃhatau aśoka puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjya bhagavantam tad agratas juhuyāt tāni puṣpāṇi tri saṃdhyam sapta patrakam pratyakṣaḥ jāyate pakṣī varam iṣṭam prayacchati gāṇapatyena saṃyojya japet lakṣam payovrataḥ mahāgaṇapatim devam pratyakṣam iha paśyati vāṇibījena saṃyuktam ṣaṣ māsam yojayet naraḥ hutvā guṅcī śakalāni arddha agula mitāni ca śanaiśvara dine samyak spṛṣṭvā śvattham ca pāṇinā japtvā ca aṣṭaśatam yuddhe hi apamṛtyum jayati asau pañcaviṃśatidhā japtvā nityam prātar pibet jalam kuṃbham saṃsthāpya vidhivat āpūrya śuddha vāriṇā candra sūrya uparāge tu hi upoṣya aṣṭa sahasrakam spṛṣṭvā brāhmī dhṛtam japtvā pibet sādhaka sattamaḥ medhām kavi tvam vāc siddhim labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ ālayaḥ sarva siddhīnām kathitaḥ tava nārada nārāyaṇāya śabda ante vidmahe padam īrayet vāsudeva padam ṅeṃtam dhīmahi iti tatas vadet tat naḥ viṣṇuḥ pracovarṇān saṃvadet codayāt iti eṣā uktā viṣṇugāyatrī sarva pāpa praṇāśinī tāraḥ hṛd bhagavān ṅeṃtaḥ vāsudevāya kīrtitaḥ strī śūdrāṇām vitāraḥ ayam sa tāraḥ tu dvijanmanām prajāpatiḥ muniḥ ca asya gāyatrī chandaḥ īritaḥ devatā vāsudevaḥ tu bījam śaktiḥ dhruvaḥ ca hṛd candra akṣi veda pañca ṛṇaiḥ samastena aṅga kalpanam mūrdhni bhāle dṛśoḥ āsye gale dos hṛdaye punar nyāset kramāt mantra varṇān sṛṣṭinyāsaḥ ayam īritaḥ hṛd ādi mastaka antam tu sthiti nyāsam pracakṣate pādāt ārabhya mūrddhānam nyāsam saṃhārakam viduḥ prāṇam tathā cittam hṛd padmam sūrya maṇḍalam candra agni maṇḍale ca eva vāsudevam tatas param nārāyaṇam cakram atas tattvāni dvādaśa eva tu mūla arṇa hṛd parāya ādyam ātmane hṛdaya antimam pūrva uktam dhyānam atra api bhānu lakṣa japaḥ manoḥ tadṛśa aṃśam tilaiḥ ājya lolitaiḥ havanam caret pīṭhe pūrva udite mantrī mūrti saṃkalpya mūlataḥ tasyām āvāhya deveśam vāsudevam prapūjayet aṅgāni pūrvam abhyarcya vāsudeva ādikāḥ tatas śānti ādi śaktayaḥ pūjyāḥ prāgvat dikṣu vidikṣu ca tṛtīya āvaraṇe pūjyāḥ proktāḥ dvādaśa mūrtayaḥ indra ādyān āyudhaiḥ yuktān pūjayet haraṇī gṛhe evam āvaraṇaiḥ iṣṭvā pañcabhiḥ viṣṇum avyayam puruṣottama saṃjñasya viṣṇoḥ bheda catuṣṭayam śrīkaraḥ ca hṛṣīkeśaḥ kṛṣaaṇaḥ ca atra caturthakaḥ tāraḥ kāmaḥ ramā paścāt ṅeṃtaḥ syāt puruṣottamaḥ varma astrāṇi agni priya antaḥ mantraḥ vahni indu varṇavān brahmā muniḥ syāt gāyatrī chandaḥ proktaḥ atha devatā puruṣottama saṃjñaḥ atra bhū candra eka rasa akṣi akṣi mantra varṇoḥ vibhāgataḥ samudyat āditya nibham śaṅkha cakra gadā aṃbujaiḥ nṛtyat deva aṅganā vṛnda kvaṇāt kiṅkiṇi nūpure lasat māṇikya vedyām tu vṛndāraka vrāta kirīṭa agra ratna abhicarcite nava lakṣam japet mantram juhuyāt tad daśa aṃśataḥ utphullaiḥ kamalaiḥ pīṭhe pūrva ukte evam ārādhya deveśam prāpnoti mahatīm śriyam putrān pautrān yaśaḥ kāntim bhuktim muktim ca vindati uttiṣṭa iti padam paścāt śrīkara agnipriya antimaḥ aṣṭa arṇaḥ asya muniḥ vyāsaḥ paṅktiḥ chandaḥ udāhṛtam śrī kāra ākhyaḥ hariḥ proktaḥ devatā sakala iṣṭa daḥ bhīṣaya dvitayam hṛd syāt trāsaya dvitayam śiraḥ asram rakṣa dvayam sarve humantāḥ samudīritāḥ mastake netrayoḥ kaṇṭha hṛdaye nābhi deśake ūrū jaṅghām yugmeṣu mantra varṇān kramāt nyataset bāhu yugme tathā bāhūm rājanyaḥ iti vinyaset nyaset pāda dvaye mantrī padbhyām śūdraḥ ajāyata cakram śaṅkham gadām padmam kara agreṣu atha vinyaset evam nyāsa vidhim kṛtvā dhyāyet pūrva ukta maṇḍape pūrva ukta rūpiṇam devam śrīkaram loka mohanam dhyātvā evam pūjayet aṣṭa lakṣam mantrī daśa aṃśataḥ rakta aṃbu jaiḥ samidbhiḥ ca vilva kṣīri druma udbhavaiḥ payaḥ annaiḥ sarpiṣā hutvā pratyekam su samāhitaḥ aśvattha uduṃbara plakṣa vaṭāḥ kṣīri drumāḥ smṛtā pūjayet vaiṣṇave pīṭhe mūrtim saṃkalpya mūlataḥ aṅga āvaraṇa dikpāla hetibhiḥ sahitam vibhum tāraḥ hṛd bhagavān ṅeṃtaḥ varāha iti tatas param rūpāya bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svar syāt lohitakāmikā ca ye chandaḥ anuṣṭubh devatā ādi varāhaḥ samudīritaḥ ekadaṃṣṭrāya hṛdayam vyoma ulkāyaga śiraḥ smṛtam mahādaṃṣṭrāya ca astram syāt pañcāṅgam iti kalpayet athavā giri ṣaṣ sapta bāṇaiḥ vasubhiḥ akṣaraiḥ ām hrīṃ svarṇa nibham jānvoḥ adhas nābheḥ sita prabham iṣṭa abhīti gadā śaṅkha cakra śakti asi kheṭakān dadhatam ca karaiḥ daṃṣṭra agra lasat dharaṇim smaret evam dhyātvā japet lakṣam daśa aṃśam sarasīruhaiḥ mūlena mūrtim saṅkalpya tasyām sampūjayet vibhum dadyāt dhanam dhānyam mahīm śriyam siṃha arke sita pakṣasya aṣṭamyām gavyeṣu pañcasu śilām śuddhām vinikṣipya spṛṣṭvā tām ayutam japet udak mukha svatas mantrī tām śilām likhanet bhuvi bhūta preta ahi caura ādi kṛtām bādhām nivārayet prātar bhṛgu dine sādhya bhū talāt mṛdam āharet mantritām mūlamantreṇa vibhajet tām tridhā punar cullyām ekam samālipya api aparam pāka bhājane go dugdhe param āloḍya śodhitān tandulān kṣipet avatārya carum paścāt vahnau deyam yathāvidhi sampūjya dhūpa dīpa ādyaiḥ paścāt ājya plutam carum juhuyāt saṃskṛte vahnau aṣṭottaraśatam sudhīḥ bhānu udaye pi āravāre sādhya kṣetrāt mṛdam punar ādāya pūrva vidhinā haviḥ āpādya pūrvavat juhuyāt edhite vahnau pūrva saṃkhyākam ādarāt evam sa sapta āra vāreṣu juhuyāt kṣetra siddhaye juhuyāt lakṣa saṃkhyākam gavyaiḥ ca eva sa pāyasaiḥ abhīṣṭa bhūmi ādhipatyam labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ udyat dos paridham divyam sita daṃṣṭra agra bhūdharam svarṇa ābham pārthive pīte maṇḍale su samāhitaḥ dhyātvā āpnoti mahīm ramyām varāhasya prasādataḥ vāruṇe maṇḍale dhyāyet vārāham mahā upadrava śāntiḥ syāt sādhakasya na saṃśayaḥ vaśyā artham ca sadā dhyāyet varhi ābham vahnimaṇḍe dhyāyet evam ripūn cāṭe kṛṣṇa ābham vāyu maṇḍale hi a maṇḍala gatam svaccham vārāham sarva siddhi dam śatru bhūta graha kṣveḍā āmaya pīḍā ādi śāntaye pūjā ādya ardhya ādikam sarvam asyām pūrva ukta vat caret sa vāma karṇa anidrā āsyāt varāhāya hṛd antimaḥ tārā ādyaḥ vasu varṇaḥ ayam sarva aiśvarya pradāyakaḥ brahmā muniḥ syāt gāyatrī chandaḥ vārāha saṃjñakaḥ deva ścandra idu abdhi netraiḥ saveṇa aṅga kriyā matā dhyāna pūjā prayoga ādi prāgvat asya api kalpayet praṇava ādau ca ṅentam ca bhagavatī iti padam tatas ekonaviṃśati arṇa āḍhyaḥ mantraḥ vahnipriya antimaḥ varāhaḥ asya muniḥ chandaḥ gāyatrī nivṛt ādikā devatā dharaṇī bījam tāraḥ śaktiḥ vasupriyā rāma veda agni bāṇa akṣi netra arṇaiḥ aṅgara kalpanam śyāmām citra vibhūṣā āḍhyām padma sthām tuṅga su stanīm nīla aṃbuja dvayam śāli mañjarīm ca śukram karaiḥ dadhatīm citra vasanām dharām bhagavatīm smaret evam dhyātvā japet lakṣam daśa aṃśam pāyasena tu sa ājyena juhuyāt mantrī viṣṇoḥ pīṭhṭhe samarcayet mūrtim saṃkalpya mūlena tasyām vasumatīm yajet aṅgāni pūrvam ārādhya bhū vahni jala mārutān dikpātreṣu ca sampūjya koṇa patreṣu tad kalāḥ nivṛttiḥ ca pratiṣṭā ca vidyānām taiḥ ca tad kalāḥ indra ādyān api vañca ādīn pūjayet tad anantaram evam siddhe manau mantrī sādhayet iṣṭam ātmanaḥ dharaṇī prabhajan evam paśu ratna aṃbara ādibhiḥ dharamyāḥ vallabhaḥ sa syāt sukhī jīvet śatam samāḥ tāraḥ kāmaḥ ramā bījam hṛd ante puruṣottamaḥ śrīkaṇṭhaḥ pratirūpa ante lakṣmī iti ca nivāsi ca sakala ante jagat paścāt kṣobhaṇa iti padam vadet sarva strī hṛdaya ante tu vidāraṇa padam vadet sura asura ante manuja suṃdarī jana varṇataḥ manāṃsi tāpaya dvandvam dīpaya dvitayam tatas śoṣaya dvitayam paścāt māraya dvitayam tatas drāvaya dvitayam tāvat ākarṣaya yugam tatas dhyāna pūjā prayoga ādi prāgvat asya api kalpayet praṇava ādau ca ṅentam ca bhagavatī iti padam tatas ekonaviṃśati arṇa āḍhyaḥ mantraḥ vahnipriya antimaḥ varāhaḥ asya muniḥ chandaḥ gāyatrī nivṛt ādikā devatā dharaṇī bījam tāraḥ śaktiḥ vasupriyā rāma veda agni bāṇa akṣi nevā arṇaiḥ aṅga kalpanam śyāmām citra vibhūṣā āḍhyām padma sthām tuṅga su stanīm nīla aṃbuja dvayam śāli mañjarīn ca śukam karaiḥ dadhatīm citra vasanām dharām bhagavatīm smaret evam dhyātvā japet lakṣam daśa aṃśam pāyasena tu sa ājyena juhuyāt mantrī viṣṇoḥ pīṭhe samarcayet mūrtim saṃkalpya gūlena tasyām vasumatīm yajet aṅgāni pūrvam ārādhya bhū vahni jala mārutān dikpātreṣu ca sampūjya koṇa patreṣu tad kalāḥ nivṛttiḥ ca pratiṣṭā ca vidyānām taiḥ ca tad kalāḥ siddhe manau mantrī sādhayet iṣṭam ātmanaḥ dharaṇīm prabhajan evam paśu ratna aṃbara ādibhiḥ dharaṇyāḥ vallabhaḥ sa syāt sukhī jīvet śatam samāḥ tāraḥ kāmaḥ ramā bījam hṛd ante puruṣottamaḥ śrīkaṇṭhaḥ pratirūpa ante lakṣmī iti ca nivāsim ca sakala ante jagat paścāt kṣobhaṇa iti padam vadet sarva strī hṛdaya ante tu vidāraṇa padam vadet sura asura ante manuja suṃdarī jana varṇataḥ manāṃsi tāpaya dvandvam dīpaya dvitayam tatas śoṣaya dvitayam paścāt māraya dvitayam tatas drāvaya dvitayam tāvat ākarṣaya yugam tatas tatas sarva bāṇaiḥ bhedi yugam pāśena ante kaṭa dvayam aṅkuśena iti saṃprocya tāḍaya dvitayam punar hṛd antaḥ ayam mahā mantraḥ dvi śata arṇaḥ samīritaḥ devatā jagatām mohe jagannāthaḥ prakīrtitaḥ kāmaḥ bījam ramā śaktiḥ viniyogaḥ akhila āptaye hṛdayam kīrtitam paścāt jagat kṣobhaṇa śabdataḥ lakṣmī dayita varma antaḥ śiraḥ proktam śikhā punar parama ante bhṛgu karṇābhyām ca sarva padam tatas hṛdaya ante vidā paścāt raṇa sarva padam vadet ākarṣayat vayam paścāt mahābala padam tatas varma ca astram samākhyātam netram syāt tat anantaram vaśam ānaya varma ante netramantraḥ samīritaḥ ṣaṣ aṅga mantrāḥ tāra ādyāḥ phaṭ namaḥ ntāḥ prakīrtitāḥ hṛṣīkeśa iti saṃprocya apratirūpa ādi śabdataḥ mamnatha anantaram sarva strīṇām hṛdayam īrayet ākarṣaṇa padāḥ gaccha dāgaccha hṛdaya antimaḥ anena vyāpakam kṛtvā jagannātham smaret sudhīḥ kṣīrābdheḥ tu taṭe ramyam suradruma latā āñcitam udyat arka ābhu jāla ābham sva dhāmnaḥ jvāla diṅmukham divya vāta uñcalat kañja parāga uddhūlita aṃbaram śaṅkha pāśeṣu cāpāni musalam nandakam gadām aṅkuśam dadhatam dorbhiḥ śliṣṭe kamalayā urasi paśyati aṅka sthayā aṃbhoja śriyā rāga ullasadṛśā dhyātvā evam prajapet lakṣa catuṣkam tad daśa aṃśataḥ kuṇḍeḥ addhacandre padmaiḥ vā jātī puṣpaiḥ ca homayet yāga bhūmim tathā ātmānam yāga upakaraṇam tathā pūjayiṣyan jagannātham gāyatryā prokṣayet vudhaḥ smarāya dhīmahi iti uktvā tat naḥ viṣṇuḥ pracodayāt gāyatrī eṣā samākhyātā sarva śuddhi karī parā kalpayet āsanam pīṭhe pūrva ukte vaiṣṇave sudhīḥ pakṣirājāya ṭha dvandvam pīṭha mantraḥ ayam īritaḥ mūrtim saṃkalpa mūlena tasyām āvāhayet atas śrīvatsa hṛdayam tena śrīvatsam stanayoḥ yajet karṇikāyām tatas abhyarcayet vidhivat ca aṅga devatāḥ daleṣu pūjayet paścāt lakṣmī ādya āvṛtta cāmarāḥ bandhūka kusuma ābhāsāḥ muktā hāra lasat kucāḥ lakṣmī sarasvatī ca eva dhṛtiḥ prītiḥ tatas param kāntiḥ śāntiḥ tuṣṭi puṣṭi bīja ādyāḥ ṅe namaḥ ntikāḥ bhṛguḥ devyāḥ bījam udāhṛtam devyāḥ bījam kramāt āsām ādau ca viniyojayet dala agreṣu yajet śaṅkham śārṅgam cakram asim gadām aṅkuśam musalam pāśam sva mudrā manubhiḥ pṛthak mahā jalacarāḥ yānte varma astram vahni vallabhā pāñcajanyā pratāra ādyaḥ namaḥ ntaḥ śaṅkha pūjane śārṅgāya sa śaya ante ca varma astram vahnivallabhā śārṅgāya hṛdayam mantraḥ mahā ādyaḥ śārṅga pūjane chindhi dvayam tatas paścāt vidāraya yugam tatas bhūkāni trāsaya dvandvam varma phaṭ vahni suṃdarī sudarśanāya hṛdayam proktaḥ cakra arcane manuḥ mahā khaḍga tīkṣṇa padāt śivi yugmam samīrayet hum phaṭ svāhā ca khaḍgāya namaḥ khaḍga arcane manuḥ varma astra vahni jāyā anta kaumodaki hṛ kṣatimaḥ mahā aṅkuśa padāt kuṭca yugmam hum phaṭ asupriyā aṅkuśāya namaḥ proktaḥ mantra grauvāku śarcane mahā pāśa hadāt aghaṭayam ākarṣayat vayam hum phaṭe svāhā ca pāśāya namaḥ pāśa arcane manuḥ tārā ādyāḥ manavaḥ hi ete tatas śakra ādikān yajet māsa mātram tu kusumaiḥ pūjayitvā haya ari jaiḥ māsa mātreṇa vaśyāḥ syuḥ tasya sarve nṛpa uttamāḥ sādhayet sakalān kāmān viṣṇu tulyaḥ na saṃśayaḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde saptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu nārada vakṣyāmi divyān narahareḥ manūn yān samārādhya brahma ādyāḥ cakruḥ sṛṣṭi ādi karma vai eka akṣaraḥ smṛtaḥ mantraḥ bhajatām sura pādapaḥ kṣaṃ bījam śaktirī proktā ṣaṣ dīrgheṇa ṣaṣ aṅgakam lakṣam japaḥ tad daśa aṃśa homaḥ ca ghṛta pāyasaiḥ yajet pīṭhe vaiṣṇave tu kesareṣu aṅga pūjanam khageśam śaṅkaram śeṣam śatānandam digāliṣu śriyam hriyam dhṛtim puṣṭim koṇa patreṣu pūjayet dantacchadeṣu nṛharīn tāvataḥ pūjayet kramātma kṛṣṇaḥ rudraḥ mahā ghoraḥ bhīmaḥ bhīṣaṇaḥ ujjvalaḥ karālaḥ vikarālaḥ ca daitya antaḥ madhusūdanaḥ raktākṣaḥ piṅgalākṣaḥ ca añjanaḥ dīptaruciḥ tathā sughorakaḥ ca suhanuḥ viśvakaḥ rākṣasāṃtakaḥ viśālakaḥ dhūmrakeśaḥ hayagrīvaḥ ghanasvanaḥ meghavarṇaḥ kubhaghakarṇaḥ kṛtānta tīvra tejasau agni varṇaḥ mahā ugraḥ ca tatas viśva vibhūṣaṇaḥ vighna kṣamaḥ mahāsenaḥ siṃhāḥ dvātriṃśat īritāḥ tat brahiḥ prārcayet vidvān lokapālān sa hetikān viṣṇaḥ pradyumna yuj śārṅgī mahān tatas viṣṇum jvalantam bhṛgvīśaḥ jalam padmāsanam tatas hariḥ tu vāsudevāya vaikuṇṭhaḥ viṣṇu saṃyutaḥ gadī sa iṃdu nṛsiṃham ca bhīṣaṇam bhadvam eva ca mṛtyu mṛtyum tatas śauriḥ bhānoḥ nārāyaṇa anvitaḥ nṛhareḥ dvāviṃśat arṇaḥ ayam mantraḥ sāmrājya dāyakaḥ brahmā muniḥ tu gāyatrī chandaḥ anuṣṭubh udāhṛtam devatā nṛhariḥ ca asya sarva iṣṭu phala dāyakaḥ haṃ bījam iṃ tathā śaktiḥ viniyogaḥ akhila āptaye vedaiḥ caturbhiḥ vasubhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ yuga akṣaraiḥ ṣaḍaṅgāni vidhāya atha mūrdhni bhāle ca netrayoḥ mukha bāhu aṅghri saṃdhi agreṣu atha kukṣau tathā hṛdi gale pārśva dvaye pṛṣṭe kakudyā arṇān manu udbhavān praṇava antaritān kṛtvā nyaset sādhaka sattamaḥ nṛsiṃha sāṃnidhya karaḥ nyāsaḥ daśavidhaḥ yathā kara aṅghṣaṣṭa ādi aṅgulīṣu pṛthak ādi anta parvaṇoḥ sarva aṅgulīṣu vinyasya avaśiṣṭam talayoḥ nyaset dakṣān padoḥ tale kaṭyām meḍhra ūruḥ ū jānu jagha yacoḥ rakta asthi majjāsu tanau nyaset varṇān vi cakṣaṇaḥ varṇān pade gulpha jānu kaṭi nābhi hṛdi sthale bāhvoḥ kaṇṭhe ca cibuke ca oṣṭau gaṇḍe pravinyaset padāni tu mukhe mūrdhri nasi cakṣuṣi karṇayoḥ āsye ca hṛdaya nābhau pādān sarva aṅgake nyaset arddha dvayam nyaset mūrdhni āhṛt pādāt tad aṅgakam ugra ādīni padānī ha mṛtyu mṛtyum namāmi aham ityantāni āsyaka ghnāṇa cakṣuḥ śrotra iṣu pakṣmasu hṛdi nābhau ca kaṭi ādi pāda antam navasu nyaset vīra ādyān api tāni eva yathāpūrvam pravinyaset nṛsiṃha ādyāni tāni eva pūrvavat vinyaset sudhīḥ candra agni veda ṣaṣ rāma netra diś bāhu bhū mitān vibhaktā pantra varṇān ca kramāt sthāneṣu vinyaset mūle mūlāt ca nābhi antam nābhi ādi hṛdaya avadhi bāhvoḥ aṅguliṣu prāṇe mūrddha ādi caraṇa avadhi vinyaset nāmataḥ dhīmān harinyāsaḥ ayam īritaḥ nyāsasya asya tu māhātmyam jānāti ekaḥ hariḥ svayam evam nyāsa vidhim kṛtvā dhyāyet ca nṛharim hṛdi gala āsakta lasat bāhu spṛṣṭa keśaḥ abja cakra dhṛk nakha agra bhinna daitya īśaḥ jvālā mālā samanvitaḥ nṛsiṃhaḥ asmān sadā pātu sthala aṃbu gagana upagaḥ dhyātvā evam darśayet mudrām nṛsiṃhasya mahātmanaḥ jānu madhya gatau kṛtvā cibuka uṣṭau samau ubhau hastau ca bhūmi saṃlagnau kaṃpamānaḥ punar punar mukham vijṛṃbhitam kṛtvā lelihānām ca jihvikām eṣā mudrā nārasiṃhī pradhānā iti prakīrtitā vāmasya aṅguṣṭataḥ baddhvā a kaniṣṭā maṅgalī trayam triśūla vat saṃmukha ūrddhve kuryāt mudrām nṛsiṃha gām aṅguṣṭābhyām ca karayoḥ tathā ā kramya kaniṣṭake adhomukhābhiḥ śiṣṭābhiḥ śeṣābhiḥ nṛharau tatas hastau adhomukhau kṛtvā nābhi deśe prasārya ca tarjaṃnībhyām nayet skandhau proktā ca āntraṇamudrikā anāmāyām tu vāmāyām dakṣiṇām tu vinikṣipet tarjanyau pṛṣṭatas lagnau aṅguṣṭau tarjanī śritau cakra mudrā bhavet eṣā nṛhareḥ saṃnidhau matā cakra mudrā tathā kṛtvā tarjanībhyām tu madhyame pīḍayet vaṃṣṭra mudrā eṣā sarva pāpa praṇāśinī etāḥ mudrāḥ nṛsiṃhasya sarva mantreṣu saṃmatāḥ varṇa lakṣam japet mantram tad daśa aṃśam ca pāyasaiḥ aṅgāni ādau samārādhya diś patreṣu yajet punar garaḍa ādīn śrīmukhān ca vidikṣu lokapān bahis evam saṃsādhitaḥ mantraḥ sarvān kāmān prapūrayet pūrva mṛtyu pade śatroḥ nāma kṛtvā svayam hariḥ niśitaiḥ nakha daṃṣṭra agraiḥ khādyamānam ca saṃsmaret jāyate maṇḍalāt arvāk śatruḥ vai śamana atithiḥ śrī kāmaḥ satatam dhyāyet pūrva uktam nṛharim sitam vāma aṅka sthitayā lakṣmyā āliṅgatam padma hastayā viṣa mṛtyu uparoga ādi sarva upadrava nāśanam nara siṃham mahā bhīmam kāla anala sama prabham āntra mālā dharam raudram kaṇṭha hāreṇa bhūṣitam nāga yajñopavītam ca pañcānana su śobhitam bhujaiḥ parigha saṃkāśaiḥ daśabhiḥ ca upaśobhitam akṣa sūtram gadā padmam śaṅkham go kṣīra sannibham khaḍgam śūlam ca bāṇam ca nṛharim rudra rūpiṇam indragopa ābha nīla ābham candra ābham svarṇa sannibham pūrva ādi ca uttaram yāvat ūddhva ārsyam sarva varṇakam dhyāyet yadā mahāt karma tadā ṣoḍaśa hastavān nṛsiṃhaḥ sarva loka īśaḥ sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitaḥ pāśa aṅkuśa dharau dvau ca dvau ripoḥ mukuṭa arpitau iti ṣoḍaśa dos daṇḍa maṇḍitam nṛharim vibhum dhyāyet nārada nīla ābham ugra karma maṇi an anya dhīḥ nṛsiṃhaḥ sarva bhūta īśaḥ sarva siddhi karaḥ paraḥ dakṣiṇe cakra padme ca paraśuṃpāśam eva ca halam ca muśalam ca eva abhayam ca aṅkuśam tathā paṭṭiśam bhindipālam ca khaḍga mudgara tomarān vāma bhāge karaiḥ śaṃṅkham kheṭam pāśam ca śūlakam agnim ca vara dam śaktim kuṇḍikām ca tatas param kārmukam tarjanī mudrām gadām ḍamaru śūrpakau dvābhyām karābhyām ca ripoḥ jānu mastaka pīḍanam ūrddhvīkṛtābhyām bāhubhyām āntra mālā dharam vibhum adhas sthitābhyām bāhubhyām hiraṇyaka vidāraṇam priyaṅkaram ca bhaktānām daityānām ca bhayaṅkaram nṛsiham tam smaret ittham mahā mṛtyu bhaya apaham svarṇa varṇa suparṇa stham vidyut mālā saṭā anvitam koṭi pūrṇa indu varṇam ca su mukham tri akṣi vīkṣaṇam pīta vastra ūru bhūṣā āḍhyam nṛsiṃham śānta vigraham kṣveḍa roga ādi śamanam svaiḥ dhyānaiḥ su khanditam śatroḥ senā nirodhena yatnam kuryāt ca sādhakam devam nṛsiṃham saṃpūjya kusuma ādi upacārakaiḥ sa mūla mūlaiḥ juṃhuyāt caraiḥ daśa śatam pṛthak hutvā sapta dinam mantrī senām iṣṭām mahīpateḥ tasyāḥ purastāt nṛharim nighnantam ripu maṇḍalam smṛtvā japam praklarvīta yāvat āyāti sā punar nirjatya nikhilān śatrūn saha vīra śriyā asukhāt prīṇayet mantriṇam rājā vibhavaiḥ prīta mānasaḥ gaja aśva ratha ratnaiḥ ca grāma kṣetra dhana ādibhiḥ jāyate tasya rāṣṭreṣu prāṇebhyaḥ api mahā bhayam nāśayet mūṣikā lūtā vṛścika ādi utthitam viṣam lipta aṅgaḥ sarva rogaiḥ ca mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ sevantī kusumaiḥ hutvā mahatīm śriyam āpnuyāt tulasī patra homena mahatīm kīrtim āpnuyāt madhūka puṣpaiḥ iṣṭam syāt staṃbhanam dhātri khaṇḍakaiḥ dadhi madhu ājya miśrām tu guḍūcīm catur aṅgulām śanaiścara dine aśvattham spṛṣṭvā ca aṣṭa uttaram śatam japet jitvā asaḥ apamṛtyum śata varṣāṇi jīvati yasya saṃdhāraṇāt eva bhaveyuḥ sarva saṃpadaḥ śveta bhūrje likhet padmam dvātriṃśat siṃha saṃyutam pāśa aṅkuśaiḥ ca saṃveṣṭya pūjayet yantram uttamam cakrarājam mahā rājam sarva carka īśvara īśvaram dhāraṇāt jayam āpnoti satyam satyam na saṃśayaḥ atha yantra antaram vakṣye śṛṇu nārada siddhi dam aṣṭa āram vilikhet yantram ślakṣṇam karṇikayā yutam eka akṣaram nārasiṃham madhye ca eva sa sādhyakam japet aṣṭa sahasram tu sūtreṇa āveṣṭya tat bahis svarṇa raupya su tāmraiḥ ca veṣṭayet kramatas sudhīḥ lākṣayā veṣṭitam kṛtvā punar mantreṇa mantrayet kaṇṭhe bhuje śikhāyām vā dhārayet yantram uttamam nara nārī naredrāḥ ca sarve syuḥ vaśagāḥ bhuvi duṣṭāḥ tam na eva bādhante piśāca uraga rākṣasāḥ atha anyat saṃpravakṣyāmi yantram sarva vaśaṅkaram dvādaśa aram mahā cakram pūrvavat vilikhet sudhīḥ madhye mantram śakti yuktam śrī bījena tu veṣṭayeta kāla antakam nāma cakram surā sukha śaṅkaram atha sarva iṣṭa dam jvālāmāli saṃjñam vadāmi aham bījam hṛd bhagavān ṅeṃtaḥ narasiṃhāya tat param jvāline māline dīpta daṃṣṭrāya agnine padam hariḥ vināśanāya ante sarva jvara vināśanaḥ rakṣa yugmam ca varma astra ṭha dūya antaḥ dhruva ādikaḥ aṣṭaṣaṣṭi akṣaraiḥ proktaḥ jvālā mālī manu uttamaḥ puṇya ādikam tu pūrva uktam trayodaśabhiḥ akṣaraiḥ paṅktibhiḥ rudra asaṃkhyākaiḥ aṣṭādaśabhiḥ akṣaraiḥ pūrva ukta rūpiṇam nṛharim smaret lakṣam japaḥ daśa aṃśam ca juhuyāt kapilā ghṛtaiḥ raudra apasmāra bhūta ādi nāśakaḥ ayam manu uttamaḥ prāṇaḥ māyā nṛsiṃhaḥ ca sṛṣṭiḥ brahmāstram īritaḥ ṣaṣ akṣaraḥ mahā mantraḥ sarva abhīṣṭa pradāyakaḥ ṣaṣ dīrgha bhājā bījena ṣaṣ aṅgāni samācaret pūrva uktena eva vidhinā dhyānam pūjām samācaret ramā bīja ādikaḥ anuṣṭubh trayastriṃśa arṇavāt manuḥ prajāpatiḥ muniḥ chandaḥ anuṣṭubh lakṣmī nṛ kesarī devatā caja padaiḥ sarveṇa aṅga kalpanam īritam vinyasya evam tu pañcāṅgam sva ātma rakṣām samācaret saṃspṛśan dakṣiṇam bāhum śarabhasya manum japet athavā rāma mantra ante param kṣa dvitayam paṭhet athavā keśava ādyaiḥ tu rakṣām kuryāt prayatnataḥ keśavaḥ pātu pādau me jaṅghe nārāyaṇaḥ avatu nābhim viṣṇuḥ ca me pātu jaṭharam madhusūdanaḥ ūrū trivikramaḥ pātu hṛdayam pātu me naraḥ śrīdharaḥ pātu kaṇṭham ca hṛṣīkeśaḥ mukham mama padmanābhaḥ stanau pātu śīrṣam dāmodaraḥ avatu evam vinyasya ca aṅgeṣu japa kāle tu sādhakaḥ nirbhayaḥ jāyate bhūta vetāla graha rākṣasāt purastāt keśavaḥ pātuḥ cakrī jāṃbūnada prabhaḥ paścāt nārāyaṇaḥ śaṅkhī nīla jīmūta sannibhaḥ āgneyyām aravinda akṣaḥ musalī madhusūdanaḥ trivikramaḥ khaḍgapāṇiḥ nairṛtyām jvalana prabhaḥ vāyavyām mādhavaḥ vajrī taruṇa āditya sannibhaḥ aiśānyām puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ śrīdharaḥ paṭṭiśa āyudhaḥ vidyutprabhaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ urddhū pātu sa mudgaraḥ adhas ca padmanābhaḥ me sahasrāṃśu sama prabheḥ sarva āyudhaḥ sarva śaktiḥ sarva ādyaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ indragopa prabhaḥ pāyāt pāśa hastaḥ aparājitaḥ evam sarvatra niśchidram nāma dvādaśa pañjaram evam rakṣām vidhāya atha durddharṣaḥ jāyate naraḥ pūrva ukta vidhinā sarvam dhyāna pūjā ādikam caret jitam te puṇḍarīkākṣa namaḥ te viśvabhāvana namaḥ te astu hṛṣīkeśa mahāpuruṣa te namaḥ ittham saṃprārthya japtvā ca paṭitvā visṛjet vibhum jaya dvayam śrī nṛsiṃha iti aṣṭa arṇaḥ ayam manu uttamaḥ śrīmān jaya nṛsiṃhaḥ tu sarva abhīṣṭa pradāyakaḥ sa iṃdu gorvida pūrveṇa viyatā sa indunā punar ṣaṣ vīrgha āḍhye na kurvīta ṣaḍ aṅgāni viśāla dhīḥ tatas dhyāyet hṛdi vibhum nṛsiṃham candraśekharam śrīmat nṛ kesaritano jagat eka baṃndho śrī nīlakaṇṭha karuṇā arṇave sāma rāja vahni indu tīvra kara netra pinākapāṇe śītāṃśu śekhara rameśvara pāhi viṣṇo dhyātvā evam prapet lakṣa aṣṭakam mantrī daśa aṃśataḥ tāraḥ māyā sva bīja ante karṇa ugram vīram īrayet nṛsiṃham bhīṣaṇam bhadram mṛtyu mṛtyum namāmi aham pañcāśīti akṣaraḥ mantraḥ bhajatām iṣṭa dāyakaḥ ṛṣī hi aghora brahmaṇau tathā triṣṭubh anuṣṭubhau chandasī ca tathā ghora nṛsiṃhaḥ devatā mataḥ dhyāna arcana ādikam ca asya kuryāt ānuṣṭubham sudhīḥ viśeṣāt mantra varyaḥ ayam sarva rakṣā karaḥ mataḥ bījam jaya yugam paścāt nṛsiṃha iti aṣṭa varṇavān ṛṣiḥ prajāpatiḥ ca asya anuṣṭubh chandaḥ udāhṛtam vidāraṇa nṛsiṃhaḥ asya devatā parikīrtitaḥ jaṃ bījam haṃ tathā śaktiḥ viniyogaḥ akhila āptaye dīrgha āḍhyena nṛsiṃhena ṣaḍaṅganyāsam ācaret raudram dhyāyet nṛsiṃham tu śatru vakṣaḥ vidāraṇam nakha daṃṣṭra āyudham bhakta abhaya da śrīniketanam muniḥ brahmā samākhyātaḥ anuṣṭubh chandaḥ samīritaḥ devatā asya divya pūrvaḥ nṛ kesarī pādaiḥ caturbhiḥ sarveṇa pañcāṅgāni samācaret dhyāna pūjā ādikam sarvam prāgvat proktam muni īśvara pūrva uktāni ca sarvāṇi kāryāṇi āyānti siddha tām tamaḥ grasa dvayam paścāt svāhā ante ca abhayam tatas ātmani ante ca bhūyiṣṭāḥ dhruvaḥ bīja antimaḥ manuḥ dviṣaṣṭi armaḥ asya muni ādi sarvam pūrvavat īritam tāraḥ nṛsiṃha bījam ca namaḥ bhagavate tatas narasiṃhāya tāraḥ ca bījam asya yadā tatas rūpāya tāraḥ svar bījam kūrma rūpāya tārakam bījam varāha rūpāya tāraḥ nṛsiṃhataḥ rūpāya tāra svam bījam vāmana ante ca rūpataḥ pāpa dhruva trayam bījam rāmāya nigama āditas bījam kṛṣṇāya tāra ante bījam ca kalkine tatas jaya dvayam tatas śālagrāma ante ca nivāsine divyasiṃhāya ṅe ntaḥ syāt svayaṃbhūḥ puruṣāya hṛd tāraḥ svam bījam iti eṣa mahā sāmrājya dāyakaḥ nṛsiṃha mantraḥ kha aṅka arṇaḥ muniḥ atriḥ prakīrtitaḥ daśa avatāraḥ nṛharim bījam kham śaktiḥ avyayaḥ bījena kṛtvā aṅgāni ca bhāvayet aneka candra pratimaḥ lakṣmī mukha kṛta īkṣaṇaḥ daśa avatāraiḥ sahitaḥ tanotu nṛhariḥ sukham japaḥ ayutam daśa aṃśena homaḥ syāt pāyasena tu prāk ukte pūjayet pīṭhe mūrti saṃkalpya mūlataḥ indra ādyān api vajra ādyān sampūjya iṣṭam avāpnuyāt sahasra arṇam mahā mantram vakṣye tantreṣu gopitam tāraḥ māyā ramā kāmaḥ bījam krodha padam tatas mūrte nṛsiṃha śabda ante mahāpuruṣaḥ īrayet kāla antaka sadṛś toyam sva īśvara ante sadṛś jalam śrānta ante tu niviṣṭā iti caitanya cit sadā tatas udaya astamaya ākrānta mahā kāruṇika iti ca hṛdaya abja catuḥ ca uktā dala ante tu niviṣṭitaḥ caitanya ātman catur āman dvādaśa ātman tatas param caturviṃśa ātman ante tu pañcaviṃśa ātman iti api koṭi ābha ante mahādeva nikāya daśa śabdataḥ śatayajñātalam jñeyam tatas ca amala yugmakam piṅgala īkṣaṇa saṭā daṣṭrāḥ daṃṣṭra āyudha nakha āyudha dānava indra antaka avahniṇa śoṇita padam tatas sam sakti vigraha ante tu bhūta apasmāra yātudhān sura asura vandyamāna pāda paṅkaja śabdataḥ rūpeṇa uttiṣṭa ca uttiṣṭa avidyā nicayam daha daha jñāna aiśvaryam ante prakāśaya yugam tatas om sarvajñaiḥ a roṣa ante jaṃbha a jṛṃbhi avatārakam niviṣṭam mama duḥsvapna bhayam nigaḍa śabdataḥ bhayam kāntāra śabda ante bhayam viṣa padāt tatas jvara ante ḍākinī kṛtyā adhvarevatī bhayam tatas bhayam durbhikṣa bhayam mārī śabdataḥ bhayam mārīca śabda ante bhayam chāyā padam tatas skanda apasmāra śabda ante bhayam caura bhayam tatas bhayam janma jarā ante maraṇa ādi śabdam īrayet jñeya rūpa dhāraṇa ante nṛsiṃha bṛhatsāmataḥ puruṣa ante sarva bhaya nivāraṇa padam tatas aṣṭa aṣṭakam catuḥṣaṣṭi ceṭikā bhayam īrayet vidyā āvṛtaḥ trayastriṃśat devatā koṭi śabdataḥ sahasra īkṣaṇa śabda ante sahasra pādam īrayet ghora aṭṭahāsa hasita viśvāvāsa padam tatas paramahaṃsa viśveśa viśva ante tu viḍaṃbana niviṣṭa ante tatas pradurbhāva kārakaḥ īrayet hṛṣīkeśa ca svacchanda niḥśeṣa jīva vinyaset grāsaka ante mahā paścāt piśita asṛj iti īrayet laṃpaṭa ante khecarī iti tu māla paṇḍita muṇḍa iti matsya kūrmam tatas param varāha ante nṛsiṃha iti vāmana ante samīrayet trailokya ākramaṇa ante tu pādaśālikaḥ īrayet niviṣṭa vahnijāyā ante svadhā ca eva tatas vaṣaṭ prāṇādhāraḥ ādideva padāt prāṇa apāna paścāt niviṣṭitaḥ mahāmāyā amogha ante daryam daitya andra śabdataḥ teja svara ante satya pūruṣa astra tāraḥ acyutāstram ca tāraḥ vācā sudeva phaṭ tāra māyā mūrteḥ phaṭ vaḥ kāmaḥ svara ādimaḥ māyā viśva ātmane ṣaṣ ca tāraḥ saucam tura ātmane hraḥ hiraṇa aya garbha rūpa dhāraṇa ante ca phaṭ dhruvaḥ hraiṃ anaupamya rūpa dhāriṇā astram dhruvaḥ tatas kṣaiṃ nṛsiṃha rūpa dhārin om klaṃ ślas ca svara ādikaḥ ṣṭāṅga vinyāsa vinya sta mūrti dhārin tatas ca phaṭ tāraḥ varma trayam saṃkaram vaṃ cāmuka mastakam khaṇḍa dvayam khāda yeti dvayam klīṃ sādhyam ānaya ṣaṣ dīrgha āḍyām sva bījam ca kṣapita ante tu kalmaṣa uttarāyam dvayam pañcabāṇa bījāni vā uñcaret nṛsiṃha ante tatas jvālā ātmane svāhā samīrayet nṛsiṃha ante tatas kāla ātmane svāhā dhruvaḥ tatas khabījam kāmabījam ca lakṣmībīja dvayam tatas māyā tāra antimaḥ mantraḥ sahasra akṣara saṃmitaḥ śrī lakṣmīḥ nṛhariḥ bījam kṣaiṃ śaktiḥ vahnivallabhā śvetaḥ varṇaḥ udāttaḥ ca svaraḥ proktaḥ manīṣibhiḥ nṛsiṃha antam vahnijāyā astra āya phaṭū mantraḥ īritaḥ anena kara śuddhim ca kṛtvā aṅgāni samācaret tāraḥ kṣāṃ ca sahasra ante kṣara śabdāt vijṛṃbhitam nṛsiṃhāya agnijāya antaḥ hṛdaye manuḥ īritaḥ māraḥ kṣīṃ ca mahātenum prabhā ante vikara iti ca nṛsiṃhāya agnijāyā ante śiraḥ mantraḥ prakīrtitaḥ tāraḥ kṣūm īrayet tāraḥ kṣaiṃ ca suvarṇam te mada matta padam tatas vihvalita nṛsiṃhāya svāhā antam kavacam smṛtam tāraḥ ṛkṣau ca sahasrākṣa viśvasrākṣa viśvarūpa padam vadet dhāraṇa igni priya antaḥ ayam netramantraḥ prakīrtitaḥ tāraḥ kṣaḥ ca sahasra ante vārāvepadam īrayet sahasra ante yudhāya atham nṛsiṃhāya agni suṃdarī udyat arka sahasra ābham trīkṣaṇam bhīsa bhūṣaṇam su tīkṣṇa agra bhujaḥ daṇḍaiḥ daitya dāraṇakam smaret evam dhyātvā japet mantrī sahasram pāyena prāc ukte vaiṣṇave pīṭhe mūrtim saṃkalpya mūlataḥ saṃpūjya nṛharim paścāt ādau aṅgāni pūjayet cakra śaṅkham ca pāśam vā aṅkuśam kuliśam eva ca gadā kṛpāṇi kṣveḍāni daleṣu paripūjayet bhūta preta piśācāḥ ca naśyanti eva na saṃśayaḥ tīrtha toyena saṃpūrya japet aṣṭa uttaram śatam kim bahu uktena sarva iṣṭa dāyakaḥ ayam manu uttamaḥ vajra nakhāya vidmahe tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭrāya dhīmahi tat naḥ nṛsiṃhaḥ śabda ante vaden ca eva pracodayāt eṣā nṛsiṃha gāyatrī sarva abhīṣṭa pradāyinī etasyāḥ smaraṇāt eva sarva pāpa kṣayaḥ bhavet iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde nṛsiṃhopāsanāmantragāyatryādinirūpaṇam nāma ekasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ praṇavaḥ hṛdayam viṣṇuḥ na intaḥ surapatiḥ tathā mahābalāya svāhā antaḥ mantraḥ vasudhara akṣaraḥ tāraḥ bījam tathā śaktiḥ vahnijāyā prakīrtitā candra akṣi rāma bāṇeṃṣu netra saṃkhyaiḥ manu udbhavaiḥ varṇaiḥ ṣaḍaṅgam kṛtvā ca mūrdhni bhāle ca netrayoḥ karṇayoḥ ghrāṇayoḥ oṣṭa tālu kaṇṭha bhujeṣu ca pṛṣṭe hṛdi udare nābhau guhye ca ūru sthale punar muktā gauram ratna bhūṣam candra stham bhṛṅga sannibhaiḥ dadhi anna pūrṇa caṣakam dorbhyām saṃdadhanam bhajet lakṣa trayam japet mantram tad daśa aṃśam ghṛta plutaiḥ candra ante kalpite pīṭhe pūrva uktā īṃ pūjayet ca tam saṃkalpa mūrti mūlena saṃpūjya ca vidhānataḥ kesareṣu ṣaḍaṅgāni saṃpūjya diś daleṣu ca koṇa patreṣu śāntim ca śriyam sarasvatīm ratim śaṅkham cakram gadām śārṅgam daleṣu aṣṭasu pūjayet dala agreṣu keśava ādīn dikpālān tad anantaram tad astrāṇi ca sampūjya gajān aṣṭau samarcayet airāvataḥ puṇḍarīkaḥ vāmanaḥ kumudāeṃ'janaḥ puṣpadantaḥ sārvabhaumaḥ supratīkaḥ ca diggajāḥ kariṇyaḥ abhramu kapilaḥ piṅgala anupamāḥ kramāt tāmrakarṇī śubhradantī ca aṅganā hi añjanā vatī evam ārādhitaḥ mantrī dadyāt iṣṭāni mantriṇe śrī kāmaḥ pāyasa ājyena sahasram juhuyāt sudhīḥ mahatīm śriyam āpnoti dhānya āptiḥ dhānya homataḥ śatapuṣpā samutthaiḥ ca bījaiḥ hutvā sahasrataḥ mahā bhayam nāśayet hi na atra kāryā vicāraṇā dhyātvā traivikramam rūpam japet mantram samāhitaḥ anna ājyaiḥ juhuyāt nityam aṣṭāviṃśati saṃkhyayā alakṣmīm ca parābhūya mahatīm śriyam āpnuyāt mahā lakṣmīm sa labhate tatra tatra na saṃśayaḥ lakṣam japtvā tad daśa aṃśam putrajīva phalaiḥ hunet tad kāṣṭaiḥ edhite vahnau śreṣṭham putram avāpnuyāt sa sādhya tāram vilasat karṇikam ca suvarṇakaiḥ śeṣa yugma arṇa antya patram dvādaśa akṣara veṣṭitam tad bahis mātṛkā varṇaiḥ yantram sampad pradam nṛṇām raktam trivikramam dhyātvā prasūnaiḥ rakta varṇakaiḥ dhyāyet candra āsana gatam padmānām ayutam hunet labhet akaṇṭakam rājyam sarva lakṣaṇa saṃyutam ayutam sādhya nāma āḍhyam sa vaśyaḥ jāyate dhruvam aṣṭottaraśatam hutvā hi apāmārga dalaiḥ śubhaiḥ tāvat japtvā ca sapta ahāt mahā rogāt pramucyate śabdataḥ ayam mantraḥ tāra ādiḥ īritaḥ ṛṣiḥ brahmā asya nirdiṣṭaḥ chandaḥ anuṣṭubh udāhṛtam tāreṇa pādaiḥ mantrasya pañcāṅgāni prakalpayet tuṣāra adri sama chāyam tulasī dāma bhūṣitam dhyātvā evam prajapet mantram ayutam tad daśa aṃśataḥ pūjayet veṣṇave pīṭhe mūrtim saṃkalpya mūlataḥ karṇikāyām catur dikṣu yajet pūrva ādeḥ kramāt sanandanam ca sanakam śriyam ca pṛthivīm tathā tad vahis dikṣu vedāḥ ca ṣaṣ koṇeṣu tatas racayet niruktam jyotiṣam paścāt yajet vyākaraṇam tatas kalpam śikṣām ca chandāṃsi vedāṅgāni tu imāni vai tatas aṣṭadala mūle tu mātaraḥ aṣṭau samarcayet vakratuṇḍa ādikān aṣṭaḥ dala madhye prapūjayet dala agreṣu arcayet paścāt sādhakaḥ ca aṣṭa bhairavān asitāṅgam rurum ca eva bhīṣaṇam raktakanetrakam baṭukam kāladamanam danturam vikaṭam tathā tad bahis ṣoḍaśa daleṣu avatārān hareḥ daśa śaṅkham cakram gadām padmam nandakam śārṅgam eva ca tad bahis bhūgṛhe śakra mukhān daśa digīśvarān vajra ādyān tad bahis ca iṣṭvā a dvāreṣu ca tatas kramāt mahāgaṇapatim durgām kṣetreśam baṭukam tathā tad bāhye parvatān aṣṭau nakṣatrāṇi ca tad bahis evam pañcadaśa āvṛttyā saṃpūjya turagānanam bījena māsa mātram yaḥ pibet dhīmān jita indriyaḥ dugdham vacām tatas mantrī kaṇṭha mātra udake sthitaḥ sarva veda āgama ādīnām vyākhyātā jñānavān bhavet iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne sanatkumāra vibhāge tṛtīya pāde hayagrīvopāsanānirūpaṇam nāma dvisaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha rāmasya manavaḥ vakṣyante siddhi dāyākāḥ yeṣām ārādhanāt martyāḥ taranti bhava sāgaram sarveṣu mantra varyeṣu śreṣṭham vaiṣṇavam ucyate gāṇapatyeṣu saureṣu śākta śaiveṣu abhīṣṭa dam vaiṣṇaveṣu api mantreṣu rāma mantrāḥ phala adhikāḥ gāṇapatya ādi mantrebhyaḥ koṭi koṭi guṇa adhikāḥ viṣṇu śayyā sthitaḥ vahniḥ indu bhūṣita mastakaḥ rāmāya hṛdaya antaḥ ayam mahā ghaudha vināśanaḥ sarveṣu hi atiśreṣṭhaḥ ṣaṣ akṣaraḥ brahmahatyā sahasrāṇi jñāta ajñāta kṛtāni ca koṭi koṭi sahasrāṇi hi upapāpāni yāni vai mantrasya uñcāraṇāt sadyas layam yānti na saṃśayaḥ brahmā muniḥ syāt gāyatrī chandaḥ rāmaḥ ca devatā ādyam bījam ca hṛd śaktiḥ viniyogaḥ akhila āptaye ṣaṣ dīrgha bhājā bījena ṣaṣ aṅgāni samācaret pīṭhanyāsa ādikam kṛtvā dhyāyet hṛdi raghūttamam kāla aṃbhodhara kāntam ca vīrā sana samāsthitam jñāna mudrām dakṣa haste dadhatam jānuni itaram saroruha karām sītām vidyut ābhām ca pārśva gām paśyantīm rāma vakra abjam vividha ākalpa bhūṣitām dhyātvā evam prajapet varṇa lakṣam mantrī daśa aṃśataḥ pūjayet vaiṣṇave pīṭhe vimala ādi samanvite mūrtim mūlena saṃkalpya tasyām āvāhya sādhakaḥ sītām vāme samāsīnām tad mantreṇa prapūjayet ramā sītā padam dvi ṭha antaḥ jānakī manuḥ agreḥ śārṅgam ca sampūjya śarān pārśva dvayeḥ acayet keśareṣu ṣaṣ aṅgāni patreṣu etān samarcayet hanumantam ca sugrīvam bharatam sa bibhīṣaṇam lakṣmaṇa aṅgada śatrughnān jāṃbavantam kramāt punar dhṛta ātapatram hastābhyām lakṣmaṇam pṛṣṭatas tatas aṣṭa patre sṛṣṭim ca japantam vijayam tathā su rāṣṭram rāṣṭra pālam ca akopam dharma pālakam sumantam ca iti sampūjya loke śāna āyudhaiḥ yutān evam rāmam samārādhya jīvanmuktaḥ prajāyate candana aktaiḥ prajuhuyāt jātī puṣpaiḥ samāhitaḥ lakṣmī kāmaḥ prajuhuyāt prasūnaiḥ vilva saṃbhavaiḥ ghṛta akta śatavarvībhiḥ dīrgha āyuḥ ca nirāmayaḥ rakta utpalānām homena dhanam prāpnoti vāñchitam pālāśa kusumaiḥ hutvā medhāvī jāyate naraḥ tad japta aṃbhaḥ pibet prātar vatsarāt kavi rāj bhavet tad mantrita annam bhuñjīta mahā roga praśāntaye nadī tīre ca goṣṭhe vā japet lakṣam payaḥ brataḥ parikṣīṇa ādhipatyaḥ yaḥ śāka āhāraḥ jala antare japet lakṣam ca juhuyāt vilva puṣpaiḥ daśa aṃśataḥ tadā eva punar āpnoti svādhipatyam na saṃśayaḥ upoṣya gaṅgā tīra ante sthitvā lakṣam japet naraḥ daśa aṃśam kamalaiḥ hutvā vilva utthaiḥ vā prasūnakaiḥ mārga māse jale sthitvā kanda mūla phala aśanaḥ lakṣam japtvā daśa aṃśena pāyasaiḥ juhuyāt vasau śrī rāmacandra sadṛśaḥ putraḥ pautraḥ api jāyate ṣaṣ koṇam vasu patram ca tad bāhya arka dalam likhet ṣaṣ koṇeṣu ṣaṣ arṇāni mantrasya vilikhet budhaḥ aṣṭa patre tathā aṣṭa arṇān likhet praṇava garbhitān kāmabījam ravi dale madhye mantra āvṛta abhidhām sudarśana āvṛtam bāhye dikṣu yugma āvṛtam tathā vajra ullasat bhūmi geham kandarpa aṅkuśa pāśakaiḥ bhūmyā ca vilasat koṇam yantrarājam idam smṛtam bhūrje aṣṭa gandhaiḥ saṃlikhya pūjayet ukta vartmanā ṣaṣ koṇeṣu dala arka abjāni āveṣṭa vṛtta yugmataḥ bahis tu mātṛkām ca eva mantram vaśyā ākarṣaṇa vidveṣa drāvaṇa uccāṭana ādikam puṣya dvayam tathā āditya ārdrā maghāsu yathākramam dūrvā utthā lekhanī vaśye tathā ākṛṣṭau karañja jā nara asthi jā māraṇe tu staṃbhane rājavṛkṣa jā śānti puṣṭa ṣṭi āyuṣām siddhayai sarva āpad śamanāya ca khara carmaṇi vidveṣe dhvaje tūñcāṭanāya ca śatrūṇām jvara santāpa śoka māraṇa karmaṇi vaśyā ākṛṣṭau ca aṣṭagandhaiḥ sampūjya ca yathāvidhi citā aṅgāra ādinā ca eva tāḍana uccāṭana ādikam viṣa arka kṣīra yogena māraṇam bhavati dhruvam triloha veṣṭitam kṛtvā dhārayet sādhaka uttamaḥ bījam rāmāya ṭha dvandvam mantraḥ ayam rasa varṇakaḥ sudarśana mahā śabdāt cakrarāja īśvara iti ca duṣṭa antaka duṣṭa bhayānaka duṣṭa bhayaṅkaram trāsaya dvitayam varma astra agni jāyā antimaḥ manuḥ aṣṭaṣaṣṭi akṣaraḥ proktaḥ yantra saṃveṣṭane tu ayam tāraḥ hṛd bhagavān ṅeṃtaḥ ṅeṃtaḥ hi raghunandanaḥ bālāya ante tu rāmāya viṣṇave hṛdaya antimaḥ saptacatvāriṃśat arṇaḥ mālāmantraḥ ayam īritaḥ viśvāmitraḥ muniḥ ca asya gāyatrī chandaḥ īritam śrī rāmaḥ devatā bījam dhruvaḥ śaktiḥ ca ṭhadvayam ṣaṣ dīrgha svara yugma māyā bījena aṅgāni kalpayet dhyāna pūjā ādikam sarvam asya pūrva vat ācaret sva kāma satya vāc lakṣmī tāra āḍhyaḥ pañca varṇakaḥ ṣaṣ akṣaraḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ syāt caturvarga phala pradaḥ brahmā saṃmohanaḥ śaktiḥ dakṣiṇāmūrti saṃjñakaḥ agastyaḥ śrī śivaḥ proktāḥ te teṣām munayaḥ kramāt athavā kāma bīja ādeḥ viśvāmitraḥ muniḥ smṛtaḥ chandaḥ proktam ca gāyatrī śrī rāmaḥ devatā punar bīja śaktiḥ ādhama antyam mantra arṇaiḥ syāt ṣaṣ aṅgakam bījaiḥ ṣaṣ dīrgha yuktaiḥ vā mantra arṇān pūrvavat nyaset puṣpaka ākhya vimāna antar siṃhāsana paricchade vīrāsana samāsīnam jñāna mudrā upaśobhitam ratnākalpam vibhun dhyātvā varṇa lakṣam japet manum yat vā smāra ādi mantrāṇām jaya ābham ca harim smaret yejanam kāmya karmāṇi sarvam kuryāt ṣaṣ arṇa vat mantrau aṣṭa akṣarau hi etau tāra antyau ced nava akṣarau eteṣām yajanam sarvam kuryāt mantrī ṣaṣ arṇa vat jānakīvallabhaḥ ṅeṃtaḥ dviṭha antaḥ kavaca ādikaḥ daśa arṇaḥ ayam mahā mantraḥ viśiṣṭaḥ asya muniḥ svarāj chandaḥ ca devatā sītā patiḥ bījam tathā ādimam svāhā śaktiḥ ca kāmena kuryāt aṅgāni ṣaḍ kramāt śiraḥ lalāṭa bhrū madhya tālu kaṇṭheṣu hṛdi api nābhi aṅghri jānu pādeṣu daśa arṇān vinyaset manoḥ mandāra puṣpaiḥ ābaddha vitāne toraṇa anvite siṃhāsana samāsīna puṣpaka upari rāghavam sītā alaṅkṛta vāma aṅgam lakṣmaṇena upaśobhitam śyāmam prasanna vadanam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam evam dhyātvā japet mantrī varṇa lakṣam samāhitaḥ daśa aṃśaḥ kamalaiḥ hemaḥ yajanam ca ṣaṣ arṇa vat rāmaḥ ṅeṃ ntaḥ dhanuṣpāṇiḥ ṅaitoṃ 'te vahnisuṃdarī daśa akṣaraḥ ayam mantraḥ asya muniḥ brahmā virāj punar ādyam bījam dviṭhaḥ śakti bīñjena aṅgāni kalpayet varṇa nyāsam tathā dhyānam puraścaryā arcana ādi kaman daśa akṣara ukta vat kuryāt cāpa bāṇa dharam smaret ṅeṃtau arka akṣarau mantrau ṛṣi dhyāna ādi pūrvavat śrī pūrvam jaya pūrvam ca tat dvidhā rāma nāma ca trayodaśa akṣaraḥ mantraḥ muniḥ brahmā virāj smṛtam chandaḥ tu devatā proktaḥ rāmaḥ pāpa ogha nāśanaḥ ṣaḍ aṅgāni prakurvīta dvis āvṛttyā pada trayaiḥ dhyāna arcana ādikam hi asya kuryāt daśārṇa vat puruṣāya hṛd antaḥ ayam manuḥ aṣṭādaśa akṣaraḥ viśvāmitraḥ muniḥ chadaḥ dhṛtiḥ rāmaḥ asya devatā tāraḥ bījam namaḥ śaktiḥ candra akṣi abdhi agni ṣaṣ bhujaiḥ varṇaiḥ mantra utthitaiḥ kuryāt ṣaṣ aṅgāni samāhitaḥ niḥśāṇa bherī paṭaha śaṅkha turya ādi niḥsvanaiḥ candana agaru kastūrī karpūra ādi su vāsite siṃhāsane samāsīnam puṣpaka upari rāghavam saumitri sītā sahitam jaṭā mukuṭa śobhitam cāpa bāṇa dharam śyāmam sa sugrīva vibhīṣaṇam hatvā rāvaṇam āyāntam kṛta trailokya rakṣaṇam evam dhyātvā japet varṇam lakṣam matrī daśa aṃśataḥ ghṛta aktaiḥ pāyasaiḥ hutvā yajanam pūrvavat caret rāmāya hana yugma ante varma astra agni priya antimaḥ ekonaviṃśat varṇaḥ ayam mantraḥ sarva artha sādhakaḥ viśvāmitraḥ muniḥ ca asya anuṣṭubh chandaḥ udāhṛtam devatā rāmabhadraḥ jam bījam śaktiḥ namaḥ iti pūjanam kāmya karma ādi sarvam asya ṣaṣ arṇa vat tāraḥ sva bījam kamalā rāmabhadrā iti saṃpaṭhet daśa asya antaka śabda ante mām rakṣa dehi saṃpaṭhet parama ante me śriyam syāt mantraḥ bāṇa guṇa akṣaraḥ bījaiḥ viyuktaḥ dvātriṃśat arṇaḥ ayam phala dāyakaḥ viśvāmitraḥ muniḥ ca asya anuṣṭubh chandaḥ udāhṛtam devatā rāmabhadraḥ atra bījam svam śaktiḥ indirā pañcāṅgāni ca vinyasya mantra varṇān kramāt nyaset mūrdhni bhāle dṛśoḥ śrotre gaṇḍa yugme sa nāsike āsye dos saṃdhi yugale stana hṛd nābhiṣu kramāt kaṭau meḍhre pāyu pāda saṃdhiṣu arṇān nyaset manoḥ dhyāna arcana ādikam ca asya pūrvavat samupācaret lakṣa trayam puraścaryām pāyasaiḥ havanam matam dhyātvā rāmam pīta varṇam japet lakṣam samāhitaḥ tāraḥ māyā ramā dvandvam dāśarathāya vai ekādaśa akṣaraḥ mantraḥ muni ādi arcā asya pūrvavat trailokya ante tu nāthāya hṛd antaḥ vasu varṇavān asya api pūrvavat sarvam nyāsa dhyāna arcana ādikam āñjaneya pada ante tu gurave hṛdaya antimaḥ ṅetam rāmapada paścāt hṛdayam pañca vaṇa vat muni dhyāna arcanam ca asya proktam sarvam ṣaṣ arṇa vat vahniḥ śeṣa anvitaḥ ca eva candra bhūṣita mastakaḥ brahmā muniḥ syāt gāyatrī chandaḥ rāmaḥ asya devatā ṣaṣ dīrgha āḍhyena mantreṇa ṣaṣ aṅgāni samācaret sarayū tīra mandāra vedikā paṅkaja āsane śyāmam vīrāsana āsīnam jñāna mudrā upaśobhitam vāma ūru nyastam tad hastam sītā lakṣmaṇa saṃyutam avekṣaṇāṇam ātmānam manmatha amita tejasam śuddha sphaṭika saṃkāśam kevalam mokṣa kāṅkṣayā sarvvam ṣaṣ arṇavam ca asya homa nitya arcana ādikam vahniḥ śeṣa āsanaḥ bha antaḥ kevalaḥ dvi akṣaraḥ manuḥ ekākṣara ukta vat sarvam muni dhyāna arcana ādikam tāra mānāra mānaṅga ca astra bījaiḥ dvi varṇakaḥ tri akṣaraḥ mantrarājaḥ syāt ṣaḍvidhaḥ sakala iṣṭa daḥ ekārṇa ukta vat eteṣām muni dhyāna arcana ādikam aṣṭa arṇaḥ ayam mahā mantraḥ muni ādi arcā ṣaṣ arṇa vat tāraḥ mayā hṛd ante syāt rāmāya praṇava antimaḥ śiva umā ārāma mantraḥ ayam aṣṭa arṇaḥ sarva siddhi daḥ ṛṣiḥ sadāśivaḥ proktaḥ gāyatrī chandaḥ īritam śiva umā ārāma candraḥ atra devatā parikīrtitaḥ ṣaṣ vīryayā amāya yātu dhruva pañca arṇa yuktayā ṣaḍaṅgāni vidhāya atha dhyāyet hṛdi sura arcitam rāmam trinetram soma arddha dhāriṇam śūlinam varam rāma abhirāmam saindarya sīmām soma avataṃsinīm pāśa aṅkuśa dhanuḥ bāṇa dharām dhyāyet rilocanām evam dhyātvā japet varṇa lakṣam trimadhura anvitaiḥ tāraḥ māyā ca bharata agraja rāma manobhavaḥ vahnijāyā dvādaśa arṇaḥ mantraḥ kalpadrumaḥ aparaḥ aṅgirāḥ ca muniḥ chandaḥ gāyatrī devatā punar śrī rāmaḥ bhuvanā bījam svāhā śaktiḥ samīritaḥ dhyāna pūjā ādikam ca āḥ ca sarvam kuryāt ṣaṣ arṇa vat praṇavaḥ hṛdayam sītā pate rāmaḥ ca ṅeṃtimaḥ hana dvaya ante varma astram mantraḥ ṣoḍaśa varṇavān śrī rāmaḥ aham tathā bījam rām śaktiḥ samudīritā rāma abdhi vahni veda akṣi varṇaiḥ pañcāṅga kalpanā dhyāna pūjā ādikam sarvam asya kuryāt ṣaṣ arṇa vat tāraḥ brahmaṇya sevyāya padam īrayet rāmāya ākuṇṭha śabda antam tejase ca samīrayet uttamaśloka dhuryāya svam bhṛguḥ kāmika anvitaḥ daṇḍa arpitām priye mantraḥ rāma rāma akṣaraḥ mataḥ ṛṣiḥ śukraḥ tathā anuṣṭubh chandaḥ rāmaḥ asya devatā pādaiḥ sarveṇa pañcāṅgam kuryāt śeṣam ṣaṣ arṇa vat lakṣam japaḥ daśa aṃśena juhuyāt pāyasaiḥ sudhīḥ tatas sītā vallabhāya dhīmahi iti samuccaret eṣā ukta arā ma gāyatrī sarva abhīṣṭa phala pradā padmāsītā padam ṅetam ṭha dvaya antaḥ ṣaṣ akṣaraḥ vālmīkiḥ ca muniḥ chandaḥ gāyatrī devatā punar sītā bhagavatī proktā śrīṃ bījam vahnisundarī śaktiḥ ṣaṣ dīrgha yuktena bījena aṅgāni kalpayet tatas dhyāyan mahādevīm sītām trailokya pūjitām tapta hāṭaka varṇa ābhām padma yugmam kara dvaye sat ratna bhūṣaṇa sphūrjat divya dehām śubha ātmikām nānā vastrām śaśi mukhīm padma akṣīm mudita antarām paśyantīm rāghavam puṇyam śayyā ardhyām ṣaḍguṇa īśvarīm evam dhyātvā japet varṇa lakṣam mantrī daśa aṃśataḥ mūrtim saṃkalpya mūlena tasyām āvāhya jānakīm saṃpūjya dakṣiṇe rāmam abhyarcya agre anilātmajam pṛṣaṭe lakṣmaṇam abhyarcya ṣaṭkoṇeṣu aṅga pūjanam patreṣu mantri mukhyan ca bāhye loka īśvarān punar jātī puṣpaiḥ candana aktaiḥ rāja vaśyāya homayet bilva patraiḥ śriyaḥ prāptyai dūrvā bhīroḥ āśāntaye kim saubhāgyam putrān pautrān param sukham dhanam dhānyam ca mokṣam ca sītā ārādhanataḥ labhet śakra ṛ sa induḥ lakṣmaṇāya hṛdayam sapta varṇavān lakṣmaṇa ākhyaḥ mahā vīraḥ ca āḍhyam hṛd vīja śaktike ṣaṣ dīrgha āḍhyena bījena ṣaṣ aṅgāni samācaret dhanuḥ bāṇa karam rāma sevā saṃsakta mānasam dhyātvā evam prajapet varṇa lakṣam mantrī daśa aṃśataḥ madhu āktaiḥ pāyasaiḥ hutvā rāma pīṭhe prapūjayeta sākalyam rāma pūjāyāḥ yadi icchet niyatam naraḥ śrī rāmacandra bhedāḥ tu bahavaḥ saṃti siddhi dāḥ tad sādhakaiḥ sadā kāryam lakṣmaṇa ārādhanam śubham aṣṭottarasahasram vā śatam vā su samāhitaiḥ a japtvā lakṣmaṇa manum rāma mantrān japanti ye mucyate sarva pāpebhyaḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt naṣṭa rājya āptaye mantram japet lakṣam samāhitaḥ saḥ acirāt naṣṭa rājyam svam prāpnoti eva na saṃśayaḥ dhyāyan rāmam ayodhyāyām abhiṣikta mananya dhīḥ pañca ayutam manum japtvā naṣṭa rājyam avāpnuyāt nāgapāśa vinirmuktam dhyātvā lakṣmaṇam ādarāt vātātmajena ānītābhiḥ oṣadhībhiḥ gata vyatham ghātayantam meghanādam dhyātvā lakṣam japet manum dhyātvā śūrpaṇakhā nāsā chedana udyukta mānasam rāma pāda abja sevā artham kṛta udyogam atho smaran aṣṭottaraśataiḥ puṣpaiḥ niśchedraiḥ śātapatrakaiḥ pūjayitvā vidhānena pāyasam ca sa śarkaram vijane vijita āhāraḥ ṣaṣ māsam vidhinā amunā kṣaya rogāt pramucyeta satyam satyam na saṃśayaḥ dāridrayam ca parābhūtam jāyate dhanada upamaḥ viṣa ādi doṣa saṃsparśaḥ na bhavet tu kadācana mukha netra ādi saṃbhūtān jayet dvrogān ca dāruṇān lakṣmaṇa pratimām kṛtvā dadyāt bhaktyā vidhānataḥ kanyā arthī vimalā pāṇigrahaṇa āsakta mānasaḥ dhyāyan lakṣam japet mantrī abjaiḥ hutvā daśa aṃśataḥ īpsitām labhate kanyām śīgram eva na saṃśayaḥ dīkṣitam juṃbhaṇa astrāṇām mantreṣu niyata vratam pūjā puraḥsaram sapta sahasram vijita indriyaḥ sarvāsām api vidyānām tattva jñaḥ jāyate naraḥ sarva pāpa vinirmuktaḥ yāti viṣṇoḥ param padam sa sarvān puṇya pāpa odhān dagdhvā nirmala mānasaḥ punarāvṛtti rahitaḥ śāśvatam padam aśvatam padam aśnute sa kāmaḥ vāñchitān labdhvā bhuktvā bhogān manaḥ gatān jātiḥ amaraḥ ciram bhūtvā yāti viṣṇoḥ param padam nidrā candra anvitā paścāt bharatāya hṛd antimaḥ sapta akṣaraḥ manuḥ ca asya muni ādi arcā ādi pūrvavat bakaḥ sa iṃduḥ ca ṅetam hṛd antimaḥ sapta akṣaraḥ ayam śatrudhna mantraḥ sarva iṣṭa siddhi daḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge buhat upākhyāne sanatkumāra vibhāge tṛtīya pāde rāmādyupāsanāvarṇanam nāma trisaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha ucyante hanumataḥ mantrāḥ sarva iṣṭa dāyakāḥ yān samārādhya vipra indra tad tulya ācaraṇāḥ narāḥ manuḥ gaganam ca bhaga anvitāḥ hasa pha agni niśā adhīśāḥ dvitīyam bījam īritam sva pha agnayaḥ bhaga indu āḍhyāḥ tṛtīyam bījam īritam pañcamam bhaga candra āḍhyā viyat bhṛgu svaka agnayaḥ manu indu āḍhyau hasau ṣaṣṭam ṅeṃtaḥ syāt hanumant tatas hṛdaya antaḥ mahā mantrarājaḥ ayam dvādaśa akṣaraḥ devatā hanumān bījam ṣaṣṭam śaktiḥ dvatīyakam ṣaṣ bījaiḥ ca ṣaṣ aṅgāni śiraḥ bhāle dṛśoḥ mukhe ṣaḍbījāni pada dvandvam mūrdhni bhāle mukhe hṛdi nābhau ūrvoḥ jaṅghayoḥ ca pādayoḥ vinyaset kramāt añjanī garbha saṃbhūtam tatas dhyāyet kapi īśvaram udyat koṭi arka saṃkāśam jagat prakṣobha kārakam śrī rāma aṅghri dhyāna niṣṭam sugrīva pramukha arcitam vitrāsayantam nādena rākṣasān mārutim bhajet daśa aṃśam juhuyāt bīhīn payaḥ dadhi ājya miśritān pūrva ukte vaiṣṇave pīṭhe mūrttim saṃkalpya mūlataḥ āvāhya tatra saṃpūjya pādya ādibhiḥ upāyanaiḥ keśareṣu aṅga pūjā syāt patreṣu ca tatas racayet rāma bhaktaḥ mahā tejāḥ kapi rājaḥ mahā balaḥ dakṣiṇa āśā bhāskaraḥ ca sarva vighna vināśakaḥ ittham sampūjya nāmāni dala agreṣu tatas ṛcayet sugrīvam aṅgada nīlam jāṃbavantam nalam tathā mantram nava śatam rātrau japet daśa dina avadhi dvāviṃśati brahmacāri viprān saṃbhojayet śucīn evaṅkṛte bhūta viṣa graha roga ādi upadravāḥ naśyanti tad kṣaṇāt eva vidveṣi graha dānavāḥ aṣṭottaraśatena aṃbu mantritam viṣa nāśanam bhasmabhiḥ salilaiḥ vā api tāḍayet jvariṇam krudhā sarvān rogān parābhūya sukhī bhavati tad kṣaṇāt śaskṣatam vraṇa sphoṭaḥ lūtā sphoṭaḥ api bhasmanā tris japtena ca saṃspṛṣṭāḥ śuṣyanti eva na saṃśayaḥ mantram sapta dinam yāvat ca ādāya bhasma kīlakau nikhanet abhimantrya āśu śatrūṇām dvāri a lakṣitaḥ vidveṣam mithas āpannāḥ palāyante arayaḥ acirāt gṛhītvā īśanadi skaṃstham karañja taru mūlakam kṛtvā tena aṅguṣṭa mātrām pratimām ca hanūmataḥ kṛtvā prāṇa pratiṣṭām ca siṃdūra ādyaiḥ prapūjya ca graha abhicāra roga agni viṣa caura nṛpa udbhavāḥ śatroḥ pratikṛtim kṛtvā hṛdi nāma samālikhet kṛtvā prāṇa pratiṣṭā antam bhindyāt śastraiḥ manum japan māraya iti ca tasya ante dantaiḥ oṣṭam nipūḍya ca pāṇyoḥ tale prapīḍya atha tyaktvā tam sva gṛham vrajet kurvan sapta dinam ca evam hanyāt śatrum na saṃśayaḥ rājikā lavaṇaiḥ mukta cikuraḥ pitṛ kānane dvika kāka kauśika gṛdhrāṇām pakṣaiḥ śleṣmāntaka akṣa jaiḥ vitrāsaḥ tri dinam rātrau śmaśāne ṣaṭśatam japet tatas vetālaḥ utthāya vadet bhāvi śubha aśubham bhāsma aṃbu mantritam rātrau sahasra āvṛttikam punar yāsu kāsu ca sthūlāsu laghuṣu api viśeṣataḥ mantra prabhāvāt calanam bhavati eva na saṃśayaḥ aṣṭamyām vā caturdaśyām kuje vā ravivāsare hanumat pratimām paṭṭe māṣaiḥ sneha pariplutaiḥ kuryāt ramyām viśuddha ātmā sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣitām taila dīpam vāma bhāge ghṛta dīpam tu dakṣiṇe saṃsthāpya āvāhayet paścāt mūlamantreṇa mantra vid prāṇapratiṣṭām kṛtvā ca pādya ādīni samarpayet dhūpam dīpam pradāya atha naivedyam ca samarpayet apūpam odanam śāka modakān vaṭaka ādikam akhaṇḍitāni ahi latā dalāni saptaviṃśatim tridhā kṛtvā sa pūgāni mūlena eva samarpayet evam saṃpūjya mantra jñaḥ japet daśaśanta manum karpūra ārārtikam kṛtvā stutvā ca bahudhā sudhīḥ naivedya annena saṃbhojya brāhmaṇān sapta saṃkhyayā dakṣiṇām ca yathāśakti dattvā tān visṛjet sudhīḥ tatas iṣṭa gaṇaiḥ sārddham svayam bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ prāpnuyāt sakalān kāmān kapi īśasya prasādataḥ tat pūrvam mārjayet vāma pāṇinā atha punar likhet evam aṣṭottaraśatam likhitvā mārjayet punar evam kṛte mahā kārā gṛhāt śīghram vimucyate kuṅkumaiḥ idhma kāṣṭhaiḥ vā marīcaiḥ jīrakaiḥ api jvare dūrvā guḍūcībhiḥ dadhnā kṣīreṇa vā ghṛtaiḥ śūle karañja vātāri samidbhiḥ taila lolitaiḥ taila aktābhiḥ ca nirguṇḍī samidbhiḥ vā prayatnataḥ ripu pāda rajobhiḥ ca rājī lavaṇa miśritaiḥ tila ājya kṣīra madhubhiḥ mahiṣī go samṛddhaye kim bahu uktaiḥ viṣe vyādhau śāntau mohe ca māraṇe vivāde staṃbhane dyūte bhūta bhītau ca saṃkaṭe sādhitaḥ ayam nṛṇām dadyāt mantraḥ śreyaḥ su niścitam lāṅgūla ākāra saṃyuktam valaya tritayam likhet sādhya nāma likhet madhye pāśi bīja praveṣṭitam upari aṣṭacchadam kṛtvā patreṣu kavacam likhet saiṃ bījam bhūpurasya aṣṭa vajreṣu vilikhet tatas koṇeṣu a kuṃśam ālikhya mālāmantreṇa veṣṭayet śilāyām phalake vastre tāmra patre atha kuḍyake tāḍa patre atha bhūrje vā rocanā nābhi kuṅkubhaiḥ kapeḥ prāṇān pratiṣṭāpya pūjayet tat yathāvidhi aśeṣa duḥkha śānti arthaḥ yantram saṃdhārayet budhaḥ mārī jvara abhicāra ādi sarva upadrava nāśanam yoṣitām api bālānām dhṛtam jana manoharam bhūta kṛtyā piśācānām darśanāt eva nāśanam mālāmantram atho vakṣye tāraḥ vāc viṣṇugehinī dīrgha traya anvitā māyā prāc uktam kūṭa pañcakam dhruvaḥ hṛd hanumān ṅeṃtaḥ atha prakaṭa parākramaḥ ākrānta diś maṇḍala ante yaśaḥ vitāna saṃvadet laṅkā purī tatas paścāt dahana udadhi laṅghana daśagrīva śiraḥ paścātkṛta antaka padam vadet sītā ante śvasana padam vāyu ante sutam īrayet añjanā garbha saṃbhūtaḥ śrī rāma lakṣmaṇa anvitaḥ sugrīva sakhyaka ādūrṇa ādraṇa vāli nivarhaṇa kāraṇa droṇa śabda ante parvata utpāṭana iti ca aśoka vana vīthi ante dāruṇa akṣa kumāraka lakṣmaṇa ante śakti bheda nivāraṇa padam vadet viśalya oṣadhi śabda ante samānayana saṃpaṭhet indrajit ū dhakāra ante ṇa sī tāsa kṣaka iti ca rākṣasī saṃgha śabda ante vidāraṇa padam vadet kuṃbhakarṇa ādi saṃkīrtya vadha ante ca parāyaṇa mahā tejaḥ puñja śabdāt virājamāna voñcaret svāmi vacana saṃpādita arjuna ante ca saṃyuga gaṃbhīra śabda udaya ante dakṣiṇāpatha saṃvadet mārttāṇḍa meru śabda ante vadet parvata pīṭikā ācārya mama śabda ante sarva graha vināśana sarva jvara uñcāṭana ante sarva viṣa vināśana sarva āpatti nivāraṇa sarva duṣṭa nibarhaṇa mama ājñā kārakam paścāt saṃpādaya yugam punar tatas nānā nāmadheyān sarvān rājñaḥ sa saṃpaṭhet sarva śastra vīti ante ṣa aṇi vidhvaṃsaya dvayam vilomam pañca kūṭāni sarva śatrūn hana dvayam mama sarvam kārya jātam sādhaya iti dvayam tatas dhe trayam varma tritayam phaṭ trayam hān trayam tatas vahni priya antaḥ mantraḥ ayam mālā saṃjñaḥ akhila iṣṭa daḥ vasu aṣṭa bāṇa varṇaḥ ayam mantraḥ sarva iṣṭā sādhakaḥ mahā bhaye mahā utpāte smṛtaḥ ayam duḥkha nāśanaḥ dvādaśa arṇasya ṣaṣ kūṭam tyaktvā bījam tathā ādimam pañcakūṭa ātmakaḥ mantraḥ sarva kāma pradāyakaḥ rāmacandraḥ muniḥ ca asya gāyatrī chandaḥ īritam pañca bījaiḥ samastena ṣaḍaṅgāni samācaret rāma dūtaḥ lakṣmaṇa ante prāṇa dātā añjanī sutaḥ sītā śoka vināśaḥ ayam laṅkā prāsāda bhañjanaḥ hanumat ādyāḥ pañca ete bīja ādyāḥ ṅeyutāḥ punar ṣaḍaṅga manavaḥ hi ete dhyāna pūjā ādi pūrvavat praṇavaḥ vāc bhavam padmā māyā dīrgha traya anvitā pañcakūṭāni mantraḥ ayam rudra arṇaḥ sarva siddhi daḥ dhyāna pūjā ādikam sarvam asya api pūrvavat matam ayam ārādhitaḥ mantraḥ sarva abhīṣṭa pradāyakaḥ namaḥ bhagavate paścāt anantaḥ candraśekharām aṣṭādaśa arṇaḥ mantraḥ ayam su nirīśvara saṃjñakaḥ chandaḥ anuṣṭubh devatā tu hanumān pavanātmajaḥ haṃ bījam vahnivanitā śaktiḥ proktā manīṣibhiḥ āñjaneyāya hṛdayam śiraḥ ca rudra mūrtaye śikhāyām vāyuputrāya agnigarbhāya varmaṇi rāma dūtāya netram syāt bahyāstrāya astram īritam tat paca āmīkara nibham bhī ghna saṃvihita añjalim calat kuṇḍala dīpta āsyam padma akṣam mārutim smaret dhyātvā evam ayutam japtvā daśa aṃśam juhuyāt tilaiḥ vaiṣṇave pūjayet pīṭhe prāc uddiṣṭena vartmanā aṣṭottaraśatam nityam nakta bhojī jita indriyaḥ rākṣasa ogham vinighnantam kapim dhyātvā adhana aśanam sugrīveṇa samam rāmam saṃdadhānam kapim smaran dhyātvā laṅkām tam ayutam prajapet manum acirāt eva śatrūṇām grāmān saṃpradahet sudhīḥ yaḥ yāti saḥ acirāt sva iṣṭam sādhayitvā gṛhe vrajet ārogyam ca śriyam kāntim labhate nirupadravam prasvāpa kāle śayyāyām smaret mantram an anya dhīḥ varma astra antaḥ mahā mantraḥ dvādaśa arṇaḥ aṣṭa siddhi kṛt hanumān devatām bījam ādyam śaktiḥ hum īritā ṣaṣ dīrgha bhājā bījena ṣaṣ aṅgāni samācaret mahā śailam samutpāṭya dhāvantam rāvaṇam prati lākṣā rakta aruṇam raudram kāla antaka yama upamam aṅgada ādyaiḥ mahāvīraiḥ veṣṭitam rudra rūpiṇam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha raṇe duṣṭa sṛjantam ghora niḥ svanam daśa aṃśam juhuyāt vīhīn payaḥ dadhi ājya miśritān pūrva ukte vaiṣṇave pīṭhe vimala ādi samanvite mūrtim saṃkalpya mūlena pūjā kāryā hanūmataḥ dhyāna eka mātraḥ api nṛṇām siddhiḥ eva na saṃśayaḥ atha asya sādhanam vakṣye lokānām hita kāmyayā hanumat sādhanam puṇyam mahāpātaka nāśanam prātar snātvā nadī tīre upaviśya kuśa āsane prāṇāyāma ṣaḍaṅge ca mūlena sakalam caret puṣpa añjali aṣṭakam da tvā dhyātvā rāmam sa sītakam tāmra pātre tatas padmam aṣṭa patram sa keśaram kucandanena ghṛṣṭena saṃlikhet tat śalākayā karmikāyām likhet mantram tatra āvāhya kapi īśvaram mūrtim mūlena saṃkalpya dhyātvā pādya ādikam caret kesareṣu ṣaṣ aṅgāni daleṣu ca tatas ṛcayet sugrīvam lakṣmaṇam ca eva hi aṅgadam nala nīlakau jāṃbavantam ca kumudam kesarīśam dikpālān ca api vajra ādīn pūjayet tad anantaram sādhayet sādhaka śreṣṭhaḥ bhūmi grahaṇa pūrvakam jita āhāraḥ jita śvāsaḥ jita vāc ca jita indriyaḥ digbandha na ādikam kṛtvā nyāsa dhyāna ādi pūrvakam lakṣam japet mantrarājam pūjayitvā tu pūrvavat lakṣa anti divasam prāpya kuryyāt ca pūjanam mahat divārātrau japam kuryāt yāvat saṃdarśanam bhavet su dṛḍham sādhakam matvā niśīthe pavanātmajaḥ yathā īpsitam varam da tvā sādhakāya kapi īśvaraḥ etat hi sādhanam puṇyam lokānām hita kāmyayā prakāśitam rahasyam vai devānām api durlabham anyān apiprayogān ca sādhayet ātmanaḥ hitān viyat indu yutam paścāt ṅeṃtam pavana nandanam vahnipriya antaḥ mantraḥ ayam daśa arṇaḥ sarva kāma daḥ muni ādikam ca pūrva uktam ṣaṣ aṅgāni api pūrvavat dhāvantam rāvaṇam jetum dṛṣṭvā sa tvaram utthitam lakṣmaṇam ca mahā vīram patitam raṇa bhū tale hāhākāraiḥ sa darpaiḥ ca kaṃpayantam jagattrayam ā brahmāṇḍam samākhyāpya kṛtvā bhīmam kalevaram lakṣam japet daśa aṃśena juhuyāt pūrvavat sudhīḥ pūrvavat pūjanam proktam vidhānataḥ brāhme muhūrte ca utthāya kṛta nityakriyaḥ śuciḥ gatvā nadīm snātvā tīrtham āvāhya ca aṣṭadhā mūlamantram tatas japtvā siṃcet āditya saṃkhyayā evam snāna ādikam kṛtvā gaṅgā tīre athavā punar ādya varṇaiḥ pūrakam syāt pañcavargaiḥ ca kumbhakam recakam ca punar yāt yaiḥ evam prāṇān niyanya ca vidhāya bhūtaśuddhi ādi pīṭhanyāsa avadhi punar dhyātvā pūrva ukta vidhinā saṃpūjya ca kapi īśvaram ekāgra manasā mantrī divārātram japet manum mahā bhayam prada tvā tri bhāga śeṣāsu niścitam yāminīṣu samāyāti niyatam pavanātmajaḥ yathā īpsitam varam dadyāt sādhakāya kapi īśvaraḥ vidyām vā api dhanam vā api rājyam vā śatru nigraham tad kṣaṇāt eva ca āpnoti satyam satyam na saṃśayaḥ phala ante pha kriyā netra yuktā ca kāmikā tatas lohitaḥ garuḍaḥ heti bāṇa netra akṣaraḥ manuḥ muni ādikam tu pūrva uktam plīha roga haraḥ hariḥ devatā ca samuddiṣṭā plīha yuktā udare punar nāgavallī dalam sthāpyam upari ācchādayet tatas vastram ca eva aṣṭa guṇitam tatas sādhaka sattamaḥ śakalam vaṃśa jam tasya upari muñcet kapim smaret āraṇya sāṇaka utpanne vahnau yaṣṭim pratāpayet badarī bhūruha utthām tām mantreṇa anena saptadhā tayā saṃtāḍayet vaṃśa śakalam jaṭhara sthitam sapta kṛtvas plīha rogaḥ nāśam āyāti niścitam amukasya śṛṅkhalām troṭaya dvitayam īrayet bandha mokṣam kuru yugam svāhā antaḥ ayam manuḥ mataḥ īśvaraḥ asya muniḥ chandaḥ anuṣṭubh ca devatā punar śṛṅkhalā mocaraḥ śrīmān hanūmān pavanātmajaḥ haṃ bījam ṭha dvayam śaktiḥ bandha mokṣe niyoga tā ṣaṣ dīrgha vahri yuktena bījena aṅgāni kalpayet vāme śailam vairi bhidam viśuddham ṭaṅkam anyatas dadhānam svarṇa varṇam ca dhyāyet kuṇḍalinam harim evam dhyātvā japet lakṣa daśa aṃśam cūta pallavaiḥ juhuyāt pūrvavat proktam yajanam vā asya sūribhiḥ mahākārā gṛhe prāptaḥ hi ayutam prajapet naraḥ śīghram kārā gṛhāt muktaḥ sukhī bhavati niścitam yantram ca asya pravakṣyāmi bandha mokṣa karam śubham aṣṭacchada antar ṣaṣ koṇam sādhya nāma samanvitam ṣaṣ koṇeṣu dhruvam ṅeṃtam āñjaneya padam likhet aṣṭa chadeṣu vilikhet praṇavaḥ vātu vātu iti dakṣa hastena mantra jñaḥ pratyaham maṇḍalāḥ vadhi evam kṛte mahā kārā gṛhāt mantrī vimucyate gaganam jvalanaḥ sākṣī markaṭa iti dvayam tatas toyam śaśeṣe makare parimuñcati muñcati tatas śṛṅkhalikām ca iti veda netra akṣaraḥ manuḥ imam mantram dakṣa kare likhitvā vāma hastataḥ dūrikṛtya japet mantram aṣṭottaraśatam budhaḥ lakṣam japaḥ daśa aṃśena śubhaiḥ dravyaiḥ ca homayet tad madhye aṣṭadaśa arṇam tu śatru nāma anvitam likhet jayati ari gaṇam sarvam darśanāt eva niścitam dhvajam ādāya mantra jñaḥ saṃsparśāt mokṣaṇa avadhi mātṛkām jāpayet paścāt daśa aṃśena ca homayet tilaiḥ sarṣapa saṃmiśraiḥ saṃskṛte havyavāhane gaja stham tam dhvajam dṛṣṭvā palāyante arayaḥ dhruvam mahā rakṣā karam yantram vakṣye samyak hanūmataḥ dale aṣṭa koṇam ālikhya mālāmantreṇa veṣṭayet tad bahis māyayā āveṣṭya prāṇa sthāpanam ācaret kāśmīra rocanābhyām tu trilohena ca veṣṭitam sampāta sādhitam yantram bhuje vā mūrdhni dhārayet sarvān ro gān apākṛtya ciram jīvet śatam samāḥ ṣaṣ dīrgha yuktam gagana vahni ākhyam tāra saṃpuṭam aṣṭa arṇaḥ ayam mahā mantraḥ mālāmantraḥ atha kathyate praṇavaḥ vajrakāya iti vajratuṇḍa iti saṃpaṭhet raudra daṃṣṭra utkaṭam paścāt ka ha dvandvam mahā dṛḍha prahāreṇa laṅkā īśvara vadhāt tatas vāyuḥ mahāsetu padam bandha ante ca mahā punar jaṃbhaya dvayam ābhāṣya varma astra antaḥ manuḥ mataḥ mālā āhvayaḥ dvijaśreṣṭha śara netra dhara akṣaraḥ mālā mantra aṣṭa arṇayoḥ ca muni ādi arcā tu pūrvavat japtaḥ yuddhe jayam dadyāt vyādhau vyādhi vināśanaḥ evam yaḥ bhajate mantrī vāyuputram kapi īśvaram dhanam dhānyam sutān pautrān saubhāgyam atulam yaśaḥ medhām vidyām prabhām rājyam vivāde vijayam tathā vaśyā ādyāni ca karmāṇi saṃgare vijayam tathā pradadāti alam iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne sanatkumāra vibhāge tṛtīya pāde hanumanmantrakathanam nāma catuḥsaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha dīpa vidhim vakṣye sa rahasyam hanūmataḥ yasya vijñāna mātreṇa siddhaḥ bhavati sādhakaḥ dīpa pātra pramāṇam ca taila mānam krameṇa tu sthāna bhedam ca mantram ca dīpa dāna manum pṛthak atasī tailam uddiṣṭam vaśyā karmaṇi niścitam sārṣāpam roga nāśāya kathitam karma kovidaiḥ māraṇe rājikā uttham vā vibhītaka samudbhavam uñcāṭane karaja uttham vidveṣe madhu vṛkṣa jam godhūmāḥ ca tilāḥ māṣāḥ mudgāḥ vai taṇḍulāḥ kramāt pañcadhānyam idam proktam nitya dīpam tu māruteḥ pañcadhānya samudbhūtam piṣṭa mātram su śobhanam sarva kāma pradam proktam sarvadā dīpa dānake vaśye taḍula piṣṭa uttham māraṇe māṣa piṣṭa jam uñcāṭane kṛṣṇa tila piṣṭa jam ca prakīrtitam saṃgrāme kevalāḥ māṣāḥ proktāḥ dīpasya pātrake saṃdhau tripiṣṭa jam lakṣmī hetoḥ kastūrikā bhavam alābhe sarva vastūnām pañcadhānyam varam smṛtam aṣṭa muṣṭiḥ bhavet kiñcid kiñcid aṣṭau caḥ puṣkalam puṣkalānām caturṇām ca hi āḍhakaḥ parikīrtitaḥ catur āḍhakaḥ bhavet droṇaḥ khārī droṇa catuṣṭayam khārī catuṣṭaya prastha saṃjñā ca parikīrtitā pala dvayam tu prasṛtam dviguṇam kuḍavam matam catur āḍhakaḥ bhavet droṇaḥ khārī droṇa catuṣṭayam krameṇa etena te jñeyāḥ pātre ṣaṭkarma saṃbhave pañca sapta nava tathā pramāṇāḥ te yathākramam nitya pātre tu tailānām niyamaḥ vārtika udbhavaḥ somavāre gṛhītvā atat dhvānyam toya plutam dharet paścāt pramāṇataḥ jñeyam kumārī hasta peṣaṇam tat piṣṭam śuddha pātre tu nadī toyena piṇḍitam dīpa pātram tatas kuryāt śuddhaḥ prayata mānasaḥ dīpa pātre jvālyamāne māruteḥ kavacam paṭhet śuddha bhūmau samāsthāpya bhaume dīpam pradāpayet mālā manūnām ye varṇāḥ sādhya nāma samanvitāḥ vartikāyām prakarttavyāḥ tantavaḥ tad pramāṇakāḥ tad triṃśa aṃśena vā grāhyā guru kārye akhila āḍhya tā kūṭa tulyāḥ smṛtāḥ nitye sāmānye atha viśeṣake rudrāḥ kūṭa gaṇāḥ proktāḥ na pātre niyamaḥ mataḥ ekaviṃśati saṃkhyākāḥ tantavaḥ atha adhvani smṛtāḥ kṛṣṇam uñcāṭane dveṣe aruṇam māraṇa karmaṇi kūṭa tulya palam tailam guru kārye śivaiḥ guṇam nitye pañca palam proktam athavā mānasī ruciḥ viśeṣaḥ asti atra yaḥ kaścid mārute rucyate mayā catuṣpathe tathā proktam ṣaṭsu dīpa pradāpanam nānā bhoga śriyai proktam dīpa dānam hanūmataḥ gaṇeśa sannidhau vighna mahā saṃkaṭa nāśane durgāyāḥ sannidhau proktam saṃgrāme dīpa dāpanam catuṣpathe vyādhi naṣṭau duṣṭa dṛṣṭau tathā eva ca rājadvāre bandha muktau kārā āgāre athavā matam vaśye bhaye vivāde ca veśma saṃgrāma saṃkaṭe dyūte dṛṣṭi staṃbhane ca vidveṣe māraṇe tathā krūra sattveṣu sarveṣu śaśvat ūndha vimokṣaṇe dīpa dānam hanumataḥ na atra kāryā vicāraṇā rudra ekaviṃśa piṇḍān ca tridhā maṇḍala mānakam laghu mānam smṛtam pañca sapta vā nava vā tathā kṣīreṇa nava nūtena dadhnā vā gomayena ca pratimā karaṇam proktam māruteḥ dīpa dāpane dakṣiṇa abhimukham vīram kṛtvā kesari vikramam ṛkṣa vinyasta pādam ca kirīṭena virājitam likhet bhittau paṭe vā api pīṭhe vā māruteḥ śubhe mālāmantreṇa dātavyam dīpa dānam hanūmataḥ nitya dīpaḥ prakarttavyaḥ dvādaśa akṣara vidyayā viśeṣaḥ tatra yaḥ tam vai dīpa dāne avadhāraya ṣaṣṭi ādau ca dvitīya ādau imam dīpam iti īrayet gṛhāṇa iti padam paścāt śeṣam kūṭa ādau nitya dīpe ca mantram sūrya akṣaram vadet tatra mālā ākhya manunā tad tad kāryeṣu kārayet gomayena upaliptāyām bhūmau tad gata mānasaḥ ṣaṣ koṇam vasu patram ca bhūmau rekhā samanvitam śaive vā vaiṣṇave pīṭhe pūjayet añjanā sutam kūṭa ṣaṭkam ca ṣaṣ koṇe antarāle para likhet ṣaṣ koṇeṣu ṣaṣ aṅgāni bīja yuktāni saṃlikhet ṣaṣ koṇeṣu ṣaṣ aṅgāni nāmāni ca purā ukta vat vasu patre kramāt pūjyāḥ aṣṭāvete ca vānarāḥ sugrīvāya aṅgadāya atha suṣeṇāya nalāya ca nīlāya atho jāṃbavate prahastāya tathā eva ca su veṣāya tatas paścāt yajet ṣaṣ aṅga devatāḥ ādau añjanā putrāya tatas ca rudra mūrtaye tatas vāyusutāya atha jānakījīvanāya ca rāma dūtāya brahmāstra nivāraṇāya tat param pañca upacāraiḥ saṃpūjya deśa kālau ca kīrtet kuśa udakam samādāya dīpa mantram samuñcaret tam mantram kūṭadhā japtvā jalam bhūmau vinikṣipet tatas kara puṭam kṛtvā yathāśakti japet manum trayodaśa evam dravyāṇi gomayam mṛttikā masī kastūrikā dadhi kṣīram navanītam ghaṛtam tathā paścāt vinaṣṭa dravya āptau māhiṣam gomayam smṛtam pathika āgamane dūrāt mahā durgasya rakṣaṇe bāla ādi rakṣaṇe ca eva caura ādi bhaya nāśane strī vaśyā ādiṣu kāryeṣu śastam go gomayam mane bhūmi spṛṣṭam na tat grāhyam antarikṣāt ca bhājane caturvidhā mṛttikā tu śvetā pīta aruṇa asitā maṣī lākṣā rasa udbhūtā sarvam vā anyat sphuṭam matam kṛtvā catur asram gṛham sudhīḥ tad
