madhye māhiṣeṇa atha kuryāt mūrtim hanūmataḥ bījam krodhāt ca tad puccham likhet mantrī samāhitaḥ śata patra samaḥ dhūpaḥ śāla niryāsa saṃbhavaḥ vāra trayam kaṇṭha deśe sa śeṣa viṣam uñcaran evam kṛte tu naṣṭānām mahiṣīṇām gavām api dāsī dāsa ādikānām ca naṣṭānām prāptiḥ īritā caura ādi duṣṭa sattvānām sarpa ādīnām bhaye punar tālena ca catur dvāram gṛham kṛtvā su śobhanam pūrva dvāre gajaḥ sthāpyaḥ dakṣiṇe mahiṣaḥ tathā evam krameṇa khaḍgam ca kṣurikā daṇḍa mudgarān kṛtvā ḍamaru hastām ca cakita akṣīm prayatnataḥ jātī puṣpaiḥ tu saṃpūjya śuddha dhūpa prakalpayet ghṛtena dīpam dattvā atha pāyasa annam nivedayet gaganam dīpikā indu āḍhyām śāstram ca puratas japet anayoḥ bhauṃmavāre tu kuryāt āraṃbham ādarāt śatru senā bhaye prāpte gairikeṇa tu maṇḍalam kṛtvā tad antare tālam īṣṭat namram samālikhet tatra avalaṃbamānām ca pratimām gomayena tu vāma hastena tāla agram dakṣiṇe jñāna mudrikā tāla mūlāt sva kāṣṭāyām mārge hasta mite gṛham dakṣiṇa ābha mukhīm rimyām hṛdaye vihita añjalim kṛśāra annam ca naivedyam sa ājyam tasyai nivedayet evam kṛte bhavet śīghram pathikānām samāgamaḥ śyāma pāṣāṇa khaṇḍena likhitvā bhūpateḥ gṛham prākāram tu catur dvāra yuktam dvāreṣu tatra vai jaṭāmāṃsī bhavam dhūpam taila akta ghṛta dīpakam naivedyam tila taila akta sa kṣārā māṣa roṭikā dhyeyaḥ dakṣiṇa hastena roṭikām bhakṣayan hariḥ vāma hastena pāṣāṇaiḥ trāsayan para sainikān bhrukuṭīm baddhvā bhīṣayan mathayan sthitaḥ evam kṛta vidhānena para sainyam vināśayet rakṣā bhavati durgāṇām satyam satya na saṃśayaḥ prāyogāḥ bahavaḥ tatra saṃkṣepāt gaditāḥ mayā pratyaham yaḥ vidhānena dīpa dānam hanūmataḥ na deyam duṣṭa hṛdaye duṣṭa cintana buddhaye avinītāya śiṣyāya piśunāya kadācana kṛtaghnāya na dātavyam dātavyam ca parīkṣite bahunā kim iha uktena sarvam dadyāt kapi īśvaraḥ danakṣobham samābhāṣya saṃhara dvayam īrayet ātma tattvam tatas paścāt prakāśaya yugam tatas varma astra vahni jāyā antaḥ sārddhū ṣaḍviṃśat arṇavān vasiṣṭhaḥ asya muniḥ chandaḥ anuṣṭubh ca devatāḥ punar hanumān muni sapta ṛtu veda aṣṭa nigamaiḥ kramāt mantra arṇaiḥ ca ṣaṣ aṅgāni kṛtvā dhyāyet kapi īśvaram jānu stha vāma bāhum ca jñāna mudrā param hṛdi bāla arka koṭi pratimam dhyāyet jñāna pradam harim dhyātvā evam prajapet lakṣam daśa aṃśam juhuyāt tilaiḥ sa ājyaiḥ saṃpūjayet pīṭhe pūrva ukte pūrvavat prabhum japtaḥ ayam madana kṣobham nāśayati eva niścitam atha vākṣye bhūta vidrāvaṇam param tāraḥ tāraḥ brahmā muniḥ syāt gāyatrī chandaḥ atra devatā punar hanumān kamalā bījam phaṭ śaktiḥ parikīrtitaḥ ṣaṣ dīrgha āḍhyena bījena ṣaṣ aṅgāni samācaret āñjaneya pāṭalā āsyam svarṇa adri sama vigraham evam dhyātvā japet lakṣam daśa aṃśam juhuyāt tilaiḥ ākrandan tam vimucya atha grahaḥ śīghram palāyate manavaḥ amī sadā āgopyāḥ na prakāśyāḥ yatas tatas parīkṣitāya śiṣyāya deyāḥ vā nija sūnave hanumat bhajana āsaktaḥ kārtavīrya arjunam sudhīḥ viśeṣataḥ samārādhya yathoktam phalam āpnuyāt iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde dīpavidhinirūpaṇam nāma pañcasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca kārtavīryata prabhṛtayaḥ nṛpāḥ bahuvidhāḥ bhuvi samullaṅghya nṛpān anyān etat me nuda saṃśayam śṛṇu nārada vakṣyāmi saṃdeha vinivṛttaye yaḥ sudarśana cakrasya avatāraḥ pṛthivī tale tasya kṣitīśvara idrasya smaraṇāt eva nārada śatrūn jayati saṃgrāme naṣṭam prāpnoti satvaram vahni tāra yutā raudrī lakṣmīḥ agni indu śānti yuj vedha adhara indu śānti āḍhyaḥ nidrayā āśā agni bindu yuj pāśaḥ māyā aṅkuśam padmā varma astre kārtavīpadam meṣaḥ sa dīrghaḥ pavanaḥ manuḥ uktaḥ hṛd antimaḥ ūnarviśati varṇaḥ ayam tāra ādiḥ nakha varṇakaḥ dattātreyaḥ muniḥ ca asya chandaḥ anuṣṭubh udāhṛtam kārtavīrya arjunaḥ devaḥ bīja śaktiḥ dhruvaḥ ca hṛd śeṣa āḍhya bīja yugmena hṛdayam vinyaset adhas śānti yukta caturthena kāma ādyena indu āḍhyam vāma karṇa ādya māyayā uru īśa yuktayā śikhām aṅkuśa padmābhyām sa vāgbhyām varma vinyaset varma astrābhyām astram uktam śeṣa arṇaiḥ vyāpakam punar hṛdaye jaṭhare nābhau jaṭhare guhya deśataḥ dakṣa pāde vāma pāde sakthni jānuni jaṅghayoḥ tāra ādyān atha śeṣa arṇān mastake ca lalāṭake sarva mantreṇa sarva aṅge kṛtvā vyāpakam ādṛtaḥ sarva iṣṭa siddhaye dhyāyet kārtavīryam janeśvaram dorbhiḥ pañcāśatā dakṣaiḥ bāṇān vāmaiḥ dhanūṃṣi ca dadhatam svarṇa mālā āḍhyam rakta vastra samāvṛtam cakra avatāram śrī viṣṇoḥ dhyāyet arjuna bhūpatim lakṣam ekam japet mantram daśa aṃśam juhuyāt tilaiḥ sa taṇḍulaiḥ pāyasena viṣṇu pīṭhe yajat tutam ṣaṣ koṇeṣu ṣaṣ aṅgāni tatas dikṣu vi vikṣu ca duṣṭa nāśam duḥkha nāśam durita āpad vināśakam dikṣu aṣṭa śaktayaḥ pūjyāḥ prācya ādiṣu asita prabhāḥ kṣemaṅkarī vaśya karī śrīkarī ca yaśaskarī āyuḥ karī tathā prajñā karī vidyā karī punar dhanakarī aṣṭamī paścāt lokeśāḥ astra saṃyutāḥ evam saṃsādhitaḥ mantraḥ prayoga arhaḥ prajāyate kārtavīrya arjunasya atha pūjāyantram iha ucyate sva bīja anaṅga dhruva vāc karṇikam digdalam likhet tārā ādi varma anta dalam śeṣa varṇa dala antaram ūṣma antya svara kiñjalkam śeṣa arṇaiḥ pariveṣṭitam koṇa alaṅkṛta bhūta arṇa bhūgṛham yantram īśituḥ śuddha bhūmau aṣṭa gandhaiḥ likhitvā yantram ādarāt tatra kuṃbham pratiṣṭhāpya tatra āvāhya arcayet nṛpam spṛṣṭvā kuṃbham japet mantram sahasram vijita indriyaḥ abhiṣim ced tat aṃbhobhiḥ priyam sarva iṣṭa siddhaye putrān yaśaḥ roga nāśam āyuḥ sva jana rañjanam vāc siddhim sudṛśaḥ kumbha abhiṣiktaḥ labhate naraḥ śatru upadrave āpanne grāme vā puṭabhedane saṃsthāpaṃyet idam yantram śatru bhīti nivṛttaye sarṣapa ariṣṭa laśuna kārpāsaiḥ māryate ripuḥ kaṭutaila mahiṣī ājyaiḥ hema dravya añjanam smṛtam apāmārga arka dūrvāṇām homaḥ lakṣmī pradaḥ agha nud strī vaśyā kṛt priyaṅgūṇām murāṇām bhūta śānti daḥ rocanā gomayaiḥ taṃbhaḥ bhū prāptiḥ śālibhiḥ hutaiḥ prakalpanīyāḥ mantra jñaiḥ kāryya gaurava lāghavāt kārtavīryyasya mantrāṇām ucyate lakṣaṇam budhāḥ kārtavīrya arjunam ṅeṃtam sarva mantreṣu yojayet sva bīja ādyaḥ daśa arṇaḥ asau anye nava śiva akṣarāḥ ādya bīja dvayena asau dvitīyaḥ mantraḥ īritaḥ sva kāmābhyām tṛtīyaḥ asau sva bhrūbhyām tu caturthakaḥ sva pāśābhyām pañcamaḥ asau ṣaṣṭaḥ svena ca māyayā sva aṅkuśābhyām saptamaḥ syāt svaram ābhyām atha aṣṭamaḥ sva vāc bhavābhyām navamaḥ varma astrābhyām atha antimaḥ dvitīya ādi nava anteṣu bījayoḥ syāt vyatikramaḥ eteṣu mantra varyeṣu sva anukūlam manum bhajet eṣām ādye virāṭchadaḥ anyeṣu triṣṭubh udāhṛtam daśa mantrāḥ ime proktāḥ yadā syuḥ praṇava ādikāḥ tad ādimaḥ śiva arṇaḥ syāt anye tu dvādaśa akṣarāḥ triṣṭupūchandaḥ tathā ādye syāt anyeṣu jagatī matā evam viṃśati mantrāṇām yajanam pūrvavat matam dīrgha āḍhya mūla bījena kuryāt eṣām ṣaḍaṅgakam tāraḥ hṛd kārtavīrya arjunāya varma astra ṭha dvayam caturdaśa arṇaḥ mantraḥ ayam asya ijyā pūrvavat matā bhū netra sama netra akṣi varṇeḥ asya aṅga pañcakam tāraḥ hṛd bhagavān ṅeṃtaḥ kārtavīrya arjunaḥ tathā varma astra agni priyā mantraḥ proktaḥ hi aṣṭādaśa arṇakaḥ tri veda sapta yugma akṣi varṇaiḥ pañca aṅgakam manoḥ namaḥ bhagavate śrī iti kārtavīrya arjunāya ca sarva duṣṭa antakāya iti tapaḥ bala parākramaḥ janyacūḍāḥ maṇa ante ye mahā śaktimate tatas triṣaṣṭi varṇavān proktaḥ smaramāt sarva vighna hṛt rājanya kravartī ca vīraḥ śūraḥ tṛtīyakaḥ māhiṣmatī patiḥ paścāt caturthaḥ samudīritaḥ revā aṃbu paritṛptaḥ ca kāṇaḥ hasta prabādhitaḥ daśa āsya iti ca ṣaḍbhiḥ syāt padaiḥ ṅe taiḥ ṣaṣ aṅgakam siṃcyamānam yuvatibhiḥ krīḍantam narmadā jale pūrvam tu prajapet lakṣam pūjā yogaḥ ca pūrvavat kārtavīrya arjunaḥ nāma rājā bāhu sahasravān tasya saṃsmaraṇāt eva hṛtam naṣṭam ca saṃvadet labhyate mantra varyaḥ ayam dvātriṃśat varṇa saṃyutaḥ pādaiḥ sarveṇa pañcāṅgam dhyāna pūjā ādi pūrvavat kārtavīryāya śabda ante vidmahe padam uñcaret mahā vīryāya varṇa ante dhīmahi iti padam vadet anuṣṭubham manum rātrau japatām caura saṃcayāḥ palāyante gṛhāt dūram tarpaṇāt hravanāt api vaiśākhe śrāvaṇe mārge kārtika āśvina pauṣataḥ māgha phālgunayoḥ māsoḥ dīpa āraṃbham samācaret tithau riktā vihīnāyām vāre śani kujau vinā dvi daivate ca rohiṇyām dīpa āraṃbhaḥ hita āvahaḥ prītau harṣam ca saubhāgye śobhana āyuṣmatoḥ api karaṇe viṣṭi rahite grahaṇe arddha udaya ādiṣu yogeṣu rātrau pūrvāhne dīpa āraṃbha ghaḥ kṛtaḥ śubhaḥ kārtike śukla saptamyām niśīthe atīva śobhanaḥ ati āvaśyaka kāryeṣu māsa ādīnām na śodhanam ādye hi upoṣya niyataḥ brahmacārī sa pītakaiḥ prātar snātvā śuddha bhūmau liptāyām gomaya udakaiḥ prāṇān āyamya saṃkalpya nyāsān pūrva uditān caret ṣaṣ koṇam racayet bhūmau raktacandana taṇḍulaiḥ atas smaram samālikhya ṣaṣ koṇeṣu samālikhet nava arṇaiḥ veṣṭayet tat ca trikoṇam tad bahis punar svarṇa jam rajata uttham vā tāmra jam tad abhāvataḥ kāṃsya pātram mṛṇmayam ca kaniṣṭham loha jam mṛtau śāntaye mudga cūrṇa uttham saṃdhau godhūma cūrṇa jam ājye pala sahasre tu pātram śata palam smṛtam ājye ayuta pale pātram pala pañcaśatā smṛtam pañcasaptati saṃkhye tu pātram ṣaṣṭi palam smṛtam trisāhasrī ghṛta pale śarkarā pala bhājanam dvi sāhakhtryām dvi śata mitam ca bhājanam iṣyate nitya dīpe vahni palam pātram ājyam palam smṛtam evam pātram pratiṣṭhāpya vartīḥ sūtra utthitāḥ kṣipet ekā tisraḥ athavā pañca sapta ādyāḥ viṣamāḥ api tantu saṃkhyā vinirmitā sahasra pala saṃkhyā ādi daśa aṃśam kārya gauravāt suvarṇa ādi kṛtām ramyām śalākām ṣoḍaśa aṅgulām tad arddhām vā tad arddhām vā sūkṣma agrām sthūla mūlikām vimuñcet dakṣiṇe pātra madhye ca agre kṛta agrikām pātra dakṣiṇa diś deśe muktvām gula catuṣṭayam adhas ugrām dakṣiṇa ādhārām nikhanet churikām śubhām dīpam prajvālayet tatra gaṇeśa smṛti pūrvakam taṇḍula aṣṭadale vā api vidhivat sthāpayet hūṭam tatra āvāhya nṛpa adhīśam pūjayet pūrvavat sudhīḥ jala akṣatān samādāya dīpam saṃkalpayet tatas dīpa saṃkalpa mantraḥ ayam kathyate dvi iṣu bhū mitaḥ praṇavaḥ pāśa māye ca śikhā kārtākṣarāṇi ca vīryārjunāya māhiṣmatī nāthāya sahasra ca ātreyāya anusūyā ante garbharatnāya tat param namaḥ grīvā āma karṇa indu sthitau pāśaḥ imam tatas dīpam gṛhāṇa amukam rakṣa rakṣa padam punar duṣṭa anna āśaya yugmam syāt tathā pātaya ghātaya śatrūn māyā tāraḥ svam bījam ātmabhūḥ vahnīpriyā anena atha dīpa varyeṇa paścimā māyā ākāśa dvayam vāmanetra candra yutam śivā veda ādi kāma cāmuṇḍāḥ svāhā tu pūsa bindukau praṇavaḥ agnipriyā mantraḥ netra bāṇa adhara akṣaraḥ cāmuṇḍayā ṣaṣ aṅgāni caret ṣaṣ dīrgha yuktayā govinda āḍhyaḥ halī sa iṃduḥ cāmuṇḍā bījam īritam kūrma agnī śānti bindu āḍhyau vahni dhruvam ṛṣiḥ pūrva uditaḥ anuṣṭubh chandaḥ anyat pūrvavat punar śūdrāṇām pradhyamam proktam mlecchasya vadha bandhanam ākhvā otvoḥ darśanam duṣṭam gavāśvasya sukha āvaham dīpa jvālā samā siddhyai vakrā niśa vidhāyinī śabdāḥ bhaya dā kartuḥ ujjvalā sukha dā matā kṛṣṇā śatru bhaya utpattye vamantī paśu nāśinī kṛte dīpe yadā pātram bhagnam dṛśyate daivataḥ pakṣāt arvāk tadā gacchet yajamānaḥ yama ālayam vartyataram yadā kuryāt kāryam siddhyet vilaṃbataḥ aśuci sparśane vyādhiḥ dīpa nāśe tu caura bhīḥ śva mārjāra ākhu saṃsparśe bhavet bhūpatitaḥ bhayam pātra āraṃbhe vasu palaiḥ kṛtaḥ dīpaḥ akhila iṣṭa daḥ tasmāt dīpaḥ prayatnena rakṣaṇīyaḥ oṃ'tarāyataḥ āsamāpteḥ prakurvīta brahmacaryam ca bhū śayaḥ strī śūdra patita ādīnām saṃbhāṣām api varjayet stotra pāṭham pratidinam niśīthinyām viśeṣataḥ sahasram prajapet vātrau saḥ abhīṣṭam kṣipram āpnuyāt kartā tu dakṣiṇām dadyāt puṣkalām toṣa hetave gurau tuṣṭe dadāti iṣṭam kṛtavīrya sutaḥ nṛpaḥ guru ājñayā svayam kuryāt yadi vā kārayet guruḥ dattvā dhana ādikam tasmai dīpa dānāya nārada guru ājñām antarā kuryāt yaḥ dīpam sva iṣṭa siddhaye uttamam goghṛtam proktam madhyamam mahaṣībhavam tila tailam tu tādṛś syāt kanīyaḥ aja ādi jam ghṛtam siddhvā artha saṃbhavena atha dviṣatām nāśanāya ca kārya siddhaḥ tadā kuryāt tri vāram dīpa jam vidhim stuti proyaḥ mahāviṣṇuḥ gaṇeśaḥ staparṇa priyaḥ durga arcana priyāḥ nūnam abhiṣeka priyaḥ śivaḥ tasmāt teṣām pratoṣāya vidadhyāt tad tad ādarāt iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde kārtavīryamāhātmyamantradīpakathanam nāma ṣaṭsaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca sādhu sādhu mahā prājña sarva tantra viśārada tvayā mahyam samākhyātam vidhānam tantra gopitam adhunā tu mahābhāga kīrta vīrya hanūmatoḥ śṛṇu vipra indra vakṣyāmi kavacam parama adbhutam sahasra āditya saṃkāśe nānā ratna samujjvaṃle bhāsvat dhvaja patākā āḍhye turaga ayuta bhūṣite mahā saṃvartaka aṃbhodhi bhīma rāva virāviṇi vāmaiḥ uddaṇḍa kodaṇḍān dadhānam aparaiḥ śarān kirīṭa hāra mukuṭa keyūra valaya aṅgadaiḥ mudrikā udara bandha ādyaiḥ māaiñjī nūpuraka ādibhiḥ bhūṣitam vividha ākalpaiḥ bhāsvaraiḥ su mahādhanaiḥ ābaddha kavacam vīram su prasanna ānana aṃbujam sarva śatru kṣaya karam sarva vyādhi vināśanam sarva saṃpad pradātāram vijaya śrī niṣevitam divya mālya anulepa āḍhyam sarva lakṣaṇa saṃyutam ratha nāga aśva pādāta vṛnda madhya gam īśvaram śrīmat ṭatam hareḥ aṃśāt avatīrṇam mahī tale samyak ātma ādi bhedena dhyātvā rakṣām udīrayet asya aṅga mūrtayaḥ pañca pāntu mām sphaṭika ujjvalāḥ agni īśa asura vāyavya koṇeṣu hṛdaya ādikāḥ sarvatas usra jvalat rūpāḥ dara carma asi pāṇayaḥ kṣemaṅkarī śakti yutaḥ caura varga vibhañjanaḥ prācīm diśam rakṣatu me bāṇa bāṇāsana āyudhaḥ śrīkarī śakti sahitaḥ mārī bhaya vināśakaḥ śara cāpa dharaḥ śrīmān diśam me pātu dakṣiṇām mahā vaśyā karī yuktaḥ sarva śatru vināśa kṛt mahā iṣu cāpa dhṛk pātu mama prācetasīm diśam yaśaḥ karyā samāyuktaḥ daitya saṃgha vināśanaḥ vidyākarī samāyuktaḥ su mahā huḥkha nāśanaḥ pātu me nairṛtīm cāpa pāṇiḥ vidiśam īśvaraḥ dhanakaryā samāyuktaḥ mahā durita nāśanaḥ iṣu āsanā iṣudhṛk pātu vidiśam mama vāyavīm āyuḥ karyā yutaḥ śrīmān mahā bhaya vināśanaḥ cāpa iṣu dhārī śaivīm me vidiśam parirakṣatu vijaya śrī yutaḥ sākṣāt sahasra ara dharaḥ vibhuḥ diśam ūrddhvām avatu me sarva duṣṭa bhayaṅkaraḥ śaṅkhabhṛt su mahā śakti saṃyutaḥ api adharām diśam mahā yoga samāyuktaḥ sarva diś cakra maṇḍalaḥ mahā yogi īśvaraḥ pātu sarvatas mama padma bhṛt etāḥ tu mūrtayaḥ raktāḥ rakta mālya aṃśuka āvṛtāḥ pradhāna devatā rūpāḥ sthitāḥ śaktayaḥ padma hastāḥ cata nīla indīvara sannnibhāḥ śukla mālya anuvasanāḥ su lipta tilaka ujjvalāḥ tad pārśada īśvarāḥ sva sva vāhana āyudha bhūṣaṇāḥ sva sva dikṣu sthitāḥ pāntu mām indra ādyāḥ mahā balāḥ samākhyātāḥ sarva āvaraṇa devatāḥ sarvatas mām sadā pātum sarva śakti samanvitāḥ tejaḥ rūpāḥ sthitāḥ pātum vāñchā sukhana drumāḥ diśam ca anye mahā varṇāḥ mantra rūpāḥ mahā ujjvalāḥ kārtavīryaḥ śiraḥ pātu lalāṭam haihaya īśvaraḥ sukumāraḥ hanum pātu bhrū yugam me dhanurdharaḥ nayanam nāsikām me guṇa ākaraḥ adhara uṣṭhau sadā pātu brahjñeyaḥ dvijān kaviḥ sarva śāstra kalā dhārī jihvām cibukam avyayaḥ dattātreya priyaḥ kaṇṭham skandhau rāja kula īśvaraḥ bhujau daśa āsya darpa ghnaḥ hṛdayam me mahā balaḥ kukṣim rakṣatu me vidvān vakṣaḥ parapurañjayaḥ karau sarva artha daḥ pātu kara agrāṇi jagat priyaḥ revā ambagu līlā saṃhaptaḥ jaṭharam parirakṣatu vīra śūraḥ tu me nābhim pārśvau me sarva duṣṭa hā sahasra bhuja nṛt pṛṣṭam saptadvīpā adhipaḥ kaṭim ūrū māhiṣmatī nāthaḥ jānunī vallabhaḥ bhuvaḥ jaṅghe vīrādhipaḥ pātu pātu pādau manojavaḥ sarva duṣṭa antakaḥ pātu dhātu aṣṭaka kalevaram prāṇa ādi daśa jīva īśān sarva śiṣṭa iṣṭa daḥ avatu vaśīkṛta indriya grāmaḥ pātu sarva indriyāṇi me tat sarvam pātu me sarva loka nātha īśvara īśvaraḥ vajrāt sārataram ca idam śarīram kavaca āvṛtam vicarāmi divā rātrau nirbhayena antarātmanā rājamārge mahā durge mārge caurāḥ disaṃkule saṃgrāme śastra saṃghāte siṃha vyāghra niṣevite gahvare sarva saṃkīrṇe saṃdhyā kāle nṛpa ālaye paripanthi jana ākīrṇe deśe dasyu gaṇa āvṛte sarva sva haraṇe prāpte prāpte prāṇasya saṃkaṭe nānā roga jvara āveśe piśāca preta yātane mārī duḥsvapna pīḍāsu kliṣṭe viśvāsa ghātake śārīre ca mahā duḥkhe mānase ca mahā jvare āṅgutu kāmān akhilān asmad vasu viluṃpakān nivārayatu dos daṇḍa sahasreṇa mahā rathaḥ saṃruddhū gati sāmarthyān karotu kṛta vīrya jaḥ sṛṇi sāhasra nirbhinnān sahasra śara khaṇḍitān rāja cūḍāmaṇiḥ kṣipram karotu asmad virodhakān khaḍga sāhasra dalitān sahasra muśala arditān caura ādi duṣṭa sattva oghān karotu kamala īkṣaṇaḥ sva śaṅkha nāda saṃtrastān sahasra āra sahasra bhṛt avatāraḥ hareḥ sākṣāt pālayatu akhilam mama kārtavīrya mahā vīrya sarva duṣṭa vināśana sarvatra sarvadā duṣṭa caurān nāśāya nāśaya kim tvam svapiṣi duṣṭa ghna kim tiṣṭasi cirāya asi ye caurāḥ vasu hartāraḥ vidviṣaḥ ye ca hiṃsakāḥ sādhu bhīti karāḥ duṣṭāḥ chadmakāḥ ye durāśayāḥ durhṛdaḥ pālāḥ duṣṭa amātyāḥ ca pāpakāḥ sarva sva hāriṇām ye ca pañca māyāvinaḥ mahā kleśa karāḥ mlecchāḥ dasyavaḥ vṛṣalāḥ ca ye ye agnidāḥ gara dātāraḥ vañcakāḥ śastra pāṇayaḥ ye pāpāḥ duṣṭa karmāṇaḥ duḥkha dāḥ duṣṭa buddhayaḥ vyājakāḥ kupatha āsaktāḥ ye ca nānā bhaya pradāḥ chidra anveṣa ratāḥ nityam ye asmān bādhitum udyatāḥ te sarve kārtavīryasya mahā śaṅkhara vāhatāḥ sahasā vilayam yāntu vimohitāḥ ye dānavāḥ mahā ādityāḥ ye yakṣāḥ ye ca rākṣasāḥ piśācāḥ ye mahāsattvāḥ ye bhūta brahmarākṣasāḥ apasmāra grahāḥ ye ca ye grahāḥ piśita aśanāḥ mahālohita bhoktāraḥ vetālāḥ ye ca guhyakāḥ ḍākinyaḥ druṇasāḥ pretāḥ kṣetrapālāḥ vināyakāḥ mahā vyāghra mahā meghāḥ mahā turāga rūpakāḥ mahā gajāḥ mahā siṃhāḥ mahā mahiṣa yonayaḥ ṛkṣa vārāha śunaka vānara ulūka mūrtayaḥ mahā uṣṭra khara mārjāra sarpa govṛṣa mastakāḥ nānā rūpāḥ mahāsattvāḥ nānā kleśa sahasra dāḥ nānā roga karāḥ kṣudrāḥ mahā vīryāḥ mahā balāḥ vātikāḥ paittikāḥ ślaiṣmikāḥ sānnipātikāḥ māheśvarāḥ vaiṣṇavāḥ ca vairiñcyāḥ ca mahāgrahāḥ skāndāḥ vaināyakāḥ krūrāḥ ye ca pramatha guhyakāḥ mahā śatru hāḥ raudrāḥ mahā mārī masūrikāḥ aikāhikāḥ vdyāhikāḥ ca tryāhikāḥ ca mahājvarāḥ cāturthikāḥ pākṣikāḥ ca māsyāḥ ṣāṇmāsikāḥ ca ye sāṃvatsarāḥ durnivāryāḥ jvarāḥ parama dāruṇāḥ svāpnikāḥ ye mahā utpātāḥ ye ca duḥsvāpnikāḥ grahāḥ kūṣmāṇḍāḥ jṛṃbhikāḥ bhaumāḥ droṇāḥ sānnidhya vañcakāḥ bhramikāḥ prāṇa hartāraḥ ye ca bālagraha ādayaḥ manaḥ budvi indriya harāḥ sphoṭakāḥ ca mahā grahāḥ mahā aśanāḥ balibhujaḥ mahā kuṇapa bhojanāḥ divācarāḥ rātri carāḥ ye ca saṃdhyāsu dāruṇāḥ pramattāḥ vā apramattāḥ vai ye mām bādhitum udyatāḥ ye sarpāḥ ye mahā nāgāḥ mahā giri bileśayāḥ kālavyālāḥ mahādaṃṣṭrāḥ mahājagara saṃjñakāḥ ananta śūlikā ādyāḥ ca daṃṣṭra viṣa mahā bhayāḥ aneka śata śīrṣāḥ ca khaṇḍa pucchāḥ ca dāruṇāḥ mahāviṣa jalaukāḥ ca vṛścikāḥ ruktapucchakāḥ āśīviṣāḥ kālakūṭāḥ mahā hālāhala āhvayāḥ jala sarpāḥ jala vyālāḥ jala grāhāḥ ca kacchapāḥ matsyakāḥ viṣapucchāḥ ca ye ca anye jala vāsinaḥ jala jāḥ sthala jāḥ ca eva kṛtrimāḥ ca mahāviṣāḥ guptarūpāḥ guptaviṣāḥ mūṣikāḥ gṛhagodhikāḥ nānā viṣāḥ ca ye ghorāḥ mahopaviṣa saṃjñakāḥ ye asmān bādhitum icchanti śarīra prāṇa nāśakāḥ te sarve kārtavīryasya khaṅka sāhasra dāritāḥ dūrāt eva vinaśyantu praṇaṣṭa indriya sāhasāḥ manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ tu ṛkṣa vānarāḥ vana gocarāḥ siṃha vyāghra varāhāḥ ca mahiṣāḥ ye mahā mṛgāḥ gajāḥ turaṅgāḥ gavayāḥ rāsabhāḥ śarabhāḥ vṛkāḥ śunakāḥ dvīpinaḥ śubhrāḥ mārjārāḥ bila lolupāḥ śṛgālāḥ śaśakāḥ śyenāḥ gurutmantaḥ vihṝṅgamāḥ bheruṇḍāḥ vāyasāḥ gūdhrāḥ haṃsa ādyāḥ pakṣi jātayaḥ udbhid jāḥ ca aṇḍa jāḥ ca eva sveda jāḥ ca jarāyu jāḥ nānā bheda kule jātāḥ nānā bhedāḥ pṛthagvidhāḥ te sarve kārtavīryasya gadā sāhasra dāritāḥ dūrāt eva vinaśyantu vinaṣṭa gati pauruṣāḥ ye ca a kṣema pradātāraḥ kūṭa māyāvinaḥ ca ye māraṇa utsādana unmūla dveṣa mohana kārakāḥ viśvāsa ghātakāḥ duṣṭāḥ ye ca svāmi druhaḥ narāḥ ye ca ātatāyinaḥ duṣṭāḥ ye pāpāḥ gopya hāriṇaḥ dāha upadyāta garala śastrapāta ati duḥkha dāḥ kṣetra vitta ādi haraṇa bandhana ādi bhaya pradāḥ ītayaḥ vividha ākāraḥ ye ca anye duṣṭa jātayaḥ pīḍā karāḥ ye satatam chidram icchanti bādhitum te sarve kārtavīryasya cakra sāhasra dāritāḥ dūrāt eva kṣayam yāntu vinaṣṭa bala sāhasāḥ ye meghāḥ ye mahā varṣāḥ ye vātāḥ yāḥ ca vidyutaḥ ye mahā aśanayaḥ dīptāḥ ye nirghātāḥ ca dāruṇāḥ ulkā pātāḥ ca ye ghorāḥ ye mahā indrāyudha ādayaḥ sūrya indu kuja saumyāḥ ca guru kāvya śanaiścarāḥ rāhuḥ ca ketavaḥ ghorāḥ nakṣatrāḥ rāśayaḥ tathā tithayaḥ saṃkramāḥ māsāḥ hāyanāḥ yuga nāyakāḥ manvantara adhipāḥ siddhāḥ ṛṣayaḥ yoga siddhayaḥ nidhayaḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāma atharvāṇaḥ ca eva vahnayaḥ ṛtavaḥ lokapālāḥ ca pitaraḥ deva saṃhatiḥ vidyāḥ ca eva catuḥṣaṣṭi bhedāḥ yāḥ bhuvanatraye ye tu atra kīrtitāḥ sarve caye ca anye na anukīrtitāḥ te saṃtu naḥ sadā saumyāḥ sarva kāla sukha āvahāḥ ājñayā kārtavīryasya yogi indrasya amita dyuteḥ kārtavīrya arjunaḥ dhanvī rāja indraḥ haihaya īśvaraḥ daśa āsya darpa hā revā līlā dṛptakaḥ su durjayaḥ duḥkha hā caura damanaḥ rāja rāja īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva daḥ śrīmān sarva śiṣṭa iṣṭa daḥ kṛtī rāja cūḍāmaṇiḥ yogī saptadvīpā adhināyakaḥ vijayī viśvajit vāgmī mahā gatiḥ a lolupaḥ māhiṣmatī patiḥ yodhāḥ mahā kīrtiḥ mahā bhujaḥ sukumāraḥ mahāvīraḥ mārīghnaḥ madirā īkṣaṇaḥ śatrughnaḥ śāśvataḥ śūraḥ śaṅkhabhṛt yogivallabhaḥ mahā bhāgavataḥ dhīmān mahā bhaya vināśanaḥ sarva śāstra kalā dharī virajāḥ loka vanditaḥ vīraḥ vimala sattva āḍhyaḥ mahā bala parākramaḥ khaḍgabhṛt kāma daḥ kāntaḥ kālaghnaḥ kamala īkṣaṇaḥ yoga āḍhyaḥ sarva roga ghnaḥ rājita akhila bhū talaḥ sarva āyudha dharaḥ abhīṣṭa pradaḥ para purañjayaḥ yoga siddhaḥ mahā kāyaḥ mahā vṛnda śata adhipaḥ iti aṣṭaśata nāma uttyāḥ mūrtayaḥ daśa diś pathi samyak daśa diśaḥ vyāpya pālayantu ca mām sadā svasthāḥ sarva indriyāḥ śāntiḥ astu sadā mama śeṣa ādyāḥ mūrtayaḥ aṣṭau ca vikrameṇa eva bhāsvarāḥ agni nirṛti vāyu īśa koṇa gāḥ pāntu mām sadā duḥkha hāniḥ avighnaḥ ca prajā vṛddhiḥ sukhaḥ dayaḥ vāñchā āptiḥ atikalyāṇam avaiṣamyam anāmayam anālasyam abhīṣṭam syāt mṛtyu hāniḥ bala unnatiḥ bhaya hāniḥ yaśaḥ kāntiḥ vidyā ṛddhiḥ mahā śriyaḥ anaṣṭa dravya tā ca eva naṣṭasya punarāgamaḥ dīrgha āyuṣyam manaḥ harṣaḥ saukumāryam abhīpsitam sarva śānti karam guhyam samasta bhaya nāśanam vijaya artha pradam nṝṇām sarva saṃpad pradam śubham śṛṇuyāt vā paṭhet vā api sarva kāmān avāpnuyāt cauraiḥ hṛtam yadā paśyet paśu ādi dhanam ātmanaḥ sapta vāram tadā japyet niśi paścima diś mukhaḥ sapta rātreṇa labhate naṣṭa dravyam na saṃśayaḥ saptaviṃśatidhā japtvā prācī diś vadanaḥ pumān sarva roga prapīḍāsu tredhā vā pañcadhā paṭhet tri dināt nigaḍāt ūddhvaḥ mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ yātrā kāle paṭhitvā idam mārge gacchati yaḥ pumān japan āsecanam kurvan jalena añjalinā tanau na ca asau viṣa kṛti ādi roga sphoṭaiḥ prabādhyate kārtavīryaḥ khala dveṣī kṛtavīrya sutaḥ balī rakta gandhaḥ rakta mālyaḥ rājā smartuḥ abhīṣṭa daḥ dvādaśa etāni nāmāni kārtavīryasya yaḥ paṭhet yaḥ sevate sadā vipra śrīmat cakra avatārakam tasya rakṣām sadā kuryāt cakram viṣṇoḥ mahātmanaḥ śrutam tubhyam nigaditam dhārayasva akhila iṣṭa dam iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde kārtavīryakavacakathanam nāma saptasaptatitomaḥ adhyāyaḥ kārtavīryasya kavacam kathitam te muni īśvara moha vidhvaṃsanam jaitram māruteḥ kavacam śṛṇu yasya saṃdhāraṇāt sadyas sarve naśyanti upadravāḥ bhūta preta ari jam duḥkham nāśam eti na saṃśayaḥ ekadā aham gataḥ draṣṭum rāmam ramayatām varam ānanda vanikā saṃstham dhyāyantam sva ātmanaḥ padam tatra rāmam ramānātham pūjitam tridaśa īśvaraiḥ namaskṛtya tad ādiṣṭam āsanam sthitavān puras tatra sarvam mayā vṛttam rāvaṇasya vadha antakam pṛṣṭam provāca rāja indraḥ śrī rāmaḥ svayam ādarāt tatas kathā ante bhagavān māruteḥ kavacam dadau bhaviṣyat etat nirddiṣṭam bāla bhāvena nārada śrī rāmeṇa añjana asūnā sūnoḥ bhukti mukti pradāyakam hanumān pūrvatas pātu dakṣiṇe pavanātmajaḥ pātu pratīcyām akṣaghnaḥ saumye sāgaratārakaḥ pātu kapi śreṣṭhaḥ kesari priya nandanaḥ laṅkā vidāhakaḥ pātu sarva āpadbhyaḥ nirantaram sugrīva sacivaḥ pātu mastakam vāyu nandanaḥ netre chāyā apahārī ca pātu naḥ plavaga īśvaraḥ kapolau karṇa mūle ca pātu śrī rāma kiṅkaraḥ nāsā agram añjanā sūnuḥ pātu vaktram hari īśvaraḥ pātu kaṇṭhe tu daityāriḥ skandhau pātu surāri jit bhujau pātu mahā tejāḥ karau ca caraṇa āyudhaḥ nakhān nākha āyudhaḥ pātu kukṣau pātu kapi īśvaraḥ vakṣaḥ mudrā apahārī ca pātu pārśve bhuja āyudhaḥ laṅkā nibhañjanaḥ pātu pṛṣṭadeśe nirantaram nābhim śrī rāma bhaktaḥ tu kaṭim pātu anilātmajaḥ guhyam pātu mahā prajñaḥ sakthinī atithi priyaḥ ūrū ca jānunī pātu laṅkā prāsāda bhañjanaḥ jaṅghe pātu kapi śreṣṭhaḥ gulphau pātu mahā balaḥ acala uddhārakaḥ pātu pādau bhāskara sannibhaḥ aṅgāni pātu sattva āḍhyaḥ pātu pāda aṅgulīḥ sadā mukha aṅgāni mahā śūraḥ pātu romāṇi ca ātmavān sthitam vrajantam āsīnam pibantam jakṣatam kapiḥ loka uttara guṇaḥ śrīmān pātu tryaṃbaka saṃbhavaḥ pramattam apramattam vā śayānam gahaneṃ'buni saṃgrāme saṃkaṭe ghore virāj rūpa dharaḥ avatu ḍākinī śākinī mārī kālarātri marīcikāḥ śayānam mām vibhuḥ pātu piśāca uraga rākṣasīḥ sādhaka indrāvanaḥ śaśvat pātu sarvatas eva mām yad rūpam bhīṣaṇam dṛṣṭvā palāyante bhayānakāḥ sa sarva rūpaḥ sarvajñaḥ sṛṣṭi sthiti karaḥ avatu svayam brahmā svayam viṣṇuḥ sākṣāt devaḥ maheśvaraḥ sūrya maṇḍala gaḥ śrīdaḥ pātu kāla traye api mām yasya śabdam upākarṇya daitya dānava rākṣasāḥ devāḥ manuṣyāḥ tiryañcaḥ sthāvarāḥ jaṅgamāḥ tathā sa bhayāḥ bhaya nirmuktāḥ bhavanti sva kṛta anugāḥ yasya aneka kathāḥ puṇyāḥ śrūyante pratikalpake saḥ avatāt sādhaka śreṣṭham sadā rāma parāyaṇam vaidhātra dhātṛ prabhṛti yat kiñcid dṛśyate atyalam viddhvi vyāptam yathā kīśa rūpeṇa anañjanena tat yaḥ vibhuḥ saḥ aham eṣaḥ aham svīyaḥ svayam aṇuḥ bṛhat ṛk yajuḥ sāma rūpaḥ ca praṇavaḥ trivṛt adhvaraḥ aneka ananta brahmāṇḍa dhṛte brahma svarūpiṇe samīraṇa ātmane tasmai nataḥ asmi ātma svarūpiṇe namaḥ śrī rāma bhaktāya śyāmāya mahate namaḥ namaḥ vānara vīrāya sugrīva sakhya kāriṇe saṃkā vidahanāya atha mahā sāgara tāriṇe sītā śoka vināśāya rāma mudrā dharāya ca rāvaṇa anta nidānāya namaḥ sarva uttara ātmane megha nāda makha dhvaṃsa kāraṇāya namaḥ namaḥ vāyu putrāya vīrāya ākāśa udara gāmine vanapāla śiraḥ chetre laṅkā prāsāda bhañjine jvalat kāñcana varṇāya dīrgha lāṅgūla dhāriṇe lakṣmaṇa aṅga mahā śakti jāta kṣata vināśine ṛkṣa vānara vīra ogha prāsādāya namaḥ namaḥ mahī ripu bhaya ghnāya bhakta trāṇa eka kāriṇa para prerita mantrāṇām mantrāṇām staṃbha kāriṇe payaḥ pāṣāṇa taraṇa kāraṇāya namaḥ namaḥ bāla arka maṇḍala grāsa kāriṇe duḥkha hāriṇe nakha āyudhāya bhīmāya danta āyudha dharāya ca vihṝṅgamāya śavāya vajra dehāya te namaḥ kara stha śaila śastrāya rāma śastrāya te namaḥ dakṣiṇa āśā bhāskarāya satām candra udaya ātmane kṛtyā akṣata vyathā ghnāya sarva kleśa harāya ca svāmi ājñā pārtha saṃgrāma sakhya saṃjaya kāriṇe bhaktānām divya vādeṣu saṃgrāme jaya kāriṇe sarva agni vyādhi saṃstaṃbha kāriṇe bhaya hāriṇe sadā vana phala āhāra saṃtṛptāya viśeṣataḥ mahā arṇava śilā baddhva setu bandhāya te namaḥ yasmai kasmai na dātavyam rakṣaṇīyam prayatnataḥ kaṇṭhe vā dakṣiṇe bāhau jayaḥ tasya pade pade kim punar bahunā uktena sādhitam lakṣam ādarāt iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde hanumatkavacanirūpaṇam nāma aṣṭasaptatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha aparam vāyusūnoḥ caritam pāpa nāśanam yat uktam svāsu rāmeṇa ānanda vana vāsinā śṛṇuṣva gadataḥ mattaḥ kumārasya kumāraka caritam sarva pāpa ghnam śṛṇvatām paṭhatām sadā vāñchāmi aham sadā vipra saṃgamam kīśa rūpiṇā krīḍanti sarvadā ca atra prākaṭye api rahasi api tat atra prakaṭam tubhyam karomi prīta mānasaḥ āvirbhūtaḥ asmi aham pūrvam rājñaḥ daśaratha kṣaye viśvāmitraḥ ṛthayāmāsa pitaram mama bhūpatim yakṣa rakṣaḥ vighāta artham lakṣmaṇena saha eva mām preṣayāmāsa dharma ātmā siddhāśramam aramyakam tatra gatvā āśramam ṛbeḥ dūṣayantī niśācarau astra grāmam dadau mahyam māsam ca avāsayat tathā tatas gādhi sutaḥ adhīmān jñātvā bhāvi artham ādarāt tasya kanyām paṇībhūtām sītām sura sutā upamām vyaṣanīya agamam paścāt ayodhyām sva pituḥ purīm tatas rājñā aham ājñāya prajā śīlana mānasaḥ tat śutvā supriyā bhāryā kaikaiyī bhūpatim mune deva kārya vidhāna artham vidūṣita matiḥ jagau rāmaḥ caturdaśa samāḥ daṇḍakān pravivāsyatām tat ākarṇya ham udyuktaḥ araṇyam bhāryā anujā anvitaḥ gantum nṛpatinā an uktaḥ api agamam citrakūṭakam māntṛ varga yutau dīnau sa ācārya amātya nāgarau vyajijñapatam āgatya pañcavaṭyām nija āśramam tatas trayodaśe varṣe rāvaṇaḥ nāma rākṣasaḥ māyayā hṛtavān sītām priyām mama parokṣataḥ tatas aham dīna vadanaḥ ṛṣyamūkam hi parvatam saha vānara yūthaiḥ ca sāhāyyam kṛtavān mama virudhya rāvaṇena alam mama bhaktaḥ vibhīṣaṇaḥ āgataḥ hi abhiṣicya āśulaṅkeśaḥ hi vikalpitaḥ hatvā tu rāvaṇam saṃkhye sa putra amātya bāndhavam sītām ādāya saṃśuddhvām ayodhyām samupāgataḥ tatas kāla antare vipra sugrīvaḥ ca vibhīṣaṇaḥ nimantritau pituḥ śrāddhve ṣaṣ kulāḥ ca dvijottamāḥ ayodhyāyām samājagmuḥ te tu sarve nimantritāḥ ṛte vibhīṣiṇam tatra cintayāne raghūttame śaṃbhuḥ brāhmaṇa rūpeṇa ṣaṣ kulaiḥ ca saha āgataḥ atha pṛṣṭaḥ mayā śaṃbhuḥ vibhīṣaṇa samāgame nītvā mām draviḍe deśe mocaya dvija bandhanāt mayā nimantritāḥ śraddhe hi agastya ādyāḥ muni īśvarāḥ saṃbhojitāḥ tu prayayuḥ sva svam āśrama maṇḍalam tatas kāla antare viprāḥ devāḥ daityāḥ nareśvarāḥ gautamena samāhūtāḥ sarve yajña sabhājitāḥ te sarve sphaāṭikam liṅgam tryaṃbaka adrau niveśitam saṃpūjya nyavaṃsaḥ tatra deva daitya nṛpa agrajāḥ gautamaḥ api atha madhyāhne pūjayāmāsa śaṅkaram sarve śukla aṃbara dharāḥ bhasma uddhvūlita vigrahāḥ natvā tu bhārgavam sarve bhūtaśuddhim pracakramuḥ teṣām madhye mahā ākāśam ākāśe nirmala amalam tad madhye ca maheśānam dhyāyet dīpti mayam śubham ajñāna saṃyutam bhūtam sa malam karma saṃgataḥ tam deham ākāśa dīpe pradahet jñāna vahninā ākāśasya avṛttim ca aham dagdhvā ākāśam atho dahet dagdhvā ākāśam atho vāyum agni bhūtam tathā dahet ap bhūtam ca tatas dagdhvā pṛthivī bhūtam eva ca tad āśritān guṇān dagdhvā tatas deham pradāhayet evam pradagdhvā bhūta ardi dehī tad jñāna vahninā niṣpanna candrakiraṇa saṃkāśa kiraṇam kiraṇam śivam śiva aṅga utpanna kiraṇaiḥ amṛta drava saṃyutaiḥ su śītalā tatas jvālā praśāntā candra raśmi vat prasārita sudhā rugbhiḥ sāṃdrībhūtaḥ ca saṃplavaḥ anena plāvitam bhūta grāmam saṃcintayet param ittham kṛtvā bhūtaśuddhim kriyā arhe martyaḥ śuddhaḥ jāyate hi eva sadyas pūjām kartum japya karma api paścāt evam dhyāyet brahmahatyā ādi śuddhyai evam dhyātvā cadran dīpti prakāśam dhyānena āropya āśu liṅge śivasya sadāśivam dīpa madhye vicintya pañcākṣareṇa arcanam avyayam tu āvāhana ādīn upacārān atathā api kṛtvā snānam pūrvavat śaṅkarasya auduṃbaram rājatam svarṇa pīṭham vastra ādi channam sarvam eva iha pīṭham ante kṛtvā budbudābhyām ca sṛṣṭim pīṭhe pīṭhe nāgam ekam purastāt kuryāt pīṭhe ca ūrddhvake nāga yugmam deva abhyāśe dakṣiṇe vāmatas ca japā puṣpam nāga madhye nidhāya madhye vastram dvādaśa prātiguṇye su śvetena tasya madhye maheśam liṅga ākāram pīṭha yuktam prapūjyam evam kṛtvā sādhakāḥ te tu sarve dattvā dattvā puṣpaiḥ patraiḥ śrītilaiḥ akṣataiḥ ca tila unmiśraiḥ kevalaiḥ ca prapūjya dhūpam dattvā vidhivat saṃprayuktam dīpam dattvā ca uktam eva upahāram pūjā śeṣam te samāpya atha sarve gītam nṛtyam tatra tatra api cakruḥ kāle ca asmin suvrate gautamasya śiṣyaḥ prāptaḥ śaṅkarātmā iti nāmnā unmatta veṣaḥ digvāsāḥ anekām vṛttim āsthitaḥ kvacid dvijāti pravaraḥ kvacid caṇḍāla sannibhaḥ śiva jñāna eka saṃpannaḥ parama ānanda nirbharaḥ saṃprāptaḥ bhojya velāyām gautamasya antikam yayau bubhuje guruṇā sākam kvacid ucchiṣṭam eva ca kvacid lihati tat pātram tūṣṇīm eva abhyagāt kvacid sarvadā tam guruḥ dṛṣṭvā karam ālaṃbya mandiram praviśya svīya pīṭhe tam upaveśya api abhojayat tasya cittam parijñātum kadācid atha suṃdarī ahalyā śiṣyam āhūya bhuṅkṣva iti prāha tam mudā nirdiṣṭaḥ guru patnyā tu bubhuje saḥ aviśeṣatas yathā papau hi pānīyam tathā vahnim api dvijāḥ kaṇṭakān anna vat bhuktvā yathāpūrvam atiṣṭhata kardamam kāṣṭha daṇḍam ca bhuktvā pītvā atha harṣitaḥ etādṛśaḥ muniḥ asau caṇḍāla sadṛśa ākṛtiḥ su jīrṇa upānahau haste gṛhītvā pralapan hasan antyaja ucita veṣaḥ ca vṛṣaparvāṇam abhyagāt vṛṣaparva īśayoḥ madhye digvāsāḥ samatiṣṭata vṛṣaparvā tam a jñātvā pīḍayitvā śiraḥ acchinat atīva kaluṣam hi āsīt tatrasthāḥ munayaḥ tathā gautamasya mahā śokaḥ saṃjātaḥ su mahātmanaḥ niryayau cakṣuṣaḥ vāri śokam saṃdarśayan iva kim anena kṛte pāpam yena chinnam idam śiraḥ mama prāṇa adhikasya iha sarvadā śiva yoginaḥ mama api maraṇam satyam śiṣya chadmā yatas guruḥ śaivānām dharma yuktānām sarvadā śiva vartinām maraṇam yatra dṛṣṭam syāt tatra no maraṇam dhruvam tat śrutvā hi asura ācāryaḥ sukraḥ prāha vidām varaḥ enam saṃjīvayiṣyāmi bhārgavam śaṅkara priyam tasmin mṛte atha śukraḥ api prāṇān tatyāja yogataḥ tasya evam hatim ājñāya prahlāda ādyāḥ diti īśvarāḥ devāḥ nṛpāḥ dvijāḥ sarve mṛtāḥ āsan tat adbhutam mṛtam āsīt atha balam tasya bāṇasya dhīmataḥ ahalyā śoka saṃtaptā ruroda uñcais punar punar vīrabhadraḥ mahā yogī sarvam dṛṣṭvā cukopa ha aho kaṣṭam ahokaṣṭam maheśāḥ bahavaḥ hatāḥ śivam vijñāpayiṣyāmi tena uktam karavāṇi atha namaskṛtvā virūpākṣam vṛtta sarvam atha uktavān brahmāṇam ca harim tatra sthitau prāha śivaḥ vacaḥ mad bhaktaiḥ sāhasam karma kṛtam jñātvā vara pradam gatvā paśyāmi he viṣṇo sarvam tat kṛta sāhasam iti uktvā vṛṣam āruhya vāyunā dhūta cāmaraḥ maheśa anumatim labdhvā hariḥ nāgāntake sthitaḥ ārakta nīla chatrābhyām śuśubhe lakṣma kaustubhaḥ śiva anumatyā brahmā api haṃsa ārūḍhaḥ abhavat tadā indragopa prabhā kāra chatrābhyām śuśubhe vidhiḥ indra ādi sarva devāḥ ca sva sva vāhana saṃyutāḥ atha te niryayuḥ sarve nānā vādya anumoditāḥ koṭi koṭi gaṇa ākīrṇāḥ gautamasya āśramam gatāḥ brahma viṣṇu maheśānāḥ dṛṣṭvā tat parama adbhutam sva bhaktam jīvayāmāsa vāma koṇa nirīkṣaṇāt śaṅkaraḥ gautamam prāha tuṣṭaḥ aham te varam vṛṇu vṛtam etat mayā deva trinetra śṛṇu ca aparam śiṣyaḥ ayam me mahābhāgaḥ heya ādeya ādi varjitaḥ prekṣaṇīyam mamatvena na ca paśyati cakṣuṣā na ghrāṇa grāhyam deveśa na pātavyam na ca itarat iti buddhvyā tathā kurvan sa hi yogī mahā yaśaḥ unmatta vikṛta ākāraḥ śaṅkara ātmā iti kīrtitaḥ na kaścid tam prati dveṣī na ca tam hiṃsayet api etat me dīyatām deva mṛtānām amṛtiḥ tathā sva aṃśena vāyunā deham āviśat jagat īśvaraḥ hari rūpaḥ śaṅkara ātmā mārutiḥ kapi sattamaḥ paryāyaiḥ ucyate adhīśaḥ sākṣāt viṣṇuḥ śivaḥ paraḥ ākalpateṣu pratyekam kāmarūpam upāśritaḥ mama ājñā kārakaḥ rāma bhaktaḥ pūjita vigrahaḥ ananta kalpam īśānaḥ sthāsyati prīta mānasaḥ tvayā kṛtam idam veśma vistṛtam su pratiṣṭitam nityam vai sarva rūpeṇa tiṣṭhāmaḥ kṣaṇam ādarāt samarcitāḥ prayāsyāmaḥ sva sva vāsam tatas param athā ābabhāṣe viśveśam gautamaḥ muni puṅgavaḥ ayogyam prārthayāmi īśa hi arthī doṣam na paśyati brahma ādya labhyam deveśa dīyatām yadi rocate atha īśaḥ viṣṇum ālokya gṛhītvā tad karam kare prahasan aṃbujābhākṣam iti uvāca sadāśivaḥ gaccha vā pārvatī geham yā kukṣim pūrayiṣyati ādiśya nandinam devaḥ dvāra adhyakṣam yathā ukta vat sa gatvā gautamam vā atha hi uktavān viṣṇu bhāṣaṇam saṃpādaya annam deveśāḥ bhoktu kāmāḥ vayam mune mṛdu śayyām samāruhya śayitau devatā uttamau anyonyam bhāṣaṇam kṛtvā prottasthatuḥ ubhau api gatvā taḍāgam gaṃbhīram srāsyantau deva sattamau munayaḥ rākṣasāḥ ca eva jala krīḍām pracakrire atha viṣṇuḥ maheśaḥ ca jala pānāni śīghratas cakratuḥ padma kiñjalka añjalinā hareḥ netre keśara saṃpātāt pramīlayata keśavaḥ hari uttamāṅgam bāhubhyām gṛhītvā saṃnyamajjayat unmajjayitvā ca punar punar ca api punar punar pīḍitaḥ sa hariḥ sūkṣmam pātayāmāsa śaṅkaram atha pādau gṛhītvā tam bhrāmayan vicakarṣa ha atāḍayat hvareḥ vakṣaḥ pātayāmāsa ca acyutam atha utthitaḥ hariḥ toyam ādāya añjalinā tatas śīrṣe ca eva akirat śaṃbhum atha śaṃbhuḥ atho hariḥ jala krīḍā saṃbhrameṇa visrasta jaṭa bandhanāḥ itare jaṭāsu ca muni īśvarāḥ ākāśe vānara īśaḥ tu nanarta ca nanāda ca vipañcīm vādayan vādyam lalitām gītim ujjagau su gītyā lalitā yāḥ tu āgāyata vidhāḥ daśa śuśrāva gītim madhurām śaṅkaraḥ loka bhāvataḥ svayam gāyati deveśe viśrāmam galadeśikam svaram dhruvam samādāya sarva lakṣaṇa saṃyutam sva dhārā amṛta saṃyuktam gānena evam aponayan gāyake madhuram gītam hanūmati kapi īśvare mlāna malmānam abhavat kṛśāḥ puṣṭāḥ tadā abhavan svām svām gītimataḥ sarve tiraskṛtya eva mūrcchitā tūṣṇībhūtam samabhavat deva ṛṣi gaṇa dānavam ekaḥ sa hanumān gātā śrotāraḥ sarve eva te sva sva vāha nama āruhya nirgatāḥ sarva devatāḥ plavaga tvam mayā ājñaptaḥ niḥśaṅkaḥ vṛṣam āruha mama ca abhimukhaḥ bhūtvā gāyasva aneka gāyanam atha āha kapi śārdūlaḥ bhagavantam maheśvaram vṛṣabha āroha sāmarthyam tava na anyasya vidyate sa tava vāhanam āruhya pātakī syām aham vibho mām eva āruha deveśa vihṝṅgaḥ śiva dhāraṇaḥ tava ca abhimukham gānam kariṣyāmi vilokaya atha īśvaraḥ hanūmantam āruroha yathā vṛṣam ārūḍhe śaṅkare deve hanumat kandharām śivaḥ chitvā tvacam parāvṛtya sukham gāyati pūrvavat śṛṇvan gīti sudhām śaṃbhuḥ gaunta masya gṛham tatas sarve ca api āgatāḥ tatra deva ṛṣi gaṇa dānavāḥ yat śuṣkam dāru saṃbhūtam gṛha upakaraṇa ādikam prarūḍham abhavat sarvam gāyamāne hanūmati tasmin gāne samastānām citram dṛṣṭiḥ atiṣṭata dvi bāhuḥ īśasya danaḥ samasta gātra ābharaṇa upapannaḥ śiraḥ karābhyām parigṛhya śaṅkaraḥ hanūmataḥ pūrva mukham cakāra nidhāya pādam tu aparam mukhe ca pāda aṅgulībhyām atha nāsikām vibhuḥ snehena jagrāha ca mandamandam tatas ca kukṣau atha nābhi maṇḍalam pādam dvitīyam vidadhāti ca añjalau śiraḥ gṛhītvā avanamayya śaṅkaraḥ pasparśa pṛṣṭham cibukena saḥ adhvani hāram ca muktā parikalpitam śivaḥ hanūmataḥ kaṇṭha gatam cakāra hanūmatā samaḥ nā asti kṛtsna brahmāṇḍa maṇḍale yama ādi sādhanaiḥ ṃyogaiḥ na kṣaṇam te padam sthiram mahā yogi hṛd aṃbhoje param svastham hanūmati bhaktyā saṃpūjitaḥ api īśa pādaḥ naḥ darśitaḥ tvayā loke vādaḥ hi su mahān śaṃbhuḥ nārāyaṇa priyaḥ tat śrutvā vacanam śaṃbhuḥ viṣṇoḥ prāha mudā anvitaḥ atha ācamya mahādevaḥ viṣṇunā sahitaḥ vibhuḥ ratna aṅgulīya iratha nūpurābhyām dukūla bandhena taḍit su kāñcyā hāraiḥ anekaiḥ atha kaṇṭha niṣka yajñopavīta uttara vāsasī ca vilaṃbi cañcat maṇi kuṇḍalena su puṣpa dhaṃmilla vareṇa ca eva pañcāṅga gandhasya vilepanena bāhu aṅgadaiḥ kaṅkaṇaka aṅgulīyaiḥ atho vibhūṣitaḥ śivaḥ niviṣṭaḥ uttama āsane sva saṃmukham harim tathā nyaveśayat varāsane deva śreṣṭhau hari īśau tau anyonya abhimukha sthitau triṃśat prabhedān bhakṣyān tu pāyasam ca caturvidham śatam śatam su kandānām śākānām ca prakalpitam pañcaviṃśatidhā sarpiḥ saṃskṛtam vyañjanam tathā śarkarā ādyam tathā cūta mocā kharjūra dāḍimam drākṣā ikṣu nāga raṅgam ca miṣṭam pakvam phala utkaram evamādīni ca anyāni dravyāṇi īśe samarpya ca dattvā apośānakam vipraḥ bhuñjadhvam iti ca abravīt bhuñjāna eṣu ca sarveṣu vyajanam sūkṣma vistṛtam gautamaḥ svayam ādāya śiva viṣṇū avījayat paśya viṣṇo hanūmantam katham bhuṅkte sa vānaraḥ vānaram paśyati harau maṇḍakam viṣṇu bhājane cakṣepa paśyatsu api maheśvaraḥ hanūmate dattavān ca sva ucchiṣṭam pāyasa ādikam a bhukte nūnam bhukte ca api kṛpā tava bāṇa liṅge svayaṃbhūte candrakānte hṛdi sthite cāndrāyaṇa samam jñeyam śambhoḥ naivedya bhakṣaṇam bhuktvā tu nirviśaṅkam vibhuṅkṣva tat atha asau jala saṃskāram kṛtavān gautamaḥ muniḥ ārakta su snigdha su sūkṣma gātrān anekadhā dhauta su śobhita aṅgān nadyāḥ saikata vedikām navatarām saṃchādya sūkṣma aṃbaraiḥ śuddhvaiḥ śvetataraiḥ atha upari ghaṭān toyena pūrṇān kṣipet liptvā nālaka jātim āstapuṭakam tat kaulakam kārikā cūrṇam candana candra raśmi viśadām mālām puṭa antam kṣipet kṛtvā atho mṛdutaram sūkṣma vastra khaṇḍena āveṣṭet sṛṇika mukham ca sūkṣma candram siṃcet śītaiḥ jalaiḥ ca api vāsitaiḥ sṛṇikām api saṃskṛtāḥ su āyatāḥ tatra narāḥ nāryaḥ athavā nṛpāḥ tad kanyāḥ vā kṣālita aṅgāḥ dhauta pādāḥ su vāsasaḥ bāhumūle ca kaṇṭhe ca vilipya asāṃdram eva ca puṣpa naddhva su keśāḥ tu tāḥ śubhāḥ syuḥ su nirmalāḥ evam eva arcitāḥ nāryaḥ āpta kuṅkuma vigrahāḥ yuvatyaḥ cāru sarva aṅgyaḥ nitarām bhūṣaṇaiḥ api etādṛś vanitābhiḥ vā naraiḥ vā dāpayet jalam te api prādāna samaye sūkṣma vastra alpa veṣṭanam evam sa kārayāmāsa gautamaḥ bhagavān muniḥ prakṣālita aṅghri hasteṣu gandha udvartita pāṇiṣu uñca āsana samāsīne devadeve maheśvare atha nīca samāsīnāḥ devāḥ sa ṛṣi gaṇāḥ tathā maṇi pātreṣu saṃveṣṭtha pūga khaṇḍān su dhūpitān a koṇān vartulān sthūlān a sūkṣmān a kṛśān api śveta patrāṇi saṃśodhya kṣiptvā karpūra khaṇḍakam cūrṇam ca śaṅkarāya atha nivedayati gautame gṛhāṇa deva tāṃbūlam iti ukta vacane munau kape gṛhāṇa tāṃbūlam prayaccha mama khaṇḍakān aneka phala bhoktṛ ātvāt vānaraḥ tu katham śuciḥ tat śrutvā tu virūpa akṣāḥ prāha vānara sattamam mad vākyāt akhilam śuddhyā id mad vākyāt amṛtam viṣam mad vākyāt akhilāḥ vedāḥ mad vākyāt devatā ādayaḥ mad vāṅkyāt dhvarma vijñānam mad vākyāt mokṣaḥ ucyate purāṇāni āgamāḥ ca eva smṛtayaḥ mama vākyataḥ atas gṛhāṇa tāṃbūlam mama dehi su khaṇḍakān hariḥ vāma kareṇa adhāt tāṃbūlam pūga khaṇḍakam tatatas patrāṇi saṃgṛhya tasmai khaṇḍān samarpayat karpūram agratas dattam gṛhītvā abhakṣayat śivaḥ deve tu kṛta tāṃbūle pārvatī mandara acalāt jayāvijayayoḥ hastam gṛhītvā ayāt muneḥ gṛham tvad artham devadeveśi aparādhaḥ kṛtaḥ mayā yat tvām vihāya bhuktam hi tathā anyat śṛṇu suṃdari nirgacchantīm muniḥ jñātvā daṇḍa vat praṇanāma ha atha āha gautamaḥ devīm pārvatīm prekṣya sa smitām kṛtakṛtyaḥ bhaveyam vai bhuktāyām mad gṛhe tvayi tatas prāha śivā vipram gautamam racita añjalim bhokṣyāmi tvad gṛhe vipra śaṅkara anumatena vai atha gatvā śivam viṃśe labdha anujñaḥ tvarā gataḥ bhojayāmāsa girijām devīm ca arundhatīm tathā bhuktvā atha pārvatī sarva gandha puṣpa ādi alaṅkṛtā saṃdhyā upāstim aham kṛtvā hi āgamiṣye tava antikam saṃdhyā vadana kāmāḥ tu sarve eva vinirgatāḥ kṛta saṃdhyāḥ taḍāge tu maheśa ādyāḥ ca kṛtsnaśas atha uttara mukhaḥ śaṃbhuḥ nyāsa kṛtvā jajāpa ha atha viṣṇuḥ mahā tejāḥ maheśam idam abravīt hūyatam sarva yajñeṣu sa bhavān kim japiṣyati sa bhavān devadeveśaḥ kasmai viracita añjaliḥ namaskāra ādi puṇyānām phala daḥ tvam maheśvara ra tat śrutvā śaṅkaraḥ prāha devadevam janārdanam kintu nāstika jantūnām pravṛtti artham idam mayā darśanīyam hare ca etat anyathā pāpa kāriṇaḥ tasmāt loka upakāra artham idam sarvam kṛtam mayā atha te gautama gṛham prāptāḥ devarṣayaḥ tadā devaḥ hanūmatā sārddhvam gāyan āste muni īśvara pañcākṣarīm mahāvidyām sarve eva tadā ajapan hanumat karam ālaṃbya devābhyām saṃgataḥ haraḥ eka śayyā samāṃsīnau tau ubhau deva daṃpatī gāyan āste ca hanumān tuṃburu pramukhāḥ tathā nānāvidha vilāsān ca cakāra parameśvaraḥ āhūya pārvatīm īśaḥ idam vākyam uvāca ha devī āha na ca yuktam tad bharttrā śuśrūṣaṇam striyaḥ keśa prasādhana kṛtau anartha antaram āpatet tatas carama saṃlagna keśa puṣpa ādi mārjanam na āyānti ced atha vibho bhītiḥ nāśam upaiṣyati evam hi bhāṣamāṇām tām kareṇa ākṛṣya śaṅkaraḥ viṣṇu dattām pārijāta srajam kaca gatām api kṛtvā dhaṃmillam akarot atha mālām kara āgatām kalpaprasūna mālām ca brahmadattām maheśvaraḥ pārvatī vasane gūḍha gandha āḍhye ca samādadāt atha aṃsa pṛṣṭha saṃlagna mārjanam kṛtavān vibhuḥ ślathat nīveḥ adhas devyāḥ vastra veṣṭāt adhas gataḥ kim idam devi ca iti uktvā nīvī bandham cakāra ha nāsā bhūṣaṇam etat te satyam eva vadāmi te tatas prāha śivā śaṃbhum smitvā parvatanandinī pūrvam eva mayā sarvam jñāta prāyam abhūt kila śiraḥ vibhūṣitam deva brahmaśīrṣasya mālayā narakasya tathā mālā vakṣa sthala vibhūṇam śeṣaḥ ca vāsukiḥ ca eva sa viṣau tava kaṅkaṇau jaṭāḥ keśāḥ ca aṅgarāgakam mahā ukṣaḥ vāhanam gotram kulam ca ajñātam eva ca jñāyete pitarau nā eva virūpākṣam tathā vapuḥ evam vadantīm girijām viṣṇuḥ prāha ati kopanaḥ duṣprāṇā na priyā bhadre tava nūnam asaṃyamāt iti uktvā atha nakhābhyām hi hariḥ chettum śiraḥ gataḥ maheśaḥ tad karam gṛhya prāha mā sāhasam kṛthāḥ pārvatī vacanam sarvam priyam mama na ca apriyam mama apriyam hṛṣīkeśa kartum yat kiñcid iṣyate om iti uktvā atha bhagavān tūṣṇīṃbhūtaḥ abhavat hvariḥ hanumān atha devāya vyajñāpayat idam vacaḥ arthayāmi viniṣkāmam mama pūjā vratam tathā pūjā artham api aham gacche mām anujñātum arhasi tat śratvā śaṅkaraḥ devaḥ smitvā prāha vapīśvaram kasya pūjā kva vā pūjā kim puṣpam kim dalam vada kaḥ guruḥ kaḥ ca mantraḥ te kīdṛśam tathā evam vadati devaiśe hanumān nīti saṃyutaḥ namaḥ devāya mahate śaṅkarāya amita ātmane yoga gamyāya devāya jñāninām pataye namaḥ vedānām pataye tubhyam devānām pataye namaḥ dhyānāya dhyāna gamyāya dhyātṝṇām gurave namaḥ aṣṭamūrte namaḥ tubhyam paśūnām pataye namaḥ aṃbakāya trinetrāya soma sūrya agni cakṣuṣe su bhṛṅgarāja dhattūra droṇapuṣpa priyasya te bṛhatī pūga punnāga capaka ādi priyāya ca śiva liṅga arcanam kāryam bhasma uddhvūlita dehinā divā saṃpāditaiḥ taiyaiḥ puṣpa ādyaiḥ api tādṛśaiḥ deva vijñāpayiṣyāmi śiva pūja vidhim śubham sāyaṅkāle tu saṃprāpte aśiraḥsnānam ācaret kṣālitam vasanam śuṣkam dhṛtvā ācamya tris anya dhīḥ atha bhasma samādāya āgneyam snānam ācaret praṇavena samāmantrya vā pañca akṣareṇa mantreṇa nāmnā vā yena kenacid īśānaḥ sarva vidyānām uktvā śirasi pātayet sadyojātam prapadyāmi nikṣipet atha pādayoḥ uddhvūlayet samasta aṅgam praṇavena vicakṣaṇāḥ traivarṇikānām udita ṛ snāna ādi vidhiḥ uttamaḥ śūdra ādīnām pravakṣyāmi yat uktam guruṇā sapta vāram atha ādāya śivāya iti śirasi atha śaṅkarāya mukhe proktam sarvajñāya hṛdi kṣipet uccārya pādayoḥ kṣiptvā bhasma śuddhvam atas param namaḥ śivāya iti uccārya sarva aṅga uddhvūlanam smṛtam prakṣālya hastau ācamya darbha pāṇiḥ samāhitaḥ darbha abhāve suvarṇam syāt tad abhāve gavālukāḥ tad abhāve tu dūrvāḥ syuḥ tad abhāve tu rājatam saṃdhyā upāstim japam devyāḥ kṛtvā devagṛham vrajet devavedīm atho vā api kalpitam sthaṇḍilam tu vā mṛṇmayam kalpitam śuddhūm padma ādi racanā yutam cāturvarṇakaram gaiḥ ca śvetena ekena vā punar utpala ādi gadā śaṅkha triśūla ḍamarūn tathā śara ukta pañca prāsādam śiva liṅgam atha eva ca sarvakāmaphalam vṛkṣam kulakam kolakam tathā ṣaṣ koṇam ca tri koṇam ca nava koṇam atha api vā koṇe dvādaśaka āndolā pādukā vyajanāni ca cāmara chattra yugalam viṣṇu brahma ādikān tathā cūrṇaiḥ viracayet vedyām dhīmān devālaye api vā yācitam tu kaniṣṭam syāt balātkāram atho adhamam arheṣu yat tu anarheṣu balātkārāt tu niṣphalam raktaśāli japā śāṇa kalama asita raktakaiḥ āsanam ca pravakṣyāmi yathādṛṣṭam yathā śrutam kauśam cārmam caila talpe dāravam tālapatrakam kāṃbalam kāñcanam ca eva rājatam tāmram eva ca vaiyāghram rauravam ca eva hāriṇa mārgam eva ca darbha bhasma samāsīnaḥ prāṇān āyamya vāgyantaḥ tāvat sa devatā rūpaḥ dhyānam ca antar samācaret śikhā ante dvādaśa aṅgulye sthitam sūkṣma tanum śivam antar carantam bhūteṣu guhāyām viśvatomukham sarva ābharaṇa saṃyuktam imā ādi guṇa anvitam dhyātvā tam dhārayet citte tad dīptyā pūrayet tanum tayā dīptyā śarīra stham pāpam nāśam upāgatam svarṇa pādaiḥ asaṃparkāt raktam śvetam yathā bhavet tat dvādaśa dala āvṛttam aṣṭa pañca tris eva vā parikalpya āsanam śuddhavam tatra liṅgam nidhāya ca guhā sthitam maheśānam rliṅga īśam cintaya itthā śodhite kalaśe toyam śodhitam gandha vāsitam prāṇāyāmaḥ ca praṇavaḥ śūdreṣu na vidhīyate prāṇāyāma pade dhyānam śiva iti oṅkāra mantritam gandha puṣpa akṣata ādīni pūjā dravyāṇi yāni ca tāni sthāpya samīpe tu tatas saṃkalpa mācaret śiva pūjām kariṣyāmi śiva tuṣṭi artham eva ca kṛtvā tu snāna paryantam tatas snānam prakalpayet avicchinnā tu yā dhārā mukti dhārā iti kīrtitā tayā yaḥ snāpayet māṃsa eka vāram tri vāram ca pañca sapta nava api vā ekādaśa tathā vāram atha ekādaśadhā anvitam mukti snānam idam jñeyam māsam mokṣa pradāyakam śaivayā avidyayā snānam kevalam praṇavena vā kāṃsyena muktā śuktyā ca puṣpa ādi kesareṇa vā snāpayet devadeveśam yathāsaṃbhavam īritaiḥ śṛṅgasya ca vidhim vakṣye snāna yogyam yathā bhavet su grigdham laghu kṛtvā atha na aṅgam chindyāt kathaṃcana nīca eka deśa vinyasta dvāra droṇyā suhṛd tayā kṛśānu yuktam snānam tu devāya parikalpayet yoga vakram nāga daṇḍam nāga ākāram mukti dhārā kṛtā tena pavitra pāpa nāśanam vibhūṣya bhūṣaṇaiḥ devam punar snāpya maheśvaram śīta upacāram kṛtvā atha tatas ācamana ādikam karpūram agarum ca api pāṭīram athavā bhavet ubhaya miśritam ca api śiva liṅgam prapūjayet kṛtsnam pīṭham gandha pūrṇam yat vā vibhava sārataḥ tūṣṇīm atha upacāram vā kālīyam puṣpam eva ca śrīpanna maruci tyājyam yathāśakta khilam yathā kapilā ghṛta saṃyuktam sarva dhūpam praśasyate dhūpam da tvā yathāśakti kapilā ghṛta dīpakān athavā pūjā mātreṇa mukha śuddhim tatas kṛtvā dattvā tāṃbūlam ādarāt pradakṣiṇa namaskārau pūjā evam hi samāpyate gīti aṅga pañcakam paścāt tāni vijñāpayāmi te gītiḥ vādyam purāṇam ca nṛtyam hāsa uktiḥ eva ca nīrājanam ca puṣpāṇām añjaliḥ ca akhila arpaṇam kṣamāpanam ca udrasanam proktam pañca upacārakam bhūṣaṇam ca tathā chatram cāmara vyajane api ca kaikaryam ṣoḍaśa anupacārakān dvātriṃśat upacāraiḥ tu yaḥ samārādhayet śivam ekena ahnā samastānām pātakānām kṣayaḥ bhavet etat śrutvā hanumataḥ vacanam prāha śaṅkaraḥ evam etat kapi śreṣṭha yudh uktam pūjanam mama sāra bhūtam aham tubhyam upadekṣyāmi sāṃpratam ārādhanam yathā liṅge vistareṇa tvayā uditam mad pāda yugalam prārcya pūjā phalam avāpnuhi tatas prāha kapi śreṣṭhaḥ devadevam umāpatim guriṇā liṅga pūjā eva niyatā parikalpitā tām karomi purā deva paścāt tvad pāda pūjanam iti uktvā īśa namaskṛtya śiva liṅga arcanāya ca prakṣālya pādau hastau ca samācamya samāhitaḥ prāṇān āyamya saṃnyasya śulka dhyāna samanvitaḥ praṇamya gurum īśānam japan āsīt atas param palāśa patra puṭaka dvaya ānīta jalam śuci śiraḥ kamaṇḍalu gatam nidhāya agni nimantritam āvāhana ādi kṛtvā atha snāna paryantam eva ca atha snāpayitum devam ādāya kara saṃpuṭe kṛtvā nirīkṣaṇam devapīṭham naḥ dṛṣṭavān kapiḥ liṅga mātram kara gatam dṛṣṭvā bhīti samanvitaḥ idam āha mahā yogī kiṃvā pāpam mayā kṛtam yat etat pīṭha rahitam śiva liṅgam kara sthitam mama adya maraṇam siddham na pīṭham ca āgamiṣyati atha rudram japiṣyāmi tadā āyati maheśvaraḥ yadā tu na samāyātaḥ maheśaḥ atha kapi īśvaraḥ rudram nyapātayat bhūmau vīrabhadraḥ samāgataḥ pīṭha hīnam idam liṅgam paśya me pāpa saṃcayam vīrabhadraḥ tatas prāha śrutvā kapi samīritam yadi na āyāti pīṭham te liṅge mā sāhasam kuru dāhayiṣyāmi aham lokān yadi na āyāti pīṭhakam paśya darśaya me liṅgam pīṭham ca atra āgatam na vā dṛṣṭvā vīrabhadraḥ liṅge pīṭham anāgatam dagdhu kāmaḥ akhilān lokān vīrabhadraḥ prātāpavān analam bhuvi cikṣepa kṣaṇāt dagdhā mahī tadā lalāṭa netra saṃbhūtam nakhena ādāya ca analam jaṃbīra phala saṃkāśam kṛtvā kara tale vibhuḥ tapaḥ satyam ca saṃdagdhum udyataḥ abhūt muni īśvaraḥ tatas tu munayaḥ dṛṣṭvā atapaḥ loka nivāsinaḥ dagdhu kāmam vīrabhadram gautama āśramam āgatāḥ na dṛṣṭvā tatra deveśam śaṅkaram sva ātmani sthitam brahma ādi adhīśāya sṛṣṭi ādi kartre namaḥ te akhila adhīśvarāya aṃbarāya namaḥ te cara sthāvara vyāpakāya namaḥ te surā bindu varṣāpanāya trayī mūrtaye kāla kālāya nātha dharitrī marut vyoma toya indu vahni prabhā maṇḍala ātma aṣṭadhā mūrti dhartre śivāya aśiva ghnāya vīrāya bhūyāt sadā naḥ prasannaḥ jagannāthaka ijyaḥ ātmā mahātmā manaḥ hi agra yānaḥ nirūpyaḥ na vāgbhiḥ yatas saṃprasūtam jagat jātam īśāt sthitam yena rakṣāvatā bhāvitam ca layam yāsyate yatra vācām vidūre sa vai naḥ prasannaḥ astu kāla traya ātmā yadā ardi ca madhyam tathā antam na ke api vijānanti vijñāḥ api sva anumānāḥ etām stutim atha ākarṇya bhaga netra pradaḥ śivaḥ viṣṇum āha munīn etān ānayasva mad antikam atha viṣṇuḥ samāgatya tapoloka nivāsinaḥ munīn sāṃtvayya viśveśam darśayāmāsa śaṅkaram tān āha śaṅkaraḥ vākyam kimartham yūyam āgatāḥ tapolokāt bhūmilokam munayaḥ mukta kilbiṣāḥ tat śrutvā śūlinaḥ vākyam procuḥ te muni sattamāḥ deva dvādaśa lokānām dṛśyante bhasma rāśayaḥ tat śrutvā giriśaḥ prāha tān munīn ūrddharetasaḥ bhūrlokasya tu saṃdāhe pātālānām tathā eva ca ūrddhapañcaka lokānām dāhe saṃdehaḥ eva naḥ katham aṅgāra vṛṣṭiḥ ca katham no vā mahā dhvaniḥ tat ākarṇya vibhoḥ vākyam śaṅkarasya muni īśvarāḥ saḥ eva aṅgāra vṛṣṭim ca pipāsuḥ apibat vibhoḥ devaḥ atha vīram āhūya kim vīra iti abravīt vacaḥ vīraḥ api āha kapeḥ liṅge pīṭha abhāvāt idam kṛtam kapeḥ cittam parijñātum mayā kṛtam idam dvijāḥ mā bhaiṣṭa bhavatām saukhyam sadā saṃpādayāmi aham iti uktvā tu yathāpūrvam devadevaḥ kṛpā nidhiḥ dagdhān api akhilān lokān pūrvatas śobhanān vibhuḥ kalpayāmāsa viśvātmā vīrabhadram atha abravīt sādhu vatsa yatas bhadram bhaktānām īhase sadā tatas te vipulā kīrtiḥ loke sthāsyati śāśvatī iti uktvā āliṅgya śirasi samāghrāya maheśvaraḥ tāṃbūlam vīrabhadrāya dattavān prīta mānasaḥ atha asau hanumānī pūjanam kṛtavān yathā samāptāyām tu pūjāyām hanumān prīta mānasaḥ dadarśa tam atha abhyāha vīṇā me dīyatām iti gandharvaḥ api āha na mayā tyājyā vīṇā priyā mama mama api iṣṭā iham gandharva vīṇā iti āha kapi īśvaraḥ tadā muṣṭi prahāreṇa gandharvaḥ pātitaḥ kṣitau vīṇām ādāya mahatīm svara tantu samanvitām hanumān vānara śreṣṭhaḥ gāyan prāgāt śiva antikam bṛhatī kusumaiḥ śuddhaiḥ deva pādau apūjayat tatas prasannaḥ viśvātmā munīnām sannidhau tadā daityānām devatānām ca nṛpāṇām śaṅkaraḥ api ca tasmai varam atha prādāt kalpa antam jīvitam punar samullaṅghane śaktim śāstra jña tvam bala unnatim evam dattam varam prāpya maheśena mahātmanā samasta bhūṣāsu ṣita aṅgaḥ sva dīptiḥ madīkṛta deva dīptiḥ prasanna mūrtiḥ taruṇaḥ śiva aṃśaḥ saṃbhāvayāmāsa samasta devān ājñaptaḥ hanumān tatra mad sevāyai muni īśvaraḥ kim bahu uktena viprarṣe yādṛśaḥ vānara īśvaraḥ iti te sarvam ākhyātam caritam pāpa nāśanam paṭhatām śṛṇvatām ca eva gaccha vipra yathāsukham vacanam dakṣiṇīkṛtya natvā ca agām yathāgataḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne tṛtīya pāde hanumaccaritram nāma ekonāśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca śrutvā tu nāradaḥ viprāḥ kumāra vacanam muniḥ caritam ca mahat puṇyam śrutvā bhūyas abravīt vacaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca sādhu sādhu muni śreṣṭha tvayā ati karuṇa ātmanā śrāvitam caritam puṇyam śivasya ca hanūmataḥ krama prāptam kathanīyam ca yat tvayā tat prabrūhi mahābhāga kim pṛṣṭvā anyat vidām vara brahma ādyāḥ yān samārādhya sṛṣṭi ādi karaṇe kṣamāḥ kāmaḥ kṛṣṇa padam ṅatam govindam ca tathāvidham gopī janapadam paścāt vallabhāya agnisuṃdarī aṣṭādaśa arṇaḥ mantraḥ ayam durgā adhiṣṭhātṛ daivataḥ nāradaḥ asya muniḥ chandaḥ gāyatrī devatā punar śrī kṛṣṇaḥ paramātmā ca kāmaḥ bījam prakīrtitam ṛṣim śirasi vaktre tu chandaḥ ca hṛdi devatām guhye bījam padoḥ śaktim nyaset sādhaka sattamaḥ pañcāṅgāni pravinyasya tattva nyāsam samācaret hṛd antima ādika anta arṇam apara ādyāni ca ātmane mati antāni ca tatvāni jīva ādyāni nyaset kramāt jīvam prāṇam matim ahṝṅkāram manaḥ tathā eva ca śabdam sparśam rūpa rasau gandham śrotram tvacam tathā netram ca rasanā aṅghrāṇam vācam pāṇim pada indriyam pāyum śiśnam atha ākāśam vāyum vahnim jalam mahīm jīvam prāṇam ca sarva āge mati ādi tritayam hṛdi mūrdha āsya hṛd guhya pādeṣu atha śabda ādikān nyaset karṇa ādi sva sva sthāneṣu śrotra ādīni indriyāṇi ca tathā vāc ādi indriyāṇi sva sva sthānaṣu vinyaset mūd hasya hṛd guhya pādeṣu ākāśa ādīn nyaset tatas hṛd puṇḍarīkam arka indu hni biṃbāni anukramāt dvi ṣaṭhī aṣṭa daśa kalā vyāptāni ca tathā mataḥ bhūta aṣṭām ga akṣi pada gaiḥ varṇaiḥ pragvid nyaset hṛdi atha ākāśa ādi sthaleṣu vāsudeva ādikān tatas vāsudevaḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ pradyumnaḥ ca aniruddhakaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ ca kramaśas parameṣṭhi ādibhiḥ yutāḥ parameṣṭhi pumāñcchau ca viśva nivṛtti sarvakāḥ śveta anila agni ambu bhūmi varṇaiḥ prāgvat pravinyaset sva bīja ādyam nṛsiṃham vyāpakena ca makāra ādyāḥ ādya varṇāḥ sarve syuḥ candra bhūṣitāḥ vāsudeva ādikāḥ jñeyāḥ ṅeṃtāḥ sādhaka sattamaiḥ prāṇāyāmam tatas kṛtvā pūra kumbhaka recakaiḥ caturbhiḥ ṣaḍbhaḥ dvābhyām ca mūlamantreṇa mantra vid kecid āhuḥ iha ācāryāḥ prāṇāyāma uttaram punar pīṭhanyāsam vidhāya atha nyāsān anyān samācaret daśa tattva ādi vinyasya vakṣyamāṇa vidhānataḥ mūrtipañjara nāmānam pūrva uktam vinyaset budhaḥ sarva aṅge vyāpakam kṛtvā kirīṭa manunā sudhīḥ tatas tāra puṭam mantram vyāpayya karayoḥ triśas pañca aṅgulīṣu karayoḥ pañcāṅgam vinyaset tatas triśas mūlena mūrddha ādi pāda antam vyāpakam nyaset sakṛt vyāpayya tāreṇa mantra nyāsam tatas caret śiraḥ lalāṭe bhrū madhye karṇayoḥ cakṣuṣoḥ tathā ghrāṇayoḥ vadane kaṇṭhe hṛdi nābhau tathā punar kaṭyām liṅge jānunoḥ ca pādayoḥ vinyaset kramāt hṛd antān mantra varṇān ca tatas mūrdhni dhruvam nyaset vinyaset hṛdaya antāni manoḥ pañca padāni ca bhūyas muni ādikam nyasya pañcāṅgam pūrvavat nyaset yasya vijñāna mātreṇa jīvanmuktaḥ bhavet naraḥ aṇima ādi aṣṭa siddhīnām īśvaraḥ syāt na saṃśayaḥ yasya ārādhanataḥ mantrī kṛṣṇa saṃnidhya tām vrajet tārā ādyābhiḥ vyāhṛtibhiḥ saṃpuṭam vinyaset manum mantreṇa puṭitān ca api praṇava ādyān tatas nyaset gāyatryā mantram vinyaset mātṛkā sthale mantreṇa puṭitām tām ca gāyatrīm vinyaset kramāt mātṛkā puṭitam mūlam vinyaset sādhaka uttamaḥ mūlena puṭitām ca eva mātṛkām vinyaset kramāt tṛcam na mātṛkā varṇān pūrvam tad tad sthale sudhīḥ vinyaset nyāsa ṣaṭkam ca ṣoḍhā nyāsaḥ ayam īritaḥ anena nyāsa varyeṇa sākṣāt kṛṣṇa samaḥ bhavet nyāsena puṭitam dṛṣṭvā siddha gandharva kinnarāḥ devam dhyāyan sva hṛdaye sarva abhīṣṭa pradāyakam sasmeya mañjarī vṛnda vallarī veṣṭitaiḥ śubhaiḥ galat parāga dhūlibhiḥ surabhīkṛta diṅmukhaḥ smaret śiśiritam vṛndāvanam mantrī samāhitaḥ lubdha antar karaṇaiḥ guñjat dvirepha paṭalaiḥ śubham mukharīkṛtam ānṛtyat māyūra kula mañjulam unnidra aṃburuha vrāta rajobhiḥ dhūsaraiḥ śivaiḥ pradīpita smaraiḥ goṣṭha suṃdarī mṛdu vāsasām ratna kuṭṭima pīṭhe asmin aruṇam kamalam smaret pīta aṃśukam candra mukham sarasīruha netrakam kaustubha udbhāsita aṅgam ca śrīvatsa aṃkam subhūṣitam gopa vṛnda yutam vaṃśīm vādayantam smaret sudhīḥ evam dhyātvā japet ādau ayuta dvitayam budhaḥ juhuyāt aruṇa aṃbhojaiḥ tad daśa aṃśam samāhitaḥ japet paścāt mantra siddhyai bhūtalakṣam samāhitaḥ pūrva ukte vaiṣṇave pīṭhe mūrtim saṃkalpya mūlataḥ śrīvatsam ca hṛdi prārcya tatas puṣpa añjalim kṣipet tatas śvetām ca tulasīm śukla candana paṅkilām raktām ca tulasīm raktañcadana aktām krasāt sudhīḥ tatas sarvāṇi puṣpāṇi sarva aṅgeṣu samarpayet vāme ca rukmiṇīm raktām rajaḥ guṇām evam saṃpūjya gopālam kuryāt āvaraṇa arcanam yajet dāma sudāmau ca vasudāmam ca kiṅkiṇīm pūrva ādi āśāsu dāma ādyāḥ ṅeṃ namaḥ nta dhruva ādikāḥ agni nairṛti vāyu īśa koṇeṣu hṛdaya ādikān rukmiṇī satyabhāmā ca nāgnajitī abhidhā punar suvindā mitravindā ca lakṣmaṇā ca ṛkṣajā tatas su śīlā ca lasat ramya citrita aṃbara bhūṣaṇā gopān ū gopīḥ ca govinda vilīna mati locanān jñāna mudrā abhaya karau pitarau pīta pāṇḍurau divya mālya aṃbara ālepa bhūṣaṇe mātarau punar dhārayantyau carum ca eva pāyasīm pūrṇa pātrikām aruṇa śyāmale hāra maṇi kum ḍala maṇḍite balaḥ śaṅkha indu dhavalaḥ muśalam lāṅgalam dadhat hālā lolaḥ nīla vāsāḥ halavān eka kuṇḍalaḥ kalā yā śyāmalā bhadrā subhadrā bhadra bhūṣaṇā vara abhaya yutā pīta vasanā rūḍha yauvanā veṇu vīṇā hema yaṣṭi śaṅkha śṛṅga ādi pāṇayaḥ gopāḥ gopyaḥ ca vividha prābhṛta anna kara aṃbujāḥ mandāradīn ca tad bāhye pūjayet kalpapādapān mandāraḥ ca tathā saṃtānakaḥ vai pārijātakaḥ tad astrāṇi ca saṃpūjya yajet kṛṣṇa aṣṭakena ca kṛṣṇam ca vāsudevam ca devakīnandanam tathā nārāyaṇam yadu śreṣṭham vārṣṇeyam dharma pālakam asura ākrānta bhū bhāra hāriṇam pūjayet tatas ebhiḥ āvaraṇaiḥ pūjā kartavyā a sukhairiṇaḥ saṃsāra sāgara utthīrtyai sarva kāma āptaye budhaḥ evam pūjā ādibhiḥ siddhāḥ bhavat vaiśravaṇaḥ yamaḥ śrīmat udyāna saṃvīti hema bhū ratna maṇḍape su trāma ratna saṃkāśam guḍa snigdha alakam śiśum samuddhūsara urasthale dhenu dhūlyā su puṣṭa aṅgam aṣṭāpada ākalpa dīptam kaṭīla sthale cāru jaṅghā anta yugmam pinaddham kvaṇat kiṅkiṇī jāla dāmnā hasantam hasat vandhujīva prasūna prabhā pāṇi pāda aṃbuja udāra kāntyā dadhānam karaḥ dakṣiṇe pāyasa anna su haiyaṅgavīnam tathā vāma haste mahā bhāra bhūta amara arāti yūthān tatas pūtanā ādīn nihṝntum pravṛttam evam dhyātvā arccayet devam pūrvavat sthira mānasaḥ dadhnā guḍena naivedyam da tvā daśa śatam japet madhyandine yajet evam viśiṣya rūpa dhāriṇam nārada ādyaiḥ muni gaṇaiḥ sura vṛndaiḥ ca pūjitam lasat gopa gopī gavām sāṃdra megha prabham suṃndara aṅgam śikhaṇḍi chada āpīḍam abja āyata akṣam lasan cillikam pūrṇa cadra ānanam ca calat kuṇḍala ullāsi gaṇḍa sthala śrī bharam sundaram manda hāsam su nāsam su kārtasvara ābha aṃbaram divya bhūṣam kvaṇat kiṅkiṇī jāla matta anulepam veṇum dhamantam sva kare dadhānam savye daram yaṣṭim udāra veṣam evam dhyātvā arcayet kṛṣṇam pūrvavat vaiṣṇava uttamaḥ hutvā ca aṣṭattaraśatam payaḥ anaiḥ sarpiṣā āplutaiḥ sva sva dikṣu balim dadyāt diśet ācamanam tatas ahnaḥ madhye yajet evam yaḥ kṛṣṇam vaiṣṇava uttamaḥ devāḥ sarve namasyanti lokānām vallabhaḥ naraḥ medhā āyuḥ śrī kānti yuktaḥ putraiḥ pautraiḥ ca varddhate tṛtīya kāla pūjāyām asti kāla vikalpanā daśa akṣareṇa ced rātrau sāyāhne aṣṭādaśa arṇataḥ sāyāhne dvāravatyām tu citra udyāna upaśobhite aṣṭa sāhasra saṃkhyātaiḥ bhavanaiḥ upamaṇḍite haṃsa sārasa saṃkīrṇa kamala utpala śālibhiḥ hema aṃbhoja āsana āsīnam kṛṣṇam trailokya mohanam unnidra idīvara śyāmam padma patra āyata īkṣaṇam kāśmīra kapiśa uraskam pīta kauśeya vāsasam hāra keyūra kaṭaka kaṭi sūtraiḥ alaṅkṛtam hṛta viśvaṃbharā bhūri bhāram mudita mānasam śaṅkha cakra gadā padma rājat bhuja catuṣṭayam evam dhyātvā arcayet mantrī syāt aṅgaiḥ prathama āvṛttiḥ dvitīyā mahiṣībhiḥ tu tṛtīyāyām samarcayet nāradam parvatam jiṣṇum niśaṭha uddhava dārukān lokapālaiḥ ca vajra ādyaiḥ pūjayet vaiṣṇava uttamaḥ japet aṣṭaśatam mantrī bhāvayan puruṣottamam pūjāsu homam sarvāsu kuryāt madhyandine athavā āsanāt arghya paryantam kṛtvā stutvā namet sudhīḥ samartha ātmānam udvāsya svīya hṛd sarasīruhe sarvān kāmān avāpya ante sa yāti paramām gatim yajet rāsa pariśrāntam gopī maṇḍala madhya gam rajobhiḥ dhūsaraiḥ manda mārutaiḥ śiśirīkṛte pīyūṣa aṃśu karaiḥ viśālita harit prānte smara uddīpane kālindī pulina aṅgaṇe smita mukham veṇum raṇantam muhur antar toya lasat nava aṃbuda ghaṭā saṃghaṭṭa kāra tviṣam cañcat cillikam aṃbuja āyata dṛśam bimba adharam sundaram kāñcī nūpura hāra kaṅkaṇa lasat keyūra bhūṣā anvitam gopīnām dvitayām tare su lalitam vanya prasūna srajam bhramamāṇam amūbhiḥ udāra maṇi sphuṭa maṇḍana siṃjita cāru tanum evam dhyātvā arcayet mantrī syāt aṅgaiḥ prathama āvṛtiḥ śrī kāmaḥ sa svara ādyāni kalā abjaiḥ vaiṣṇava uttamaḥ yajet keśava kīrti ādi mithunāni ca ṣoḍaśa pṛnthu su vṛttam masṛṇam vitasti mātra unnatam kau vinikhanya śaṅkum stutvā natvā ca saṃprārthya pūjā śeṣam samāpayet evam yaḥ pūjayet kṛṣṇam sa sa smṛddheḥ padam bhavet aṇima ādi aṣṭa siddhīnām īśvaraḥ syāt na saṃśayaḥ evam pūjā ādibhiḥ siddhe manau kāmyāni sādhayet aṣṭāviṃśati vāram vā tri kālam pūjayet sudhīḥ sva kāla vihitān bhūyas parivārān ca tarpayet prātar dadhnā guḍa aktena madhyāhne payasā punar sa sitopala miśreṇa payasā vaiṣṇava uttamaḥ tarpayāmi padam yojyam mantra ante sveṣu nāmasu dvitīya anteṣu tu punar pūjā śeṣam samāpayet abhyukṣya tad prasāda adbhiḥ ātmānam prapabet apaḥ atha dravyāṇi kāmyeṣu procyante tarpaṇeṣu ca tāni prokta vidhānānām āśritya anyatamam bhajet pāyasam dādhikam ca ājyam gauḍa annam kṛsaram payaḥ dadhīni kadalī mocā ciñcā rajasvalā tathā apūpāḥ modakāḥ lājāḥ pṛthukāḥ navanītakam dravya ṣoḍaśakam hi etat kathitam padmaja ādibhiḥ dhyātvā kṛṣṇa padam matrī maṇḍala ādiṣṭam āpnuyāt dhārā uṣṇa pakka payasā navanītam dadhīni ca matsyaṇḍī kṣaudram kīlālam eva ca evam aṣṭotaraśatam saṃkhyākam tarpaṇam punar yaḥ kuryāt vaiṣṇava śreṣṭhaḥ pūrva uktam phalam āpnuyāt kim bahu uktena sarva iṣṭa dāyakam tarpaṇam tu idam kṛṣṇam prataparyan grāmam vrajan prāpnoti sādhakaḥ dhana vastrāṇi bhojyam ca parivāra gaṇaiḥ saha tarpaṇena eva kāryāṇi sādhayet akhilāni api kāmya homam atho vakṣye sādhakānām hitāya ca śrī puṣpaiḥ juhuyāt mantrī śriyam icchan nininditām sa ājyena annena juhuyāt ghṛta annasya samṛddhaye vanya puṣpaiḥ dvijān jātī puṣpaiḥ ca pṛthivīpatīn asitaiḥ kusumaiḥ vaiśyān śūdrān nīlotpalaiḥ tathā vaśayet lavaṇaiḥ sarvān aṃbujaiḥ yuvatī janam go śālāsu kṛtaḥ homaḥ pāyasena sa sarpiṣā gavām śāntim karoti āśu gopālaḥ go kula īśvaraḥ śikṣā veṣa dharam kṛṣṇam kiṅkiṇī jāla śobhitam dhanam dhānyam sutān kīrtim prītaḥ tasmai dadāti saḥ vaśaye d brāhmaṇān ca atha rājavṛkṣa samudbhavaiḥ prasūnaiḥ kṣatriyān vaiśyān kuraṇḍa kusumaiḥ tathā pāṭalā utthaiḥ ca kusumaiḥ vaśayet antimān sudhīḥ śvetapadmaiḥ raktapapdaiḥ caṃpakaiḥ pāṭalaiḥ kramāt hutvā ayutam trimadhu āktaiḥ vaśayet tat vara aṅganāḥ vara strīḥ vaśayet prājñaḥ samyak dhṛtvā dina aṣṭakam pratyaham juhvataḥ māsāt sureśaḥ api vaśībhavet āhṛtya ballavī vastrāṇi ārūḍham nīpa bhūruhe smaret kṛṣṇam japet rātrau sahasram kha indu ūhāt sudhīḥ haṭhāt ākarṣayet śīghram urvaśīm api sādhakaḥ rahasyam paramam ca atha vakṣye mokṣa pradam nṛṇām vande vedyam muni indraiḥ kaṇika muni lasat divya bhūṣā abhirāmam divya aṅga ālepa bhāsam sakala bhaya haram pīta vastram nurārim evam dhyātvā pumāṃsam sphuṭa hṛdaya saroja āsana āsīnam ādyam sāṃdra aṃbhoda accha biṃba adbhuta kanaka nibham saṃjapet arka lakṣam evam lokeśvara ārādhyam kṛṣṇam sva hṛdaya aṃbuje sāyāhna uktena vidhinā saṃpūjya havanam punar kṛtvā pūrva ukta vidhinā mantrī tad gata mānasaḥ madhye keṇeṣu bāhyeṣu analapura puṭasya ālikhet karṇikāyām kandarpam sādhya yuktam vivara gata ṣaṣ arṇa dviṣaḥ keśareṣu śaktiḥ śrī pūrvika aṇi dvi nava lipi manoḥ rakṣa rāṇi chadānām madhye varṇān daśa antaḥ daśa lipi manu varyasya vā ekaikaśas abjam smaraḥ trivikrama ākrāntaḥ ca ākrīṣṭyāya hṛd iti asau ṣaṣ akṣaraḥ ayam saṃproktaḥ sarva siddhi karaḥ manuḥ kroḍaḥ śānti indu vahni āḍhyaḥ govinda vahni candra āḍhyaḥ manuḥ śrī bījam īritam ābhyām aṣṭādaśa klipaḥ syāt viṃśati akṣaraḥ manuḥ śālagrāme maṇau yantre maṇḍale pratimāsu vā nityam pūjā hareḥ kāryā na tu kevala bhū tale evam yaḥ bhajante kṛṣṇam sa yāti paramām gatim viṃśa arṇasya muniḥ brahmā gāyatrī chandaḥ īritam kṛṣṇaḥ ca devatā kāmaḥ bījam śaktiḥ dviṭhaḥ budhaiḥ mūlena vyāpakam kṛtvā manunā puṭitān atha mātṛkā arṇān nyaset tad tad sthāneṣu su samāhitaḥ śīrṣe lalāṭe bhrū madhye netrayoḥ karṇayoḥ tathā kaṭyām jānvoḥ jaṅghayoḥ ca gulphayoḥ pādayoḥ kramāt nyaset hṛd antāt mantrāṇām sṛṣṭinyāsaḥ ayam īritaḥ kaṭyām jānvoḥ jaṅghayoḥ ca gulphayoḥ pādayoḥ tathā namotān mantra varṇān ca sthiti nyāsaḥ ayam īritaḥ kaṭyām mūle dhvaje nābhau jaṭhare hṛdaye punar mūrdhni nyaset mantra varṇān saṃhāra ākhyaḥ ayam īritaḥ punar sṛṣṭi sthiti nyāsau vidhāya vaiṣṇava uttamaḥ mūrtipañjara nāmānam vinyaset pūrvavat tatas punar ṣaḍaṅgam kṛtvā atha dhyāyet kṛṣṇam hṛd aṃbuje analpaiḥ kalpavṛkṣaiḥ ca parīte maṇi maṇḍape udyat āditya saṃkāśa maṇi siṃhāsana aṃbuje sarva aṅga suṃdaraḥ saumyaḥ sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitaḥ vāma pāda aṃbuja agreṇa muṣṇatā pallava chavim nāgnajitī sunandā ca diśantyau kalaśau tayoḥ tābhyām ca dakṣa vāma stha mitravindā su lakṣmaṇe ratna nadyāḥ samuddhṛtya ratna pūrṇauṃ ghaṭau tayoḥ jāṃbavatī suśīlā ca diśantyau dakṣa vāmake bahis ṣoḍaśa sāhasra saṃkhyākāḥ paritas priyāḥ dhyeyāḥ kanaka ratna ogha dhārā yuj kalaśa ujvalāḥ tad bahis ca aṣṭa nidhāyaḥ pūrayantaḥ dhanaiḥ dharām tad bahis vṛṣṇayaḥ sarve purovat ca svara ādayaḥ evam dhyātvā japet lakṣa pañcakam tad daśa aṃśataḥ aruṇaiḥ kamalaiḥ hutvā pīṭhe pūrva udite yajet karṇikāyām ca ṣaṣ koṇam sa sādhyam tatra manmatham śiṣṭaiḥ tu saptadaśabhiḥ akṣaraiḥ veṣṭayet svaram prāk rakṣaḥ anila koṇeṣu śriyam śiṣṭeṣu saṃvidam ṣaṭsu saṃdhiṣu ṣaṣ karṇe kesareṣu triśas triśas vilikhet smara gāyatrīm mālāmantram dala aṣṭake saṃlikhya tad bāhye veṣṭayet mātṛkā akṣaraiḥ bhū biṃbam ca likhet bāhye śrī māyā diś vidikṣu api bhū graham catur asram syāt aṣṭa vajra vibhūṣitam etat yantram hāṭaka ādi paṭṭeṣu ālikhya pūrvavat syāt gāyatrī vāmadeva puṣpabāṇau tu ṅeṃtimau japyā japa ādau gopāla manūnām jana rañjanī hṛdayam kāmadevāya ṅeṃtam sarva jana priyam hṛdayam mama ca brūyāt vaśaṅkuru yugam śiraḥ proktaḥ madana mantraḥ aṣṭacatvāriṃśadbhiḥ akṣaraiḥ japa ādau smarabīja ādyaḥ jagattraya vaśīkaraḥ prāgvat samabhyarcya mūrti saṃkalpya mūlataḥ tatra āvāhya acyutam bhaktyā sakalīkṛtya pūjayet āsana ādi vibhūṣā antam punar nyāsa kramāt yajet sṛṣṭim sthitim ṣaṣ aṅgam ca kirīṭam kuṇḍala dvayam śaṅkham cakram gadām padmam mālām śrīvatsa kaustubhau ṣaṣ koṇeṣu ṣaṣ aṅgāni diś daleṣu kramāt yajet vāsudeva ādikān koṇeṣu tu śānti ādikān tatas patra agra gāḥ mahiṣyaḥ aṣṭau yajet sādhaka sattamaḥ tatas ṣoḍaśa sāhasram sakṛt eva arcayet priyāḥ indranīla mukundān ca karāla ānanda kacchapān śaṅkha padmau tatas padmān nidhīn aṣṭau kramāt yajet tad bahis lokapālān ca vajra ādyān api pūjayet evam sapta āvṛtti vṛtam kṛṣṇam abhyarcya ca ādarāt prīṇayet dadhi khaṇḍa ājya miśreṇa tu divya upacāram da tvā atha stutvā natvā ca keśavam ratna abhiṣeka dhyāna ijyā viṃśati arṇa āśrite ritā pṛthvī pṛthvī kare tasya sarva sasya samākulā tasya anna ādi samṛddhiḥ syāt tat ūśe sarva yoṣitaḥ śriyā tasya aindram aiśvaryam tṛṇaleśāyate dhruvam evamādi prayogān ca sādhayet manunā amunā smṛtiḥ sadyā anvitā sākṣiḥ lohitaḥ jana vallabhā pavanaḥ agni priya antaḥ ayam daśa arṇaḥ mantraḥ īritaḥ nāradaḥ asya muniḥ chandaḥ virāj kṛṣṇaḥ asya devatā kāmaḥ bījam vahnijāyā śaktiḥ proktā manīṣibhiḥ etaiḥ ṅeṭha dvaya antaiḥ ca cakraiḥ pañca aṅgakam manoḥ tatas tāra puṭam mantram vyāpayya karayoḥ triśas sa iṃdūn hṛd antān mantra arṇān praṇava antaritān nyaset dakṣa aṅguṣṭhāt ca vāma aṅguṣṭha antam aṅguli parvasu sṛṣṭi nyāsaḥ ayam uditaḥ sthiti nyāsaḥ adhunā ucyate nyaset vāma kaniṣṭhā ādi kaniṣṭha antam sthitau sudhīḥ vāma aṅguṣṭhān nyaset dakṣām guṣṭha antam saṃhṛtau tathā saṃhṛtiḥ deṣa saṃghāta hāriṇī parikīrtitā vidyā pradaḥ ca sṛṣṭi antaḥ varṇinām śuddha cetasām sthiti antaḥ syāt gṛhasthānām evam kāmya ādi rūpataḥ saṃhāra ante muni indrāṇām viraktānām ca sarvaśas punar sthiti krameṇa arṇān manoḥ aṅguliṣu nyaset punar cakraiḥ ca pūrva uktaiḥ pañca agam karayoḥ nyaset tatas mūlena puṭitān mātṛkā arṇān sa bindukān vinyaset mātṛkā nyāsa sthāneṣu praṇataḥ sudhīḥ tatas tāra puṭam mūlam vyāpaka tvena vinyaset saṃhāra sṛṣṭi bhedena daśa tattvāni vinyaset namaḥ nta mūlamantra arṇa pada āyāmyāni ca ātmane pṛthvī jalam tathā vahniḥ vāyuḥ ākāśam eva ca ahṝṅkāraḥ prakṛtim puruṣam param vadane hṛdaye nābhau liṅge jānvoḥ ca pādayoḥ praṇava antaritān varṇān hṛd antān vijyaset manoḥ sṛṣṭi nyāsaḥ ayam ākhyātaḥ sthiti nyāsam śṛṇu dvija padoḥ jānvoḥ liṅga deśe nābhau hṛdi mukhe nasoḥ karṇayoḥ netrayoḥ mūrdhni saṃhāra ākhyaḥ ayam īritaḥ sṛṣṭi antaḥ varṇinām nyāsaḥ sthiti antaḥ gṛhamedhinām yateḥ vairāgya yuktasya saṃhāra antaḥ prakīrtitaḥ caturddhā varṇinām ca eva gṛhasthānām ca pañcadhā yatīnām ca tridhā nyāsaḥ proktaḥ ayam kramatas śubhaḥ kecid virakte gṛha ge saṃhāra antam viduḥ budhāḥ vibhūtipañjaram nyāsam kuryāt iṣṭa āptaye tatas manoḥ daśa āvṛtti mayam kṛṣṇa sāṃnidhya kārakam ādhāre ca dhvaje nābhau hṛdi kaṇṭhe mukhe śaye ūrvoḥ ca kandharāyām ca nābhau kukṣau tathā hṛdi stanayoḥ pārśvayoḥ śroṇyoḥ mastake vadane tathā netrayoḥ karṇayoḥ nāsā puṭayoḥ ca kapolayoḥ evam dakṣiṇa dos mūsa saṃdhi agreṣu aṅgulīṣu ca tatas śirasi tad pūrva ādya aṃśāsu sva kalāsu ca doṣṇoḥ sakthnoḥ śira ukṣi āsya kaṇṭha hṛd jaṭhareṣu ca mūlādhāre liṅga deśe jānunoḥ pādayoḥ tathā śrotra gaṇḍa aṃsa vakṣoja pārśva liṅgeṣu vinyaset vibhūtipañjara ākhyaḥ ayam nyāsaḥ sarva artha siddhi daḥ anena nyāsa varyeṇa sākṣāt kṛṣṇa tanuḥ bhavet mūrti pañjara nāmānam nyāsam pūrva uditam nyaset tatas daśa aṅga pañcāṅgau nyāsa varyaum nyase kramāt hṛdi mūrdhni śikhāyām ca sarva aṅge dikṣu pārśvayoḥ kaṭyām pṛṣṭhe tathā mūrdhni vinyaset vaiṣṇava uttamaḥ pañcāṅgāni nyaset bhūyas cakraiḥ prāgvat samāhitaḥ anyaḥ api aṣṭādaśa arṇa uktaḥ kartavyaḥ nyāsa saṃcayaḥ tatas kirīṭamantreṇa vyāpakam racayet sudhīḥ veṇu bilva ādi mudrān ca darśayet sādhaka uttamaḥ an aṅguṣṭhāḥ ca ṛjavaḥ karaśākhāḥ bhavanti ced hṛnmudrā iyam samākhyātā śiraḥ mudrā tathā bhavet adhas uṅguṣṭhā tu yā muṣṭiḥ śikhāmudrā iyam īritā nārāca muṣṭyā dhṛta bāhu yugmaḥ aṅguṣṭha tarjanī uditaḥ dhvaniḥ tu oṣṭhe vāma kara aṅguṣṭaḥ lagnaḥ tasya kaniṣṭikā dakṣiṇa aṅguṣṭa saṃsaktā tad kaniṣṭhā prasāritā tarjanī cālitā na ucyante tatra siddha tvāt mālā śrīvatsa kaustubhāḥ vāma aṅguṣṭham sa mudram tam apara kara aṅguṣṭhakena atha baddhvā saṃpīḍya agram ca dakṣa aṅgulibhiḥ api ca tām vāma hasta aṅgulībhiḥ gāḍham baddhvā svakīye hṛdaya sarasije sthāpayet kāmabījam proccārya eṣā tu gopyā sakala sukha karī vilva mudrā muni indraiḥ kāyena manasā vācā yat pāpam samupārjitam mudrāyāḥ jñāna mātreṇa sarvam nāśam upaiṣyati dhyānam japaḥ tri kāla arcā kāryā pūrva uditā manoḥ sarveṣu ekaḥ kramaḥ proktaḥ daśa arṇa aṣṭādaśa arṇayoḥ uddaṇḍa bāhu dos daṃha dhṛta govarddhana acalam anya hasta agulī vyakta svara vaṃśa arpita ānanam dhyāyan kṛṣṇam japet mantram vrajet chatram vinā sudhīḥ varṣa vāta aśanibhyaḥ api bhayam tasya na jāyate loṇaiḥ ayuta saṃkhyaiḥ syāt anāvṛṣṭiḥ na saṃśayaḥ krīḍantam arkajā tīre majjana snāpana ādibhiḥ tat śīkara jala āsāraiḥ sicyamānam priyā janaiḥ dhyātvā ayutam payaḥ siktaiḥ hunet vā nīra tarpaṇaiḥ vṛṣṭiḥ bhavati akāle api mahatī na atra saṃśayaḥ athavā garuḍa ārūḍham pradyumna bala saṃyutam nija jvara niṣpiṣṭa jvara abhiṣṭutam acyutam juhuyāt amṛtā khaṇḍaiḥ ayutam jvara śāntaye śilīmukha vinirbhinna bhīṣma tāpa haram harim dhyātvā japet spṛśan ārtam pāṇibhyām jvara śāntaye sāṃdīpanāya dadatam putram dhyātvā ayutam hunet yathā uktaiḥ amṛta akhaṇḍaiḥ apamṛtyu nivṛttaye sutam dhyātvā japet lakṣam putra pautra ādi vṛddhaye tad kāṣṭhaiḥ edhite vahnau sutān dīrgha āyuṣaḥ labhet kṣīra druh tvātha saṃpūrṇam abhyarcya kalaśam niśi prātar japtvā ayutam nārīm abhiṣiñcet diṣaṣ dinam evam kṛte tu vandhyā api labhet putrān cira āyuṣaḥ prātar vācaṃyama aśvattha dala saṃpuṭakam jalam aṣṭottaraśatam japtam māsam putra arthinī pibet jitvā kṛtyām kāśi rāja preṣitām ca nija ariṇaḥ kṛtyā kartāram eva asmai kupitā nāśayet dhruvam badarī druma saṃkīrṇe sthitam divya āśrame śubhe spṛśantam kara padmābhyām ghaṇṭā karṇa kalevaram mahā pāpa yutaḥ api evam pūtaḥ bhavati tad kṣaṇāt juhuyāt iṣṭayoḥ dviṣṭyai gulikāḥ gomaya udbhavāḥ varṣantam garuḍa ārūḍham jvalat agni mukhaiḥ śaraiḥ uccāṭanam bhavati eva śatrūṇām saptabhiḥ dinaiḥ prajapet ayutam śatrum uñcāṭayati tad kṣaṇāt ātmānam kaṃsa mathanam dhyāyan mañcāt nipātitam kaṃsa ātmānam vyakarṣantam gatāsum tam japet manum niśā ādiṣṭa dala vyoṣa kārpāsa asthi karaiḥ niśi hunet eraṇḍa taila aktaiḥ śmaśāne ripu śāntaye na śastam māraṇam karma kuryyāt ced ayutam hunet pāyasaiḥ vā hunet tāvat śāntaye śānta mānasaḥ pārijāta haram kṛṣṇam dhyāyan lakṣam japet manum vyākhyā mudrā karam kṛṣṇam ratha stham bhāvayan japet pārthe diśantam gīta artham dharma vṛddhyai su mānavaḥ pāvāśa puṣpaiḥ madhu aktaiḥ lakṣam vidyā āptaye hunet rāṣṭra pūḥ grāma vastūnām śarīrasya api rakṣaṇe agrīṣoma ātmakam kṛṣṇam druta cāmīkara prabham arka agni dyotita āsya aṅghrim praṅkaja divya bhūṣaṇam nānā āyudha dharam prāptam viśva ākāśa avakāśakam dhyātvā lakṣa japet mantram rakṣaṇāya samāhitaḥ sahasra maṇḍalān mantrī vaśayet mukharān dvijān jāti puṣpaiḥ kṣatriyān ca gopa veṣa dharam smaran dhyāyan krīḍā ratam kṛṣṇam raktaiḥ aśva ari puṣpakaiḥ vaśayet vaiśya jātīyān śūdrān nīlotpalaiḥ smaran gīta nṛtya ratam śveta puṣpaiḥ sa ājyaiḥ ca tandulaiḥ dhārayan vaśayet kāntām sā api tadvat patim dhruvam tāṃbūlam kusumam vāsaḥ ajanam candanam eva ca saḥ acirāt eṣa vaśagaḥ sa putra paśu bāndhavaḥ vṛndāraṇya sthitam dhyāyan ballavī saṃyutam harim saṃprāpya sat guroḥ dīkṣām kṛṣṇam yaḥ vidhinā amunā arcayet vaiṣṇava śreṣṭhaḥ saḥ aṣṭa siddhi īśvaraḥ bhavet tasya darśana mātreṇa vādinaḥ niṣprabhāḥ smṛtāḥ bhuktvā nānāvidhān bhogān ante viṣṇu padam vrajet iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge tṛtīya pāde kṛṣṇamantranirūpaṇam nāma aśītitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī sanatkumāraḥ uvāca atha kṛṣṇasya mantrāṇām vakṣye bhedān muni īśvara yān samārādhya manujāḥ sādhayanti iṣṭam ātmanaḥ śakti śrī māra pūrvaḥ ca śrī śakti smara pūrvakaḥ māra śaktiḥ amā pūrvaḥ daśa arṇāḥ manavaḥ trayaḥ muniḥ syāt nā rada chandaḥ gāyatrī devatā punar kṛṣṇaḥ govinda nāmā atra sarva kāma pradaḥ nṛṇām cakraiḥ pūrvavat aṅgāni trayāṇām api kalpayet tatas kirīṭa manunā avyāpakam hi samācaret viṃśati arṇa ukta vat kuryāt ādye dhyāna arcana ādikam dvitīye tu daśārṇa uktam dhyāna pūjā ādikam caret tṛtīye tu harim dhyāyet samāhita manāḥ sudhīḥ śakha cakra dhanuḥ bāṇa pāśa aṅkuśa dhara aruṇam dorbhyām dhṛtam dhamantam ca veṇum kṛṣṇa divākaram evam dhyātvā japet mantrān pañca lakṣam pṛthak sudhīḥ juhuyāt tad daśa aṃśena pāyasena sa sarpiṣā śrī śakti kāmaḥ kṛṣṇāya govindāya agnisundarī ratri arṇaḥ brahma gāyatrī kṛṣṇāḥ ṛṣi ādayaḥ asya tu bījaiḥ ama abdhi yugma arṇaiḥ ṣaṣ aṅgāni prakalpayet viṃśati arṇa udita japa dhyāna homa arcana ādikam kim bahu uktena mantraḥ ayam sarva abhīṣṭa phala pradaḥ śrī śakti smara pūrvaḥ ūga janmā śakti ramāntikaḥ daśa akṣaraḥ saḥ eva ādau proktaḥ śakti ramā yutaḥ mantrau ṣoḍaśa ravya arṇaum cakraiḥ aṅgāni kalpayet varada abhaya hastābhyām śliṣyantam sva aṅgake priye padma utpala kare tābhyām śliṣṭam cakra dara ujvalam dhyātvā evam prajapet lakṣa daśakam tad daśa aṃśataḥ aṣṭādaśa arṇaḥ kāma antaḥ manuḥ suta dhana pradaḥ nāradaḥ asya muniḥ chandaḥ gāyatrī devatā manoḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kāmaḥ bījam uktam śaktiḥ vahnipriyā matā ṣaṣ vīrya āḍhyena bījena ṣaṣ aṅgāni samācaret pāṇau pāyasa pakvam ca dakṣe haiyaṅgavīnakam dhyātvā evam prajapet mantram dvātriṃśat lakṣa mānataḥ daśa aṃśam juhuyāt agnau sita āḍhyena pūrva ukta vaiṣṇave pīṭhe yajet aṣṭādaśa arṇa vat kṣīreṇa kadalī pakkaiḥ dadhnā haiyaṅgavena ca vāc kāmaḥ ṅeyutam kṛṣṇa padam māyā tatas pagaram govindāya ramā paścāt daśa arṇam ca samuddharet dvāviṃśati akṣaraḥ mantraḥ vāc īśatva pradāyakaḥ ṛṣiḥ syāt nāradaḥ chandaḥ gāyatrī devatā punar vidyā pradaḥ ca gopālaḥ kāmaḥ bījam prakīrtitam śaktiḥ tu vāc bhavam vidyā prāptaye viniyojanā akṣamālām ca dakṣa ūrddhva sphaāṭikīm mātṛkā mayīm śabdabrahma mayam veṇum adhas pāṇi dvaye punar gāyatrī gīta vasanam śyāmalam komala chavim barha avataṃsam sarvajñam sevitam muni puṅgavaiḥ dhyātvā evam pramadā veśa vilāsam bhuvaneśvaram veda lakṣam japet mantram kiṃśukaiḥ tad daśa aṃśataḥ hutvā tu pūjayet mantrī viṃśati arṇa vidhānataḥ adṛṣṭāni api śāstrāṇi tasya gaṅgā taraṅga vat tāraḥ kṛṣṇa yugam paścāt mahākṛṣṇaḥ iti īrayet sarvajña tvaṃ praśam śabda ante sīdame agniḥ ca māram vidyeśa vidyām āśu prayaccha tatas ca me trayastriṃśat akṣaraḥ ayam mahāvidyā pradaḥ manuḥ nāradaḥ asya muniḥ chandaḥ anuṣṭubh kṛṣṇaḥ asya devatā pādaiḥ sarveṇa pañcāṅgam kṛtvā dhyāyet tatas harim vedaiḥ kalpadru rūpaiḥ śikhari śata samālaṃbi kośaiḥ caturbhiḥ nyāyaiḥ tarkaiḥ purāṇaiḥ smṛtibhiḥ abhivṛtaḥ tādṛśaiḥ ca amara ādyaiḥ dadyāt bibhrat kara agraiḥ api dara muralī puṣpa bāṇa ikṣu cāpān akṣa spṛś pūrṇa kuṃbhau smara lalita vapuḥ divya bhūṣā aṅga rāgaḥ evam dhyātvā japet lakṣam daśa aṃśam pāyasaiḥ hunet aṣṭādaśa arṇa vat kuryāt yajanam ca asya mantra vid ānanda vapuṣe dadyāt ṛśa arṇam tad anantaram aṣṭāviṃśati varṇaḥ ayam mantraḥ sarva iṣṭa dāyakaḥ nandaputra padam ṅeṃtam śyāmalāṅga padam tathā tathā bāla vapuḥ kṛṣṇam govindam ca tathā punar daśa arṇaḥ atas bhavet mantraḥ dvātriṃśat akṣara anvitaḥ anayoḥ nārada ṛṣiḥ chandaḥ tūṣṇih anuṣṭubhau cakraiḥ pañcāṅgam arcā āsyāt aṅga dikpāla hetibhiḥ dakṣiṇe ratna caṣakam vāme sauvarṇa netrakam kare dadhānam devībhyām śliṣṭam saṃcintayet vibhum lakṣam japaḥ daśa aṃśena juhuyāt pāyasena tu etābhyām siddha mantrābhyām mantrī kuryāt yathā īpsitam praṇavaḥ kamalā māyā namaḥ bhagavate tatas nanda putrāya tat paścāt bāla ante vapuṣe padam ūnaviṃśati varṇaḥ ayam muniḥ brahmā samīritaḥ chandaḥ anuṣṭubh devatā ca kṛṣṇaḥ bāla vapuḥ svayam tāraḥ rukmiṇī vallabhāya ca vahnijāyā avadhiḥ proktaḥ mantraḥ ṣoḍaśa varṇavān nāradaḥ asya muniḥ chandaḥ anuṣṭubh ca devatā manoḥ pañcāṅgāni prakurvīta tatas dhyāyet sureśvaram tāpiccha chaviḥ aṅka gām priyatamām svarṇa prabhām aṃbuja prodyat dāma bhujām sva vāma bhujayā āśliṣyan sva citta āśayā śliṣyantīm svayam anya hasta vilat sauvarṇa vetraḥ ciram pāyāt naḥ su viśuddha pīta vasanaḥ nānā vibhūṣaḥ hariḥ dhyātvā evam prajapet lakṣam raktaiḥ padmaiḥ daśa aṃśataḥ aṅgaiḥ nārada mukhyaiḥ ca lokeśaiḥ ca tad āyudhaiḥ evam siddhaḥ manuḥ dadyāt sarvān kāmān ca mantriṇe līlādaṇḍa pada abjaḥ api jana saṃsakta dos padam daṇḍa ante vā dharā vahniḥ adhīśa āḍhyaḥ atha lohitaḥ megha śyāma padam paścāt bhagavān salilaṃsadṛś viṣṇo iti uktvā ṭha dvayam syāt ekonatriṃśat arṇavān nāradaḥ asya muniḥ chandaḥ anuṣṭubh ca devatā manoḥ vedaiḥ bhāgaiḥ mantra varṇa utthitaiḥ kramāt saṃmohayan ca nija vāma kara stha līlā daṇḍena gopa yuvatīḥ para suṃdarīḥ ca lakṣam japaḥ daśa aṃśena juhuyāt tila taṇḍulaiḥ līlādaṇḍa harim yaḥ vai bhajate nityam ādarāt sadya ārūḍhā smṛtiḥ toyam keśava āḍhya dharā yugam bhayā agni vallabhā mantraḥ sapta arṇaḥ sarva siddhi daḥ ṛṣiḥ syāt nāradaḥ chandaḥ uṣṇih govallamasya tu devatā pūrvavat cakraiḥ pañca aṅgāni tu kalpayet pāśam sa yaṣṭim aparatra payoda nīlaḥ pīta ambara ahi ripu piccha kṛta avataṃsaḥ sapta lakṣam japet mantram daśa aṃśam juhuyāt tatas go dugdhaiḥ pūjayet pīṭhe syāt aṅgaiḥ prathama āvṛtiḥ suvarṇa piṅgalām gaura piṅgalām rakta piṅgalām guḍa piṅgām babhru varṇām ca uttamām kapilām tathā catuṣka piṅgalām pīta piṅgalām ca uttamām śubhām go gaṇa aṣṭakam abhyarcya lokeśa anuyudhaiḥ yutān pakṣāt sa go gaṇaḥ muktaḥ daśārṇe ca api ayam vidhiḥ tāraḥ hṛd bhagavān ṅeṃtaḥ śrī govindaḥ tathā bhavet dvādaśa arṇaḥ manuḥ proktaḥ nāradaḥ asya muniḥ mataḥ chandaḥ proktam ca gāyatrī śrī govindaḥ asya devatā candra akṣi yuga bhūta arṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ pañcāṅga kalpanam dhyāyet kalpadru mūla āśrita maṇi vilasat divya siṃhāsana stham megha śyāmam piśaṅga aṃśukam ati subhagam śaṅkha retre karābhyām ravi lakṣam japet mantram dugdhaiḥ hutvā daśa aṃśataḥ yajet ca pūrvavat goṣṭha sthitam vā pratimā ādiṣu pūrva ukte vaiṣṇave pīṭhe mūrtim saṃkalpya mūlataḥ tatra āvāhya yajet kṛṣṇam guru pūjana pūrvakam rukmiṇīm satyabhāmām ca pārśvayoḥ indram agratas pṛṣṭhatas surabhim ca iṣṭvā kesareṣu aṅga pūjanam kālim dyā ādyāḥ mahiṣyaḥ aṣṭau vasu patreṣu saṃsthitāḥ pīṭha koṇeṣu baddhvā ādi kiṅkaṇīm ca tathā punar dāmāni pṛṣṭhayoḥ veṇum puras śrīvatsa kaustubhau agratas
