api atra tṛtīyaḥ ayam udāhṛtaḥ pṛthoḥ puṇya samākhyānam tatas prācīnabarhiṣam priyavratasya caritam tat vaṃśyānām ca puṇya dam brahmāṇḍa antargatānām ca lokānām varṇanam tatas ajāmilasya caritam dakṣa sṛṣṭi nirūpaṇam vṛtra ākhyānam tatas paścāt marutām janma puṇya dam ṣaṣṭhaḥ ayam uditaḥ skandhaḥ vyāsena paripoṣaṇe prahlāda caritam puṇyam varṇa āśrama nirūpaṇam gaja indra mokṣaṇa ākhyānam manvantara nirūpaṇe matsyāktāracaritam aṣṭamaḥ ayam prakīrtitaḥ sūryavaṃśa samākhyānam soma vaṃśa nirūpaṇam kṛṣṇasya bāla caritam kaumāram ca vraja sthitiḥ kaiśoram mathurā sthānam yauvanam dvārakā sthitiḥ bhū bhāra haraṇam ca atra nirodhe daśamaḥ smṛtaḥ yadoḥ ca dattātreyeṇa śrī kṛṣṇā una uddhavasya ca yādavānām mithas ntaḥ ca muktau ekādaśaḥ smṛtaḥ bhaviṣya kali nirddeśaḥ mokṣaḥ rājñaḥ parīkṣitaḥ veda śākhā praṇayanam mārkaṇḍeya tapaḥ kriyā saurī vibhūtiḥ uditā sātvatī ca tatas param purāṇa saṃkhyā kathanam āśraye dvādaśaḥ hi ayam iti evam kathitam vatsa śrīmat bhāgavatam tava prauṣṭhapadyām pūrṇimāyām hema siṃha samanvitam deyam bhāgavatāya idam yaḥ api anukramaṇīm etām śrāvayet śṛṇuyāt tathā sa purāṇa śravaṇa jam prāpnoti phalam uttamam iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde śrīmadbhāgavatānukramaṇīnirūpaṇam nāma ṣaṇṇavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī brahmā uvāca śṛṇu vipra pravakṣyāmi purāṇam nāradīyakam pañcaviṃśati sāhasram bṛhatkalpa kathā āśrayam sūta śaunaka saṃvādaḥ sṛṣṭi saṃkṣepa varṇanam nānā dharma kathāḥ puṇyāḥ pravṛtte samudāhṛtāḥ dvitīye mokṣadharma ākhye mokṣa upāya nirūpaṇam vedāṅgānām ca kathanam śuka utpattiḥ ca vistarāt mahā tantre samuddiṣṭam paśu pāśa vimokṣaṇam mantrāṇām śodhanam dīkṣā mantra uddhāraḥ ca pūjanam gaṇeśa sūrya viṣṇūnām śiva śaktyoḥ anukramāt sanatkumāra muninā nāradāya tṛtīyake purāṇa lakṣaṇam ca eva pramāṇam dānam eva ca pṛthak pṛthak samuddiṣṭam dāna kāla puraḥsaram caitra ādi sarva māseṣu tithīnām ca pṛthak pṛthak proktam pratipad ādīnām vratam sarva agha nāśanam pūrva bhāgaḥ ayam uditaḥ bṛhat ākhyāna saṃjñitaḥ vasiṣṭhena atha saṃvādaḥ māndhātuḥ parikīrtitaḥ vasu śāpaḥ ca mohinyai paścāt uddharaṇa kriyā gaṅgā kathā puṇyatamā gayā yātrā anukīrtanam kāśyāḥ māhātmyam atulam puruṣottama varṇanam yātrā vidhānam kṣetrasya bahu ākhyāna samanvitam hari dvārasya ca ākhyānam kāmoda ākhyānakam tathā badarītīrtha māhātmyam kāmākṣāyāḥ tathā eva ca prabhāsasya ca māhātmyam puṣkara ākhyānakam tatas gautama ākhyānakam paścāt veda pāda stavaḥ tatas gokarṇa kṣetra māhātmyam lakṣmaṇa ākhyānakam tathā avantyāḥ ca eva māhātmyam madhurāyāḥ tatas param bṛndāvanasya mahimā paśoḥ brahma antike gatiḥ mohinīcaritam paścāt evam paścāt evam vai nāradīyakam yaḥ śṛṇoti naraḥ bhaktyā āśrāvayet vā samāhitaḥ sa yāti brahmaṇaḥ dhāma na atra kāryā vicāraṇā yaḥ tu etat iṣu pūrṇāyām dhenūnām saptaka anvitam yaḥ ca anukramaṇīm etām nāradīyasya varṇayet iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde nāradīyapurāṇānukramaṇīkathanam nāma saptanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī brahmā uvāca atha te saṃpravakṣyāmi mārkaṇḍeya abhidham mune purāṇam su mahat puṇyam paṭhatām śṛṇvatām sadā yatra adhikṛtya śakunīn sarva dharma nirūpaṇam mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇam tat nava sāhasram īritam mārkaṇḍeya muneḥ praśnaḥ jaimineḥ prāk samīritaḥ pakṣiṇām dharma saṃjñānam tatas janma nirūpaṇam pūrva janma kathā ca eṣām vikriyā divaspateḥ hariścandra kathā puṇyā yuddham āḍībaka abhidham pitāputra samākhyānam tatas madālaka sākathā proktā hi alarka carita anvitā sṛṣṭi saṃkīrtanam puṇyam navadhā pārikīrtitam rudra ādi sṛṣṭiḥ api uktā dvīpa caryā anukīrtanam manūnām ca kathāḥ nānā kīrtitāḥ pāpa hārikāḥ tāsu durgā kathā atyantam puṇya dā ca aṣṭame atare mārtaṇḍasya ca janma ākhyā tad māhātmya samanvitā vaivasvata anvayaḥ ca api vatsaprīḥ caritam tatas khanitrasya tatas proktā kathā puṇyā mahātmanaḥ nariṣyantasya caritam ikṣvāku caritam tatas kuśa vaṃśa samākhyānam soma vaṃśa anukīrttanam pururavaḥ kathā puṇyā nahuṣasya kathā adbhutā yayāti caritam puṇyam yadu vaṃśa anukīrttanam śrī kṛṣṇa bāla caritam māthuram caritam tatas dvārakā caritam ca atha kathā sarva avatāra jā tatas sāṃkhya samuddeśaḥ prapañca asattva kīrtanam mārkaṇḍeyasya caritam purāṇa śravaṇe phalam yaḥ śṛṇoti naraḥ bhaktyā purāṇam idam ādarāt mārkaṇḍeya abhidham vatsa sa labhet paramām gatim śṛṇoti śrāvayet vā api yaḥ ca anukramaṇīm imām mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇasya sa labhet vāñchitam phalam iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇānukramaṇīnirūpaṇam nāma aṣṭanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī brahmā uvāca atha atas saṃpravakṣyāmi tava āgneyapurāṇakam īśāna kalpa vṛttāntam vasiṣṭhāya analaḥ abravīt tat pañcadaśa sāhasram nānā caritam adbhutam paṭhatām śṛṇvatām ca eva sarva pāpa haram nṛṇām praśnaḥ pūrvam purāṇasya kathā sarva avatāra jā sṛṣṭi prakaraṇam ca atha viṣṇu pūjā ādikam tatas agni kāryam tatas paścāt mantra mudrā ādi lakṣaṇam sarva dīkṣā vidhānam ca abhiṣeka nirūpaṇam lakṣaṇam maṇḍala ādīnām kuśa apāmārjanam tatas śālagrāma ādi pūjā ca mūrti lakṣma pṛthak pṛthak nyāsa ādīnām vidhānam ca pratiṣṭhāpūrtakam tatas vināyaka ādi pūjā ca nānā dīkṣā vidhiḥ param pratiṣṭhā sarva devānām brahmaṇḍasya nirūpaṇam gaṅgā ādi tīrtha māhātmyam dvīpa varṣa anuvarṇanam ūrddhva adhas loka racanā jyotiścakra nirūpaṇam jyotiṣam ca tatas proktam śāstram yuddha jaya arṇavam ṣaṭkarma ca tatas proktam mantra mantra oṣadhī gaṇaḥ kubjikā ādi sama ṛca tvam ṣoḍhā nyāsa vidhiḥ tathā brahmacarya ādi dharmān ca śrāddha kalpa vidhiḥ tatas prāyaścitta anukathanam tithīnām ca vrata ādikam navavyūha arcanam proktam narakāṇām nirūpaṇam vratānām ca api dānānām nirūpaṇam iha uditam nāḍī cakra samuddeśaḥ saṃdhyā vidhiḥ anuttamaḥ rājya abhiṣeka mantra uktiḥ dharma kṛtyam ca bhūbhujām svapnādhyāyaḥ tatas proktaḥ śakuna ādi nirūpaṇam maṇḍala ādika nirddeṃśaḥ ratna dīkṣā vidhiḥ tatas rāma ukta nīti nirddeśaḥ ratnānām lakṣaṇam tatas deva asura vimarda ākhyā hi āyurveda nirūpaṇam gaja ādīnām cikitsā ca teṣām śāntiḥ tatas param gonara ādi cikitsā ca nānā pūjāḥ tatas param śāntayaḥ ca api vividhāḥ chandaḥ śāstram atas param sāhityam ca tatas paścāt ekārṇa ādi samāhvayāḥ siddha śabda anuśiṣṭiḥ ca kośaḥ sarga ādi vargakaḥ pralayānām lakṣaṇam ca śārīraka nirūpaṇam varṇanam narakāṇām ca yoga aśtram atas param brahma jñānam tatas paścāt purāṇa śravaṇe phalam etat āgneyakam vipra purāṇam parikīrtitam tiladhenu yutam ca api mārgaśīrṣyām vidhānataḥ eṣā anukramaṇī proktā tava āgneyasya mukti dā śṛṇvatām paṭhatām ca eva nṛṇām ca iha paratra ca iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde agnipurāṇānukramaṇīnirūpaṇam nāma ekonaśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī brahmā uvāca bhaviṣyam bhavataḥ sarva loka abhīṣṭa pradāyakam yatra aham sarva devānām ādikartā samudgataḥ sṛṣṭi artham tatra saṃjātaḥ manuḥ sva ārya bhuvaḥ purā aham tasmai tadā prītaḥ prāvocam dharma saṃhitām purāṇānām yadā vyāsaḥ vyāsam caktre mahāmatiḥ tadā tām saṃhitām sarvām pañcadhā vyabhajat muniḥ tatra ādimam smṛtam parvam brāhmam yatra asti upakramaḥ sūta śaunaka saṃvāde purāṇa praśna saṃkramaḥ āditya carita prāyaḥ sarva ākhyāna samanvitaḥ sṛṣṭi ādi lakṣaṇa upetaḥ śāstra sarva svarūpakaḥ pusta lekhaka lekhānām lakṣaṇam ca tatas param saṃskārāṇām ca sarveṣām lakṣaṇam ca atra kīrtitam pakṣasya ādi tithīnām ca kalpāḥ sapta ca kīrtitāḥ aṣṭamī ādyāḥ śeṣa kalpāḥ vaiṣṇave parvaṇi smṛtāḥ śaive ca kāyataḥ bhinnāḥ saure ca antya kathā anvayaḥ pratisarga āhvayam paścāt nānā ākhyāna samanvitam purāṇasya upasaṃhāra sahitam parva pañcamam eṣu pañcasu pūrvasmin brahmaṇaḥ mahima adhikāḥ dharme kāme ca mokṣe tu viṣṇoḥ ca api śivasya ca dvitīyam ca tṛtīye ca saure varga catuṣṭaye sabhaviṣyam vinirddiṣṭam parva vyāsena dhīmatā caturddaśa sahasram tu purāṇam parikīrtitam bhaviṣyam sarva devānām sāmyam yatra prakīrtitam guṇānām tāratamyena samam brahma iti hi śrutiḥ tam likhitvā tu yaḥ dadyāt pauṣyām vidvān vimatsaraḥ guḍadhenu yutam hema vastra mālya vibhūṣaṇaiḥ vācakam pustakam ca api pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ gandha ādyaiḥ bhojya bhakṣyaiḥ ca kṛtvā nīrājana ādikam yaḥ vai jita indriyaḥ bhūtvā sa upavāsaḥ samāhitaḥ atha vā eka haviṣya āśī kīrtayet śṛṇuyāt api yaḥ api anukramaṇīm etām bhaviṣyasya nirūpitām paṭhet vā śṛṇuyāt ca etām bhuktim muktim ca vindati iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde bhaviṣyapurāṇānukramaṇī nirūpaṇam nāma śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī brahmā uvāca śṛṇu vatsa pravakṣyāmi purāṇam daśamam tava sāvarṇiḥ yatra bhagavān sākṣāt devarṣaye sthitaḥ nāradāya purāṇa artham prāha sarvam alaukikam dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām sāraḥ prītiḥ harau hare śatakoṭipurāṇe tat saṃkṣipya prāha veda vid aṣṭādaśa sahasram tat purāṇam parikīrtitam brahma prakṛti vighneśa kṛṣṇa khaṇḍa samanvitam tatra sūta ṛṣi saṃvāde purāṇa upakramaḥ tatas sṛṣṭi prakaraṇam tu ādyam tatas nārada vedhasoḥ vivādaḥ su mahān yatra dvayoḥ āsīt parābhavaḥ śiva loka gatiḥ paścāt jñāna lābhaḥ śiva ātmane śiva vākyena tat paścāt marīceḥ nāradasya tu gamanam ca eva sāvarṇeḥ jñāna artham siddha sevite āśrame su mahā puṇye trailokya āścarya kāriṇī etat hi brahmakhaṇḍam hi śrutam pāpa vināśanam tatas sāvarṇi saṃvādaḥ nāradasya samīritaḥ kṛṣṇa māhātmya saṃyuktaḥ nānā ākhyāna kathā uttaram prakṛteḥ aṃśa bhūtānām kalānām ca api varṇitam māhātmyam pūjana ādyam ca vistareṇa yathā sthitam etat prakṛti khaṇḍam hi śrutam bhūti vidhāyakam gaṇeśa janma saṃpraśnaḥ sa puṇyaka mahāvratam vivādaḥ su mahān āsīt jāmadagrya gaṇeśayoḥ śrī kṛṣṇa janma saṃpraśnaḥ janma ākhyānam tatas adbhutam go kule gamanam bālya kaumāra jāḥ līlāḥ vividhāḥ tatra varṇitāḥ rāsakrīḍā ca gopībhiḥ śāradī samudāhṛtā rahasye rādhayā krīḍā varṇitā bahu vistarā saha akrūreṇa tad paścāt mathurā gamanam hareḥ kaṃsa ādīnām vadhe vṛtte kṛṣṇasya dvija saṃskṛtiḥ kāśya sāṃdīpaneḥ paścāt vidyā upādānam adbhutam yavanasya vadhaḥ paścāt dvārakā āgamanam hareḥ kṛṣṇa khaṇḍam idam vipra nṛṇām saṃsāra khaṇḍanam paṭhitam ca śrutam dhyātam pūjitam ca abhivanditam vyāsa uktam ca ādi saṃbhūtam paṭhan śṛṇvan vimucyate vijñāna ajñāna śamanāt horāt saṃsāra sāgarāt yaḥ ca anukramaṇīm ca api paṭhet vā śṛṇuyāt api saḥ api kṛṣṇa prasādena labhate vāñchitam phalam iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne brahmavaivartapurāṇānukramaṇīnirūpaṇam nāma ekottaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyāḥ śṛṇu putra pravakṣyāmi purāṇam liṅga saṃjñitam paṭhatām śṛṇvatām ca eva bhukti mukti pradāyakam yat ca liṅga abhidham tiṣṭhan vahni liṅge haraḥ abhyadhāt purāṇam liṅgam uditam bahu ākhyāna vicitritam tat ekādaśa sāhasram hara māhātmya sūcakam param sarva purāṇānām sāra bhūtam jagattraye purāṇa upakrame praśnaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ saṃkṣepataḥ purā yoga ākhyānam tatas proktam kalpa ākhyānam tatas param liṅga udbhavaḥ tad aṃbā ca kīrtitā hi tatas param sanatkumāra śaila ādi saṃvādaḥ ca atha pāvanaḥ tatas bhuvana kośa ākhyā sūryasoma anvayaḥ tatas liṅga pratiṣṭhā ca tatas paśu pāśa vimokṣaṇam śivavratāni ca tathā sat ācāra nirūpaṇam prāyaścitāni ariṣṭāni kāśī śrīśaila varṇanam andhaka ākhyānakam paścāt vārāhacaritam punar śaivam sahasranāma atha dakṣa yajña vināśanam kāmasya dahanam paścāt girijāyāḥ karagrahaḥ tatas vināyaka ākhyānam nṛpa ākhyānam śivasya ca upamanyu kathā ca api pūrva bhāgaḥ iti īritaḥ viṣṇu māhātmya kathanam aṃbarīṣa kathā tatas sanatkumāra nandīśa saṃvādaḥ ca punar mune śivam āha tmya se yuktaḥ strāna yāga ādikam tatas sūrya pūjā vidhiḥ ca eva śiva pūjā ca mukti dā dānāni bahudhā aktāni śrāddha prakaraṇam tatas vajreśvarī mahāvidyā gāyatrī mahimā tatas tryaṃbakasya ca māhātmyam purāṇa śravaṇasya ca vyāsena hi nibaddhasya rudrā māhātmya sūcitaḥ phaālgunyām pūrṇimāyām yaḥ dadyāt bhaktyā dvijātaye yaḥ paṭet śṛṇuyāt vā api laiṅgam pāpa apaham naraḥ liṅga anukramaṇīm etām paṭhet yaḥ śṛṇuyāt tathā jāyatām girijā bhartuḥ prasādāt na atra saṃśayaḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde liṅgapurāṇānukramaṇīnirūpaṇam nāma dvyuttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu vatsa pravakṣyāmi vārāham vai purāṇakam bhāga dvaya yutam śaśvat viṣṇu māhātmya sūcakam mānavasya tu kalpasya prasaṃgam mad kṛtam purā nibabandha purāṇe asmin caturviṃśa sahasrake vyāsaḥ hi viduṣām śreṣṭhaḥ sākṣāt nārāyaṇaḥ bhuvi tatra ādau śubha saṃvādaḥ smṛtaḥ bhūmi varāhayoḥ atha ādi kṛta vṛttānte raṃbhasya caritam tatas mahā tapasaḥ ākhyānam gaurī utpattiḥ tatas parā vināyakasya nāgānām senānī ādityayoḥ api gaṇānām ca tathā devyāḥ dhanadasya vṛṣasya ca agastya gītā tad paścāt rudragītā prakīrtitā mahiṣa asura vidhvaṃsa māhātmyam ca tri śakti jam parva adhyāyaḥ tatas śveta upākhyānam gopradānikam ityādi kṛta vṛttāntam prathame darśitam mayā dvātriṃśat aparādhānām prāyaścittam śarīra gam tīrthānām ca api sarveṣām māhātmyam pṛthak īritam mathurāyāḥ viśeṣeṇa śrāddha ādīnām vidhiḥ tatas varṇanam yama lokasya ṛṣi putra prasaṃgataḥ vipākaḥ karmaṇām ca eva viṣṇu vrata nirūpaṇam gokarṇasya ca māhātmyam kīrtitam pāpa nāśanam iti evam pūrva bhāgaḥ ayam purāṇasya nirūpitaḥ saṃvāde sarva tīrthānām māhātmyam vistarāt pṛthak aśeṣa dharmāḥ ca ākhyātāḥ pauṣkaram puṇya parva ca iti evam tava vārāham proktam pāpa vināśanam paṭhatām śṛṇvatām ca eva bhagavat bhakti vardhanam kāñcanam garuḍa kṛtvā tiladhenu samanvitam sa labhet vaiṣṇavam dhāma deva ṛṣi gaṇa vanditaḥ yaḥ vā anukramaṇīm entām śṛṇoti api paṭhati api saḥ api bhaktim labhet viṣṇau saṃsāra uccheda kāriṇīm iti śrī bṛhat nāradīya purāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde vārāhapurāṇānukramaṇīvarṇanam nāma tryuttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu vatsa pravakṣyāmi purāṇam skanda saṃjñakam purāṇe tu yat śaivam varṇitam mayā lakṣam tasya artham jātasya sāraḥ vyāsena kīrtitaḥ skanda āhvayaḥ tatra khaṇḍāḥ sapta eva parikalpitāḥ ekāśīti sahasram tu skāndam yaḥ śṛṇoti paṭhet vā api sa tu sākṣāt śivaḥ sthitaḥ yatra māheśvarāḥ dharmāḥ ṣaṇmukhena prakāśitāḥ kalpe tatpuruṣe vṛttāḥ sarva siddhi vidhāyakāḥ tasya māheśvaraḥ ca atha khaṇḍaḥ pāpa praṇāśanaḥ kiñcid nyūna arka sāhasraḥ bahu puṇyaḥ bṛhat kathaḥ yatra kedāramāhātmye purāṇa upakramaḥ purā dakṣa yajña kathā paścāt śiva liṅga arcane phalam pārvatyāḥ samupākhyānam vivāhaḥ tad anantaram tatas pāśupata ākhyānam caṇḍa ākhyāna samanvitam dyūta pravartana ākhyānam nāradena samāgamaḥ tatas kumāramāhātmye pañcatīrtha kathānakam dharmavarma nṛpa ākhyānam nadī sāgara kīrtanam indradyumna kathā paścāt nāḍījaṅgha kathā anvitam mahī sāgara saṃyogaḥ kumāra īśa kathā tatas vadhaḥ ca tārakasya atha pañca liṅga niveśanam dvīpa ākhyānam tatas puṇya mūrddha loka vyavasthitiḥ brahmāṇḍa sthiti mānam ca varkara īśa kathānakam mahākāla samudbhūtiḥ kathā ca asya mahā adbhutā vāsudevasya māhātmyam koṭitīrtham tatas param nānā tīrtha samākhyānam gupta kṣetre prakīrtitam pāṇḍavānām kathā puṇyā mahāvidyā prasādhanam aruṇācala māhātmyam sanaka brahma saṃkathā gaurītapaḥ samākhyānam tad tad tīrtha nirūpaṇam māhiṣa asuram ākhyānam vadhaḥ ca asya mahā adbhutaḥ droṇa acale śivā sthānam nityadā parikīrtitam iti eṣa kathitaḥ skānde khaṇḍaḥ māheśvaraḥ adbhutaḥ dvitīyaḥ vaiṣṇavaḥ khaṇḍaḥ tasya ākhyānāni me śuṇu prathamam bhūmi vārāha samākhyānam prakīrtitam yatra veṅkaṭa kudhrasya māhātmyam pāpa nāśanam kamalāyāḥ kathā puṇyā śrīnivāsa sthitiḥ tatas kulā lākhyānakam ca atra suvarṇamukharī kathā nānā ākhyāna samāyuktā bhāradvāja kathā adbhutā mataṅga añjana saṃvādaḥ kīrtitaḥ pāpa nāśanaḥ puruṣottama māhātmyam kīrtitam ca utkale tatas mārkaṇḍeya samākhyānam aṃbarīṣasya bhūpateḥ indradyumnasya ca ākhyānam vidyāpati kathā śubhā jaimineḥ samupākhyānam nāradasya api vāḍava nīlakaṇṭha samākhyānam narasiṃha upavarṇanam rathayāvrā vidhiḥ paścāt janmasthāna vidhiḥ tathā dakṣiṇāmūrti upākhyānam guṇḍiva ākhyānakam tatas ratha rakṣā vidhānam ca śayana utsava kīrtanam śveta upākhyānam atra uktam pṛthutsava nirūpaṇam pūjā ca ākāmikā viṣṇoḥ uddālaka niyogataḥ yoga sādhanam atra uktam nānā yoga nirūpaṇam daśa avatāra kathanam srāna ādi parikīrtanam tatas badarikāyāḥ ca māhātmyam pāpa nāśanam agni ādi tīrtha māhātmyam vainateyaśilā bhavam kāraṇam bhagavat vāse tīrtham kāpālamocanam pañcadhāra abhidham tīrtham meru saṃsthāpanam tathā tatas kārtikamāhātmye māhātmyam madana alasam dhūmrakeśa samākhyānam dinakṛtyāni kartike pañca bhīṣma vrata ākhyānam kīrtitam bhukti mukti dam tatas mārgasya māhātmye vidhānam snāna jam tathā puṇḍra ādi kīrtanam ca atra mālā dhāraṇa puṇyakam pañcāmṛta snāna puṇyam ghaṇṭā nāda ādi jam phalam nānā puṣpa arcana phalam tulasī dala jam phalam akhaṇḍa ekādaśī puṇyam tathā jāgaraṇasya ca yasya utsava vidhānam ca nāma māhātmya kīrtanam dhyāna ādi puṇya kathanam māhātmyam mathurā bhavam mathurā tīrtha māhātmyam pṛthak uktam tatas param vanānām dvādaśānām ca māhātmyam kīrtitam tatas śrīmat bhāgavatasya atra māhātmyam kīrtitam param vajraśāṇḍilya saṃvādaḥ antar līlā prakāśakam nānā ākhyāna samāyuktam daśa adhyāyaiḥ nirūpitam tatas vaiṣṇavamāhātmye śayyā dāna ādi jam phalam jaladāḥ na ādi vidhayaḥ kāma ākhyānam atas param tathā akṣaya tṛtīya ādeḥ viśeṣāt puṇya kīrtanam surā pāpa vimokṣa ākhye tathā ādhāra sahasrakam svarṇa vṛṣṭeḥ upākhyānam sītākuṇḍam gupta hari saraṃyu gharghara anvayaḥ gopratāram ca dugdhodam gurukuṇḍa ādi pañcakam soma arka ā dīni tīrthāni trayodaśa tatas param gayākūpasya māhātmyam sarva agha vinivartakam māṇḍavya āśrama pūrvāṇi tīrthāni tad anantaram ajita ādi mānasa ādi tīrthāni gaditāni ca iti eṣa vaiṣṇavaḥ khaṇḍaḥ dvitīyaḥ parikīrtitaḥ atas param brahmakhaṇḍam marīce śṛṇu puṇya dam gālavasya tapaḥ caryā rākṣasa ākhyānakam tatas cakratīrtha ādi māhātmyam devīpattana saṃyute vetālatīrtha mahimā pāpa nāśa ādi kīrtanam maṅgala ādika māhātmyam brahmakuṇḍa ādi varṇanam rāmatīrtha ādi kathanam lakṣmītīrtha nirūpaṇam śaṅkha ādi tīrtha mahimā tathā sādhya amṛta ādi jaḥ dhanuṣkoṭi ādi māhātmyam kṣīrakuṇḍa ādi jam tathā gāyatrī ādika tīrthānām māhātmyam ca atra kīrtitam rāma nāthasya mahimā tattva jñāna upadeśanam yātrā vidhāna kathanam mukti pradam nṛṇām dharmāraṇyasya māhātmyam tatas param udīritam sthāṇuḥ skandāya bhagavān yatra tattvam upādiśat karṃma siddheḥ samākhyānam ṛṣi vaṃśa nirūpaṇam apsaraḥ tīrtha mukhyānām māhātmyam yatra kīrtitam varṇānām āśramāṇām ca dharma tattva nirūpaṇam divaḥ sthāna vibhāgaḥ ca bakula arka kathā śubhā chatrānandā tathā śāntā śrīmātā ca mataṅginī puṇyadā ca samākhyātā yatra devyaḥ samāsthitāḥ indreśvara ādi māhātmyam dvārakā ādi nirūpaṇam lohāsura samākhyānam gaṅgākūpa nirūpaṇam tatas tu vaiṣṇavāḥ dharmāḥ nānā ākhyānaiḥ udīritāḥ cāturmāsye tatas puṇye sarva dhama nirūpaṇam dāna praśaṃsā tad paścāt vratasya mahimā tatas tapaḥ ca eva pūjāyāḥ sa chidra kathanam tatas tad vṛttīnām bhidā ākhyānam śālagrāma nirūpaṇam bhārakasya vadha upāyaḥ vṛkṣācām ahimā tathā viṣṇoḥ śāpaḥ ca vṛkṣa tvam pārvatī anutapaḥ tatas harasya tāṇḍavam nṛtyam rāma nāma nirūpaṇam praṇava aiśvarya kathanam tārakā caritam punar dakṣa yajña samāptiḥ ca dvādaśa akṣara bhūṣaṇam jñāna yoga samākhyānam mahimā dvādaśa akṣareḥ śravaṇa ādika puṇyam ca kīrtitam śarma dam nṛṇām pañcākṣarasya mahimā gokarṇa mahimā tatas śivarātraiḥ ca mahimā pradoṣa vra ta kīrtanam somavāravratam ca api sīmantinyāḥ kathānakam bhadrā yutpatti kathanam sat ācāra nirūpaṇam śivavarma samuddeśaḥ bhadrāyu udvāha varṇanam bhadrāyu mahimā ca api bhasma māhātmya kīrtanam śabara ākhyānakam ca eva umāmāheśvaram vratam rudrākṣasya ca māhātmyam rudrādhyāyasya puṇyakam śravaṇa ādika puṇyam ca brahmakhaṇḍaḥ ayam īritaḥ atas param caturtham tu kāśīkhaṇḍam anuttamam satya loka prabhāvaḥ ca agastya āvāse sura āgamaḥ pativratā caritram ca tīrtha yātrā praśaṃsanam tatas ca saptapurī ākhyā saṃyaminyāḥ nirūpaṇam budhasya ca tathā indra agnyoḥ loka āptiḥ śivaśarmaṇaḥ candra arka budha lokānām kuja ijyā arka bhuvām kramāt dhruva loka kathā puṇyā satya loka nirīkṣaṇam skanda agastya samālāpaḥ maṇikarṇī samudbhavaḥ prabhāvaḥ ca api gaṅgāyāḥ gaṅgā nāma sahasrakam vārāṇasī praśaṃsā ca bhairava āvirbhavaḥ tatas daṇḍa pāṇi jñāna vāpyoḥ udbhavaḥ samanantaram tatas kalau ati ākhyānam sat ācāra nirūpaṇam brahmacāri samākhyānam tatas strī lakṣaṇāni ca kṛtyākṛtya vinirdeśaḥ hi avimukta īśa varṇanam gṛhastha yoginaḥ dharmāḥ kāla jñānam tatas param divodāsa kathā puṇyā kāśikā varṇanam tatas māyā gaṇapateḥ ca atha bhuvi prādurbhavaḥ tatas viṣṇu māyā prapañcaḥ atha divodāsa vimokṣaṇam tatas vaiṣṇavatīrtha ākhyā śūlinaḥ kāśika āgamaḥ jaigīṣavyena saṃvādaḥ jyeṣṭheśākhyāḥ maheśituḥ kṣetra ākhyānam kandukeśaḥ vyāghreśvara samudbhavaḥ śaileśa ratneśvarayoḥ kṛttivāsasya ca udbhavaḥ devatānām adhiṣṭānam durga asura parākramaḥ durgāyāḥ vijayaḥ ca atha oṅkāra īśasya varṇanam māhātmya kedāra ākhyā ca dharmeśa kathā viṣṇu bhuja udbhavā vīreśvara samākhyānam gaṅgā māhātmya kīrtanam viśvakarmā īśa mahimā dakṣa yajña udbhavaḥ tathā satīśasya amṛteśa ādeḥ bhuja staṃbhaḥ parāśare kṣetra tīrtha kadaṃbaḥ ca mukti maḍapa saṃkathā viśveśa vibhavaḥ ca atha tatas yātrā parikramaḥ atas param tu avanti ākhyam śṛṇu khaṇḍa ca pañcamam mahākāla vana ākhyānam brahma śīrṣa chidā tatas prāyaścitta vidhiḥ ca agneḥ utpattiḥ ca surā āgamaḥ deva dīkṣā śiva stotram nānā pātaka nāśanam kapola mocana ākhyānam mahākāla vana sthitiḥ tīrtham kanakhaleśasya sarva pāpa praṇāśanam kuḍaveśam ca vidyādhram markaṭeśvaratīrthakam śaṅkarāka gandhavatītīrtham pāpa praṇāśanam daśāśvamedhikān aṃśatīrthe ca hari siddhi dam piśācaka ādi yātrā ca hanumat kavaca īśvarau mahākāla īśa yātrā ca valmīkeśvara tīrthakam śukre ca pañcame ca ākhye kuśasthalyāḥ pradakṣiṇāḥ karabheśa ākhya tīrtham ca laṭukeśa ādi tīrthakam mārkaṇḍeśam yajña vāpī someśam naraka antakam kedāreśvara rāmeśa saubhāgyeśa nara arkakam keśava arkam śakti bhedam svarṇa sāra mukhāni ca oṅkāra īśa ādi tīrthāni andhaka śruti kīrtanam kālāraṇye liṅga saṃkhyā svarṇa śṛṅga abhidhānakam viśālā pratikalpa abhidhānam ca jvara śāntikam śivānām ādika phalam nāgodgītā śiva stutiḥ hiraṇyākṣa vadha ākhyānam tīrtham suṃdarakuṇḍakam nīlagaṅgā puṣkara ākhyam vindhyavāsana tīrthakam puruṣottama abhidhānam tu tat tīrtham ca agha nāśanam gomatī vāmanam kuṇḍaḥ viṣṇoḥ nāma sahasrakam mahimā nāga pañcamyāḥ nṛsiṃhasya jayantikā kuṭumba īśvara yātrā ca deva sādhaka kīrtanam rundrakuṇḍa prabhṛtiṣu bahu tīrtha nirūpaṇam yātrā aṣṭa tīrtha jā puṇyā revāmāhātmyam ucyate kalpe kalpe pṛthak nāma narmadāyāḥ prakīrtitam stava mārṣam nāma idam ca kālarātri kathā tatas mahādeva stutiḥ paścāt pṛthak kalpa kathā adbhutā viśalya ākhyānakam paścāt jāleśvara kathā tathā gorīvrata samākhyānam tripura jvālanam tatas dehapāta vidhānam ca kāverīsaṃgamaḥ tatas dārutīrtham brahmāvartam yatra īśvara kathānakam agnitīrtham ravitīrtham meghanāda ādi dārukam deva tīrtham narmadā īśam kapila ākhyam karañjakam kuṇḍaleśam pippalādam vimaleśam ca śūlabhid śacīharaṇam ākhyā nam abhrakasya vadhaḥ tatas śūlabheda udbhavaḥ yatra dāna dharmāḥ pṛthagvidhāḥ ākhyānam dīrghatapasaḥ ṛṣyaśṛṅga kathā tatas citrasena kathā puṇyā kāśi rājyasya lakṣaṇam tatas devaśilā ākhyānam śabarītīrthaka anvitam vyādha ākhyānam tatas puṇyam puṣkariṇī arkatīrthakam āpretya īśvaratīrtham ca śakratīrtham karoṭikam kumāra īśam agastya īśam ānanda īśam ca mātṛ jam lokeśam dhanadeśam ca maṅgaleśam ca kāma jam nāgeśam ca api gopāram gautamam śaṅkhacūḍakam nāradeśam nandikeśam varuṇeśvaratīrthakam dadhiskanda ādi tīrthāni hanūmatā īśvaram tatas rāmeśvara ādi tīrthāni someśam piṅgaleśvaram ṛṇamokṣam kapileśam pūtikeśam jaleśayam caṇḍārkam yamatīrtham ca kālhoḍīśam vanādike nārāyaṇam ca koṭīśam vyāsatīrtham prabhāsakam nāgeśa saṃkarṣaṇakam praśrayeśvara tīrthakam airaṇḍīsaṃgamam puṇyam suvarṇa śila tīrthakam karañjam tīrtham bhāṇḍīraḥ rohiṇībhavam cakratīrtham dautapāpam skandam āṅgirasa āhvayam indra īśam kaṃbuka īśam ca soma īśam kohanam śakam nārmadam ca arkam āgneyam bhārgaveśvaram uttamam brāhmam daivam ca mārgeśam ādi vārāhaka īśvaram rāmeśam atha siddheśam āhalyam kaṅkaṭeśvaram śākram saumyam ca nādeśam toyeśam rukmiṇībhavam yojana īśam varāha īśam dvādaśī śiva tīrthakam siddheśam maṅgaleśam ca liṅga vārāhatīrthakam kuṇḍeśam śvetavārāham garbhāveśam ravīśvaram śukla ādīni ca tīrthāni huṅkāra svāmi tīrthakam saṃgameśam nahuṣeśam mokṣaṇam pañcagopakam nāgaśāvam ca siddheśam mārkaṇḍāṅkrūratīrthake kāmoda śūla āropa ākhye māṇḍavyam gopakeśvaram kapileśam piṅgaleśam bhūteśam gāṅga gautame āsvamedham bhṛgukaccham kedāreśam ca pāpa nud kalakaleśam jāleśam śālagrāmam varāhakam candraprabhāsam ādityam śrīpati ākhyam ca haṃsakam mūlya sthānam ca śūla īśam ugra ākhyam citra daivakam śikhīśam kāṇṭitīrtham ca daśakanyam suvaṇakam ṛṇamokṣam bhārabhūti puṅkhām muḍim ca ḍiṇḍimam āmala īśam kapāla īśam śṛṅgairaṇḍī bhavam tatas koṭitīrtham loṭaṇeṣam phala stutiḥ atas param dṛmijaṅgalamāhātmye rohitāśva kathā tatas mahimā asya tatas caḍīśa prabhāvaḥ rati īśvaraḥ kedāra īśaḥ lakṣatīrtham tatas viṣṇupadī bhavam mukhāram cyavana andha āsyam brahmaṇaḥ ca saraḥ tatas cakra ākhyam lalitā ākhyānam tīrtham ca bahu gomayam rudrāvartam ca markaṇḍam tīrtham pāpa praṇāśanam śravaṇeśam śuddhapaṭam devāndhupretatīrthakam śivodbhandam phalastutiḥ eṣa khaṇḍaḥ hi avantya ākhyaḥ śṛṇvatām pāpa nāśanaḥ atas param nāgara ākhyaḥ khaṇḍaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ abhidhīyate liṅga utpatti samākhyānam hariścandra kathā śubhā viśvāmitrasya māhātmyam triśaṅku svargatiḥ tathā hāṭake śvara māhātmye vṛtra asura vadhaḥ tathā nāgabilam śaṅkhatīrtham acaleśvara varṇanam camatkāra purā ākhyānam camatkāra karam param viṣṇu pādam ca gokarṇam yuga rūpam samāśrayaḥ siddheśvaram nāgasaraḥ sapta ārṣeyam hi agastyakam bhrūṇagartam naleśam ca bhaiṣmam vaiḍuram arkakam śāramiṣṭham somanātham ca daurgamātarjaka īśvaram jāmadagnya vadha ākhyānam naiḥkṣatriya kathānakam rāmahradam nāgapuram ṣaāḍliṅgam ca eva yajñabhūḥ muṇḍīra ādi trika arkam ca satī pariṇaya āhvayam rudraśīrṣam ca yāgeśam vālakhilyam ca gāruḍam lakṣmī śāpaḥ saptaviṃśa somaprāsādam eva ca aṃbābaddham pāṇḍuka ākhyam āgneyam brahmakuṇḍakam gomukham lohayaṣṭi ākhyam ajāpāleśvarī tathā śānaiścaram rājavāpī rāmeśaḥ lakṣmaṇeśvaraḥ kuśeśākhyam laveśākhyam liṅgam sarva uttamottamam aṣṭaṣaṣṭi samākhyānam damayantyāḥ tri jātakam kṣemaṅkarī ca kedāram śuklatīrtham ukhārakam satya saṃdhā īśvara ākhyānam tathā karṇa utpalā kathā aṭeśvaram yājñavalkya gauryam gāṇeśam eva ca tatas vāstupada ākhyānam ajā gṛha kathānakam saubhāgyāndhuḥ ca śuleśam dharmarāja kathānakam miṣṭānna idaśvara ākhyānam gāṇāpatya trayam tatas jābāli caritam ca eva makareśa kathā tatas kāleśvarī andhaka ākhyānam kuṇḍam āpya rasam tathā puṣya ādityam rauhitāśvam nāgara utpatti kīrttanam bhārgavam caritam ca eva vaiśvāmaitram tatas param sārasvatam paippalādam kaṃsārīśam ca paiṇḍakam brahmaṇaḥ yajña caritam sāvitrī ākhyāna saṃyutam raivatam bhārtayajña ākhyam mukhya tīrtha nirīkṣaṇam kauravam hāṭakeśa ākhyam prabhāsam kṣetraka trayam pauṣkaram naimiṣam dhārmam araṇya tritayam smṛtam vārāṇasī dvārakā ākhyā avantī ākhyā iti purī trayam bṛndāvanam khāṇḍava ākhyam advaika ākhyam vana trayam asiśuklapitṛ saṃjñam tīrtha trayam udāhṛtam nadīnām tritayam gaṅgā narmadā ca sarasvatī kūṣikā śaṅkhatīrtham cāmarakam bālamaṇḍanam hāṭa keśa kṣetra phala pradam proktam catuṣṭayam sa aṃba ādityam śrāddha kalpam yaudhiṣṭhiram atha andhakam jala śāyi catur māsam a śūnya śayana vratam maṅkaṇeśam śivarātriḥ tulāpuruṣadānakam pṛthvīdānam vānakeśam kapālamocaneśvaram pāpa piṇḍam māsa laiṅgam yuga māna ādi kīrtanam niṃveśa śākaṃbharyā ākhyā rudra ekādaśa kīrtanam dāna māhātmya kathanam dvādaśa āditya kīrtanam iti eṣa nāgaraḥ khaṇḍaḥ prabhāsa ākhyaḥ adhunā ucyate siddheśvara ādika ākhyānam pṛthak atra prakīrtitam agnitīrtham kapaddarśim kedāreśam gati pradam bhīma bhairava caṇḍīśa bhāskara indu kuja īśvarāḥ budha ijya bhṛgu saura āgu śiravī īśāḥ hara vigrahāḥ siddheśvara ādyāḥ pañca anye rudrāḥ tatra varārohā hi ajā pālā maṅgalā lalitā īśvarā lakṣmīśaḥ vāḍaveśaḥ ca urvīśaḥ kāmesvaraḥ tathā gaurīśa varuṇa īśa ākhyam durvāsa īśam gaṇeśvaram kumāreśam caṇḍakalpam śakulīśvara saṃjñakam tatas proktaḥ atha koṭīśa bāla brahma ādi sat kathā naraka īśa saṃvartta īśa nidhi īśvara kathā tatas balabhadra īśvarasya atha gaṅgāyāḥ gaṇapasya ca jāṃbavatī ākhya saritaḥ pāṇḍukūpasya sat kathā durvāsa arka ghaṭa sthāna hiraṇya āsaṃgama utkathā nagara arkasya kṛṣṇasya saṃkarṣaṇa samudrayoḥ kumāryāḥ kṣetrapā asya brahmeśasya kathā pṛthak piṅgalā saṃgama īśasya śaṅkara arka ghaṭeśayoḥ ṛṣitīrthasya nanda arka tritakūpasya kīrtanam sa sopānasya parṇa arka nyaṅkumatyoḥ kathā adbhutā vārāhasvāmi vṛttāntam chāyāliṅga ākhya gulphayoḥ kathā kanakanandāyāḥ kutī gaṅgeśayoḥ tathā maṅkaṇeśa traipura īśa ṣaṇḍatīrtha kathāḥ tathā sūryaprācī trīkṣaṇayā uru mānāta kathā tathā bhūddhāra śūla sthalayoḥ cyavana arkeśayoḥ tathā ajāpāla īśa bāla arka kubera sthala jā kathā ṛṣi toyā kathā puṇyā saṃgāla īśvara kīrtanam taptakuṇḍasya māhātmyam mūlacaṇḍīśa varṇanam caturvaktra gaṇādhyakṣa kalaṃba īśvarayoḥ kathā gopāla svāmī iva kula svāminoḥ marutām kathā tatas śaṅkha āvarta mokṣatīrtha goṣpada acyuta sadmanām jāleśvarasya huṅkāreśvara caṇḍīśayoḥ kathā āśā pura stha vighneśa kalā kuṇḍa kathā adbhutā nala karkeṭa īśvarayoḥ hāṭaka īśvara jā kathā nāra deśa yantra bhūṣā durga kūṭa gaṇeśa jā bahu svarṇa īśa śṛṅga īśa koṭīśvara kathā tatas mārkaṇḍeśvara koṭīśa dāmodara gṛha utkathā svarṇarekhā brahmakuṇḍam kuntī bhīmeśvarau tathā mṛgī kuṇḍam ca sarva svam kṣetre vastrāpathe smṛtam durgā bhilla īśa gaṅgā īśa raivatānām kathā adbhutā nāgatīrthasya ca kathā vasiṣṭa āśrama varṇanam kedārasya ca māhātmyam tīrtha aṅgamana kīrtanam koṭīśvara rūpatīrtha hṛṣīkeśa kathāraḥ tatas siddheśa śukra īśvarayoḥ maṇikarṇīśa kīrtanam paṅgutīrtha yamatīrtha vārāhatīrtha varṇanam candraprabhā sarpiḍoda śrīmātā śuklatīrtha jam kātyāyanyāḥ ca māhātmyam tatas piṇḍārakasya ca tatas kanakhalasya atha cakra mānuṣa tīrthayoḥ kapila agnitīrtha kathā tathā rakta anubandha jā gaṇeśa pārtha īśvarayoḥ yā antrāyām ujjvalasya ca caṇḍīsthāna nāgodbhava śivakuṇḍa maheśajā kāmeśvarasya mārkaṇḍeya utpatteḥ ca kathā tatas uddālaka īśa siddha īśa gata tītha kathā pṛthak śrīdevara vāta utpattiḥ ca vyāsa gautamatīrthayoḥ kulasaṃtāra māhātmyam rāma koṭi āhva tīrthayoḥ mahā ojasaḥ prabhāvaḥ ca jaṃbūtīrthasya varṇanam gaṅgādhara miśrakayoḥ kathā vātha phala stutiḥ dvārakāyāḥ ca māhātmye candraśarma kathānakam jāgara ādi arcana ādi ākhyā vratam ekādaśī bhavam mahādvādaśika ākhyānam prahlāda ṛṣi samāgamaḥ durvāsasaḥ upākhyānam yātrā upakrama kīrtanam sanaka ādi hrada ākhyānam nṛgatīrtha kathā tatas go pracāra kathā puṇyā gopīnām dvārakā āgamaḥ gopīsaraḥ samākhyānam brahmatīrtha ādi kīrtanam pañca nadī āgama ākhyānam nānā ākhyāna samanvitam śiva liṅga gadā tīrtha kṛṣṇa pūjā ādi kīrtanam trivikramasya mūrta ākhyā durvāsaḥ kṛṣṇa saṃkathā kuśa daitya vadha uñcāra viśeṣa arcana jam phalam gomatyām dvārakāyām ca tīrtha āgamana kīrtanam kṛṣṇa mandira saṃprekṣā drāravatī abhiṣecanam tatra tīrtha āvāsa kathā dvārakā puṇya kīrtanam iti eṣa saptamaḥ proktaḥ khaṇḍaḥ prābhāsikaḥ dvijāḥ mādhyām satkṛtya viprāya sa śaive modate pade iti śrī bṛhat nāradīya purāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde skandapurāṇānukramaṇīvarṇanam nāma catur adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu vatsa pravakṣyāmi purāṇam vāmana abhidham bhāga dvaya samāyuktam vaktṛ śrotṛ śubha āvaham purāṇapraśnaḥ prathamam brahma śīrṣa chidā tatas kapāla mocana ākhyānam dakṣa yajña vihiṃsanam harasya kāla rūpa ākhyā kāmasya dahanam tatas prahlāda nārāyaṇayoḥ yuddham deva asura āhavaḥ tatas kāmya vrata ākhyānam śrī durgā caritam tatas tapatīcaritam paścāt kurukṣetrasya varṇanam satyā māhātmyam atulam pārvatī janma kīrtanam tapaḥ tasyāḥ vivāhaḥ ca gaurī upākhyānakam tatas tatas kauśikyupākhyānam kumāracaritam tatas tatas andhaka vadha ākhyānam sādhya upākhyānakam tatas jābāli caritam paścāt arajāyāḥ kathā adbhutā marutām janma kathanam baleḥ ca caritam tatas prahlāda tīrtha yātrāyām procyante atha kathāḥ śubhāḥ nakṣatrapuruṣa ākhyānam śrī dāma caritam tatas iti eṣa pūrva bhāgaḥ asya purāṇasya tava uditaḥ śṛṇṇataḥ asya uttaram bhāgam bahadvāmana saṃjñakam māheśvarī bhāgavatī saurī gāṇeśvarī tathā catasraḥ saṃhitāḥ ca atra pṛthak sāhasra saṃkhyayā māheśvaryām tu kṛṣṇasya tad bhaktānām ca kīrtanam bhāgavatyām jaganmātu khatāra kathā adbhutā sauryām sūryasya mahimā gaditaḥ pāpa nāśanaḥ gāṇeśvaryām gaṇeśasya caritam ca maheśituḥ iti etat vāmanam nāma purāṇam su vicitrakam pulastyena samākhyātam nāradāya mahātmane tatas nāradataḥ prāptam vyāsena su mahātmanā vyāsāt tu labdhavān ca etat tad śiṣyaḥ romaharṣaṇaḥ evam paraṃparā prāptam purāṇam vāmanam śubham ye paṭhanti ca śṛṇvanti te api yānti parām gatim iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde vāmanapurāṇānukramaṇīvarṇanam nāma pañca adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu vatsa marīce tvam purāṇam kūrma saṃjñakam lakṣmī kalpa anucaritam yatra kūrma vapuḥ hariḥ dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām māhātmyam ca pṛthak pṛthak tat saptadaśa sāhasram su catuḥ saṃhitam śubham yatra brāhmāḥ purā proktāḥ dharmāḥ nānāvidhāḥ mune na ānanā kathā prasaṃgena nṛṇām sat gati dāyakāḥ tatra pūrva vibhāge tu purāṇa upakramaḥ purā lakṣmī indradyumna saṃvādaḥ kūrṃma ṛṣi gaṇa saṃkathā varṇa āśrama ācāra kathā jagat utpatti kīrtanam kāla saṃkhyā samāsena laya ante stavanam vibhoḥ tatas saṃkṣepataḥ sargaḥ śāṅkaram caritam tathā bhṛgu vaṃśa samākhyānam tatas svāyambhuvasya ca deva ādīnām samutpattiḥ dakṣa yajña āhatiḥ tatas dakṣa sṛṣṭi kathā paścāt kaśyapa anvaya kīrtanam ātreya vaṃśa kathanam caritam śubham mārtaṇḍa kṛṣṇa saṃvādaḥ vyāsa pāṇḍava saṃkathā vārāṇasyāḥ ca māhātmyam prayāgasya tatas param trailokya varṇanam ca eva veda śākhā nirūpaṇam uttare asyāḥ vibhāge tu purā gītā aiśvarī tatas vyāsagītā tatas proktā nānā dharma prabodhinī nānāvidhānām tīrthānām māhātmyam ca pṛthak tatas pratisarga prakathanam brāhmī iyam saṃhitā smṛtā atas param bhāgavatīsaṃhitā artha nirūpaṇam kathitā yatra varṇānām pṛthak vṛttiḥ udāhṛtā pāda asyāḥ prathame proktā brāhmaṇānām vyavasthitiḥ dvitīye kṣattriyāṇām tu vṛttiḥ samyak prakīrtitā yayā tu āśritayā pāpam vidhūya iha vrajet divam tṛtīye vaiśya jātīnām vṛttiḥ uktā caturvidhā caturthe asyāḥ tathā pāde śūdra vṛttiḥ udāhṛtā yayā saṃtuṣyati śrīśaḥ nṛṇām śreyaḥ vivarddhanaḥ pañcame asyāḥ tatas pāde vṛttiḥ saṃkara jā uditā yayā caritayā āpnoti bhāvinīm gatim uttamām iti eṣā pañca padī uktā dvitīyā saṃhitā mune tṛtīyā atra uditā saurī nṝṇām kārya vidhāyinī ṣoḍhā bodhayantī ca kāminām caturthīvaiṣṇavaḥ nāma mokṣa dā parikīrtitā catuṣpadī dvijātīnām sākṣāt brahma svarūriṇī tāḥ kramāt ṣaṣ catur dvi iṣu sāhasrāḥ parikīrtitāḥ paṭhatām śṛṇvatām nṝṇām sarva utkṛṣṭa gati pradam brāhmaṇāyāḥ yane dadyāt sa yāti paramām gatim iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde kūrmaparāṇānukramaṇīkathanam nāma ṣaḍuttaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ yatra uktam sapta kalpānām vṛttam saṃkṣipya bhū tale vyāsena veda viduṣā nārasiṃha upavarṇane manu matsya susaṃvādaḥ brahmāṇḍa kathanam tatas madanadvādaśī tadvat lokapāla abhipūjanam pitṛ vaṃśa anukathanam śraddhā kālaḥ tathā eva ca kīrtanam soma vaṃśasya yayāti caritam tathā pitṛ vaṃśa anukathanam sṛṣṭa vaṃśa anukīrtanam bhṛgu śāpaḥ tathā viṣṇoḥ daśadhā janmane kṣitau kīrttanam pūru vaṃśasya vaṃśaḥ hautāśanaḥ param kriyāyogaḥ tatas paścāt purāṇa parikīrtanam vratam nakṣatrapuruṣam mārtaṇḍaśayanam tathā kṛṣṇa aṣṭamīvratam tadvat rohiṇīcandra saṃjñitam taḍāga vidhi māhātmyam pādapa utsargaḥ eva ca tathā ananta tṛtīyāyāḥ rasakalyāṇinīvratam tathā eva anam dakaryāḥ ca vratam sārasvatam punar uparāga abhiṣekaḥ ca saptama īśanam tathā bhīma ākhyā dvādaśī tadvat anaṅgaśayanam tathā a śūnya śayanam tadvat tathā eva aṅgārakavratam saptamī saptakam tadvat viśoka dvādaśīvratam meru pradānam daśadhā graha śāntiḥ tathā eva ca graha svarūpa kathanam tathā śivacaturdaśī tathā sarva phala tyāgaḥ sūryavāravratam tathā saṃkrānti snapanam tadvat vibhūti dvādaśīvratam ṣaṣṭīvratānām māhātmyam tathā snāna vidhi kamaḥ prayāgasya tu māhātmyam dvīpa loka anuvarṇanam tathā antarikṣa cāraḥ ca dhruva māhātmyam eva ca bhavanāni suredrāṇām tripura udyotanam tathā pitṛ pravara māhātmyam manvantara vinirṇayaḥ tāraka asura māhātmyam brahma deva anukīrtanam pārvatī ṛṣi saṃvādaḥ tathā airā udvāha maṅgalam vārāṇasyāḥ tu māhātmyam narmadāyāḥ tathā eva ca tathā ubhaya mukhī dānam dānam kṛṣṇājinasya ca tatas sāvitrī upākhyānam rāja dharmāḥ tathā eva ca vāmanasya tu māhātmyam vārāhasya tatas param samudra mathanam tadvat kālakūṭa abhiśāntanam pratimā lakṣaṇam tadvat devatāyatanam tathā prāsāda lakṣaṇam ca lakṣaṇam bhaviṣya rājñām uddeśaḥ mahādāna anukīrtanam yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api sa yāti bhavanam hareḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde matsyapurāṇānukramaṇīkathanam nāma saptottaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ marīce śṛṇu vakṣya abhi purāṇam gāruḍam śubham garuḍāya abravīt pṛṣṭaḥ bhagavān garuḍāsanaḥ ekonaviṃśa sāhasram tārkṣya kalpa kathā anvitam purāṇa upakrama praśnaḥ sargaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ tatas sūrya ādi pūjana vidhiḥ dīkṣā vidhiḥ atas param śrāddha pūjā tatas paścāt navavyūha arcanam dvija pūjā vidhānam ca tathā vaiṣṇavam pañjaram tatas yoga adhyāyaḥ tatas viṣṇoḥ nāma sāhasra kīrtanam dhyānam viṣṇoḥ tatas sūrya pūjā mṛtyuñjaya arcanam mālāmantraḥ śiva arcā atha gaṇa pūjā tatas param gopāla pūjā trailokya mohana śrīdhara arcanam viṣṇu arcā pañcatattva arcā cakra arcā deva pūjanam nyāsa ādi saṃdhyā upāstiḥ ca durga arcā atha sura arcanam pūjā māheśvarī ca atas pavitra āropaṇa arcanam mūrti dhyām na vāstu mānam prāsādānām ca lakṣaṇam pratiṣṭhā sarva devānām pṛthak pūjā vidhānataḥ yogaḥ aṣaṭ aṅgaḥ dāna dharmāḥ prayaścitta vidhi kriyā dvīpa īśa naraka ākhyānam sūrya vyūhaḥ ca jyotiṣam sāmudrikam svara jñānam nava ratna parīkṣaṇam māhātmyam atha tīrthānām gayāmāhātmyam uttamam tatas manvantara ākhyānam pṛthak pṛthak vibhāgaśaḥ pitṛ ākhyānam varṇa dharmāḥ dravya śuddhiḥ samarpaṇam śrāddham vināyakasya arcā graha yajñaḥ tathaā śramāḥ janana ākhyam preta śaucam nīti śāstram vrata uktayaḥ sūryavaṃśaḥ somavaṃśaḥ avatāra kathanam hareḥ rāmāyaṇam hareḥ vaṃśaḥ bhārata ākhyānakam tatas āyurveda nidānam prāk cikikatsā dravya jāḥ guṇāḥ roga ghnam kavacam viṣṇoḥ gāruḍam traipuraḥ manuḥ praśna cūḍāmaṇiḥ ca antaḥ haya āyurveda kīrtanam oṣaghī nāma kathanam tatas vyākaraṇa ūhanam chandaḥ śāstram sat ācāraḥ tatas snāna vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ tarpaṇam vaiśvadevam ca saṃdhyā pārvaṇa karma ca pratisaṃkrame uktāḥ sma yuga dharmāḥ kṛteḥ phalam yoga śāstram viṣṇu bhaktiḥ namaskṛti phalam hareḥ māhātmyam vaiṣṇavam ca atha nārasiṃha stava uttamam jñānāmṛtam guhuṣṭakam stotram viṣṇu arcana āhvayam vedānta sāṃkhya siddhāntaḥ brahma jñānam tathā almakam gītā sāraḥ phala utkīrtiḥ pūrva khaṇḍaḥ ayam īritaḥ yatra tārkṣyeṇa saṃpṛṣṭaḥ bhagavān āha vāḍavāḥ dharma prakaṭanam pūrvam yoginām gati kāraṇam ṣoḍaśa śrāddha phalakaḥ vṛttāntaḥ ca atra varṇitaḥ preta pīḍām vinirddeśaḥ preta cihna nirūpaṇam pretānām carita ākhyānam kāraṇam preta tām prati preta kṛtya vicāraḥ ca sarpiḍīkaraṇa uktayaḥ preta tva mokṣaṇa ākhyānam dānāni ca vimuktaye mṛtyoḥ pūrva kriyā ākhyānam paścāt karma nirūpaṇam madhya ṣoḍaśaka śrāddham svarga prāpti kriyā ūhanam sūtakasya atha saṃkhyā aṃnam nārāyaṇa bali kriyā apamṛtyu kriyā uktiḥ ca vipākaḥ karmaṇām nṛṇām kṛtyā akṛtya vicāraḥ ca viṣṇu dhyāna vimuktaye brahmāṇḍa aneka caritam brahmajīva nirūpaṇam ātyantikam laya ākhyānam phala stuti nirūpaṇam iti etat gāruḍam nāma purāṇam bhukti mukti dam kīrtitam pāpa śamanam paṭhatām śṛṇvatām nṛṇām sauvarṇa haṃsa yugma āḍhyam viprāya sa divam vrajet iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde gāruḍānukramaṇīvarṇanam nāma aṣṭottaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu vatsa pravakṣyāmi brahmāṇḍa ākhyam purātanam prakriyā ākhyaḥ anuṣaṅga ākhyaḥ upodghātaḥ tṛtīyakaḥ caturthaḥ upasaṃhāraḥ pādāḥ catvāraḥ eva hi pūrva pāda dvayam pūrvaḥ bhāgaḥ atra samudāhṛtaḥ ādau kṛtya samuddeśaḥ naimiṣa ākhyānakam tatas eṣa vai prathamaḥ pādaḥ dvitīyam śṛṇu mānada kalpa manvantara ākhyānam loka jñānam tatas param mānasī sṛṣṭi kathanam rudra prasava varṇanam mahādeva vibhūtiḥ ca ṛṣi sargaḥ tatas param agnīnām vijayaḥ ca atha kāla sadbhāva varṇanam priyavrata anvaya uddeśaḥ pṛthivī āyāma vistaraḥ varṇanam bhāratasya asya tatas anyeṣām nirūpaṇam nīlakaṇṭha āhvaya ākhyānam mahādevasya vaibhavam amāvāsyā anukathanam yuga tattva nirūpaṇam yuga prajā lakṣaṇam ca ṛṣi pravara varṇanam vedānām vyasana ākhyānam svāyambhuva nirūpaṇam śeṣa manvantara ākhyānam pṛthivīdohanam tatas cākṣuṣe adyatane sarge dvitīyaḥ aṅghriḥ puras dale prajāpati anvayaḥ tasmāt deva ādīnām samudbhavaḥ kāśyapeya anukathanam ṛṣi vaṃśa nirūpaṇam ikṣvāku vaṃśa kathanam vaṃśaḥ atreḥ su mahātmanaḥ yayāticaritam ca atha yadu vaṃśa nirūpaṇam vṛṣṇi vaṃśa anukathanam sagarasya atha saṃbhavaḥ bhārgavasya anucaritam pitṛ kārya vadha āśrayam deva asura āhava kathā kṛṣṇa āvirbhāva varṇanam indrasya tu stavaḥ puṇyaḥ śukreṇa parikīrtitaḥ viṣṇu māhātmya kathanam bali vaṃśa nirūpaṇam vaivasvata antar ākhyānam vistareṇa yathātathām pūrvam eva samuddiṣṭam saṃkṣepāt iha kathyate bhaviṣyāṇām manūnām ca caritam hi tatas param kalpa pralaya nirdeśaḥ kāla mānam tatas param lokāḥ caturddaśa tatas kathitāḥ prāpta lakṣaṇaiḥ varṇanam narakāṇām ca vikarma ācaraṇaiḥ tatas manaḥ maya pura ākhyānam layaḥ prākṛtikaḥ tatas śaivasya atha purasya api varṇanam ca tatas param trividhā guṇa saṃbandhāt jantūnām kīrtitā gatiḥ anvaya vyatirekābhyām varṇanam hi tatas param iti eṣaḥ upasaṃhāra pādaḥ vṛttaḥ saha uttaraḥ catuṣpādam purāṇam te brahmāṇḍam samudāhṛtakam aṣṭādaśam anaupamyam sārāt sārataram dvija brahmāṇḍam yat catur lakṣam purāṇam yena vaṭhyate tat etat asya gaditam atra aṣṭādaśadhā pṛthak pāsaśaryeṇa muninā sarveṣām api mānada vastutas tu upadeṣṭrā atha munīnām bhāvitātmanām mattaḥ śrutvā purāṇāni lokebhyaḥ pracakāśire munayaḥ dharma śīlāḥ te dīna anugraha kāriṇaḥ mayā acā idam purāṇam tu vasiṣṭāya purā uditam tena śakti sutāya uktam jātūkarṇyāya tena ca yaḥ idam kīrtayet vatsa śṛṇoti ca samāhitaḥ vastreṇa ācchāditam yaḥ tu brāhmaṇāya prayacchati sa yā ādi brahmaṇaḥ lokam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā marīce aṣṭādaśa etāni mayā proktāni yāni te purāṇāni tu saṃkṣepāt śrotavyāni ca vistarāt aṣṭādaśa purāṇāni yaḥ śṛṇoti narottamaḥ sūtram etat purāṇānām yat mayā uktam tava adhunā tat nityam śīlanīyam hi purāṇa phalam icchatā na dāṃbhikāya pāpāya deva guru anusūyave deyam kadāpi sādhūnām dveṣiṇe na śaṭhāya ca śāntāya śama cittāya śuśrūṣā abhiratāya ca nirmatsarāya śucaye deyam sat vaiṣṇavāya ca iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde brahmāṇḍapurāṇānukramaṇīnirūpaṇam nāma navottaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca purāṇa sūtram akhilam śrutam tava mukhāt vibho marūcaye yathā proktam brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā adhunā tu mahābhāga tithīnām vai kathānakam yasmin māse tu yā puṇyā tithiḥ yena uvāsitā yat vidhānam ca pūjā ādeḥ tat sarvam vada sāṃpratam sanātanaḥ uvāca śṛṇu nārada vakṣyāmi tithīnām te vratam pṛthak tatra kāryā mahāśāntiḥ sarva kalmaṣa nāśinī sarva utpāta praśamanī kali duṣkṛta hāriṇī āyuḥ pradā puṣṭi karī dhana saubhāgya varddhinī pādya ardhya puṣpa dhūpaiḥ ca vastra alaṅkāra bhojanaiḥ homaiḥ bali upahāraiḥ ca tathā brāhmaṇa tarpaṇaiḥ tatas krameṇa devebhyaḥ pūjā kāryā pṛthak pṛthak kṛtvā uṅkāra namaskāram kuśa udaka tila akṣataiḥ dakṣiṇām veda viduṣe vrata saṃpūrti hetave evam pūjā viśeṣeṇa vratam syāt sauri saṃjñakam ārogya dam nṛṇām vipra tasmin eva dine mune tilakam nāma ca proktam kṛṣṇena ajātaśatrave atha jyeṣṭhe site pakṣe pakṣatyām divasa udaye deva udyāna bhavam hṛdyam karavīram samarcayet prarūḍha saptadhānyaiḥ ca nāragaiḥ bījapūrakaiḥ abhyukṣya akṣata toyena mantreṇa ittham kṣamāpayet karavīra vṛṣāvāsa namaḥ te bhānu vallabha daṃbholi mṛḍa durga ādi devānām satatam priya ākṛṣṇena iti veda ukta mantreṇa ittham kṣamāpayet evam bhaktyā samabhyacya dattvā viprāya dakṣiṇām pradakṣiṇam tatas kuryāt paścāt sva bhavanam vrajet dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām nidānam paramam vratam somavāram samārabhya sa ardha māsa trayam dvija kārtika sita bhūtāyām upoṣyam vrata tatparaḥ pūrṇāyām śivam abhyarcya vaṃśa saṃyutam vāyanam su mahat puṇyam devatā prīti vardhakam naivedyam tu pacet maunī ṣoḍaśa triguṇāni ca phalāni piṣṭa pakvāni dadyāt viprāya ṣoḍaśa devāya ṣoḍaśa anyāni bhujyante ṣoḍaśa ātmanā idam kṛtvā vratam vipra deva devasya śūlinaḥ caturdaśa abdam deha antam bhukta bhogaḥ śivam vrajet āśvine sita pakṣatyām katvā aśokavratam naraḥ aśoka pūjanam tatra kāryam niyama tatparaiḥ vrata ante dvādaśe varṣe mūrtim ca aśoka śākhinaḥ pūrvāhne pūjayet devīm ghaṭa sthāpana pūrvakam aṅkura āropaṇam kṛtvā yavaiḥ godhūma miśritaiḥ upavāsam yathāśakti pūjā pāṭha japa ādikam mārkaṃṇḍeya purāṇa uktam carita tritayam dvija paṭhanīyam nava dinam bhukti muktī abhīpsatā kumārī pūjanam tatra praśastam bhojana ādibhiḥ jāyate bhuvi durgāyāḥ prasādāt na atra saṃśayaḥ viśeṣāt annakūṭa ākhyam viṣṇu prīti vivardhanam samarcya dakṣiṇīkṛtya bhukti muktī samāpnuyāt naktam viṣṇu arcanam homaiḥ sauvarṇīm hutabhuj tanum evam kṛtvā dhanaiḥ dhānyaiḥ samṛddhaḥ jāyate bhuvi māgha śukla ādya divase vahnim sākṣāt maheśvaram dhūli dhūsara sarva aṅgam jalaiḥ ukṣet samantataḥ karmaṇā laukikena api saṃtuṣṭaḥ hi maheśvaraḥ vaiśākhe tu sita ādyāyām viṣṇum viśva vihāriṇam evam śuci sita ādyāyām brahmāṇam jagatām gurum viṣṇunā sahitaḥ brahmā sarva loka īśvara īśvaraḥ āsu dvādaśa māsānām pratipatsu dvijottama bhojane tu haviṣyānnam sāmānyatas udāhṛtam iti śrī bṛhat anāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde dvādaśamāsapratipadvratanirūpaṇam nāma daśottaraśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sanātanaḥ uvāca śṛṇu vipra pravakṣyāmi dvitīyāyāḥ vratāni te caitra śukla dvitīyāyām ca sa śaktikam pūrṇa yātrā vrate hi asmin dadhnā vā api ghṛtena ca surūpa rūpaḥ ari gaṇa pratāpī dharma abhirāmaḥ nṛpa varga mukhyaḥ rādha śukla dvitīyāyām brahmaṇam viṣṇu rūpiṇam samarcya sapta dhānyāni āḍhya kuṃbha upari vidhānataḥ viṣṇu lokam avāpnoti bhuktvā bhogān manoramān jyeṣṭha śukla dvitīyāyām bhāskaram bhuvana adhipam bhojayitvā dvijān bhaktyā bhāskaram lokam āpnuyāt āṣāḍhasya site pakṣe dvitīyā puṇya saṃyutā tasyām ratham samāropya rāmam saha subhadrayā jalāśaya antikam gatvā kārayet ca mahā utsavam nabhaḥ śukla dvitīyāyām viśvakarmā prajāpatiḥ svapiti iti tithiḥ puṇyā hi aśokaśayana āhvayā śrīvatsa dhārin śrīkānta śrīvāsa śrīpate prabho gārhasthyam mā praṇāśam me yātu dharma artha kāma da bhādra śukla dvitīyāyām śakra rūpam jagat vidhim āśvine māsi vai puṇyā dvitīyā śuklapakṣa gā ūrjja śukla dvitīyāyām yamaḥ yamunayā purā bhojitaḥ sva gṛhe tena dvitīyā eṣā yama āhvayā puṣṭi pravarddhanam ca atra bhaginyāḥ bhojanam gṛhe mārga śukla dvitīyāyām śrāddhena pitṛ pūjanam pauṣa śukla dvitīyāyām gośṛṅga udaka mārjanam sarva kāma pradam nṝṇām āste bāla indu darśanam bāla indum haviṣya āśī jita indriyaḥ māgha śukla dvitīyāyām bhānu rūpam prajāpatim raktaiḥ gaṃvaiḥ tathā svarṇa mūrtim nirmāya śaktitaḥ tatas pūrṇam tāmra pātram gā ghṛmaiḥ vāpī taṇḍulaiḥ evam kṛte vrate vipra sākṣāt sūryaḥ iva uditaḥ durāsadaḥ durādharṣaḥ jāyate bhuvi mānavaḥ iha kāmān varām bhuktvā yātyante brahmaṇaḥ padam sarva deva stutaḥ abhīkṣṇam vimāna varam āsthitaḥ atha phaālguna śuklāyāḥ dvitīyāyām dvijottamaḥ puṣpaiḥ vitānakam kṛtvā puṣpa alaṅkaraṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ prasādya praṇamet ca eva sa aṣṭāṅgam patitaḥ bhuvi yat vidhānam dvitīyāsu śuklapakṣa gatāsu vā proktam tat eva kṛṣṇāsu karttavyam vidhi kovidaiḥ vahniḥ eva pṛthak māḥsu nānā rūpa vapurddharaḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde dvādaśamāsadvitīyāvratanirūpaṇam nāma ekādaśa adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sanātanaḥ uvāca śṛṇu nārada vakṣyāmi tṛtīyāyāḥ vratāni te yāni samyak vidhāya āśu nārī saubhāgyam āpnuyāt caitra śukla tṛtīyāyām gaurīm kṛtvā sa bhartṛkām sauvarṇāḥ rājatīm vā api tāmnīm vā mṛṇyayīm dvija dūrvā kāṇḍaiḥ ca vidhivat sa upavāsā tu kanyakā dvija bhāryāḥ bhartṛmatīḥ kanyakām vā su lakṣaṇāḥ siṃdūra añjana vastra ādyaiḥ pratoṣya prīta mānasā rātrau jāgaraṇam kuryāt vrata saṃpūrti kāmyayā dhātu jām mṛd mayīm vā tu nikṣipet ca jalāśaye evam dvādaśa varṣāṇi kṛtvā gaurīvratam śubham strīṇām yathā tathā na anyā vidyate bhuvanatraye dhanam putrān patim vidyām ājñā siddhim yaśaḥ sukham rādha śukla tṛtīyā yā sā akṣayā parikīrtitā tithiḥ trotā yuga ādyā sā kṛtasya akṣaya kāriṇī dve śukle dve tathā kṛṣṇe yuga ādī kavayaḥ viduḥ śukle pūrvāhnike grāhye kṛṣṇe ca eva tapaḥ tatha dvāparam hi kaliḥ bhādre pravṛttāni yugāni vai tatra rādha tṛtīyāyām śrī sametam jagadgurum nārāyaṇam samabhyarcet puṣpa dhūpa vilepanaiḥ yat vā gaṅgā aṃbhasi snātaḥ mucyate sarva kilbiṣaiḥ akṣatnaiḥ pūjayet viṣṇum snāyāt api akṣataiḥ naraḥ evam kṛta vidhiḥ vipra naraḥ viṣṇu parāyaṇaḥ atha jyeṣṭha tṛtīyā tu śuklā raṃbhā iti nāmataḥ tasyām sa bhāryam vidhivat pūjayet vāhmaṇa uttamam gandha puṣpa aṃśuka ādyaiḥ tu nārī saubhāgya kāmyayā dadāti vittam putrān ca matim dharme śubha āvahām atha āṣāḍha tṛtīyāyām śuklāyām śukla vāsasā bhojanaiḥ surabhī dānaiḥ vastraiḥ ca api vibhūṣaṇaiḥ priyeḥ vākyaiḥ bhṛśam prītā nārī saubhāgya vāñchayā nabhaḥ śukla tṛtīyāyām svarṇagaurīvratam caret upacāraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ bhavānīm abhipūjayet evam saṃprārthya deveśīm bhavānīm bhava saṃyutām vrata saṃpūrti kāmā tu vāyanam dāpayet tathā evam ṣoḍaśa varṣāṇi kṛtvā nārī vratam śubham udyāpanam caret bhaktyā vitta śāṭhya vivarjitā maṇḍape maṇḍale śuddhe gaṇeśa ādi sura arcanam kṛtvā tāmra mayam pātram kalaśa upari vinyaset sauvarṇīm pratimām tatra bhavānyāḥ pratipūjayet veṇu pātraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ pakva anna paripūritaiḥ vāyanam ca tatas paścāt dadyāt saṃbandhi bandhuṣu pratimām gurave dattvā dvijebhyaḥ dakṣiṇām tathā pūrṇam labhet phalam nārī vrata ācaraṇa tatparā bhādra śukla tṛtīyāyām vratam vai hāritālakam kuryāt bhaktyā vidhānena pādya ardhya arcana pūrvakam tatas tu kāñcane pātre rājate ca api tāmrake vaiṇave mṛd maye vā api vinyasya annam sa dakṣiṇam tad ante pāraṇam kuryāt iṣṭa bandhu janaiḥ saha evam kṛta vratā nārī bhuktvā bhogān manoramān saubhāgya dravya vastrāṇi vaṃśa pātrāṇi ṣoḍaśa bhūyasīm ca tatas dadyāt viprebhyaḥ devi tuṣṭaye yadā tṛtīyā bhādre tu hasta ṛkṣa sahitā bhavet hastagaurīvratam nāma tat uddiṣṭam hi śauriṇā tathā koṭīśvarī nāma vratam proktam pinākinā lakṣeśvarī ca eva tathā tat vidhānam udīryate asyām vratam tu saṃgrāhyam yāvat varṣa catuṣṭayam akhaṇḍānām taṇḍulānām tilānām vā munīsvara lakṣam ekam viśodhya atha kṣipet payasi saṃsṛte tad pakkena tu nirmāya devyāḥ mūrtim su śomanām prakare gandha puṣpāṇām puṣpa mālā vibhūṣitām saṃsthāpya pārvatīm tatra pūjayet bhakti bhāvitaḥ iṣa śukla tṛtīyāyām bṛbadgaurīvratam caret pañca varṣam vidhānena pūrva uktena eva nārada ācāryam pūjayet ante viprān anyān dhana ādibhiḥ suvāsinīḥ pañca pūjyāḥ vastra alaṅkāra candanaiḥ kañcukaiḥ ca eva tāṭaṅkaiḥ kaṇṭha sūtraiḥ haripriyāḥ vaṃśa pātrāṇi pañca eva sūtraiḥ saṃveṣṭitāni ca siṃdūram jīrakam ca eva saubhāgya dravya saṃyutam godhīma piṣṭa jātam ca nava apūpam argham dattvā vāyanāni paścāt bhuñjīta vāgyatā tatas prātar samutthāya sa alaṅkārā sakhī janaiḥ gīta vādya yutāḥ nadyām gaurīm tām tu visarjayet āhūtā asi mayā abhadre pūjitā ca yathā vidhi mama saubhāgya dānāya yatheṣṭam gamyatām tvayā evam kṛtvā vratam bhaktyā dvija devī prasādataḥ bhuktvā bhogān tu dehānte gaurī lokam avāpnuyāt ūrja śukla tṛtīyāyām viṣṇugaurīvratam caret pūjayitvā jagat vandyām upacāraiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ suvāsinīm bhojayitvā maṅgala dravya pūjitām visarjayet praṇamya enām viṣṇu gaurī pratuṣṭaye mārga śukla tṛtīyāyām haragaurīvratam śubham kṛtvā pūrva vidhānena pūjayet jagat aṃbikām pauṣa śukla tṛtīyāyām brahmagaurīvratam caret māgha śukla tṛtīyāyām pūjyā saubhāgyasuṃdarī pūrva uktena vidhānena nālikera arghya dānataḥ prasannā diśati svīyam lokam tu vrata toṣitā phaālgunasya site pakṣe tṛtīyā kula saukhya dā pūjitā gandha puṣpa ādyaiḥ sarva maṅgala dā bhavet sarvāsu ca tṛtīyāsu vidhiḥ sādhāraṇaḥ mune devī pūjā vipra pūjā dānam homaḥ visarjanam iti evam kathitāni iha tṛtīyāyāḥ vratāni te bhaktyā kṛtāni ca iṣṭān tu kāmān dardyu manaḥ gatān iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde dvādaśamāsatṛtīyāvratakathanam nāma dvādaśa adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sanātanaḥ uvāca śṛṇu vipram pravakṣyāmi caturthyāḥ te vratāni aham yāni kṛtvā narāḥ nāryaḥ abhīṣṭān kāmān avāpnuyuḥ caitra māsa caturthyām tu vāsudeva svarūpiṇam gaṇapam samyak abhyarcya dattvā kāñcana dakṣiṇām viprāya viṣṇu lokam tu gacchet deva namaskṛtaḥ vaiśākhasya caturthyām tu prārthyam saṃkarṣaṇa āhvayam prāpya saṃkarṣaṇam lokam modate bahu kalpakam jyeṣṭha māsa caturthyām tu prārcya pradyumna rūpiṇam āṣāḍhasya caturthyām tu saṃprapūjya aniruddhakam yatibhyaḥ alābu pātrāṇi dattvā abhīṣṭam labhet naraḥ caturmūrti vratāni evam kṛtvā dvādaśa vatsaram tathā āṣāḍha caturthyām tu vratam anyat śubha āvaham śraddhā pūtena manasā gaṇeśam vidhinā naraḥ śrāvaṇasya caturthyām tu jāti candra udaye mune gaṇeśāya pradadyāt ca hi arghyam vidhi vidām varaḥ nānā ratna vibhūṣā āḍhyam prasanna āsyam vicintayet āvāhana ādibhiḥ sarvaiḥ upacāraiḥ samarcayet naivedyam modakam dadyāt gaṇeśa prīti dāyakam sukham svapyāt niśāyām tu bhūmau eva kṛta arcanaḥ vratasya asya prabhāveṇa kāmān manasi cintitān labdhvā leke param ca api gaṇeśa padam āpnuyāt tasmāt kāryam prayatnena sarvān kāmān abhīpsatā bilva patram apāmārgam śamī dūrvā haripriyā ācāryāya vidhi jñāya satkṛtya vinivedayet tatas saṃprārathya vighneśa mūrtim sa upaskarām mune ācāryāya vidhi jñāya satkṛtya vinivedayet kṛtvā evam pañca varṣāṇi samupāsya yathāvidhi tatas pradakṣiṇīkṛtya śaktaḥ ced dānam ācaret pañca abdam vā adaśa abdam vā ṣoḍaśa abdam atha api vā vratam kṛtvā samudyāpya dhenum dadyāt payasvinīm satkṛtaḥ devatā vṛndaiḥ golokam samavāpnuyāt āvāhana ādibhiḥ sarvaiḥ upacāraiḥ samarcanam ekāgra mānasaḥ bhūtvā dhyāyet siddhivināyakam pāśa aṅkuśa dharam devam tapta kāñcana sannibham ekaviṃśati patrāṇi ca ekaviṃśati nāmabhiḥ samarpayet bhakti yuktaḥ tāni nāmāni vai śṛṇu sumukhāya śamī patram gaṇa adhīśāya bhṛṅga jam umā putrāya bailvam tu dūrvām gajamukhāya ca laṃbodarāya badarīm dhattūram hara sūnave śūrpakarṇāya tulasīm vakratuṇḍāya śiṃbijam guhā agrajāya apāmārgam eka dantāya bārhatam dūrvā yugmam tatas gṛhya gandha puṣpa akṣataiḥ yutam vināyakasya pratimām haimīm sa upaskarām mune evam kṛta arcanaḥ bhaktyā pañca varṣāṇi nārada upāsya labhate kāmān aihika āmuṣmikān śubhān asyām caturthyām śaśinam na paśyet ca kadācana paśyan mithyā abhiśāpa tu labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ atha tad doṣa nāśāya mantram paurāṇikam paṭhet siṃhaḥ prasenam amadhīt siṃhaḥ jāṃbavatā hataḥ iṣa śukla caturthyām tu kaparddīśam vināyakam tu sūktena pūjayet upacārakaiḥ akāraṇāt muṣṭi gatān taṇḍulān sa kaparddikān viprāya baṭave dadyāt gandha puṣpa arcitāya ca taṇḍulāḥ vaiśvadaivatyāḥ hara daivatya miśritāḥ kapardi gaṇanāthaḥ asau prīyatām taiḥ samarpitaiḥ caturthyām kārtike kṛṣṇe karaka ākhyam vratam smṛtam strīṇām eva adhikāraḥ atra tad vidhānam udīryate pūjayet ca gaṇādhīśam snātā strī samalaṅkṛtā tad agre pūrṇa pakva annam vinyaset karakān daśa su vāsinībhyaḥ viprebhyaḥ yathākāmam ca sādaram bhuñjīta miṣṭam annam ca vratasya paripūrtaye yat vā kṣīreṇa karakam pūrṇam toyena vā mune sa pūga akṣata ratna āḍhyam dvijāya pratipādayet etat kṛtvā vratam nārī ṣoḍaśa dvādaśa abdakam yāvajjīvam tu vā nāryā kāryyam saubhāgya vāñchayā vratena anena sadṛśam strīṇām saubhāgya dāyakam ūrjja śukla caturthyām tu nāgavratam udāhṛtam prātar vratam tu saṃkalpya dhenu śṛñjagalam śuci pītvā snātvā atha madhyāhne śaṅkhapāla ādi pannagān śeṣam ca āhvāma pūrvaiḥ tu pūjayet upacārakaiḥ kṣīreṇa āpyāyanam kuryāt etat nāgavratam smṛtam viṣāṇi naśyanti acirāt na daśanti ca pannagāḥ mārga śukla caturthyām tu varṣam yāvat muni īśvarā a yācita upavāsābhyām tṛtīyaka caturthake evam krameṇa vidhivat catvāri abdāni mānavaḥ kārayet hema ghaṭitam bhū gaṇeḥ mūṣakam ratham tasya upari ghaṭam sthāpya tāmra pātreṇa saṃyutam pūrayet taṇḍalaiḥ śubhraiḥ tasya upari gaṇeśvaram naivedyam modakam kalpyam gaṇeśaḥ prīyatām iti jāgaraiḥ śīta vādya ādyaiḥ purāṇa ākhyānakaiḥ caret prabhāte vimale snātvā homam kṛtvā vidhānataḥ tila vrīhi yava śveta surṣapa ājyaiḥ sa khaṇḍakaiḥ gaṇaḥ gaṇādhipaḥ ca eva kūṣmāṇḍaḥ tripurāntakaḥ brahmā yamaḥ atha varuṇaḥ soma sūrya hutāśanāḥ gandha mādī parameṣṭhī iti evam ṣoḍaśa nāmabhiḥ praṇava ādyaiḥ ṅeṃ namaḥ om ataiḥ pratyekam dahane hunet vakratuṇḍā iti barma antena aṣṭa yuj śatam tatas vyāhṛtibhiḥ śaktyā hutvā pūrṇāhutim caret dikpālān pūjayitvā ca brāhmaṇān bhojayet tatas catutviṃśati saṃkhyākān modakaiḥ pāyasaiḥ tathā sa vatsām gām tatas dadyāt ācāryāya sa dakṣiṇām praṇamya dakṣiṇīkṛtya pravisṛjya dvijottamām bandhubhiḥ saha bhuñjīta svayam ca prīta mānasaḥ etat vratam naraḥ kṛtvā bhuktvā bhogān iha uttamān sāyujyam labhate viṣṇoḥ gaṇeśasya prasādataḥ pauṣa māsa caturthyām tu vighneśam prārthya bhaktitaḥ evam kṛte mune bhūyāt vratī saṃpatti bhājanam māgha kṛṣṇacaturthyām tu saṃkaṣṭavratam ucyate tatas candra udaye prāpte mṛd mayam gaṇanāyakam vidhāya vinyaset pīṭhe sa āyudham ca sa vāhanam upacāraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ samabhyarcya vidhānataḥ modakam ca api naivedyam sa guḍam tilakuṭṭakam sa kuśam ca sa dūrvam ca puṣpa akṣata samanvitam sa śamī patra dadhi ca kṛtvā candrāya dāpayet gagana arṇava māṇikya candra dākṣāyaṇīpate gṛhāṇa arghyam mayā dattam gaṇeśa pratirūpaka evam dattvā gaṇeśāya divya arghyam pāpa nāśanam śaktyā saṃbhojya vipra agryān svayam bhuñjīta ca ājñayā evam kṛtvā vratam vipra saṃkaṣṭa ākhyam śūbha āvaham samṛddhaḥ dhana dhānyaiḥ syāt na ca saṃkaṣṭam āpnuyāt tasyām tu gaurī saṃpūjyā saṃyuktā yoginī gaṇaiḥ naraiḥ strībhiḥ viśeṣeṇa kunda puṣpaiḥ sa kuṅkumaiḥ dhūpaiḥ dīpan ca balibhiḥ sa guḍaina ārdrakeṇa ca payasā pāyasena api lavaṇena ca pālakaiḥ pūjyāḥ ca avidhavāḥ nāryaḥ tathā viprāḥ su śobhanāḥ prativarṣam prakarttavyam nārībhiḥ ca naraiḥ tathā ḍhuṇḍhivratam paraiḥ proktam kaiścid kuṇḍavratam smṛtam snānam dānam japaḥ homaḥ sarvam asyām kṛtam mune bhavet saha sraj uṇitam prasādāt dantinaḥ sadā caturthyām phaālgune māsi ḍhuṇḍhirājavratam śubham tila siṣṭaiḥ dvijān bhojya svayam ca aśnīta mānavaḥ gaṇeśa ārādhana paraḥ dāna homa prapūjanaiḥ tilaiḥ eva kṛtaiḥ siddhim prāpnuyāt tad prasādataḥ sauvarṇam gajavaktram ca kṛtvā saṃpūjya yatnatas sāṃgārakā vā vipra indra sā viśeṣa phala pradā sarvāsu ca caturthīṣu śuklāsu api asitāsu ca iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde dvādśanāsa caturthīvratānirūpaṇam nāma trayodaśa adhika satatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sanātanaḥ uvāca śṛṇu vipra pravakṣyāmi pañcamyāḥ te vratāni aham yāni bhaktyā samāsthāya sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt proktā matsyajayantī tu pañcamī madhu śukla gā asyām matsya avatāra arcā bhaktaiḥ kāryā mahā utsavā śrīpañcamī iti ca eṣā uktā tatra kāryam śriyoḥ acanam yaḥ lakṣmīm pūjayet ca atra tam vai lakṣmīḥ na muñcati pṛthvīvratam tathā cāndram hayagarīvavratam tathā atha vaiśākha pañcamyām śeṣam ca abhyarcya mānavaḥ tathā jyeṣṭhasya pañcamyām pitṝn abhyarcayet sudhīḥ atha āṣāḍhasya pañcamyām vāyum sarva gatam mune dhvajam ca pañca varṇam tu vaṃśa daṇḍa agra saṃsthitam lokapālān samabhyarcya kuryāt vāyu parīkṣaṇam prathama ādiṣu yāmeṣu yaḥ yaḥ vāyuḥ pravartate evam sthitvā nirāhāraḥ tatra yāma catuṣṭayam sāyam āgatya geham svam bhuktvā su alpam samāhitaḥ lokapālān namaskṛtya svapyāt bhūmi tale śucau saḥ eva bhavitā nūnam svapnaḥ iti āha vai śivaḥ aśubhe tu samutpanne śiva pūjā parāyaṇaḥ sa upavāsaḥ nayet aṣṭa yāmam tad dinam eva vā bhojayitvā dvijān aṣṭau tatas śubha phalam labhet śrāvaṇe kṛṣṇa pañcamyām vratam hi anna samṛddhi dam caturthyām dina śeṣe tu sarvāṇi annāni nārada pṛthak pātreṣu saṃsthāpya jalaiḥ āplāvayet sudhīḥ pātra antare tat tu niṣkāsya aṃbu nidhāpayet prātar bhānau samudite pitṝn ca eva tathā ṛṣīn devān ca abhyarcya su snātam kṛtvā naivedyam agratas sarvam dinam kṣipet evam pradoṣe tu śivālaye gatvā saṃpūjayet devam liṅga rūpiṇam īśvaram japet pañcākṣarī vidyām śatam ca api sahasrakam stutvā sarvaiḥ vaundikaiḥ ca paurāṇaiḥ ca api an ākulaḥ prārthayet devam īśānam śaśvat sarva anna siddhaye śāradīyāni ca annāni tathā vāsaṃtikāni api yāni syuḥ taiḥ samṛddhaḥ aham bhūyām janmani janmani evam saṃprārthya deveśam gṛham āgatya vai svakam da tvā annam brāhmaṇa ādibhyaḥ pakvam bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ śrāvaṇe śukla pañca jamyām nṛbhiḥ āstikya tatparaiḥ dvārasya ubhayatas lekhyāḥ gomayena viṣa ulbaṇāḥ gandha ādyaiḥ pūjayet tān ca tathā indrāṇīm anantaram saṃpūjya svarṇa rūpya ādi dadhi akṣata kuśa aṃbubhiḥ tatas pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tat dravyam saṃpraṇamya ca prasannaḥ syāt dhanādhyakṣaḥ svarṇa ādika samṛddhi daḥ etat vratam naraḥ kṛtvā viprān saṃbhojya bhaktitaḥ paścāt svayam ca bhuñjīta dāra apatya suhṛd dṛtaḥ bhādre tu kṛṣṇa pañcamyām nāgān kṣīreṇa tarpayet bhādrasya śukla pañcamyām pūjayet ṛṣi sattamān prātar nadī ādike snātvā kṛtvā nityam atandritaḥ gṛham āgatya yatnena vedikām kārayet mṛdā gomayena upalipya atha kṛtvā puṣpa upaśobhitām tatra āstīrya kuśān vipra ṛṣīn sapta samarcayet gandhaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ dhūpaiḥ dīpaiḥ jamadagniḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca saptā ete ṛṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ naivedyam vipacet vīmān śyāmāka ādyaiḥ akṛṣṭakaiḥ kṛtvā vrata ante varayet ācāryān sapta vaidikān jaṭilāḥ sa akṣasūtrāḥ ca kamaṇḍalu samanvitāḥ saṃsthāpya kalaśeṣu etān tāmreṣu mṛd mayeṣu vā upacāraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ tatas saṃpūjya bhaktitaḥ arghyam da tvā tatas homam tila vrīhi yava ādibhiḥ ṭha saha stomāḥ iti ṛkhāḥ nāma nantraiḥ tu vā pṛthak tatas tu sapta gāḥ dadyāt vastra alaṅkāra saṃyutāḥ ācāryam vastra alaṅkāra bhūṣaṇaiḥ anujñayā guroḥ paścāt mūrtīḥ vipreṣu ca arpayet tatas ca iṣṭaiḥ saha āsīnaḥ svayam brāhmaṇa śeṣitam bhuṅktvā vai ṣaṣ rasa upetam pramudyāt saha bandhubhiḥ etat kṛtvā vratam gāṅgam bhogān bhuktvā atha vāñchitān saptarṣīṇām prasādena vimāna vara gaḥ bhavet āśvine śukla pañcamyām upāṅgalalitāvratam tasyāḥ svarṇa mayīm mūrtim śaktyā nirmāya nārada upacāraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ pūjayet tām vidhānataḥ pakva annam phala saṃyuktam sa ghṛtam dakṣiṇā anvitam sa vāhanā śakti yutā vara dā pūjitā mayā mātar mām anugṛhya atha gamyatām nija mandiram kārtike śukla pañcamyām jayāvratam anuttamam kartavyam pāpa nāśāya śraddhayā dvijasattama pūjayitvā jayām vipra yathāvidhi samāhitaḥ upacāraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ tatas śuciḥ alaṅkṛtaḥ visarjayet tatas paścāt svayam bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ naśyanti tasya pāpāni siṃha ākrāntāḥ mṛgāḥ yathā mārgaśukle ca pañcamyām nāgān iṣṭvā vidhānataḥ pauṣe api śukla pañcamyām sampūjya madhusūdanam labhate bāñchitān kāmān na atra kāryā vicāraṇā pañcamyām pratimāse tu śukle kṛṣṇe ca nārada pitṝṇām pūjanam śastam nāgānām ca api sarvathā iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde dvādaśamāsasthapañcamīvratanirūpaṇam nāma caturdaśa adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sanātanaḥ uvāca śṛṇu vipra pravakṣyāmi ṣaṣṭhyāḥ ca eva vratāni te caitra māse śukla ṣaṣṭhyām kumāravratam uttamam tatra iṣṭvā ṣaṇmukham devam nānā pūjāḥ vidhānataḥ putram sarva guṇa upetam prāpnuyāt cira jīvinam vaiśākha śukla ṣaṣṭhyām ca pūjayitvā ca kārtikam labhate mātṛ jam saukhyam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā jyeṣṭha māse śukla ṣaṣṭhyām vidhinā iṣṭvā divākaram labhate vāñchitān kāmān tad prasādāt na saṃśayaḥ āṣāḍha śukla ṣaṣṭhyām vai skandavratam anuttamam upoṣya pūjayitvā enam śiva umā priyam ātmajam labhate abhīpsitān kāmān putra pautra ādi saṃtatīḥ śrāvaṇe śukla ṣaṣṭhyām tu śarajanmānam arcayet upacāraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ bhaktyā paramayā anvitaḥ labhate abhīpsitān arthān ṣaṇmukhasya prasādataḥ bhādra māse kṛṣṇa ṣaṣṭyām lalitāvratam ucyate prātar snātvā vidhānena nārī śukla ambara āvṛtā śukta mālyaya dharāḥ vā api nadyāḥ saṃgama vālukām gṛhītvā vaṃśa pātre tu dhṛtvā piṇḍa ākṛtim ca tām pañcadhā lalitām tatra dhyāyet vana vilāsinīm paṅkajam karavīram ca nepālīm mālatīm tathā nīlotpalam ketakīm ca saṃgṛhya tagaram tathā ekaika aṣṭaśatam grāhyam aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ eva ca akṣatāḥ kalikāḥ gṛhya tābhiḥ devīm prapūjayet prārthayet agratas sthitvā devīm tām giriśa priyām gaṅgādvāre kuśāvartte vilvake nīlaparvate trapuṣaiḥ api kūṣmāṇḍaiḥ nālikeraiḥ sudāḍimaiḥ bījapūraiḥ su tuḍīraiḥ kāravallaiḥ sa cirbhaṭaiḥ phalaiḥ tad kāla saṃbhūtaiḥ kṛtvā śobhām tad agratas virūḍha dhānya aṅkurakaiḥ su dīpa āvalibhiḥ tathā sāddhai sargaṇakaiḥ dhūpaḥ sauhālaka karañjakaiḥ guḍa puṣpaiḥ karṇaveṣṭaḍaiḥ modakaiḥ upamodakaiḥ gīta vādya naṭaiḥ nṛtyaiḥ prokṣaṇīyaiḥ anekadhā sakhībhiḥ sahitā sādhvī tām rātrim prasabham nayet na ca saṃmīlayet netre nārī yāma catuṣṭayam durbhagā duṣkṛtā vandhyā netra saṃmīlanāt bhavet evam jāgaraṇam kṛtvā saptamyām saritam nayet snātvā gṛham samāgatya hutvā vaiśvānaram tatas devān pitṝn manuṣyān ca pūjayitvā su vāsinīḥ kanyakāḥ ca eva saṃbhojya brāhmaṇān daśa pañca ca bhakṣya bhojyaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ da tvā dānāni bhūriśas naraḥ vā yadi vā nārī tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu mṛteḥ anantaram prāpya śiva lokam sanātanam nabhasye māsi yā śuklā ṣaṣṭhī sā candana āhvayā rohiṇī pāta bhaumaiḥ tu saṃyutā kapilā bhavet labhate vāñchitān kāmān bhāskarasya prasādataḥ anna dānam japaḥ homam pitṛ deva ṛṣi tarpaṇam sarvam eva akṣayam jñeyam kṛtam deva ṛṣi sattama pradadyāt veda viduṣe dvādaśa ātma pratuṣṭaye atha iṣu śukla ṣaṣṭhyām tu pūjyā kātyāyanī dvija tatas kṣamāpya deveśīm praṇipatya visarjayet pūjyā atra saikatī mūrtiḥ yat vā dvijasatī mudā vastra alaṅkaraṇaiḥ bhavyaiḥ kātyāyinyāḥ pratuṣṭaye kanyā varam prāpnuyāt ca vāñcitam putram aṅganā kātyāyinī prasādāt vai na atra kāryā vicāraṇā kārtike śukla ṣaṣṭhyām tu ṣaṇmukhena mahātmanā devasenāḥ mahābhāgā labdhā sarva sura arpitā atas tasyām sura śreṣṭhām devasenām ca ṣaṇmukham prāpnuyāt atulām siddhim manaḥ bhīṣṭām dvijottama atra eva vahni pūjā uktām tām ca sampad samācaret mārgaśīrṣe śakla ṣaṣṭhyām nihataḥ tāraka asuraḥ skandena satkṛtiḥ prāptā brahama ādyaiḥ parikalpitā tatas asyām pūjayet skandam gandha puṣpa akṣataiḥ phalaiḥ vastraiḥ ābhūṣaṇaḥ ca api naivedyaiḥ vividhaiḥ tathā ravi vāreṇa saṃyuktā tathā śatabhiṣā anvitā yadi ced sā samuddiṣṭā caṃpā āhvā muni sattama tasyām viśveśvaraḥ devaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ pāpa nāśanaḥ snāna dāna ādikam ca atra sarvam akṣayyam ucyate pauṣa māse śukla ṣaṣṭhyām devaḥ dinapatiḥ dvija viṣṇu rūpī jagattrātā pradurbhūtāḥ sanātanaḥ sa tasmāt pūjanīyaḥ asyām dravyaiḥ gandha puraskṛtaiḥ māgha māse sitā ṣaṣṭhī varuṇa āhvā smṛtā tu sā tasyām varuṇam abhyarcyet viṣṇu rūpam sanātanam raktaiḥ gandha aṃśukaiḥ puṣpaiḥ naivedyaiḥ dhūpa dīpakaiḥ phaālgune śukla ṣaṣṭhyām tu devam paśupatim dvija mṛd mayam vidhinā kṛttvā pūjayet upacārakaiḥ saṃsnāpya śatarudreṇa pṛthak pañcāmṛtaiḥ jalaiḥ gandhaiḥ ālipya su śvetaiḥ akṣataiḥ śveta puṣpakaiḥ evam naraḥ nārī athavā mune iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde dvādaśamāsasthitaṣaṣṭhīvratanirūpaṇam nāma pañcadaśa adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sanātanaḥ uvāca śṛṇu nārada vakṣyāmi saptamyāḥ te vratāni aham yāni kṛtvā naraḥ bhaktyā sūrya sāyujyam āpnuyāt caitre tu śukla saptamyām bahis snānam samācaret sthaṇḍile gomaya ālipte gauramṛttikayā āstṛte likhitvā aṣṭadalam padmam karṇikāyām vibhāvam kādraveyau mahā nāgau paścime kṛta cārakau teṣām saṃpūjanam kāryam gandha mālya anulepanaiḥ dīpaiḥ dhūpaiḥ sa naivedyaiḥ tāṃbūla kramuka ādibhiḥ evam saṃpūjya homam tu ghṛtena aṣṭaśatam caret sūryasya aṣṭa aṣṭa ca anyeṣām pradadyāt āhutīḥ kramāt nāma mantreṇa vedyām vā tatas pūrṇāhutim dadet dakṣiṇā ca tatas deyā dvijebhyaḥ śaktitas dvija dehānte maṇḍalam bhānoḥ bhattvā gacchet param padam vaiśākha śukla saptamyām jahnunā jāhnavī svayam krodhāt pītā punar tyaktā karṇa randhrāt tu dakṣiṇāt tām tatra pūjayet snātvā pratyūṣe vimale jale gandha puṣpa akṣata ādyaiḥ ca sarvaiḥ eva upacārakaiḥ bhaktyā kṛtam sapta kulam nayet svargam asaṃśayaḥ tila mātram tu sauvarṇam vidhāya kamalam śubham vastra yugma āvṛtam kṛtvā gandha dhūpa ādinā arcayet iti saṃprārthya deveśam sūrye ca astam upāgate saṃbhojya brāhmaṇān bhaktyā vrata sākalyam āpnuyāt ca tatra iva tat vidhānam śṛṇuṣva me niṃba patraiḥ smṛtā pūjā bhāskarasya dvijottama niṃba patram tatas aśnīyāt śayet bhūmau ca vāgyataḥ niṃbapatravratam ca etat kartṛāṇām sarva saukhya dam saptamī śarkarā ākhyā eṣā proktā tat ca api me śṛṇu amṛtam pibataḥ hastāt sūryasya amṛta bindavaḥ niṣpetuḥ bhuvi ca utpannāḥ śāli mudga yavekṣavaḥ śarkarā ca tatas tasmāt ikṣu sāra amṛta upamā iṣṭā raveḥ atas puṇyā śarkarā havya kavyayoḥ śarkarā dānam śarkarā bhojanam tathā yaḥ kuryāt parāyāḥ bhaktyā sa vai sat gatim āpnuyāt jyeṣṭhe tu śukla saptamyām jātaḥ indraḥ raviḥ svayam tam saṃpūjya vidhānena sa upavāsaḥ jita indriyaḥ āṣāḍha śukla saptamyām vivasvān nāma bhāskaraḥ jātaḥ tam tatra saṃprārcya gandha puṣpa ādibhiḥ pṛthak labhate sūrya sāyujyam vipra indra atra na saṃśayaḥ śrāvaṇe śukla saptamyām avyaṅga ākhyam vratam śubham kārpāsam tu catur hastam sārddha vastram hi gopateḥ yadi ced hasta yuktā iyam tadā syāt pāpa nāśinī asyām dānam japaḥ homaḥ sarvam ca akṣayya tām vrajet gaṅgā ādibhiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ upacāraiḥ samarcanam nālikeram ca vṛntākam nāraṅgam bījapūrakam kūṣmāṇḍam bṛhatī pūgam iti sapta phalāni vai saṃpūjya parayā bhaktyā dhārayet vāmake kare strī naraḥ dakṣiṇe ca eva yāvat varṣam samāpyate svayam bhuñjīta matimān vrata saṃpūrti hetave evam tu sapta varṣāṇi kṛtvā upāsya yathāvidhi āśvine śuklapakṣe tu vijñeyā śubhasaptamī tasyām kṛta snāna pūjaḥ vācayitvā dvijottamān ārabhya kapilā aṅgām ca saṃpūjya prārthayet tatas tvām aham dadmi kalyāṇi prīyatām aryamā svayam iti uktvā veda viduṣe dattvā kṛtvā ca dakṣiṇām bhojayitvā svayam ca adyāt tat annam dvija śeṣitam kṛtam hi etat gatam vipra subhāṣyam śraddhayā anvitaḥ atha kārtika śuklāyām śāka ākhyam saptamīvratam tasyām tu sapta śākāni sa svarṇa kamalāni ca pradadyāt sapta viprebhyaḥ śāka āhāraḥ tatas svayam visṛjya bandhubhiḥ sārddham svayam bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ yat viṣṇoḥ dakṣiṇam netram tat eva kṛtavān iha adityām kaśyapāt jajñe mitraḥ nāmā divākaraḥ kṛtvā dvijān bhojayitvā sapta eva madhura ādinā suvarṇa dakṣiṇām da tvā visṛjya aśnīta ca svayam dvijaḥ brāhmam tathā śūdraḥ sat kule janma ca āpnuyāt pauṣasya śukla saptamyām vratam ca abhaya saṃjñitam kṣīra sikta anna saṃbaddham modakam prastha saṃmitam dvijāya da tvā bhojya anyān sapta aṣṭabhyaḥ ca dakṣiṇām pṛthavī vā suvarṇam vā visṛjya aśnīta ca svayam mārtaṇḍa ākhyam vratam nāma kathayanti dvijāḥ pare māghe tu kṛṣṇa saptamyām vratam sarvāpti saṃjñakam sauvarṇam gandha puṣpa ādyaiḥ kṛtvā rātrau ca jāgaram dakṣiṇām nālikerāṇi tebhyaḥ da tvā gurum tatas sauvarṇam tu raveḥ bimbam yuktam dakṣiṇayā nyayā samarpya ca bhṛśam prārthya visṛjya adyāt svayam tatas etat sarva āpti dam nāma saṃproktam sārvakāmikam māghasya śukla saptamyām acala ākhyam vratam smṛtam trilocanajayantī iyam sarva pāpa harā smṛtā ratha ākhyā saptamī ca iyam cakravarti tva dāyinī asyām samarcya savituḥ pratimām tu haimīm haima aśva yukta ratha gām tu dadet saha ibhām bhāskarī saptamī ca iyam koṭi bhāsvat graha upamā aruṇa udaya velāyām asyām snānam vidhīyate nidhāya śirasi snāyāt sapta janma agha śāntaye putra pradam vratam ca atra prāha ādityaḥ svayam prabhuḥ yaḥ māgha sita ptamyām pūjayet mām vidhānataḥ tasya aham putra tām yāsye sva aṃśena bhṛśa toṣitaḥ tasmāt jita indriyaḥ bhūtvā samupoṣya divāniśam pūjayet apare ca ahni homam kṛtvā sarvāsu sarva māseṣu saptamīṣu dvijottamaḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde dvādaśamāsasthitasappamīvratanirūpaṇam nāma ṣoḍaśādhikaśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sanātanaḥ uvāca śukla aṣṭamyām caitra māse bhavānyāḥ procyate janiḥ pradakṣiṇa śatam kṛtvā kāryaḥ yātrā mahā utsavaḥ darśanam jagadambāyāḥ sarva ānanda pradam nṛṇām atra eva aśo kakalikāprāśanam samudāhṛtam aśoka kalikāḥ ca aṣṭau ye pibanti punarvasau caitre māsi sita aṣṭamyām na te śokam avāpnuyuḥ mahāṣṭamī iti ca proktā devyāḥ pūjā vidhānataḥ vaiśākhasya sita aṣṭamyām samupoṣya atra vāriṇā snātvā aparājitām devīm māṃsī bālaka vāribhiḥ kumārīḥ bhojayet ca api navamyām pāraṇa agratas kṛṣṇa aṣṭamyām jyeṣṭha māse pūjayitvā trilocanam jyeṣṭha śukle tathā aṣṭamyām yaḥ devīm pūjayet naraḥ sa vimānena carati gandharva apsarasām gaṇaiḥ śukla aṣṭamyām tathā āṣāḍhe snātvā ca eva niśā aṃbunā tena eva snāpayet devīm pūjayet ca vidhānataḥ tatas śuddha jalaiḥ snāpya viliṃpet sa iṃdu candanaiḥ bhojayitvā tatas viprān datvā svarṇam ca dakṣiṇām visṛjya ca tatas paścāt svayam bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ etat vratam naraḥ kṛtvā devī lokam avāpnuyāt nabhaḥśukle tathā aṣṭamyām devīm iṣṭvā vidhānataḥ kṣīreṇa snāpayitvā ca miṣṭānnam vinivedayet nabhaḥ māse sita aṣṭamyām daśā phalam iti vratam upavāsam tu saṃkalpya snātvā kṛtvā ca naityikam tulasyāḥ kṛṣṇa avarṇāyāḥ dalaiḥ daśabhiḥ arcayet kṛṣṇam viṣṇum tathā anantam govindam garuḍadhvajam dāmodaram hṛṣīkeśam padmanābham harim prabhum etaiḥ ca nāmabhiḥ nityam kṛṣṇa devam samarcayet evam daśa dinam kuryāt vratānām uttamam vratam ādau madhye tathā ca ante homam kuryāt vidhānataḥ kṛṣṇa mantreṇa juhuyāt caruṇā aṣṭa uttaram śatam homa ante vidhinā samyak ācāryyam pūjayet sudhīḥ sauvarṇe tāmra pātre vā mṛd maye veṇu pātrake tulasī dalam suvarṇena kārayitvā su lakṣaṇam haimīm ca pratimām kṛtvā pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ nidhāya pratimām pātre hi ācāryāya nivedayet dātavyā gauḥ sa vatsā ca vastra alaṅkāra bhūṣitā daśa aham kṛṣṇa devāya pūrikāḥ daśa ca arpayet tāḥ ca dadyāt vidhi jñāya svayam vā bhakṣayet vratī śayanam ca pradātavyam yathāśakti dvijottama vrata ante daśa viprebhyaḥ pratyekam daśa pūrikāḥ dadyāt eva daśa abdam tu kṛtvā vratam anuttamam upoṣya vidhinā bhūyāt sarva kāma samanvitaḥ ante kṛṣṇasya sāyujyam labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ kṛṣṇajanmā aṣṭamī ca iyam smṛtā pāpa harā nṛṇām sapta janma kṛtāt pāpāt mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ su deśe maṇḍape kḷpte maṇḍalam racayet sudhīḥ tad madhye kalaśam sthāpya tāmra jam vā api mṛd mayam haimīm vastra yuga ācchannām kṛṣṇasya pratimām śubham devakīm vasudevam ca yaśodām nandam eva ca vrajam gopān tathā gopīḥ gāḥ ca dikṣu samarcayet tatas ārārtikam kṛtvā kṣamāpya ānamya bhaktitaḥ pañcāmṛtaiḥ śuddha jalaiḥ gandha ādyaiḥ pūjayet punar dhānyākam ca yavānīm ca śuṇṭhīm khaṇḍam ca nārada punar ārārtikam kṛtvā daśadhā rūpa dhāriṇam tatas kṣamāpya deveśam rātrikhaṇḍam nayet vratī paurāṇikaiḥ stotra pāṭhaiḥ gīta vādyaiḥ anekadhā da tvā ca dakṣiṇām tebhyaḥ visṛjet tuṣṭa mānasaḥ tatas tām pratimām viṣṇoḥ svarṇa dhenu dharā anvitām gurave dakṣiṇām da tvā visṛjya āśrīta ca svayam dāra apatya suhṛd bhṛtya revam kṛtvā naraḥ sākṣāt gokam āpnoti vimāna varam āsthitaḥ śukla aṣṭamyām nabhasyasya kuryāt rādhāvratam naraḥ pūrvavat rādhikām haimīm kalaśa sthām prapūjayet śaktaḥ bhaktaḥ ca upavāsam pare ahni vidhinā tatas kṛtvā svayam ca bhuñjītam vratam evam samāpayet rahasyam goṣṭha jam labdhvā rādhā parikare vaset dūrvāṣṭamīvratam ca atra kathitam tat ca me śṛṇu śucau deśe prajātāyām dvarvāyām dvijasattama sthāpya liṅgam tatas gandhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ dhūpaiḥ ca dīpakaiḥ arghyam pradadyāt pūjā ante mantrābhyām su samāhitaḥ tvam dūrve amṛta janmā asi sura asura namaskṛte yathā śākhā praśākhābhiḥ vistṛtā asi mahī tale tathā vistṛta saṃtānam dehi me api ajara amaram tatas pradakṣiṇīkṛtya viprān saṃbhojya tatra vai bhuktvā svayam gṛham gacchet atvā vipreṣu dakṣiṇām phalāni ca praśastāni miṣṭāni surabhīṇi ca evam puṇyā pāpa harā nṛṇā dūrvā aṣṭamī dvija caturṇām api varṇānām strī janānām viśeṣataḥ yā na pūjayate dūrvāḥ nārī mohāt yathāvidhi janmāni trīṇi vaidhavyam labhate sā na saṃśayaḥ yadā jyeṣṭha ṛkṣa saṃyuktā bhavet jaivā aṣṭabhī dvija jyeṣṭhā nāmnī tu sā jñeyā pūjitā pāpa nāśinī atha enām tu samārabhya vratam ṣoḍaśa vāsaram mahā lakṣmyāḥ samuddiṣṭam sarva saṃpad vivardhanam kariṣye aham mahā lakṣmī vratam te tvad parāyaṇaḥ ṣoḍaśa granthi sahitam guṇaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ yutam tatas anvaham mahālakṣmīm gandha ādyaiḥ arccayet vratī yāvat kṛṣṇa aṣṭamī tatra caret udyāpanam sudhīḥ vastra maṇḍapikām kṛtvā sarvatobhadra maṇḍale kalaśam su pratiṣṭhāpya dīpam uddyotayet tatas uttārya ḍorakam bāhoḥ kuṃbhasya adhas nivedayet catasraḥ pratimāḥ kṛtvā sauvarṇīḥ tad svarūpiṇīḥ snapanam kārayet tāsāḥ jalaiḥ pañcāmṛtaiḥ tathā upacāraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ tatas niśīthe saṃprāpte abhyudite amṛtadīdhitau datvā arghyam bandhanam dravyaiḥ śrīkhaṇḍa ādyaiḥ vidhānataḥ candra maṇḍala saṃsthāyai mahālakṣyai pradāpayet kṣīroda arṇava saṃbhūta mahā lakṣmī sahodara pīyūṣa dhāma rohiṇyāḥ sahita ar'ghyam gṛhāṇa me kṣīroda arṇava sambhūte kamale kamala ālaye reṇuke trāhi mām devi rāmamātar śivam kuru mantraiḥ etaiḥ mahā lakṣmīm prārthya śrotriya yoṣitaḥ mṛtyuñjayāya ca param sarva roga praśāntaye candanam tāla patram ca puṣpa mālām tathā akṣatān durvām kausumbha sūtram ca yugam śrīphalam eva vā bhakṣyāṇi ca nave śūrpe pratidravyam tu ṣoḍaśa samācchādya anya śūrpeṇa vratī dadyāt sa mantrakam kṣīroda arṇava saṃbhūtā lakṣmīḥ candra sahodarā vratena anena saṃtuṣṭā bhavatāt viṣṇu vallabhā tatas tu caturaḥ viprān ṣoḍaśa api suvāsinīḥ miṣṭānnena āśayitvā tu visṛjet tāḥ sa dakṣiṇāḥ samāpti niyamaḥ paścāt bhañjīta iṣṭaiḥ samanvitaḥ etat vratam mahā lakṣmyāḥ kṛtvā vipra vidhānataḥ bhuktvā iṣṭān aihikān kāmān lakṣmī loke vaset ciram eṣā aṣokā aṣṭamī ca uktā yasyām pūrṇam ramāvratam atra aśokasya pūjā syāt eka bhaktam tathā smṛtam kṛtvā aśokavratam nārī hi aśokā śoka janmani yatra kutra api saṃjātāḥ na atra kāryā vicāraṇā āśvine śukla pakṣe tu proktā vipra mahāṣṭamī upavāsam ca eka bhaktam mahāṣṭamyām vidhāya tu ūrje kṛṣṇa ādike aṣṭamyām karaka ākhyam vratam smṛtam tatra umā sahitaḥ śaṃbhuḥ pūjanīyaḥ prayatnataḥ gopāṣṭamī iti saṃproktā kārtike dhavale dale tatra kuryāt gavām pūjām gogrāsam go pradakṣiṇām gavānugamanam dānam vāñchan sarvāḥ ca saṃpadaḥ kṛṣṇa aṣṭamyām mārgaśīrṣe mithunam darbha nirmitam pūjayet gandha puṣpa ādyaiḥ upacāraiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ saṃbhojya dvija dāṃpatyam visṛjet labdha dakṣiṇam vratam etat naraḥ kṛtvā nārī vā vidhi pūrvakam putram sat lakṣaṇa upetam labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ mārgāśīrṣa sita aṣṭamyām kālabhairava sannidau upoṣya jāgaram kṛtvā mahā pāpaiḥ pramucyate yat kiñcid aśubham karma kṛtam mānuṣa janmani tat sarvam vilayam yāti kālabhairava darśanāt atha pauṣa sita aṣṭamyām śrāddham aṣṭaka saṃjñitam pitṝṇām tṛpti dam varṣam kula santati varddhanam śukla aṣṭamyām tu pauṣasya śivam sampūjya bhaktitaḥ kṛṣṇa aṣṭamyām tu māghasya bhadrakālīm samarcayet māgha māse sita aṣṭamyām bhīṣmam saṃtarpayat dvija saṃtatim tu avyavacchinnām icchan ca api aparājayam phaālgune tu asita aṣṭamyām bhīprām devīm samarcayet śukla aṣṭamyām phaālgunasya śivam ca api śivām dvija phaālguna aparapakṣe tu śītalām aṣṭamī dine pūjayet sarva avapakkānaiḥ saptamyām vidhivat kṛtaiḥ śītale tvam jagat mātā śītale tvam jagat pitā śītale tvam jagat vātrī śītalāyai namaḥ namaḥ vande aham śītalām devīm rāsabha sthām diś aṃbarām mārjanī kalaśa upetām visphoṭaka vināśinīm śītale śītale ca ittham ye japanti jale //ṭha teṣām tu śītalā devī syāt visphoṭaka śānti dā tasya varṣam bhavet śāntiḥ śītalāyāḥ prasādataḥ sarva māsa ubhaye pakṣe vidhivat ca aṣṭamī dine śivām vā api śivam prārcya labhate vāñchitam phalam iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde dvādaśa māsasthitāṣṭamīvratakathanam nāma saptadaśa adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sanātanaḥ uvāca yāni kṛtvā narāḥ loke labhante vāñchitam phalam caitrasya śukla pakṣe tu śrī rāma navamīvratam viprān saṃbhojya miṣṭa annaiḥ rāma prīti sumācaret go bhū tila hari raṇya ādyeḥ vastra alaṅkaraṇeḥ tathā eva yaḥ kurute bhaktyā śrī rāma navamīvratam vidhūya ca iha pāpāni vraje dviṣṇoḥ param padam uktam mātṛvratam ca atra bhairaveṇa samanvitāḥ atra eva tu yoginīnām mahā balā brāhmaṇa śreṣṭhaḥ sarvāsām ādhipatye abhiṣecitā tasmāt tām pūjayet ca atra sa upavāsaḥ jita indriyaḥ rādhe navamyām dalayoḥ caṇḍikām yaḥ tu pūjayet jyeṣṭha śukla navamyām tu sa upavāsaḥ nara uttamaḥ umām saṃpūjya vidhivat kumārīḥ bhojayet dvijān sva bhaktyā dakṣiṇām da tvā śāli annam payasā aśnuyāt āṣāḍhe māsi vipra indra yaḥ kuryāt pakṣayoḥ dvija naktam ca aindrīm samabhyarcyet airāvata gatām sitām pakṣayoḥ upavāsam vā kaumārīm caṇḍikām yajet evam pāpa harām gandhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ dhūpaiḥ ca dīpakaiḥ bhādre tu navamī śuklā nandāhvā parikīrtitā tasyām yaḥ pūjayet durgām vidhivat ca upacārakaiḥ saḥ aśvamedha phalam labdhvā viṣṇu loke mahīyate āśvine śukla navamī mahā pūrvā prakīrtitā aparāhne śamī pūjā kāryā asyām prāc diśi dvija tatas niśāyām prāc yāme khaḍgam dhanuḥ iṣūn gadām śūlam śaktim ca paraśum śirikām carma kheṭakam chatram dhvajam gajam ca aśva go vṛṣam pustakam tulām daṇḍam pāśam cakra śaṅkhau gandha ādyaiḥ upacārakaiḥ evam balim vidhāya atha bhuktvā pakka annam eva ca dvijebhyaḥ dakṣiṇām da tvā vratam tatra samāpayet evam yaḥ pūjayet durgām nṝṇām durgati nāśinīm kārtike śukla navamī yā akṣayā sā devānām ca ṛṣīṇām ca pitṝṇām ca api nārada sva śākhā uktaiḥ tathā mantraiḥ sūryāya arghyam tatas dvijān bhojayitvā miṣṭānnena muni īśvara evam yaḥ kurute bhaktyā japa dānam dvija arcanam mārge tu śukla navamī nandinī parikīrtitā tasyām upoṣitaḥ yaḥ tu jagadaṃbām prapūjayet gandha ādyaiḥ saḥ aśvamedhasya phala bhāj na atra saṃśayaḥ pauṣe śukla navamyām tu mahāmāyām prapūjayet māgha māse tu vā śuklā navamī loka pūjitā mahānandā iti sā proktā sat ānanda karī nṛṇām tasyām snānam tathā dānam japaḥ homaḥ upoṣaṇam sarvam akṣaya tām yāti na atra kāryā vicāraṇā ānandā sā mahā puṇyā sarva pāpa harā smṛtā sa labhet vāñchitān kāmān satyam satyam mayā uditam iti śrī bṛhat nāradīyapurāṇe pūrva bhāge bṛhat upākhyāne caturtha pāde dvādaśa māsasthitanavamīvratakathanam nāma aṣṭādaśa adhika śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sanātanaḥ uvāca atha te aham pravakṣyāmi daśamyāḥ vai vratāni ca caitra śukla da śamyām tu dharmarājam prapūjayet caturddaśa tatas tebhyaḥ śaktyā dadyāt ca dakṣiṇām daśamyām mādhave śukle viṣṇum
